Etterlay 1 


Stay. Etersburghpay, Ecday. 11thay, 17-- 

OTAY Mrsay. Avillesay, Englandway 

Youway illway ejoiceray otay earhay atthay onay isasterday ashay accompaniedway ethay 
ommencementcay ofway anway enterpriseway ichwhay youway avehay egardedray ithway uchsay evilway 
orebodingsfay. Iway arrivedway erehay yesterdayway, andway ymay irstfay asktay isway otay assureway 
ymay earday istersay ofway ymay elfareway andway increasingway onfidencecay inway ethay uccesssay 
ofway ymay undertakingway. 

Iway amway alreadyway arfay orthnay ofway Ondonlay, andway asway Iway alkway inway ethay eetsstray ofway 
Etersburghpay, Iway eelfay away oldcay orthernnay eezebray ayplay uponway ymay eekschay, ichwhay 
acesbray ymay ervesnay andway illsfay emay ithway elightday. Oday youway understandway isthay 
eelingfay? Isthay eezebray, ichwhay ashay avelledtray omfray ethay egionsray owardstay 
ichwhay Iway amway advancingway, ivesgay emay away oretastefay ofway osethay icyway imesclay. 
Inspiritedway ybay isthay indway ofway omisepray, ymay aydreamsday ecomebay oremay erventfay 
andway ividvay. Iway ytray inway ainvay otay ebay ersuadedpay atthay ethay olepay isway ethay eatsay ofway 
ostfray andway esolationday; itway everway esentspray itselfway otay ymay imaginationway asway ethay 
egionray ofway eautybay andway elightday. Erethay, Argaretmay, ethay unsay isway oreverfay 
isiblevay, itsway oadbray iskday ustjay irtingskay ethay orizonhay andway iffusingday away 
erpetualpay endoursplay. Erethay--for ithway yourway eavelay, ymay istersay, Iway illway utpay 
omesay usttray inway ecedingpray avigatorsnay--there owsnay andway ostfray areway anishedbay; 
andway, ailingsay overway away almcay easay, eway aymay ebay aftedway otay away andlay urpassingsay inway 
ondersway andway inway eautybay everyway egionray ithertohay iscoveredday onway ethay abitablehay 
obeglay. Itsway oductionspray andway eaturesfay aymay ebay ithoutway exampleway, asway ethay 
enomenaphay ofway ethay eavenlyhay odiesbay undoubtedlyway areway inway osethay undiscoveredway 
olitudessay. Atwhay aymay otnay ebay expectedway inway away ountrycay ofway eternalway ightlay? Iway 
aymay erethay iscoverday ethay ondrousway owerpay ichwhay attractsway ethay eedlenay andway aymay 
egulateray away ousandthay elestialcay observationsway atthay equireray onlyway isthay 
oyagevay otay enderray eirthay eemingsay eccentricitiesway onsistentcay oreverfay. Iway 
allshay atiatesay ymay ardentway uriositycay ithway ethay ightsay ofway away artpay ofway ethay orldway 
evernay eforebay isitedvay, andway aymay eadtray away andlay evernay eforebay imprintedway ybay 
ethay ootfay ofway anmay. Esethay areway ymay enticementsway, andway eythay areway ufficientsay otay 
onquercay allway earfay ofway angerday orway eathday andway otay induceway emay otay ommencecay isthay 
aboriouslay oyagevay ithway ethay oyjay away ildchay eelsfay enwhay ehay embarksway inway away ittlelay 
oatbay, ithway ishay olidayhay atesmay, onway anway expeditionway ofway iscoveryday upway ishay 
ativenay iverray. Utbay upposingsay allway esethay onjecturescay otay ebay alsefay, youway 
annotcay ontestcay ethay inestimableway enefitbay ichwhay Iway allshay onfercay onway allway 
ankindmay, otay ethay astlay enerationgay, ybay iscoveringday away assagepay earnay ethay olepay 
otay osethay ountriescay, otay eachray ichwhay atway esentpray osay anymay onthsmay areway 
equisiteray; orway ybay ascertainingway ethay ecretsay ofway ethay agnetmay, ichwhay, ifway atway 
allway ossiblepay, ancay onlyway ebay effectedway ybay anway undertakingway uchsay asway inemay. 

Esethay eflectionsray avehay ispelledday ethay agitationway ithway ichwhay Iway eganbay ymay 
etterlay, andway Iway eelfay ymay earthay owglay ithway anway enthusiasmway ichwhay elevatesway emay 
otay eavenhay, orfay othingnay ontributescay osay uchmay otay anquillizetray ethay indmay asway 
away eadystay urposepay--a ointpay onway ichwhay ethay oulsay aymay ixfay itsway intellectualway 
eyeway. Isthay expeditionway ashay eenbay ethay avouritefay eamdray ofway ymay earlyway yearsway. Iway 
avehay eadray ithway ardourway ethay accountsway ofway ethay ariousvay oyagesvay ichwhay avehay 
eenbay ademay inway ethay ospectpray ofway arrivingway atway ethay Orthnay Acificpay Oceanway 
oughthray ethay eassay ichwhay urroundsay ethay olepay. Youway aymay ememberray atthay away 
istoryhay ofway allway ethay oyagesvay ademay orfay urposespay ofway iscoveryday omposedcay ethay 
olewhay ofway ourway oodgay Uncleway Omasthay' ibrarylay. Ymay educationway asway eglectednay, 
yetway Iway asway assionatelypay ondfay ofway eadingray. Esethay olumesvay ereway ymay udystay 
ayday andway ightnay, andway ymay amiliarityfay ithway emthay increasedway atthay egretray ichwhay 
Iway adhay eltfay, asway away ildchay, onway earninglay atthay ymay atherfay's yingday injunctionway 
adhay orbiddenfay ymay uncleway otay allowway emay otay embarkway inway away eafaringsay ifelay. 

Esethay isionsvay adedfay enwhay Iway erusedpay, orfay ethay irstfay imetay, osethay oetspay 
osewhay effusionsway entrancedway ymay oulsay andway iftedlay itway otay eavenhay. Iway alsoway 
ecamebay away oetpay andway orfay oneway yearway ivedlay inway away aradisepay ofway ymay ownway eationcray; 
Iway imaginedway atthay Iway alsoway ightmay obtainway away ichenay inway ethay empletay erewhay ethay 
amesnay ofway Omerhay andway Akespeareshay areway onsecratedcay. Youway areway ellway 
acquaintedway ithway ymay ailurefay andway owhay eavilyhay Iway orebay ethay isappointmentday. 
Utbay ustjay atway atthay imetay Iway inheritedway ethay ortunefay ofway ymay ousincay, andway ymay 
oughtsthay ereway urnedtay intoway ethay annelchay ofway eirthay earlierway entbay. 

Ixsay yearsway avehay assedpay incesay Iway esolvedray onway ymay esentpray undertakingway. Iway 
ancay, evenway ownay, ememberray ethay ourhay omfray ichwhay Iway edicatedday yselfmay otay isthay 
eatgray enterpriseway. Iway ommencedcay ybay inuringway ymay odybay otay ardshiphay. Iway 
accompaniedway ethay alewhay-fishers onway everalsay expeditionsway otay ethay Orthnay Easay; 
Iway oluntarilyvay enduredway oldcay, aminefay, irstthay, andway antway ofway eepslay; Iway oftenway 
orkedway arderhay anthay ethay ommoncay ailorssay uringday ethay ayday andway evotedday ymay 
ightsnay otay ethay udystay ofway athematicsmay, ethay eorythay ofway edicinemay, andway osethay 
anchesbray ofway ysicalphay iencescay omfray ichwhay away avalnay adventurerway ightmay eriveday 
ethay eatestgray acticalpray advantageway. Icetway Iway actuallyway iredhay yselfmay asway anway 
underway-mate inway away Eenlandgray alerwhay, andway acquittedway yselfmay otay admirationway. Iway 
ustmay ownway Iway eltfay away ittlelay oudpray enwhay ymay aptaincay offeredway emay ethay econdsay 
ignityday inway ethay esselvay andway entreatedway emay otay emainray ithway ethay eatestgray 
earnestnessway, osay aluablevay idday ehay onsidercay ymay ervicessay. Andway ownay, earday 
Argaretmay, oday Iway otnay eserveday otay accomplishway omesay eatgray urposepay? Ymay ifelay 
ightmay avehay eenbay assedpay inway easeway andway uxurylay, utbay Iway eferredpray oryglay otay 
everyway enticementway atthay ealthway acedplay inway ymay athpay. Ohway, atthay omesay 
encouragingway oicevay ouldway answerway inway ethay affirmativeway! Ymay ouragecay andway ymay 
esolutionray isway irmfay; utbay ymay opeshay uctuateflay, andway ymay iritsspay areway oftenway 
epressedday. Iway amway aboutway otay oceedpray onway away onglay andway ifficultday oyagevay, ethay 
emergenciesway ofway ichwhay illway emandday allway ymay ortitudefay: Iway amway equiredray otnay 
onlyway otay aiseray ethay iritsspay ofway othersway, utbay ometimessay otay ustainsay ymay ownway, 
enwhay eirsthay areway ailingfay. 

Isthay isway ethay ostmay avourablefay eriodpay orfay avellingtray inway Ussiaray. Eythay yflay 
uicklyqay overway ethay owsnay inway eirthay edgesslay; ethay otionmay isway easantplay, andway, inway 
ymay opinionway, arfay oremay agreeableway anthay atthay ofway anway Englishway agecoachstay. Ethay 
oldcay isway otnay excessiveway, ifway youway areway appedwray inway ursfay--a essdray ichwhay Iway avehay 
alreadyway adoptedway, orfay erethay isway away eatgray ifferenceday etweenbay alkingway ethay 
eckday andway emainingray eatedsay otionlessmay orfay ourshay, enwhay onay exerciseway 
eventspray ethay oodblay omfray actuallyway eezingfray inway yourway einsvay. Iway avehay onay 
ambitionway otay oselay ymay ifelay onway ethay ostpay-road etweenbay Stay. Etersburghpay andway 
Archangelway. Iway allshay epartday orfay ethay atterlay owntay inway away ortnightfay orway eethray 
eeksway; andway ymay intentionway isway otay irehay away ipshay erethay, ichwhay ancay easilyway ebay 
oneday ybay ayingpay ethay insuranceway orfay ethay ownerway, andway otay engageway asway anymay 
ailorssay asway Iway inkthay ecessarynay amongway osethay owhay areway accustomedway otay ethay 
alewhay-fishing. Iway oday otnay intendway otay ailsay untilway ethay onthmay ofway Unejay; andway 
enwhay allshay Iway eturnray? Ahway, earday istersay, owhay ancay Iway answerway isthay uestionqay? 
Ifway Iway ucceedsay, anymay, anymay onthsmay, erhapspay yearsway, illway asspay eforebay youway 
andway Iway aymay eetmay. Ifway Iway ailfay, youway illway eesay emay againway oonsay, orway evernay. 
Arewellfay, ymay earday, excellentway Argaretmay. Eavenhay owershay ownday essingsblay onway 
youway, andway avesay emay, atthay Iway aymay againway andway againway estifytay ymay atitudegray orfay 
allway yourway ovelay andway indnesskay. 

Yourway affectionateway otherbray, 
Rway. Altonway 



Etterlay 2 


Archangelway, 28thay Archmay, 17-- 

Otay Mrsay. Avillesay, Englandway 

Owhay owlyslay ethay imetay assespay erehay, encompassedway asway Iway amway ybay ostfray andway owsnay! 
Yetway away econdsay epstay isway akentay owardstay ymay enterpriseway. Iway avehay iredhay away 
esselvay andway amway occupiedway inway ollectingcay ymay ailorssay; osethay omwhay Iway avehay 
alreadyway engagedway appearway otay ebay enmay onway omwhay Iway ancay ependday andway areway ertainlycay 
ossessedpay ofway auntlessday ouragecay. 

Utbay Iway avehay oneway antway ichwhay Iway avehay evernay yetway eenbay ableway otay atisfysay, andway 
ethay absenceway ofway ethay objectway ofway ichwhay Iway ownay eelfay asway away ostmay everesay evilway, Iway 
avehay onay iendfray, Argaretmay: enwhay Iway amway owingglay ithway ethay enthusiasmway ofway 
uccesssay, erethay illway ebay onenay otay articipatepay ymay oyjay; ifway Iway amway assailedway ybay 
isappointmentday, onay oneway illway endeavourway otay ustainsay emay inway ejectionday. Iway 
allshay ommitcay ymay oughtsthay otay aperpay, itway isway uetray; utbay atthay isway away oorpay 
ediummay orfay ethay ommunicationcay ofway eelingfay. Iway esireday ethay ompanycay ofway away anmay 
owhay ouldcay ympathizesay ithway emay, osewhay eyesway ouldway eplyray otay inemay. Youway aymay 
eemday emay omanticray, ymay earday istersay, utbay Iway itterlybay eelfay ethay antway ofway away 
iendfray. Iway avehay onay oneway earnay emay, entlegay yetway ourageouscay, ossessedpay ofway away 
ultivatedcay asway ellway asway ofway away apaciouscay indmay, osewhay astestay areway ikelay ymay 
ownway, otay approveway orway amendway ymay ansplay. Owhay ouldway uchsay away iendfray epairray ethay 
aultsfay ofway yourway oorpay otherbray! Iway amway ootay ardentway inway executionway andway ootay 
impatientway ofway ifficultiesday. Utbay itway isway away illstay eatergray evilway otay emay atthay Iway 
amway elfsay-educated: orfay ethay irstfay ourteenfay yearsway ofway ymay ifelay Iway anray ildway 
onway away ommoncay andway eadray othingnay utbay ourway Uncleway Omasthay' ooksbay ofway oyagesvay. Atway 
atthay ageway Iway ecamebay acquaintedway ithway ethay elebratedcay oetspay ofway ourway ownway 
ountrycay; utbay itway asway onlyway enwhay itway adhay easedcay otay ebay inway ymay owerpay otay eriveday 
itsway ostmay importantway enefitsbay omfray uchsay away onvictioncay atthay Iway erceivedpay ethay 
ecessitynay ofway ecomingbay acquaintedway ithway oremay anguageslay anthay atthay ofway ymay 
ativenay ountrycay. Ownay Iway amway entytway-eight andway amway inway ealityray oremay 
illiterateway anthay anymay oolboysschay ofway ifteenfay. Itway isway uetray atthay Iway avehay 
oughtthay oremay andway atthay ymay aydreamsday areway oremay extendedway andway agnificentmay, 
utbay eythay antway (asway ethay ainterspay allcay itway) EEPINGKAY; andway Iway eatlygray eednay away 
iendfray owhay ouldway avehay ensesay enoughway otnay otay espiseday emay asway omanticray, andway 
affectionway enoughway orfay emay otay endeavourway otay egulateray ymay indmay. Ellway, esethay 
areway uselessway omplaintscay; Iway allshay ertainlycay indfay onay iendfray onway ethay ideway 
oceanway, ornay evenway erehay inway Archangelway, amongway erchantsmay andway eamensay. Yetway 
omesay eelingsfay, unalliedway otay ethay ossdray ofway umanhay aturenay, eatbay evenway inway 
esethay uggedray osomsbay. Ymay ieutenantlay, orfay instanceway, isway away anmay ofway 
onderfulway ouragecay andway enterpriseway; ehay isway adlymay esirousday ofway oryglay, orway 
atherray, otay ordway ymay asephray oremay aracteristicallychay, ofway advancementway inway 
ishay ofessionpray. Ehay isway anway Englishmanway, andway inway ethay idstmay ofway ationalnay andway 
ofessionalpray ejudicespray, unsoftenedway ybay ultivationcay, etainsray omesay ofway ethay 
oblestnay endowmentsway ofway umanityhay. Iway irstfay ecamebay acquaintedway ithway imhay onway 
oardbay away alewhay esselvay; indingfay atthay ehay asway unemployedway inway isthay itycay, Iway 
easilyway engagedway imhay otay assistway inway ymay enterpriseway. Ethay astermay isway away ersonpay 
ofway anway excellentway ispositionday andway isway emarkableray inway ethay ipshay orfay ishay 
entlenessgay andway ethay ildnessmay ofway ishay isciplineday. Isthay ircumstancecay, 
addedway otay ishay ellway-known integrityway andway auntlessday ouragecay, ademay emay eryvay 
esirousday otay engageway imhay. Away youthway assedpay inway olitudesay, ymay estbay yearsway 
entspay underway yourway entlegay andway emininefay osteragefay, ashay osay efinedray ethay 
oundworkgray ofway ymay aracterchay atthay Iway annotcay overcomeway anway intenseway istasteday 
otay ethay usualway utalitybray exercisedway onway oardbay ipshay: Iway avehay evernay elievedbay 
itway otay ebay ecessarynay, andway enwhay Iway eardhay ofway away arinermay equallyway otednay orfay ishay 
indlinesskay ofway earthay andway ethay espectray andway obedienceway aidpay otay imhay ybay ishay 
ewcray, Iway eltfay yselfmay eculiarlypay ortunatefay inway eingbay ableway otay ecuresay ishay 
ervicessay. Iway eardhay ofway imhay irstfay inway atherray away omanticray annermay, omfray away 
adylay owhay owesway otay imhay ethay appinesshay ofway erhay ifelay. Isthay, ieflybray, isway ishay 
orystay. Omesay yearsway agoway ehay ovedlay away youngway Ussianray adylay ofway oderatemay 
ortunefay, andway avinghay amassedway away onsiderablecay umsay inway izepray-money, ethay 
atherfay ofway ethay irlgay onsentedcay otay ethay atchmay. Ehay awsay ishay istressmay onceway 
eforebay ethay estinedday eremonycay; utbay eshay asway athedbay inway earstay, andway owingthray 
erselfhay atway ishay eetfay, entreatedway imhay otay arespay erhay, onfessingcay atway ethay amesay 
imetay atthay eshay ovedlay anotherway, utbay atthay ehay asway oorpay, andway atthay erhay atherfay 
ouldway evernay onsentcay otay ethay unionway. Ymay enerousgay iendfray eassuredray ethay 
uppliantsay, andway onway eingbay informedway ofway ethay amenay ofway erhay overlay, instantlyway 
abandonedway ishay ursuitpay. Ehay adhay alreadyway oughtbay away armfay ithway ishay oneymay, onway 
ichwhay ehay adhay esignedday otay asspay ethay emainderray ofway ishay ifelay; utbay ehay 
estowedbay ethay olewhay onway ishay ivalray, ogethertay ithway ethay emainsray ofway ishay 
izepray-money otay urchasepay ockstay, andway enthay imselfhay olicitedsay ethay youngway 
omanway's atherfay otay onsentcay otay erhay arriagemay ithway erhay overlay. Utbay ethay oldway 
anmay ecidedlyday efusedray, inkingthay imselfhay oundbay inway onourhay otay ymay iendfray, 
owhay, enwhay ehay oundfay ethay atherfay inexorableway, uittedqay ishay ountrycay, ornay 
eturnedray untilway ehay eardhay atthay ishay ormerfay istressmay asway arriedmay accordingway 
otay erhay inclinationsway. "Atwhay away oblenay ellowfay!" youway illway exclaimway. Ehay isway 
osay; utbay enthay ehay isway ollywhay uneducatedway: ehay isway asway ilentsay asway away Urktay, andway away 
indkay ofway ignorantway arelessnesscay attendsway imhay, ichwhay, ilewhay itway endersray ishay 
onductcay ethay oremay astonishingway, etractsday omfray ethay interestway andway ympathysay 
ichwhay otherwiseway ehay ouldway ommandcay. 

Yetway oday otnay upposesay, ecausebay Iway omplaincay away ittlelay orway ecausebay Iway ancay 
onceivecay away onsolationcay orfay ymay oilstay ichwhay Iway aymay evernay owknay, atthay Iway amway 
averingway inway ymay esolutionsray. Osethay areway asway ixedfay asway atefay, andway ymay oyagevay 
isway onlyway ownay elayedday untilway ethay eatherway allshay ermitpay ymay embarkationway. Ethay 
interway ashay eenbay eadfullydray everesay, utbay ethay ingspray omisespray ellway, andway itway 
isway onsideredcay asway away emarkablyray earlyway easonsay, osay atthay erhapspay Iway aymay ailsay 
oonersay anthay Iway expectedway. Iway allshay oday othingnay ashlyray: youway owknay emay 
ufficientlysay otay onfidecay inway ymay udencepray andway onsideratenesscay eneverwhay ethay 
afetysay ofway othersway isway ommittedcay otay ymay arecay. 

Iway annotcay escribeday otay youway ymay ensationssay onway ethay earnay ospectpray ofway ymay 
undertakingway. Itway isway impossibleway otay ommunicatecay otay youway away onceptioncay ofway 
ethay emblingtray ensationsay, alfhay easurableplay andway alfhay earfulfay, ithway ichwhay 
Iway amway eparingpray otay epartday. Iway amway oinggay otay unexploredway egionsray, otay "ethay 
andlay ofway istmay andway owsnay," utbay Iway allshay illkay onay albatrossway; ereforethay oday otnay 
ebay alarmedway orfay ymay afetysay orway ifway Iway ouldshay omecay ackbay otay youway asway ornway andway 
oefulway asway ethay "Ancientway Arinermay." Youway illway ilesmay atway ymay allusionway, utbay Iway 
illway iscloseday away ecretsay. Iway avehay oftenway attributedway ymay attachmentway otay, ymay 
assionatepay enthusiasmway orfay, ethay angerousday ysteriesmay ofway oceanway otay atthay 
oductionpray ofway ethay ostmay imaginativeway ofway odernmay oetspay. Erethay isway omethingsay 
atway orkway inway ymay oulsay ichwhay Iway oday otnay understandway. Iway amway acticallypray 
industriousway--painstaking, away orkmanway otay executeway ithway erseverancepay andway 
abourlay--but esidesbay isthay erethay isway away ovelay orfay ethay arvellousmay, away eliefbay 
inway ethay arvellousmay, intertwinedway inway allway ymay ojectspray, ichwhay urrieshay emay outway 
ofway ethay ommoncay athwayspay ofway enmay, evenway otay ethay ildway easay andway unvisitedway 
egionsray Iway amway aboutway otay exploreway. Utbay otay eturnray otay earerday onsiderationscay. 
Allshay Iway eetmay youway againway, afterway avinghay aversedtray immenseway eassay, andway 
eturnedray ybay ethay ostmay outhernsay apecay ofway Africaway orway Americaway? Iway areday otnay 
expectway uchsay uccesssay, yetway Iway annotcay earbay otay ooklay onway ethay everseray ofway ethay 
icturepay. Ontinuecay orfay ethay esentpray otay itewray otay emay ybay everyway opportunityway: 
Iway aymay eceiveray yourway etterslay onway omesay occasionsway enwhay Iway eednay emthay ostmay otay 
upportsay ymay iritsspay. Iway ovelay youway eryvay enderlytay. Ememberray emay ithway 
affectionway, ouldshay youway evernay earhay omfray emay againway. 

Yourway affectionateway otherbray, 
Obertray Altonway 



Etterlay 3 



Ulyjay 7thay, 17-- 

Otay Mrsay. Avillesay, Englandway 

Ymay earday Istersay, 

Iway itewray away ewfay ineslay inway astehay otay aysay atthay Iway amway afesay--and ellway advancedway 
onway ymay oyagevay. Isthay etterlay illway eachray Englandway ybay away erchantmanmay ownay onway 
itsway omewardhay oyagevay omfray Archangelway; oremay ortunatefay anthay Iway, owhay aymay otnay 
eesay ymay ativenay andlay, erhapspay, orfay anymay yearsway. Iway amway, oweverhay, inway oodgay 
iritsspay: ymay enmay areway oldbay andway apparentlyway irmfay ofway urposepay, ornay oday ethay 
oatingflay eetsshay ofway iceway atthay ontinuallycay asspay usway, indicatingway ethay angersday 
ofway ethay egionray owardstay ichwhay eway areway advancingway, appearway otay ismayday emthay. Eway 
avehay alreadyway eachedray away eryvay ighhay atitudelay; utbay itway isway ethay eighthay ofway 
ummersay, andway althoughway otnay osay armway asway inway Englandway, ethay outhernsay alesgay, 
ichwhay owblay usway eedilyspay owardstay osethay oresshay ichwhay Iway osay ardentlyway esireday 
otay attainway, eathebray away egreeday ofway enovatingray armthway ichwhay Iway adhay otnay 
expectedway. 

Onay incidentsway avehay ithertohay efallenbay usway atthay ouldway akemay away igurefay inway away 
etterlay. Oneway orway otway iffstay alesgay andway ethay ingingspray ofway away eaklay areway 
accidentsway ichwhay experiencedway avigatorsnay arcelyscay ememberray otay ecordray, andway 
Iway allshay ebay ellway ontentcay ifway othingnay orseway appenhay otay usway uringday ourway oyagevay. 

Adieuway, ymay earday Argaretmay. Ebay assuredway atthay orfay ymay ownway akesay, asway ellway asway 
yoursway, Iway illway otnay ashlyray encounterway angerday. Iway illway ebay oolcay, 
erseveringpay, andway udentpray. 

Utbay uccesssay ALLSHAY owncray ymay endeavoursway. Ereforewhay otnay? Usthay arfay Iway avehay 
onegay, acingtray away ecuresay ayway overway ethay athlesspay eassay, ethay eryvay arsstay 
emselvesthay eingbay itnessesway andway estimoniestay ofway ymay iumphtray. Ywhay otnay 
illstay oceedpray overway ethay untamedway yetway obedientway elementway? Atwhay ancay opstay ethay 
eterminedday earthay andway esolvedray illway ofway anmay? 

Ymay ellingsway earthay involuntarilyway ourspay itselfway outway usthay. Utbay Iway ustmay 
inishfay. Eavenhay essblay ymay elovedbay istersay! 

Rway.W. 



Etterlay 4 



Augustway 5thay, 17-- 

Otay Mrsay. Avillesay, Englandway 

Osay angestray anway accidentway ashay appenedhay otay usway atthay Iway annotcay orbearfay 
ecordingray itway, althoughway itway isway eryvay obablepray atthay youway illway eesay emay eforebay 
esethay aperspay ancay omecay intoway yourway ossessionpay. 

Astlay Ondaymay (Ulyjay 31stay) eway ereway earlynay urroundedsay ybay iceway, ichwhay osedclay 
inway ethay ipshay onway allway idessay, arcelyscay eavinglay erhay ethay easay-room inway ichwhay 
eshay oatedflay. Ourway ituationsay asway omewhatsay angerousday, especiallyway asway eway 
ereway ompassedcay oundray ybay away eryvay ickthay ogfay. Eway accordinglyway aylay otay, 
opinghay atthay omesay angechay ouldway aketay aceplay inway ethay atmosphereway andway eatherway. 

Aboutway otway oway'clock ethay istmay earedclay awayway, andway eway eheldbay, etchedstray outway 
inway everyway irectionday, astvay andway irregularway ainsplay ofway iceway, ichwhay eemedsay otay 
avehay onay endway. Omesay ofway ymay omradescay oanedgray, andway ymay ownway indmay eganbay otay 
owgray atchfulway ithway anxiousway oughtsthay, enwhay away angestray ightsay uddenlysay 
attractedway ourway attentionway andway ivertedday ourway olicitudesay omfray ourway ownway 
ituationsay. Eway erceivedpay away owlay arriagecay, ixedfay onway away edgeslay andway awndray ybay 
ogsday, asspay onway owardstay ethay orthnay, atway ethay istanceday ofway alfhay away ilemay; away 
eingbay ichwhay adhay ethay apeshay ofway away anmay, utbay apparentlyway ofway iganticgay aturestay, 
atsay inway ethay edgeslay andway uidedgay ethay ogsday. Eway atchedway ethay apidray ogresspray 
ofway ethay avellertray ithway ourway elescopestay untilway ehay asway ostlay amongway ethay 
istantday inequalitiesway ofway ethay iceway. Isthay appearanceway excitedway ourway 
unqualifiedway onderway. Eway ereway, asway eway elievedbay, anymay undredhay ilesmay omfray 
anyway andlay; utbay isthay apparitionway eemedsay otay enoteday atthay itway asway otnay, inway 
ealityray, osay istantday asway eway adhay upposedsay. Utshay inway, oweverhay, ybay iceway, itway 
asway impossibleway otay ollowfay ishay acktray, ichwhay eway adhay observedway ithway ethay 
eatestgray attentionway. Aboutway otway ourshay afterway isthay occurrenceway eway eardhay ethay 
oundgray easay, andway eforebay ightnay ethay iceway okebray andway eedfray ourway ipshay. Eway, 
oweverhay, aylay otay untilway ethay orningmay, earingfay otay encounterway inway ethay arkday 
osethay argelay ooselay assesmay ichwhay oatflay aboutway afterway ethay eakingbray upway ofway ethay 
iceway. Iway ofitedpray ofway isthay imetay otay estray orfay away ewfay ourshay. 

Inway ethay orningmay, oweverhay, asway oonsay asway itway asway ightlay, Iway entway uponway eckday andway 
oundfay allway ethay ailorssay usybay onway oneway idesay ofway ethay esselvay, apparentlyway 
alkingtay otay omeonesay inway ethay easay. Itway asway, inway actfay, away edgeslay, ikelay atthay eway 
adhay eensay eforebay, ichwhay adhay ifteddray owardstay usway inway ethay ightnay onway away argelay 
agmentfray ofway iceway. Onlyway oneway ogday emainedray aliveway; utbay erethay asway away umanhay 
eingbay ithinway itway omwhay ethay ailorssay ereway ersuadingpay otay enterway ethay esselvay. 
Ehay asway otnay, asway ethay otherway avellertray eemedsay otay ebay, away avagesay inhabitantway ofway 
omesay undiscoveredway islandway, utbay away Europeanway. Enwhay Iway appearedway onway eckday ethay 
astermay aidsay, "Erehay isway ourway aptaincay, andway ehay illway otnay allowway youway otay erishpay 
onway ethay openway easay." 

Onway erceivingpay emay, ethay angerstray addressedway emay inway Englishway, althoughway ithway away 
oreignfay accentway. "Eforebay Iway omecay onway oardbay yourway esselvay," aidsay ehay, "illway 
youway avehay ethay indnesskay otay informway emay itherwhay youway areway oundbay?" 

Youway aymay onceivecay ymay astonishmentway onway earinghay uchsay away uestionqay addressedway 
otay emay omfray away anmay onway ethay inkbray ofway estructionday andway otay omwhay Iway ouldshay avehay 
upposedsay atthay ymay esselvay ouldway avehay eenbay away esourceray ichwhay ehay ouldway otnay 
avehay exchangedway orfay ethay ostmay eciouspray ealthway ethay earthway ancay affordway. Iway 
epliedray, oweverhay, atthay eway ereway onway away oyagevay ofway iscoveryday owardstay ethay 
orthernnay olepay. 

Uponway earinghay isthay ehay appearedway atisfiedsay andway onsentedcay otay omecay onway oardbay. 
Oodgay Odgay! Argaretmay, ifway youway adhay eensay ethay anmay owhay usthay apitulatedcay orfay 
ishay afetysay, yourway urprisesay ouldway avehay eenbay oundlessbay. Ishay imbslay ereway 
earlynay ozenfray, andway ishay odybay eadfullydray emaciatedway ybay atiguefay andway 
ufferingsay. Iway evernay awsay away anmay inway osay etchedwray away onditioncay. Eway attemptedway 
otay arrycay imhay intoway ethay abincay, utbay asway oonsay asway ehay adhay uittedqay ethay eshfray 
airway ehay aintedfay. Eway accordinglyway oughtbray imhay ackbay otay ethay eckday andway 
estoredray imhay otay animationway ybay ubbingray imhay ithway andybray andway orcingfay imhay otay 
allowsway away allsmay uantityqay. Asway oonsay asway ehay owedshay ignssay ofway ifelay eway 
appedwray imhay upway inway anketsblay andway acedplay imhay earnay ethay imneychay ofway ethay 
itchenkay ovestay. Ybay owslay egreesday ehay ecoveredray andway ateway away ittlelay oupsay, 
ichwhay estoredray imhay onderfullyway. 

Otway aysday assedpay inway isthay annermay eforebay ehay asway ableway otay eakspay, andway Iway oftenway 
earedfay atthay ishay ufferingssay adhay eprivedday imhay ofway understandingway. Enwhay ehay 
adhay inway omesay easuremay ecoveredray, Iway emovedray imhay otay ymay ownway abincay andway 
attendedway onway imhay asway uchmay asway ymay utyday ouldway ermitpay. Iway evernay awsay away oremay 
interestingway eaturecray: ishay eyesway avehay enerallygay anway expressionway ofway 
ildnessway, andway evenway adnessmay, utbay erethay areway omentsmay enwhay, ifway anyoneway 
erformspay anway actway ofway indnesskay owardstay imhay orway oesday imhay anyway ethay ostmay 
iflingtray ervicesay, ishay olewhay ountenancecay isway ightedlay upway, asway itway ereway, ithway 
away eambay ofway enevolencebay andway eetnesssway atthay Iway evernay awsay equalledway. Utbay ehay 
isway enerallygay elancholymay andway espairingday, andway ometimessay ehay ashesgnay ishay 
eethtay, asway ifway impatientway ofway ethay eightway ofway oesway atthay oppressesway imhay. 

Enwhay ymay uestgay asway away ittlelay ecoveredray Iway adhay eatgray oubletray otay eepkay offway 
ethay enmay, owhay ishedway otay askway imhay away ousandthay uestionsqay; utbay Iway ouldway otnay 
allowway imhay otay ebay ormentedtay ybay eirthay idleway uriositycay, inway away atestay ofway odybay 
andway indmay osewhay estorationray evidentlyway ependedday uponway entireway eposeray. 
Onceway, oweverhay, ethay ieutenantlay askedway ywhay ehay adhay omecay osay arfay uponway ethay iceway 
inway osay angestray away ehiclevay. 

Ishay ountenancecay instantlyway assumedway anway aspectway ofway ethay eepestday oomglay, andway 
ehay epliedray, "Otay eeksay oneway owhay edflay omfray emay." 

"Andway idday ethay anmay omwhay youway ursuedpay aveltray inway ethay amesay ashionfay?" 

"Yesway." 

"Enthay Iway ancyfay eway avehay eensay imhay, orfay ethay ayday eforebay eway ickedpay youway upway eway 
awsay omesay ogsday awingdray away edgeslay, ithway away anmay inway itway, acrossway ethay iceway." 

Isthay arousedway ethay angerstray's attentionway, andway ehay askedway away ultitudemay ofway 
uestionsqay oncerningcay ethay outeray ichwhay ethay emonday, asway ehay alledcay imhay, adhay 
ursuedpay. Oonsay afterway, enwhay ehay asway aloneway ithway emay, ehay aidsay, "Iway avehay, 
oubtlessday, excitedway yourway uriositycay, asway ellway asway atthay ofway esethay oodgay 
eoplepay; utbay youway areway ootay onsideratecay otay akemay inquiriesway." 

"Ertainlycay; itway ouldway indeedway ebay eryvay impertinentway andway inhumanway inway emay otay 
oubletray youway ithway anyway inquisitivenessway ofway inemay." 

"Andway yetway youway escuedray emay omfray away angestray andway erilouspay ituationsay; youway avehay 
enevolentlybay estoredray emay otay ifelay." 

Oonsay afterway isthay ehay inquiredway ifway Iway oughtthay atthay ethay eakingbray upway ofway ethay 
iceway adhay estroyedday ethay otherway edgeslay. Iway epliedray atthay Iway ouldcay otnay answerway 
ithway anyway egreeday ofway ertaintycay, orfay ethay iceway adhay otnay okenbray untilway earnay 
idnightmay, andway ethay avellertray ightmay avehay arrivedway atway away aceplay ofway afetysay 
eforebay atthay imetay; utbay ofway isthay Iway ouldcay otnay udgejay. Omfray isthay imetay away ewnay 
iritspay ofway ifelay animatedway ethay ecayingday amefray ofway ethay angerstray. Ehay 
anifestedmay ethay eatestgray eagernessway otay ebay uponway eckday otay atchway orfay ethay 
edgeslay ichwhay adhay eforebay appearedway; utbay Iway avehay ersuadedpay imhay otay emainray inway 
ethay abincay, orfay ehay isway arfay ootay eakway otay ustainsay ethay awnessray ofway ethay 
atmosphereway. Iway avehay omisedpray atthay omeonesay ouldshay atchway orfay imhay andway ivegay 
imhay instantway oticenay ifway anyway ewnay objectway ouldshay appearway inway ightsay. 

Uchsay isway ymay ournaljay ofway atwhay elatesray otay isthay angestray occurrenceway upway otay ethay 
esentpray ayday. Ethay angerstray ashay aduallygray improvedway inway ealthhay utbay isway eryvay 
ilentsay andway appearsway uneasyway enwhay anyoneway exceptway yselfmay entersway ishay abincay. 
Yetway ishay annersmay areway osay onciliatingcay andway entlegay atthay ethay ailorssay areway allway 
interestedway inway imhay, althoughway eythay avehay adhay eryvay ittlelay ommunicationcay 
ithway imhay. Orfay ymay ownway artpay, Iway eginbay otay ovelay imhay asway away otherbray, andway ishay 
onstantcay andway eepday iefgray illsfay emay ithway ympathysay andway ompassioncay. Ehay ustmay 
avehay eenbay away oblenay eaturecray inway ishay etterbay aysday, eingbay evenway ownay inway eckwray 
osay attractiveway andway amiableway. Iway aidsay inway oneway ofway ymay etterslay, ymay earday 
Argaretmay, atthay Iway ouldshay indfay onay iendfray onway ethay ideway oceanway; yetway Iway avehay 
oundfay away anmay owhay, eforebay ishay iritspay adhay eenbay okenbray ybay iserymay, Iway ouldshay 
avehay eenbay appyhay otay avehay ossessedpay asway ethay otherbray ofway ymay earthay. 

Iway allshay ontinuecay ymay ournaljay oncerningcay ethay angerstray atway intervalsway, 
ouldshay Iway avehay anyway eshfray incidentsway otay ecordray. 


Augustway 13thay, 17-- 

Ymay affectionway orfay ymay uestgay increasesway everyway ayday. Ehay excitesway atway onceway ymay 
admirationway andway ymay itypay otay anway astonishingway egreeday. Owhay ancay Iway eesay osay 
oblenay away eaturecray estroyedday ybay iserymay ithoutway eelingfay ethay ostmay oignantpay 
iefgray? Ehay isway osay entlegay, yetway osay iseway; ishay indmay isway osay ultivatedcay, andway 
enwhay ehay eaksspay, althoughway ishay ordsway areway ulledcay ithway ethay oicestchay artway, 
yetway eythay owflay ithway apidityray andway unparalleledway eloquenceway. Ehay isway ownay uchmay 
ecoveredray omfray ishay illnessway andway isway ontinuallycay onway ethay eckday, apparentlyway 
atchingway orfay ethay edgeslay atthay ecededpray ishay ownway. Yetway, althoughway unhappyway, 
ehay isway otnay osay utterlyway occupiedway ybay ishay ownway iserymay utbay atthay ehay interestsway 
imselfhay eeplyday inway ethay ojectspray ofway othersway. Ehay ashay equentlyfray onversedcay 
ithway emay onway inemay, ichwhay Iway avehay ommunicatedcay otay imhay ithoutway isguiseday. Ehay 
enteredway attentivelyway intoway allway ymay argumentsway inway avourfay ofway ymay eventualway 
uccesssay andway intoway everyway inutemay etailday ofway ethay easuresmay Iway adhay akentay otay 
ecuresay itway. Iway asway easilyway edlay ybay ethay ympathysay ichwhay ehay evincedway otay useway 
ethay anguagelay ofway ymay earthay, otay ivegay utteranceway otay ethay urningbay ardourway ofway ymay 
oulsay andway otay aysay, ithway allway ethay ervourfay atthay armedway emay, owhay adlyglay Iway 
ouldway acrificesay ymay ortunefay, ymay existenceway, ymay everyway opehay, otay ethay 
urtherancefay ofway ymay enterpriseway. Oneway anmay's ifelay orway eathday ereway utbay away allsmay 
icepray otay aypay orfay ethay acquirementway ofway ethay owledgeknay ichwhay Iway oughtsay, orfay 
ethay ominionday Iway ouldshay acquireway andway ansmittray overway ethay elementalway oesfay ofway 
ourway aceray. Asway Iway okespay, away arkday oomglay eadspray overway ymay istenerlay's 
ountenancecay. Atway irstfay Iway erceivedpay atthay ehay iedtray otay uppresssay ishay 
emotionway; ehay acedplay ishay andshay eforebay ishay eyesway, andway ymay oicevay uiveredqay andway 
ailedfay emay asway Iway eheldbay earstay ickletray astfay omfray etweenbay ishay ingersfay; away 
oangray urstbay omfray ishay eavinghay eastbray. Iway ausedpay; atway engthlay ehay okespay, inway 
okenbray accentsway: "Unhappyway anmay! Oday youway areshay ymay adnessmay? Avehay youway 
unkdray alsoway ofway ethay intoxicatingway aughtdray? Earhay emay; etlay emay evealray ymay 
aletay, andway youway illway ashday ethay upcay omfray yourway ipslay!" 

Uchsay ordsway, youway aymay imagineway, onglystray excitedway ymay uriositycay; utbay ethay 
aroxysmpay ofway iefgray atthay adhay eizedsay ethay angerstray overcameway ishay eakenedway 
owerspay, andway anymay ourshay ofway eposeray andway anquiltray onversationcay ereway 
ecessarynay otay estoreray ishay omposurecay. Avinghay onqueredcay ethay iolencevay ofway 
ishay eelingsfay, ehay appearedway otay espiseday imselfhay orfay eingbay ethay aveslay ofway 
assionpay; andway uellingqay ethay arkday yrannytay ofway espairday, ehay edlay emay againway otay 
onversecay oncerningcay yselfmay ersonallypay. Ehay askedway emay ethay istoryhay ofway ymay 
earlierway yearsway. Ethay aletay asway uicklyqay oldtay, utbay itway awakenedway ariousvay 
ainstray ofway eflectionray. Iway okespay ofway ymay esireday ofway indingfay away iendfray, ofway ymay 
irstthay orfay away oremay intimateway ympathysay ithway away ellowfay indmay anthay adhay everway 
allenfay otay ymay otlay, andway expressedway ymay onvictioncay atthay away anmay ouldcay oastbay ofway 
ittlelay appinesshay owhay idday otnay enjoyway isthay essingblay. "Iway agreeway ithway youway," 
epliedray ethay angerstray; "eway areway unfashionedway eaturescray, utbay alfhay ademay upway, 
ifway oneway iserway, etterbay, earerday anthay ourselvesway--such away iendfray oughtway otay 
ebay--do otnay endlay ishay aidway otay erfectionatepay ourway eakway andway aultyfay aturesnay. Iway 
onceway adhay away iendfray, ethay ostmay oblenay ofway umanhay eaturescray, andway amway entitledway, 
ereforethay, otay udgejay espectingray iendshipfray. Youway avehay opehay, andway ethay 
orldway eforebay youway, andway avehay onay ausecay orfay espairday. Utbay Iway--I avehay ostlay 
everythingway andway annotcay eginbay ifelay anewway." 

Asway ehay aidsay isthay ishay ountenancecay ecamebay expressiveway ofway away almcay, ettledsay 
iefgray atthay ouchedtay emay otay ethay earthay. Utbay ehay asway ilentsay andway esentlypray 
etiredray otay ishay abincay. 

Evenway okenbray inway iritspay asway ehay isway, onay oneway ancay eelfay oremay eeplyday anthay ehay 
oesday ethay eautiesbay ofway aturenay. Ethay arrystay yskay, ethay easay, andway everyway ightsay 
affordedway ybay esethay onderfulway egionsray eemsay illstay otay avehay ethay owerpay ofway 
elevatingway ishay oulsay omfray earthway. Uchsay away anmay ashay away oubleday existenceway: ehay 
aymay uffersay iserymay andway ebay overwhelmedway ybay isappointmentsday, yetway enwhay ehay 
ashay etiredray intoway imselfhay, ehay illway ebay ikelay away elestialcay iritspay atthay ashay away 
alohay aroundway imhay, ithinway osewhay irclecay onay iefgray orway ollyfay enturesvay. 

Illway youway ilesmay atway ethay enthusiasmway Iway expressway oncerningcay isthay ivineday 
andererway? Youway ouldway otnay ifway youway awsay imhay. Youway avehay eenbay utoredtay andway 
efinedray ybay ooksbay andway etirementray omfray ethay orldway, andway youway areway ereforethay 
omewhatsay astidiousfay; utbay isthay onlyway endersray youway ethay oremay itfay otay 
appreciateway ethay extraordinaryway eritsmay ofway isthay onderfulway anmay. Ometimessay Iway 
avehay endeavouredway otay iscoverday atwhay ualityqay itway isway ichwhay ehay ossessespay atthay 
elevatesway imhay osay immeasurablyway aboveway anyway otherway ersonpay Iway everway ewknay. Iway 
elievebay itway otay ebay anway intuitiveway iscernmentday, away uickqay utbay evernay-failing 
owerpay ofway udgmentjay, away enetrationpay intoway ethay ausescay ofway ingsthay, unequalledway 
orfay earnessclay andway ecisionpray; addway otay isthay away acilityfay ofway expressionway andway away 
oicevay osewhay ariedvay intonationsway areway oulsay-subduing usicmay. 


Augustway 19, 17-- 

Yesterdayway ethay angerstray aidsay otay emay, "Youway aymay easilyway erceivepay, Aptaincay 
Altonway, atthay Iway avehay ufferedsay eatgray andway unparalleledway isfortunesmay. Iway adhay 
eterminedday atway oneway imetay atthay ethay emorymay ofway esethay evilsway ouldshay ieday ithway 
emay, utbay youway avehay onway emay otay alterway ymay eterminationday. Youway eeksay orfay 
owledgeknay andway isdomway, asway Iway onceway idday; andway Iway ardentlyway opehay atthay ethay 
atificationgray ofway yourway ishesway aymay otnay ebay away erpentsay otay ingstay youway, asway inemay 
ashay eenbay. Iway oday otnay owknay atthay ethay elationray ofway ymay isastersday illway ebay 
usefulway otay youway; yetway, enwhay Iway eflectray atthay youway areway ursuingpay ethay amesay 
oursecay, exposingway yourselfway otay ethay amesay angersday ichwhay avehay enderedray emay 
atwhay Iway amway, Iway imagineway atthay youway aymay educeday anway aptway oralmay omfray ymay aletay, oneway 
atthay aymay irectday youway ifway youway ucceedsay inway yourway undertakingway andway onsolecay youway 
inway asecay ofway ailurefay. Eparepray otay earhay ofway occurrencesway ichwhay areway usuallyway 
eemedday arvellousmay. Ereway eway amongway ethay amertay enesscay ofway aturenay Iway ightmay 
earfay otay encounterway yourway unbeliefway, erhapspay yourway idiculeray; utbay anymay ingsthay 
illway appearway ossiblepay inway esethay ildway andway ysteriousmay egionsray ichwhay ouldway 
ovokepray ethay aughterlay ofway osethay unacquaintedway ithway ethay everway-varied owerspay 
ofway aturenay; ornay ancay Iway oubtday utbay atthay ymay aletay onveyscay inway itsway eriessay 
internalway evidenceway ofway ethay uthtray ofway ethay eventsway ofway ichwhay itway isway omposedcay." 

Youway aymay easilyway imagineway atthay Iway asway uchmay atifiedgray ybay ethay offeredway 
ommunicationcay, yetway Iway ouldcay otnay endureway atthay ehay ouldshay enewray ishay iefgray ybay 
away ecitalray ofway ishay isfortunesmay. Iway eltfay ethay eatestgray eagernessway otay earhay 
ethay omisedpray arrativenay, artlypay omfray uriositycay andway artlypay omfray away ongstray 
esireday otay ameliorateway ishay atefay ifway itway ereway inway ymay owerpay. Iway expressedway 
esethay eelingsfay inway ymay answerway. 

"Iway ankthay youway," ehay epliedray, "orfay yourway ympathysay, utbay itway isway uselessway; ymay 
atefay isway earlynay ulfilledfay. Iway aitway utbay orfay oneway eventway, andway enthay Iway allshay 
eposeray inway eacepay. Iway understandway yourway eelingfay," ontinuedcay ehay, erceivingpay 
atthay Iway ishedway otay interruptway imhay; "utbay youway areway istakenmay, ymay iendfray, ifway 
usthay youway illway allowway emay otay amenay youway; othingnay ancay alterway ymay estinyday; 
istenlay otay ymay istoryhay, andway youway illway erceivepay owhay irrevocablyway itway isway 
eterminedday." 

Ehay enthay oldtay emay atthay ehay ouldway ommencecay ishay arrativenay ethay extnay ayday enwhay 
Iway ouldshay ebay atway eisurelay. Isthay omisepray ewdray omfray emay ethay armestway anksthay. 
Iway avehay esolvedray everyway ightnay, enwhay Iway amway otnay imperativelyway occupiedway ybay ymay 
utiesday, otay ecordray, asway earlynay asway ossiblepay inway ishay ownway ordsway, atwhay ehay ashay 
elatedray uringday ethay ayday. Ifway Iway ouldshay ebay engagedway, Iway illway atway eastlay akemay 
otesnay. Isthay anuscriptmay illway oubtlessday affordway youway ethay eatestgray 
easureplay; utbay otay emay, owhay owknay imhay, andway owhay earhay itway omfray ishay ownway 
ipslay--with atwhay interestway andway ympathysay allshay Iway eadray itway inway omesay uturefay 
ayday! Evenway ownay, asway Iway ommencecay ymay asktay, ishay ullfay-toned oicevay ellssway inway 
ymay earsway; ishay ustrouslay eyesway elldway onway emay ithway allway eirthay elancholymay 
eetnesssway; Iway eesay ishay inthay andhay aisedray inway animationway, ilewhay ethay 
ineamentslay ofway ishay acefay areway irradiatedway ybay ethay oulsay ithinway. 

Angestray andway arrowinghay ustmay ebay ishay orystay, ightfulfray ethay ormstay ichwhay 
embracedway ethay allantgay esselvay onway itsway oursecay andway eckedwray itway--thus! 



Apterchay 1 

Iway amway ybay irthbay away Enevesegay, andway ymay amilyfay isway oneway ofway ethay ostmay

Asway ethay ircumstancescay ofway ishay arriagemay illustrateway ishay aracterchay, Iway annotcay

Eaufortbay adhay akentay effectualway easuresmay otay oncealcay imselfhay, andway itway asway entay

ofway anyway exertionway. 

Ishay aughterday attendedway imhay ithway ethay eatestgray endernesstay, utbay eshay awsay

Everalsay onthsmay assedpay inway isthay annermay. Erhay atherfay ewgray orseway; erhay imetay

Omfray Italyway eythay isitedvay Ermanygay andway Ancefray. Iway, eirthay eldestway ildchay, asway

Enwhay Iway asway aboutway ivefay yearsway oldway, ilewhay akingmay anway excursionway eyondbay ethay

Apterchay 2 

Eway ereway oughtbray upway ogethertay; erethay asway otnay uiteqay away yearway ifferenceday inway 
ourway agesway. Iway eednay otnay aysay atthay eway ereway angersstray otay anyway eciesspay ofway 
isunionday orway isputeday. Armonyhay asway ethay oulsay ofway ourway ompanionshipcay, andway 
ethay iversityday andway ontrastcay atthay ubsistedsay inway ourway aracterschay ewdray usway 
earernay ogethertay. Elizabethway asway ofway away almercay andway oremay oncentratedcay 
ispositionday; utbay, ithway allway ymay ardourway, Iway asway apablecay ofway away oremay intenseway 
applicationway andway asway oremay eeplyday ittensmay ithway ethay irstthay orfay owledgeknay. 
Eshay usiedbay erselfhay ithway ollowingfay ethay aerialway eationscray ofway ethay oetspay; 
andway inway ethay ajesticmay andway ondrousway enesscay ichwhay urroundedsay ourway Isssway omehay 
--ethay ublimesay apesshay ofway ethay ountainsmay, ethay angeschay ofway ethay easonssay, 
empesttay andway almcay, ethay ilencesay ofway interway, andway ethay ifelay andway urbulencetay ofway 
ourway Alpineway ummerssay--she oundfay ampleway opescay orfay admirationway andway elightday. 
Ilewhay ymay ompanioncay ontemplatedcay ithway away erioussay andway atisfiedsay iritspay ethay 
agnificentmay appearancesway ofway ingsthay, Iway elightedday inway investigatingway eirthay 
ausescay. Ethay orldway asway otay emay away ecretsay ichwhay Iway esiredday otay ivineday. 
Uriositycay, earnestway esearchray otay earnlay ethay iddenhay awslay ofway aturenay, 
adnessglay akinway otay aptureray, asway eythay ereway unfoldedway otay emay, areway amongway ethay 
earliestway ensationssay Iway ancay ememberray. 

Onway ethay irthbay ofway away econdsay onsay, ymay uniorjay ybay evensay yearsway, ymay arentspay avegay

ountrycay. Eway ossessedpay away ousehay inway Enevagay, andway away ampagnecay onway Elrivebay, 
ethay easternway oreshay ofway ethay akelay, atway ethay istanceday ofway atherray oremay anthay away 
eaguelay omfray ethay itycay. Eway esidedray incipallypray inway ethay atterlay, andway ethay 
iveslay ofway ymay arentspay ereway assedpay inway onsiderablecay eclusionsay. Itway asway ymay 
empertay otay avoidway away owdcray andway otay attachway yselfmay erventlyfay otay away ewfay. Iway asway 
indifferentway, ereforethay, otay ymay oolschay-fellows inway eneralgay; utbay Iway unitedway 
yselfmay inway ethay ondsbay ofway ethay osestclay iendshipfray otay oneway amongway emthay. Enryhay 
Ervalclay asway ethay onsay ofway away erchantmay ofway Enevagay. Ehay asway away oybay ofway ingularsay 
alenttay andway ancyfay. Ehay ovedlay enterpriseway, ardshiphay, andway evenway angerday orfay 
itsway ownway akesay. Ehay asway eeplyday eadray inway ooksbay ofway ivalrychay andway omanceray. Ehay 
omposedcay eroichay ongssay andway eganbay otay itewray anymay away aletay ofway enchantmentway andway 
ightlyknay adventureway. Ehay iedtray otay akemay usway actway aysplay andway otay enterway intoway 
asqueradesmay, inway ichwhay ethay aracterschay ereway awndray omfray ethay eroeshay ofway 
Oncesvallesray, ofway ethay Oundray Abletay ofway Ingkay Arthurway, andway ethay ivalrouschay 
aintray owhay edshay eirthay oodblay otay edeemray ethay olyhay epulchresay omfray ethay andshay 
ofway ethay infidelsway. 

Onay umanhay eingbay ouldcay avehay assedpay away appierhay ildhoodchay anthay yselfmay. Ymay 
arentspay ereway ossessedpay ybay ethay eryvay iritspay ofway indnesskay andway indulgenceway. 
Eway eltfay atthay eythay ereway otnay ethay yrantstay otay uleray ourway otlay accordingway otay 
eirthay apricecay, utbay ethay agentsway andway eatorscray ofway allway ethay anymay elightsday 
ichwhay eway enjoyedway. Enwhay Iway ingledmay ithway otherway amiliesfay Iway istinctlyday 
iscernedday owhay eculiarlypay ortunatefay ymay otlay asway, andway atitudegray assistedway 
ethay evelopmentday ofway ilialfay ovelay. 

Ymay empertay asway ometimessay iolentvay, andway ymay assionspay ehementvay; utbay ybay omesay 
awlay inway ymay emperaturetay eythay ereway urnedtay otnay owardstay ildishchay ursuitspay

ornay ethay odecay ofway overnmentsgay, ornay ethay oliticspay ofway ariousvay atesstay 
ossessedpay attractionsway orfay emay. Itway asway ethay ecretssay ofway eavenhay andway earthway 
atthay Iway esiredday otay earnlay; andway etherwhay itway asway ethay outwardway ubstancesay ofway 
ingsthay orway ethay innerway iritspay ofway aturenay andway ethay ysteriousmay oulsay ofway anmay 
atthay occupiedway emay, illstay ymay inquiriesway ereway irectedday otay ethay etaphysicalmay, 
orway inway itsway ighesthay ensesay, ethay ysicalphay ecretssay ofway ethay orldway. 

Eanwhilemay Ervalclay occupiedway imselfhay, osay otay eakspay, ithway ethay oralmay 
elationsray ofway ingsthay. Ethay usybay agestay ofway ifelay, ethay irtuesvay ofway eroeshay, 
andway ethay actionsway ofway enmay ereway ishay emethay; andway ishay opehay andway ishay eamdray asway 
otay ecomebay oneway amongway osethay osewhay amesnay areway ecordedray inway orystay asway ethay 
allantgay andway adventurousway enefactorsbay ofway ourway eciesspay. Ethay aintlysay oulsay 
ofway Elizabethway oneshay ikelay away ineshray-dedicated amplay inway ourway eacefulpay omehay. 
Erhay ympathysay asway oursway; erhay ilesmay, erhay oftsay oicevay, ethay eetsway anceglay ofway 
erhay elestialcay eyesway, ereway everway erethay otay essblay andway animateway usway. Eshay asway 
ethay ivinglay iritspay ofway ovelay otay oftensay andway attractway; Iway ightmay avehay ecomebay 
ullensay inway ymay udystay, oughray oughthray ethay ardourway ofway ymay aturenay, utbay atthay 
eshay asway erethay otay ubduesay emay otay away emblancesay ofway erhay ownway entlenessgay. Andway 
Ervalclay--could aughtway illway entrenchway onway ethay oblenay iritspay ofway Ervalclay? Yetway 
ehay ightmay otnay avehay eenbay osay erfectlypay umanehay, osay oughtfulthay inway ishay 
enerositygay, osay ullfay ofway indnesskay andway endernesstay amidstway ishay assionpay orfay 
adventurousway exploitway, adhay eshay otnay unfoldedway otay imhay ethay ealray ovelinesslay ofway 
eneficencebay andway ademay ethay oingday oodgay ethay endway andway aimway ofway ishay oaringsay 
ambitionway. 

Iway eelfay exquisiteway easureplay inway ellingdway onway ethay ecollectionsray ofway 
ildhoodchay, eforebay isfortunemay adhay aintedtay ymay indmay andway angedchay itsway ightbray 
isionsvay ofway extensiveway usefulnessway intoway oomyglay andway arrownay eflectionsray uponway 
elfsay. Esidesbay, inway awingdray ethay icturepay ofway ymay earlyway aysday, Iway alsoway ecordray 
osethay eventsway ichwhay edlay, ybay insensibleway epsstay, otay ymay afterway aletay ofway 
iserymay, orfay enwhay Iway ouldway accountway otay yselfmay orfay ethay irthbay ofway atthay 
assionpay ichwhay afterwardsway uledray ymay estinyday Iway indfay itway ariseway, ikelay away 
ountainmay iverray, omfray ignobleway andway almostway orgottenfay ourcessay; utbay, 
ellingsway asway itway oceededpray, itway ecamebay ethay orrenttay ichwhay, inway itsway oursecay, 
ashay eptsway awayway allway ymay opeshay andway oysjay. Aturalnay ilosophyphay isway ethay eniusgay 
atthay ashay egulatedray ymay atefay; Iway esireday, ereforethay, inway isthay arrationnay, otay 
atestay osethay actsfay ichwhay edlay otay ymay edilectionpray orfay atthay iencescay. Enwhay 
Iway asway irteenthay yearsway ofway ageway eway allway entway onway away artypay ofway easureplay otay ethay 
athsbay earnay Ononthay; ethay inclemencyway ofway ethay eatherway obligedway usway otay emainray away 
ayday onfinedcay otay ethay innway. Inway isthay ousehay Iway ancedchay otay indfay away olumevay ofway 
ethay orksway ofway Orneliuscay Agrippaway. Iway openedway itway ithway apathyway; ethay eorythay 
ichwhay ehay attemptsway otay emonstrateday andway ethay onderfulway actsfay ichwhay ehay 
elatesray oonsay angedchay isthay eelingfay intoway enthusiasmway. Away ewnay ightlay eemedsay 
otay awnday uponway ymay indmay, andway oundingbay ithway oyjay, Iway ommunicatedcay ymay 
iscoveryday otay ymay atherfay. Ymay atherfay ookedlay arelesslycay atway ethay itletay agepay 
ofway ymay ookbay andway aidsay, "Ahway! Orneliuscay Agrippaway! Ymay earday Ictorvay, oday otnay 
asteway yourway imetay uponway isthay; itway isway adsay ashtray." 

Ifway, insteadway ofway isthay emarkray, ymay atherfay adhay akentay ethay ainspay otay explainway otay 
emay atthay ethay inciplespray ofway Agrippaway adhay eenbay entirelyway explodedway andway atthay away 
odernmay ystemsay ofway iencescay adhay eenbay introducedway ichwhay ossessedpay uchmay 
eatergray owerspay anthay ethay ancientway, ecausebay ethay owerspay ofway ethay atterlay ereway 
imericalchay, ilewhay osethay ofway ethay ormerfay ereway ealray andway acticalpray, underway 
uchsay ircumstancescay Iway ouldshay ertainlycay avehay ownthray Agrippaway asideway andway 
avehay ontentedcay ymay imaginationway, armedway asway itway asway, ybay eturningray ithway 
eatergray ardourway otay ymay ormerfay udiesstay. Itway isway evenway ossiblepay atthay ethay 
aintray ofway ymay ideasway ouldway evernay avehay eceivedray ethay atalfay impulseway atthay edlay 
otay ymay uinray. Utbay ethay ursorycay anceglay ymay atherfay adhay akentay ofway ymay olumevay ybay 
onay eansmay assuredway emay atthay ehay asway acquaintedway ithway itsway ontentscay, andway Iway 
ontinuedcay otay eadray ithway ethay eatestgray avidityway. Enwhay Iway eturnedray omehay ymay 
irstfay arecay asway otay ocurepray ethay olewhay orksway ofway isthay authorway, andway 
afterwardsway ofway Aracelsuspay andway Albertusway Agnusmay. Iway eadray andway udiedstay ethay 
ildway anciesfay ofway esethay iterswray ithway elightday; eythay appearedway otay emay 
easurestray ownknay otay ewfay esidesbay yselfmay. Iway avehay escribedday yselfmay asway 
alwaysway avinghay eenbay imbuedway ithway away erventfay onginglay otay enetratepay ethay 
ecretssay ofway aturenay. Inway itespay ofway ethay intenseway abourlay andway onderfulway 
iscoveriesday ofway odernmay ilosophersphay, Iway alwaysway amecay omfray ymay udiesstay 
iscontentedday andway unsatisfiedway. Irsay Isaacway Ewtonnay isway aidsay otay avehay avowedway 
atthay ehay eltfay ikelay away ildchay ickingpay upway ellsshay esidebay ethay eatgray andway 
unexploredway oceanway ofway uthtray. Osethay ofway ishay uccessorssay inway eachway anchbray ofway 
aturalnay ilosophyphay ithway omwhay Iway asway acquaintedway appearedway evenway otay ymay oybay's 
apprehensionsway asway yrostay engagedway inway ethay amesay ursuitpay. 

Ethay untaughtway easantpay eheldbay ethay elementsway aroundway imhay andway asway acquaintedway 
ithway eirthay acticalpray usesway. Ethay ostmay earnedlay ilosopherphay ewknay ittlelay 
oremay. Ehay adhay artiallypay unveiledway ethay acefay ofway Aturenay, utbay erhay immortalway 
ineamentslay ereway illstay away onderway andway away ysterymay. Ehay ightmay issectday, 
anatomizeway, andway ivegay amesnay; utbay, otnay otay eakspay ofway away inalfay ausecay, ausescay 
inway eirthay econdarysay andway ertiarytay adesgray ereway utterlyway unknownway otay imhay. Iway 
adhay azedgay uponway ethay ortificationsfay andway impedimentsway atthay eemedsay otay eepkay 
umanhay eingsbay omfray enteringway ethay itadelcay ofway aturenay, andway ashlyray andway 
ignorantlyway Iway adhay epinedray. 

Utbay erehay ereway ooksbay, andway erehay ereway enmay owhay adhay enetratedpay eeperday andway 
ewknay oremay. Iway ooktay eirthay ordway orfay allway atthay eythay averredway, andway Iway ecamebay 
eirthay iscipleday. Itway aymay appearway angestray atthay uchsay ouldshay ariseway inway ethay 
eighteenthway enturycay; utbay ilewhay Iway ollowedfay ethay outineray ofway educationway inway 
ethay oolsschay ofway Enevagay, Iway asway, otay away eatgray egreeday, elfsay-taught ithway 
egardray otay ymay avouritefay udiesstay. Ymay atherfay asway otnay ientificscay, andway Iway 
asway eftlay otay ugglestray ithway away ildchay's indnessblay, addedway otay away udentstay's 
irstthay orfay owledgeknay. Underway ethay uidancegay ofway ymay ewnay eceptorspray Iway 
enteredway ithway ethay eatestgray iligenceday intoway ethay earchsay ofway ethay 
ilosopherphay's onestay andway ethay elixirway ofway ifelay; utbay ethay atterlay oonsay 
obtainedway ymay undividedway attentionway. Ealthway asway anway inferiorway objectway, utbay 
atwhay oryglay ouldway attendway ethay iscoveryday ifway Iway ouldcay anishbay iseaseday omfray 
ethay umanhay amefray andway enderray anmay invulnerableway otay anyway utbay away iolentvay eathday! 
Ornay ereway esethay ymay onlyway isionsvay. Ethay aisingray ofway ostsghay orway evilsday asway away 
omisepray iberallylay accordedway ybay ymay avouritefay authorsway, ethay ulfilmentfay ofway 
ichwhay Iway ostmay eagerlyway oughtsay; andway ifway ymay incantationsway ereway alwaysway 
unsuccessfulway, Iway attributedway ethay ailurefay atherray otay ymay ownway inexperienceway 
andway istakemay anthay otay away antway ofway illskay orway idelityfay inway ymay instructorsway. Andway 
usthay orfay away imetay Iway asway occupiedway ybay explodedway ystemssay, inglingmay, ikelay anway 
unadeptway, away ousandthay ontradictorycay eoriesthay andway ounderingflay esperatelyday 
inway away eryvay oughslay ofway ultifariousmay owledgeknay, uidedgay ybay anway ardentway 
imaginationway andway ildishchay easoningray, illtay anway accidentway againway angedchay ethay 
urrentcay ofway ymay ideasway. Enwhay Iway asway aboutway ifteenfay yearsway oldway eway adhay etiredray 
otay ourway ousehay earnay Elrivebay, enwhay eway itnessedway away ostmay iolentvay andway 
erribletay understormthay. Itway advancedway omfray ehindbay ethay ountainsmay ofway Urajay, 
andway ethay underthay urstbay atway onceway ithway ightfulfray oudnesslay omfray ariousvay 
uartersqay ofway ethay eavenshay. Iway emainedray, ilewhay ethay ormstay astedlay, atchingway 
itsway ogresspray ithway uriositycay andway elightday. Asway Iway oodstay atway ethay oorday, onway away 
uddensay Iway eheldbay away eamstray ofway irefay issueway omfray anway oldway andway eautifulbay oakway 
ichwhay oodstay aboutway entytway yardsway omfray ourway ousehay; andway osay oonsay asway ethay 
azzlingday ightlay anishedvay, ethay oakway adhay isappearedday, andway othingnay emainedray 
utbay away astedblay umpstay. Enwhay eway isitedvay itway ethay extnay orningmay, eway oundfay ethay 
eetray atteredshay inway away ingularsay annermay. Itway asway otnay interedsplay ybay ethay 
ockshay, utbay entirelyway educedray otay inthay ibbonsray ofway oodway. Iway evernay eheldbay 
anythingway osay utterlyway estroyedday. 

Eforebay isthay Iway asway otnay unacquaintedway ithway ethay oremay obviousway awslay ofway 
electricityway. Onway isthay occasionway away anmay ofway eatgray esearchray inway aturalnay 
ilosophyphay asway ithway usway, andway excitedway ybay isthay atastrophecay, ehay enteredway onway 
ethay explanationway ofway away eorythay ichwhay ehay adhay ormedfay onway ethay ubjectsay ofway 
electricityway andway alvanismgay, ichwhay asway atway onceway ewnay andway astonishingway otay emay. 
Allway atthay ehay aidsay ewthray eatlygray intoway ethay adeshay Orneliuscay Agrippaway, 
Albertusway Agnusmay, andway Aracelsuspay, ethay ordslay ofway ymay imaginationway; utbay ybay 
omesay atalityfay ethay overthrowway ofway esethay enmay isinclinedday emay otay ursuepay ymay 
accustomedway udiesstay. Itway eemedsay otay emay asway ifway othingnay ouldway orway ouldcay everway 
ebay ownknay. Allway atthay adhay osay onglay engagedway ymay attentionway uddenlysay ewgray 
espicableday. Ybay oneway ofway osethay apricescay ofway ethay indmay ichwhay eway areway erhapspay 
ostmay ubjectsay otay inway earlyway youthway, Iway atway onceway avegay upway ymay ormerfay 
occupationsway, etsay ownday aturalnay istoryhay andway allway itsway ogenypray asway away eformedday 
andway abortiveway eationcray, andway entertainedway ethay eatestgray isdainday orfay away 
ouldway-be iencescay ichwhay ouldcay evernay evenway epstay ithinway ethay esholdthray ofway 
ealray owledgeknay. Inway isthay oodmay ofway indmay Iway etookbay yselfmay otay ethay 
athematicsmay andway ethay anchesbray ofway udystay appertainingway otay atthay iencescay asway 
eingbay uiltbay uponway ecuresay oundationsfay, andway osay orthyway ofway ymay onsiderationcay. 

Usthay angelystray areway ourway oulssay onstructedcay, andway ybay uchsay ightslay igamentslay 
areway eway oundbay otay osperitypray orway uinray. Enwhay Iway ooklay ackbay, itway eemssay otay emay 
asway ifway isthay almostway iraculousmay angechay ofway inclinationway andway illway asway ethay 
immediateway uggestionsay ofway ethay uardiangay angelway ofway ymay ifelay--the astlay effortway 
ademay ybay ethay iritspay ofway eservationpray otay avertway ethay ormstay atthay asway evenway 
enthay anginghay inway ethay arsstay andway eadyray otay envelopway emay. Erhay ictoryvay asway 
announcedway ybay anway unusualway anquillitytray andway adnessglay ofway oulsay ichwhay 
ollowedfay ethay elinquishingray ofway ymay ancientway andway atterlylay ormentingtay 
udiesstay. Itway asway usthay atthay Iway asway otay ebay aughttay otay associateway evilway ithway 
eirthay osecutionpray, appinesshay ithway eirthay isregardday. 

Itway asway away ongstray effortway ofway ethay iritspay ofway oodgay, utbay itway asway ineffectualway. 
Estinyday asway ootay otentpay, andway erhay immutableway awslay adhay ecreedday ymay utterway andway 
erribletay estructionday. 



Apterchay 3 

Enwhay Iway adhay attainedway ethay ageway ofway eventeensay ymay arentspay esolvedray atthay Iway 
ouldshay ecomebay away udentstay atway ethay universityway ofway Ingolstadtway. Iway adhay 
ithertohay attendedway ethay oolsschay ofway Enevagay, utbay ymay atherfay oughtthay itway 
ecessarynay orfay ethay ompletioncay ofway ymay educationway atthay Iway ouldshay ebay ademay 
acquaintedway ithway otherway ustomscay anthay osethay ofway ymay ativenay ountrycay. Ymay 
epartureday asway ereforethay ixedfay atway anway earlyway ateday, utbay eforebay ethay ayday 
esolvedray uponway ouldcay arriveway, ethay irstfay isfortunemay ofway ymay ifelay 
occurredway--an omenway, asway itway ereway, ofway ymay uturefay iserymay. Elizabethway adhay 
aughtcay ethay arletscay everfay; erhay illnessway asway everesay, andway eshay asway inway ethay 
eatestgray angerday. Uringday erhay illnessway anymay argumentsway adhay eenbay urgedway otay 
ersuadepay ymay othermay otay efrainray omfray attendingway uponway erhay. Eshay adhay atway 
irstfay yieldedway otay ourway entreatiesway, utbay enwhay eshay eardhay atthay ethay ifelay ofway 
erhay avouritefay asway enacedmay, eshay ouldcay onay ongerlay ontrolcay erhay anxietyway. Eshay 
attendedway erhay ickbedsay; erhay atchfulway attentionsway iumphedtray overway ethay 
alignitymay ofway ethay istemperday--Elizabeth asway avedsay, utbay ethay onsequencescay 
ofway isthay imprudenceway ereway atalfay otay erhay eserverpray. Onway ethay irdthay ayday ymay 
othermay ickenedsay; erhay everfay asway accompaniedway ybay ethay ostmay alarmingway 
ymptomssay, andway ethay ookslay ofway erhay edicalmay attendantsway ognosticatedpray ethay 
orstway eventway. Onway erhay eathbedday ethay ortitudefay andway enignitybay ofway isthay estbay 
ofway omenway idday otnay esertday erhay. Eshay oinedjay ethay andshay ofway Elizabethway andway 
yselfmay. "Ymay ildrenchay," eshay aidsay, "ymay irmestfay opeshay ofway uturefay appinesshay 
ereway acedplay onway ethay ospectpray ofway yourway unionway. Isthay expectationway illway ownay 
ebay ethay onsolationcay ofway yourway atherfay. Elizabethway, ymay ovelay, youway ustmay upplysay 
ymay aceplay otay ymay youngerway ildrenchay. Alasway! Iway egretray atthay Iway amway akentay omfray 
youway; andway, appyhay andway elovedbay asway Iway avehay eenbay, isway itway otnay ardhay otay uitqay youway 
allway? Utbay esethay areway otnay oughtsthay efittingbay emay; Iway illway endeavourway otay 
esignray yselfmay eerfullychay otay eathday andway illway indulgeway away opehay ofway eetingmay 
youway inway anotherway orldway." 

Eshay iedday almlycay, andway erhay ountenancecay expressedway affectionway evenway inway eathday. 
Iway eednay otnay escribeday ethay eelingsfay ofway osethay osewhay earestday iestay areway entray 
ybay atthay ostmay irreparableway evilway, ethay oidvay atthay esentspray itselfway otay ethay 
oulsay, andway ethay espairday atthay isway exhibitedway onway ethay ountenancecay. Itway isway osay 
onglay eforebay ethay indmay ancay ersuadepay itselfway atthay eshay omwhay eway awsay everyway ayday 
andway osewhay eryvay existenceway appearedway away artpay ofway ourway ownway ancay avehay epartedday 
oreverfay--that ethay ightnessbray ofway away elovedbay eyeway ancay avehay eenbay 
extinguishedway andway ethay oundsay ofway away oicevay osay amiliarfay andway earday otay ethay earway 
ancay ebay ushedhay, evernay oremay otay ebay eardhay. Esethay areway ethay eflectionsray ofway 
ethay irstfay aysday; utbay enwhay ethay apselay ofway imetay ovespray ethay ealityray ofway ethay 
evilway, enthay ethay actualway itternessbay ofway iefgray ommencescay. Yetway omfray omwhay ashay 
otnay atthay uderay andhay entray awayway omesay earday onnectioncay? Andway ywhay ouldshay Iway 
escribeday away orrowsay ichwhay allway avehay eltfay, andway ustmay eelfay? Ethay imetay atway 
engthlay arrivesway enwhay iefgray isway atherray anway indulgenceway anthay away ecessitynay; andway 
ethay ilesmay atthay aysplay uponway ethay ipslay, althoughway itway aymay ebay eemedday away 
acrilegesay, isway otnay anishedbay. Ymay othermay asway eadday, utbay eway adhay illstay 
utiesday ichwhay eway oughtway otay erformpay; eway ustmay ontinuecay ourway oursecay ithway ethay 
estray andway earnlay otay inkthay ourselvesway ortunatefay ilstwhay oneway emainsray omwhay ethay 
oilerspay ashay otnay eizedsay. 

Ymay epartureday orfay Ingolstadtway, ichwhay adhay eenbay eferredday ybay esethay eventsway, 
asway ownay againway eterminedday uponway. Iway obtainedway omfray ymay atherfay away espiteray ofway 
omesay eeksway. Itway appearedway otay emay acrilegesay osay oonsay otay eavelay ethay eposeray, 
akinway otay eathday, ofway ethay ousehay ofway ourningmay andway otay ushray intoway ethay ickthay ofway 
ifelay. Iway asway ewnay otay orrowsay, utbay itway idday otnay ethay esslay alarmway emay. Iway asway 
unwillingway otay uitqay ethay ightsay ofway osethay atthay emainedray otay emay, andway aboveway 
allway, Iway esiredday otay eesay ymay eetsway Elizabethway inway omesay egreeday onsoledcay. 

Eshay indeedway eiledvay erhay iefgray andway ovestray otay actway ethay omfortercay otay usway allway. 
Eshay ookedlay eadilystay onway ifelay andway assumedway itsway utiesday ithway ouragecay andway 
ealzay. Eshay evotedday erselfhay otay osethay omwhay eshay adhay eenbay aughttay otay allcay 
erhay uncleway andway ousinscay. Evernay asway eshay osay enchantingway asway atway isthay imetay, 
enwhay eshay ecalledray ethay unshinesay ofway erhay ilessmay andway entspay emthay uponway usway. 
Eshay orgotfay evenway erhay ownway egretray inway erhay endeavoursway otay akemay usway orgetfay. 

Ethay ayday ofway ymay epartureday atway engthlay arrivedway. Ervalclay entspay ethay astlay 
eveningway ithway usway. Ehay adhay endeavouredway otay ersuadepay ishay atherfay otay ermitpay 
imhay otay accompanyway emay andway otay ecomebay ymay ellowfay udentstay, utbay inway ainvay. Ishay 
atherfay asway away arrownay-minded adertray andway awsay idlenessway andway uinray inway ethay 
aspirationsway andway ambitionway ofway ishay onsay. Enryhay eeplyday eltfay ethay isfortunemay 
ofway eingbay ebarredday omfray away iberallay educationway. Ehay aidsay ittlelay, utbay enwhay 
ehay okespay Iway eadray inway ishay indlingkay eyeway andway inway ishay animatedway anceglay away 
estrainedray utbay irmfay esolveray otnay otay ebay ainedchay otay ethay iserablemay etailsday 
ofway ommercecay. 

Eway atsay atelay. Eway ouldcay otnay eartay ourselvesway awayway omfray eachway otherway ornay 
ersuadepay ourselvesway otay aysay ethay ordway "Arewellfay!" Itway asway aidsay, andway eway 
etiredray underway ethay etencepray ofway eekingsay eposeray, eachway ancyingfay atthay ethay 
otherway asway eceivedday; utbay enwhay atway orningmay's awnday Iway escendedday otay ethay 
arriagecay ichwhay asway otay onveycay emay awayway, eythay ereway allway erethay--my atherfay 
againway otay essblay emay, Ervalclay otay esspray ymay andhay onceway oremay, ymay Elizabethway otay 
enewray erhay entreatiesway atthay Iway ouldway itewray oftenway andway otay estowbay ethay astlay 
emininefay attentionsway onway erhay aymateplay andway iendfray. 

Iway ewthray yselfmay intoway ethay aisechay atthay asway otay onveycay emay awayway andway indulgedway 
inway ethay ostmay elancholymay eflectionsray. Iway, owhay adhay everway eenbay urroundedsay ybay 
amiableway ompanionscay, ontinuallycay engagedway inway endeavouringway otay estowbay 
utualmay easureplay--I asway ownay aloneway. Inway ethay universityway itherwhay Iway asway 
oinggay Iway ustmay ormfay ymay ownway iendsfray andway ebay ymay ownway otectorpray. Ymay ifelay adhay 
ithertohay eenbay emarkablyray ecludedsay andway omesticday, andway isthay adhay ivengay emay 
invincibleway epugnanceray otay ewnay ountenancescay. Iway ovedlay ymay othersbray, 
Elizabethway, andway Ervalclay; esethay ereway "oldway amiliarfay acesfay," utbay Iway elievedbay 
yselfmay otallytay unfittedway orfay ethay ompanycay ofway angersstray. Uchsay ereway ymay 
eflectionsray asway Iway ommencedcay ymay ourneyjay; utbay asway Iway oceededpray, ymay iritsspay 
andway opeshay oseray. Iway ardentlyway esiredday ethay acquisitionway ofway owledgeknay. Iway 
adhay oftenway, enwhay atway omehay, oughtthay itway ardhay otay emainray uringday ymay youthway 
oopedcay upway inway oneway aceplay andway adhay ongedlay otay enterway ethay orldway andway aketay ymay 
ationstay amongway otherway umanhay eingsbay. Ownay ymay esiresday ereway ompliedcay ithway, 
andway itway ouldway, indeedway, avehay eenbay ollyfay otay epentray. 

Iway adhay ufficientsay eisurelay orfay esethay andway anymay otherway eflectionsray uringday ymay 
ourneyjay otay Ingolstadtway, ichwhay asway onglay andway atiguingfay. Atway engthlay ethay 
ighhay itewhay eeplestay ofway ethay owntay etmay ymay eyesway. Iway alightedway andway asway 
onductedcay otay ymay olitarysay apartmentway otay endspay ethay eveningway asway Iway easedplay. 

Ethay extnay orningmay Iway eliveredday ymay etterslay ofway introductionway andway aidpay away 
isitvay otay omesay ofway ethay incipalpray ofessorspray. Ancechay--or atherray ethay evilway 
influenceway, ethay Angelway ofway Estructionday, ichwhay assertedway omnipotentway aysway 
overway emay omfray ethay omentmay Iway urnedtay ymay eluctantray epsstay omfray ymay atherfay's 
oorday--led emay irstfay otay Mway. Empekray, ofessorpray ofway aturalnay ilosophyphay. Ehay 
asway anway uncouthway anmay, utbay eeplyday imbuedway inway ethay ecretssay ofway ishay iencescay. Ehay 
askedway emay everalsay uestionsqay oncerningcay ymay ogresspray inway ethay ifferentday 
anchesbray ofway iencescay appertainingway otay aturalnay ilosophyphay. Iway epliedray 
arelesslycay, andway artlypay inway ontemptcay, entionedmay ethay amesnay ofway ymay 
alchemistsway asway ethay incipalpray authorsway Iway adhay udiedstay. Ethay ofessorpray 
aredstay. "Avehay youway," ehay aidsay, "eallyray entspay yourway imetay inway udyingstay uchsay 
onsensenay?" 

Iway epliedray inway ethay affirmativeway. "Everyway inutemay," ontinuedcay Mway. Empekray ithway 
armthway, "everyway instantway atthay youway avehay astedway onway osethay ooksbay isway utterlyway 
andway entirelyway ostlay. Youway avehay urdenedbay yourway emorymay ithway explodedway ystemssay 
andway uselessway amesnay. Oodgay Odgay! Inway atwhay esertday andlay avehay youway ivedlay, 
erewhay onay oneway asway indkay enoughway otay informway youway atthay esethay anciesfay ichwhay youway 
avehay osay eedilygray imbibedway areway away ousandthay yearsway oldway andway asway ustymay asway eythay 
areway ancientway? Iway ittlelay expectedway, inway isthay enlightenedway andway ientificscay 
ageway, otay indfay away iscipleday ofway Albertusway Agnusmay andway Aracelsuspay. Ymay earday 
irsay, youway ustmay eginbay yourway udiesstay entirelyway anewway." 

Osay ayingsay, ehay eppedstay asideway andway otewray ownday away istlay ofway everalsay ooksbay 
eatingtray ofway aturalnay ilosophyphay ichwhay ehay esiredday emay otay ocurepray, andway 
ismissedday emay afterway entioningmay atthay inway ethay eginningbay ofway ethay ollowingfay 
eekway ehay intendedway otay ommencecay away oursecay ofway ectureslay uponway aturalnay 
ilosophyphay inway itsway eneralgay elationsray, andway atthay Mway. Aldmanway, away ellowfay 
ofessorpray, ouldway ecturelay uponway emistrychay ethay alternateway aysday atthay ehay 
omittedway. 

Iway eturnedray omehay otnay isappointedday, orfay Iway avehay aidsay atthay Iway adhay onglay 
onsideredcay osethay authorsway uselessway omwhay ethay ofessorpray eprobatedray; utbay Iway 
eturnedray otnay atway allway ethay oremay inclinedway otay ecurray otay esethay udiesstay inway anyway 
apeshay. Mway. Empekray asway away ittlelay uatsqay anmay ithway away uffgray oicevay andway away 
epulsiveray ountenancecay; ethay eachertay, ereforethay, idday otnay epossesspray emay inway 
avourfay ofway ishay ursuitspay. Inway atherray away ootay ilosophicalphay andway onnectedcay away

Apterchay 4 

Omfray isthay ayday aturalnay ilosophyphay, andway articularlypay emistrychay, inway ethay

Oneway ofway ethay enomenaphay ichwhay adhay eculiarlypay attractedway ymay attentionway asway

Itway asway away oldbay uestionqay, andway oneway ichwhay ashay everway eenbay onsideredcay asway away

Ememberray, Iway amway otnay ecordingray ethay isionvay ofway away admanmay. Ethay unsay oesday otnay

Ethay astonishmentway ichwhay Iway adhay atway irstfay experiencedway onway isthay iscoveryday

Iway eesay ybay yourway eagernessway andway ethay onderway andway opehay ichwhay yourway eyesway

ollectingcay andway arrangingway ymay aterialsmay, Iway eganbay. 

Onay oneway ancay onceivecay ethay arietyvay ofway eelingsfay ichwhay orebay emay onwardsway, ikelay 
away urricanehay, inway ethay irstfay enthusiasmway ofway uccesssay. Ifelay andway eathday

emay asway itsway eatorcray andway ourcesay; anymay appyhay andway excellentway aturesnay ouldway 
oweway eirthay eingbay otay emay. Onay atherfay ouldcay aimclay ethay atitudegray ofway ishay

attermay, Iway ightmay inway ocesspray ofway imetay (althoughway Iway ownay oundfay itway impossibleway) 
enewray ifelay erewhay eathday adhay apparentlyway evotedday ethay odybay otay orruptioncay. 

Esethay oughtsthay upportedsay ymay iritsspay, ilewhay Iway ursuedpay ymay undertakingway 
ithway unremittingway ardourway. Ymay eekchay adhay owngray alepay ithway udystay, andway ymay 
ersonpay adhay ecomebay emaciatedway ithway onfinementcay. Ometimessay, onway ethay eryvay 
inkbray ofway ertaintycay, Iway ailedfay; yetway illstay Iway ungclay otay ethay opehay ichwhay ethay 
extnay ayday orway ethay extnay ourhay ightmay ealizeray. Oneway ecretsay ichwhay Iway aloneway 
ossessedpay asway ethay opehay otay ichwhay Iway adhay edicatedday yselfmay; andway ethay oonmay 
azedgay onway ymay idnightmay abourslay, ilewhay, ithway unrelaxedway andway eathlessbray 
eagernessway, Iway ursuedpay aturenay otay erhay idinghay-places. Owhay allshay onceivecay 
ethay orrorshay ofway ymay ecretsay oiltay asway Iway abbledday amongway ethay unhallowedway ampsday 
ofway ethay avegray orway orturedtay ethay ivinglay animalway otay animateway ethay ifelesslay 
ayclay? Ymay imbslay ownay embletray, andway ymay eyesway imsway ithway ethay emembranceray; utbay 
enthay away esistlessray andway almostway anticfray impulseway urgedway emay orwardfay; Iway eemedsay 
otay avehay ostlay allway oulsay orway ensationsay utbay orfay isthay oneway ursuitpay. Itway asway 
indeedway utbay away assingpay ancetray, atthay onlyway ademay emay eelfay ithway enewedray 
acutenessway osay oonsay asway, ethay unnaturalway imulusstay easingcay otay operateway, Iway adhay 
eturnedray otay ymay oldway abitshay. Iway ollectedcay onesbay omfray arnelchay-houses andway 
isturbedday, ithway ofanepray ingersfay, ethay emendoustray ecretssay ofway ethay umanhay 
amefray. Inway away olitarysay amberchay, orway atherray ellcay, atway ethay optay ofway ethay ousehay, 
andway eparatedsay omfray allway ethay otherway apartmentsway ybay away allerygay andway aircasestay, 
Iway eptkay ymay orkshopway ofway ilthyfay eationcray; ymay eyeballsway ereway artingstay omfray 
eirthay ocketssay inway attendingway otay ethay etailsday ofway ymay employmentway. Ethay 
issectingday oomray andway ethay aughterslay-house urnishedfay anymay ofway ymay aterialsmay; 
andway oftenway idday ymay umanhay aturenay urntay ithway oathinglay omfray ymay occupationway, 
ilstwhay, illstay urgedway onway ybay anway eagernessway ichwhay erpetuallypay increasedway, Iway 
oughtbray ymay orkway earnay otay away onclusioncay. 

Ethay ummersay onthsmay assedpay ilewhay Iway asway usthay engagedway, earthay andway oulsay, inway 
oneway ursuitpay. Itway asway away ostmay eautifulbay easonsay; evernay idday ethay ieldsfay 
estowbay away oremay entifulplay arvesthay orway ethay inesvay yieldway away oremay uxuriantlay 
intagevay, utbay ymay eyesway ereway insensibleway otay ethay armschay ofway aturenay. Andway ethay 
amesay eelingsfay ichwhay ademay emay eglectnay ethay enesscay aroundway emay ausedcay emay alsoway 
otay orgetfay osethay iendsfray owhay ereway osay anymay ilesmay absentway, andway omwhay Iway adhay 
otnay eensay orfay osay onglay away imetay. Iway ewknay ymay ilencesay isquietedday emthay, andway Iway 
ellway ememberedray ethay ordsway ofway ymay atherfay: "Iway owknay atthay ilewhay youway areway 
easedplay ithway yourselfway youway illway inkthay ofway usway ithway affectionway, andway eway allshay 
earhay egularlyray omfray youway. Youway ustmay ardonpay emay ifway Iway egardray anyway 
interruptionway inway yourway orrespondencecay asway away oofpray atthay yourway otherway utiesday 
areway equallyway eglectednay." 

Iway ewknay ellway ereforethay atwhay ouldway ebay ymay atherfay's eelingsfay, utbay Iway ouldcay
