otnay eartay ymay oughtsthay omfray ymay employmentway, oathsomelay inway itselfway, utbay ichwhay 
adhay akentay anway irresistibleway oldhay ofway ymay imaginationway. Iway ishedway, asway itway 
ereway, otay ocrastinatepray allway atthay elatedray otay ymay eelingsfay ofway affectionway 
untilway ethay eatgray objectway, ichwhay allowedsway upway everyway abithay ofway ymay aturenay, 
ouldshay ebay ompletedcay. 

Iway enthay oughtthay atthay ymay atherfay ouldway ebay unjustway ifway ehay ascribedway ymay eglectnay 
otay icevay orway aultinessfay onway ymay artpay, utbay Iway amway ownay onvincedcay atthay ehay asway 
ustifiedjay inway onceivingcay atthay Iway ouldshay otnay ebay altogetherway eefray omfray 
ameblay. Away umanhay eingbay inway erfectionpay oughtway alwaysway otay eservepray away almcay andway 
eacefulpay indmay andway evernay otay allowway assionpay orway away ansitorytray esireday otay 
isturbday ishay anquillitytray. Iway oday otnay inkthay atthay ethay ursuitpay ofway owledgeknay 
isway anway exceptionway otay isthay uleray. Ifway ethay udystay otay ichwhay youway applyway yourselfway 
ashay away endencytay otay eakenway yourway affectionsway andway otay estroyday yourway astetay orfay 
osethay implesay easuresplay inway ichwhay onay alloyway ancay ossiblypay ixmay, enthay atthay 
udystay isway ertainlycay unlawfulway, atthay isway otay aysay, otnay efittingbay ethay umanhay 
indmay. Ifway isthay uleray ereway alwaysway observedway; ifway onay anmay allowedway anyway ursuitpay 
atsoeverwhay otay interfereway ithway ethay anquillitytray ofway ishay omesticday 
affectionsway, Eecegray adhay otnay eenbay enslavedway, Aesarcay ouldway avehay aredspay ishay 
ountrycay, Americaway ouldway avehay eenbay iscoveredday oremay aduallygray, andway ethay 
empiresway ofway Exicomay andway Erupay adhay otnay eenbay estroyedday. 

Utbay Iway orgetfay atthay Iway amway oralizingmay inway ethay ostmay interestingway artpay ofway ymay 
aletay, andway yourway ookslay emindray emay otay oceedpray. Ymay atherfay ademay onay eproachray 
inway ishay etterslay andway onlyway ooktay oticenay ofway ymay ilencesay ybay inquiringway intoway ymay 
occupationsway oremay articularlypay anthay eforebay. Interway, ingspray, andway ummersay 
assedpay awayway uringday ymay abourslay; utbay Iway idday otnay atchway ethay ossomblay orway ethay 
expandingway eaveslay--sights ichwhay eforebay alwaysway yieldedway emay upremesay 
elightday--so eeplyday asway Iway engrossedway inway ymay occupationway. Ethay eaveslay ofway 
atthay yearway adhay itheredway eforebay ymay orkway ewdray earnay otay away oseclay, andway ownay 
everyway ayday owedshay emay oremay ainlyplay owhay ellway Iway adhay ucceededsay. Utbay ymay 
enthusiasmway asway eckedchay ybay ymay anxietyway, andway Iway appearedway atherray ikelay oneway 
oomedday ybay averyslay otay oiltay inway ethay inesmay, orway anyway otherway unwholesomeway adetray 
anthay anway artistway occupiedway ybay ishay avouritefay employmentway. Everyway ightnay Iway asway 
oppressedway ybay away owslay everfay, andway Iway ecamebay ervousnay otay away ostmay ainfulpay 
egreeday; ethay allfay ofway away eaflay artledstay emay, andway Iway unnedshay ymay ellowfay 
eaturescray asway ifway Iway adhay eenbay uiltygay ofway away imecray. Ometimessay Iway ewgray alarmedway 
atway ethay eckwray Iway erceivedpay atthay Iway adhay ecomebay; ethay energyway ofway ymay urposepay 
aloneway ustainedsay emay: ymay abourslay ouldway oonsay endway, andway Iway elievedbay atthay 
exerciseway andway amusementway ouldway enthay ivedray awayway incipientway iseaseday; andway Iway 
omisedpray yselfmay othbay ofway esethay enwhay ymay eationcray ouldshay ebay ompletecay. 



Apterchay 5 

Itway asway onway away earydray ightnay ofway Ovembernay atthay Iway eheldbay ethay accomplishmentway 
ofway ymay oilstay. Ithway anway anxietyway atthay almostway amountedway otay agonyway, Iway 
ollectedcay ethay instrumentsway ofway ifelay aroundway emay, atthay Iway ightmay infuseway away 
arkspay ofway eingbay intoway ethay ifelesslay ingthay atthay aylay atway ymay eetfay. Itway asway 
alreadyway oneway inway ethay orningmay; ethay ainray atteredpay ismallyday againstway ethay 
anespay, andway ymay andlecay asway earlynay urntbay outway, enwhay, ybay ethay immerglay ofway ethay 
alfhay-extinguished ightlay, Iway awsay ethay ullday yellowway eyeway ofway ethay eaturecray 
openway; itway eathedbray ardhay, andway away onvulsivecay otionmay agitatedway itsway imbslay. 

Owhay ancay Iway escribeday ymay emotionsway atway isthay atastrophecay, orway owhay elineateday 
ethay etchwray omwhay ithway uchsay infiniteway ainspay andway arecay Iway adhay endeavouredway otay 
ormfay? Ishay imbslay ereway inway oportionpray, andway Iway adhay electedsay ishay eaturesfay asway 
eautifulbay. Eautifulbay! Eatgray Odgay! Ishay yellowway inskay arcelyscay overedcay 
ethay orkway ofway usclesmay andway arteriesway eneathbay; ishay airhay asway ofway away ustrouslay 
ackblay, andway owingflay; ishay eethtay ofway away earlypay itenesswhay; utbay esethay 
uxurianceslay onlyway ormedfay away oremay orridhay ontrastcay ithway ishay ateryway eyesway, 
atthay eemedsay almostway ofway ethay amesay olourcay asway ethay unday-white ocketssay inway ichwhay 
eythay ereway etsay, ishay ivelledshray omplexioncay andway aightstray ackblay ipslay. 

Ethay ifferentday accidentsway ofway ifelay areway otnay osay angeablechay asway ethay eelingsfay 
ofway umanhay aturenay. Iway adhay orkedway ardhay orfay earlynay otway yearsway, orfay ethay olesay 
urposepay ofway infusingway ifelay intoway anway inanimateway odybay. Orfay isthay Iway adhay 
eprivedday yselfmay ofway estray andway ealthhay. Iway adhay esiredday itway ithway anway ardourway 
atthay arfay exceededway oderationmay; utbay ownay atthay Iway adhay inishedfay, ethay eautybay 
ofway ethay eamdray anishedvay, andway eathlessbray orrorhay andway isgustday illedfay ymay 
earthay. Unableway otay endureway ethay aspectway ofway ethay eingbay Iway adhay eatedcray, Iway 
ushedray outway ofway ethay oomray andway ontinuedcay away onglay imetay aversingtray ymay 
edbay-chamber, unableway otay omposecay ymay indmay otay eepslay. Atway engthlay assitudelay 
ucceededsay otay ethay umulttay Iway adhay eforebay enduredway, andway Iway ewthray yselfmay onway ethay 
edbay inway ymay othesclay, endeavouringway otay eeksay away ewfay omentsmay ofway orgetfulnessfay. 
Utbay itway asway inway ainvay; Iway eptslay, indeedway, utbay Iway asway isturbedday ybay ethay ildestway 
eamsdray. Iway oughtthay Iway awsay Elizabethway, inway ethay oomblay ofway ealthhay, alkingway inway 
ethay eetsstray ofway Ingolstadtway. Elightedday andway urprisedsay, Iway embracedway erhay, 
utbay asway Iway imprintedway ethay irstfay isskay onway erhay ipslay, eythay ecamebay ividlay ithway 
ethay uehay ofway eathday; erhay eaturesfay appearedway otay angechay, andway Iway oughtthay atthay Iway 
eldhay ethay orpsecay ofway ymay eadday othermay inway ymay armsway; away oudshray envelopedway erhay 
ormfay, andway Iway awsay ethay avegray-worms awlingcray inway ethay oldsfay ofway ethay annelflay. 
Iway artedstay omfray ymay eepslay ithway orrorhay; away oldcay ewday overedcay ymay oreheadfay, ymay 
eethtay atteredchay, andway everyway imblay ecamebay onvulsedcay; enwhay, ybay ethay imday andway 
yellowway ightlay ofway ethay oonmay, asway itway orcedfay itsway ayway oughthray ethay indowway 
uttersshay, Iway eheldbay ethay etchwray--the iserablemay onstermay omwhay Iway adhay 
eatedcray. Ehay eldhay upway ethay urtaincay ofway ethay edbay; andway ishay eyesway, ifway eyesway eythay 
aymay ebay alledcay, ereway ixedfay onway emay. Ishay awsjay openedway, andway ehay utteredmay omesay 
inarticulateway oundssay, ilewhay away ingray inkledwray ishay eekschay. Ehay ightmay avehay 
okenspay, utbay Iway idday otnay earhay; oneway andhay asway etchedstray outway, eeminglysay otay 
etainday emay, utbay Iway escapedway andway ushedray ownstairsday. Iway ooktay efugeray inway ethay 
ourtyardcay elongingbay otay ethay ousehay ichwhay Iway inhabitedway, erewhay Iway emainedray 
uringday ethay estray ofway ethay ightnay, alkingway upway andway ownday inway ethay eatestgray 
agitationway, isteninglay attentivelyway, atchingcay andway earingfay eachway oundsay asway ifway 
itway ereway otay announceway ethay approachway ofway ethay emoniacalday orpsecay otay ichwhay Iway 
adhay osay iserablymay ivengay ifelay. 

Ohway! Onay ortalmay ouldcay upportsay ethay orrorhay ofway atthay ountenancecay. Away ummymay 
againway enduedway ithway animationway ouldcay otnay ebay osay ideoushay asway atthay etchwray. Iway 
adhay azedgay onway imhay ilewhay unfinishedway; ehay asway uglyway enthay, utbay enwhay osethay 
usclesmay andway ointsjay ereway enderedray apablecay ofway otionmay, itway ecamebay away ingthay 
uchsay asway evenway Anteday ouldcay otnay avehay onceivedcay. 

Iway assedpay ethay ightnay etchedlywray. Ometimessay ymay ulsepay eatbay osay uicklyqay andway 
ardlyhay atthay Iway eltfay ethay alpitationpay ofway everyway arteryway; atway othersway, Iway earlynay 
anksay otay ethay oundgray oughthray anguorlay andway extremeway eaknessway. Ingledmay ithway 
isthay orrorhay, Iway eltfay ethay itternessbay ofway isappointmentday; eamsdray atthay adhay 
eenbay ymay oodfay andway easantplay estray orfay osay onglay away acespay ereway ownay ecomebay away 
ellhay otay emay; andway ethay angechay asway osay apidray, ethay overthrowway osay ompletecay! 

Orningmay, ismalday andway etway, atway engthlay awnedday andway iscoveredday otay ymay 
eeplessslay andway achingway eyesway ethay urchchay ofway Ingolstadtway, itsway itewhay eeplestay 
andway ockclay, ichwhay indicatedway ethay ixthsay ourhay. Ethay orterpay openedway ethay atesgay 
ofway ethay ourtcay, ichwhay adhay atthay ightnay eenbay ymay asylumway, andway Iway issuedway intoway 
ethay eetsstray, acingpay emthay ithway uickqay epsstay, asway ifway Iway oughtsay otay avoidway ethay 
etchwray omwhay Iway earedfay everyway urningtay ofway ethay eetstray ouldway esentpray otay ymay 
iewvay. Iway idday otnay areday eturnray otay ethay apartmentway ichwhay Iway inhabitedway, utbay 
eltfay impelledway otay urryhay onway, althoughway encheddray ybay ethay ainray ichwhay ouredpay 
omfray away ackblay andway omfortlesscay yskay. 

Iway ontinuedcay alkingway inway isthay annermay orfay omesay imetay, endeavouringway ybay 
odilybay exerciseway otay easeway ethay oadlay atthay eighedway uponway ymay indmay. Iway 
aversedtray ethay eetsstray ithoutway anyway earclay onceptioncay ofway erewhay Iway asway orway 
atwhay Iway asway oingday. Ymay earthay alpitatedpay inway ethay icknesssay ofway earfay, andway Iway 
urriedhay onway ithway irregularway epsstay, otnay aringday otay ooklay aboutway emay: 


Ikelay oneway owhay, onway away onelylay oadray, 
Othday alkway inway earfay andway eaddray, 
Andway, avinghay onceway urnedtay oundray, alksway onway, 
Andway urnstay onay oremay ishay eadhay; 
Ecausebay ehay owsknay away ightfulfray iendfay 
Othday oseclay ehindbay imhay eadtray. 

[Oleridgecay's "Ancientway Arinermay."] 


Ontinuingcay usthay, Iway amecay atway engthlay oppositeway otay ethay innway atway ichwhay ethay 
ariousvay iligencesday andway arriagescay usuallyway oppedstay. Erehay Iway ausedpay, Iway 
ewknay otnay ywhay; utbay Iway emainedray omesay inutesmay ithway ymay eyesway ixedfay onway away oachcay 
atthay asway omingcay owardstay emay omfray ethay otherway endway ofway ethay eetstray. Asway itway 
ewdray earernay Iway observedway atthay itway asway ethay Isssway iligenceday; itway oppedstay ustjay 
erewhay Iway asway andingstay, andway onway ethay oorday eingbay openedway, Iway erceivedpay Enryhay 
Ervalclay, owhay, onway eeingsay emay, instantlyway ungspray outway. "Ymay earday 
Ankensteinfray," exclaimedway ehay, "owhay adglay Iway amway otay eesay youway! Owhay ortunatefay 
atthay youway ouldshay ebay erehay atway ethay eryvay omentmay ofway ymay alightingway!" 

Othingnay ouldcay equalway ymay elightday onway eeingsay Ervalclay; ishay esencepray oughtbray 
ackbay otay ymay oughtsthay ymay atherfay, Elizabethway, andway allway osethay enesscay ofway omehay 
osay earday otay ymay ecollectionray. Iway aspedgray ishay andhay, andway inway away omentmay orgotfay 
ymay orrorhay andway isfortunemay; Iway eltfay uddenlysay, andway orfay ethay irstfay imetay 
uringday anymay onthsmay, almcay andway erenesay oyjay. Iway elcomedway ymay iendfray, 
ereforethay, inway ethay ostmay ordialcay annermay, andway eway alkedway owardstay ymay 
ollegecay. Ervalclay ontinuedcay alkingtay orfay omesay imetay aboutway ourway utualmay 
iendsfray andway ishay ownway oodgay ortunefay inway eingbay ermittedpay otay omecay otay 
Ingolstadtway. "Youway aymay easilyway elievebay," aidsay ehay, "owhay eatgray asway ethay 
ifficultyday otay ersuadepay ymay atherfay atthay allway ecessarynay owledgeknay asway otnay 
omprisedcay inway ethay oblenay artway ofway ookbay-keeping; andway, indeedway, Iway elievebay Iway 
eftlay imhay incredulousway otay ethay astlay, orfay ishay onstantcay answerway otay ymay 
unweariedway entreatiesway asway ethay amesay asway atthay ofway ethay Utchday oolmasterschay inway 
Ethay Icarvay ofway Akefieldway: 'Iway avehay entay ousandthay orinsflay away yearway ithoutway 
Eekgray, Iway eatway eartilyhay ithoutway Eekgray.' Utbay ishay affectionway orfay emay atway 
engthlay overcameway ishay islikeday ofway earninglay, andway ehay ashay ermittedpay emay otay 
undertakeway away oyagevay ofway iscoveryday otay ethay andlay ofway owledgeknay." 

"Itway ivesgay emay ethay eatestgray elightday otay eesay youway; utbay elltay emay owhay youway eftlay 
ymay atherfay, othersbray, andway Elizabethway." 

"Eryvay ellway, andway eryvay appyhay, onlyway away ittlelay uneasyway atthay eythay earhay omfray 
youway osay eldomsay. Ybay ethay ybay, Iway eanmay otay ecturelay youway away ittlelay uponway eirthay 
accountway yselfmay. Utbay, ymay earday Ankensteinfray," ontinuedcay ehay, oppingstay 
ortshay andway azinggay ullfay inway ymay acefay, "Iway idday otnay eforebay emarkray owhay eryvay illway 
youway appearway; osay inthay andway alepay; youway ooklay asway ifway youway adhay eenbay atchingway orfay 
everalsay ightsnay." 

"Youway avehay uessedgay ightray; Iway avehay atelylay eenbay osay eeplyday engagedway inway oneway 
occupationway atthay Iway avehay otnay allowedway yselfmay ufficientsay estray, asway youway eesay; 
utbay Iway opehay, Iway incerelysay opehay, atthay allway esethay employmentsway areway ownay atway anway 
endway andway atthay Iway amway atway engthlay eefray." 

Iway embledtray excessivelyway; Iway ouldcay otnay endureway otay inkthay ofway, andway arfay esslay otay 
alludeway otay, ethay occurrencesway ofway ethay ecedingpray ightnay. Iway alkedway ithway away 
uickqay acepay, andway eway oonsay arrivedway atway ymay ollegecay. Iway enthay eflectedray, andway 
ethay oughtthay ademay emay ivershay, atthay ethay eaturecray omwhay Iway adhay eftlay inway ymay 
apartmentway ightmay illstay ebay erethay, aliveway andway alkingway aboutway. Iway eadeddray otay 
eholdbay isthay onstermay, utbay Iway earedfay illstay oremay atthay Enryhay ouldshay eesay imhay. 
Entreatingway imhay, ereforethay, otay emainray away ewfay inutesmay atway ethay ottombay ofway ethay 
airsstay, Iway artedday upway owardstay ymay ownway oomray. Ymay andhay asway alreadyway onway ethay 
ocklay ofway ethay oorday eforebay Iway ecollectedray yselfmay. Iway enthay ausedpay, andway away 
oldcay iveringshay amecay overway emay. Iway ewthray ethay oorday orciblyfay openway, asway 
ildrenchay areway accustomedway otay oday enwhay eythay expectway away ectrespay otay andstay inway 
aitingway orfay emthay onway ethay otherway idesay; utbay othingnay appearedway. Iway eppedstay 
earfullyfay inway: ethay apartmentway asway emptyway, andway ymay edroombay asway alsoway eedfray 
omfray itsway ideoushay uestgay. Iway ouldcay ardlyhay elievebay atthay osay eatgray away oodgay 
ortunefay ouldcay avehay efallenbay emay, utbay enwhay Iway ecamebay assuredway atthay ymay enemyway 
adhay indeedway edflay, Iway appedclay ymay andshay orfay oyjay andway anray ownday otay Ervalclay. 

Eway ascendedway intoway ymay oomray, andway ethay ervantsay esentlypray oughtbray eakfastbray; 
utbay Iway asway unableway otay ontaincay yselfmay. Itway asway otnay oyjay onlyway atthay ossessedpay 
emay; Iway eltfay ymay eshflay ingletay ithway excessway ofway ensitivenesssay, andway ymay ulsepay 
eatbay apidlyray. Iway asway unableway otay emainray orfay away inglesay instantway inway ethay amesay 
aceplay; Iway umpedjay overway ethay airschay, appedclay ymay andshay, andway aughedlay aloudway. 
Ervalclay atway irstfay attributedway ymay unusualway iritsspay otay oyjay onway ishay arrivalway, 
utbay enwhay ehay observedway emay oremay attentivelyway, ehay awsay away ildnessway inway ymay eyesway 
orfay ichwhay ehay ouldcay otnay accountway, andway ymay oudlay, unrestrainedway, eartlesshay 
aughterlay ightenedfray andway astonishedway imhay. 

"Ymay earday Ictorvay," iedcray ehay, "atwhay, orfay Odgay's akesay, isway ethay attermay? Oday 
otnay aughlay inway atthay annermay. Owhay illway youway areway! Atwhay isway ethay ausecay ofway allway 
isthay?" 

"Oday otnay askway emay," iedcray Iway, uttingpay ymay andshay eforebay ymay eyesway, orfay Iway 
oughtthay Iway awsay ethay eadeddray ectrespay ideglay intoway ethay oomray; "EHAY ancay elltay. 
Ohway, avesay emay! Avesay emay!" Iway imaginedway atthay ethay onstermay eizedsay emay; Iway 
uggledstray uriouslyfay andway ellfay ownday inway away itfay. 

Oorpay Ervalclay! Atwhay ustmay avehay eenbay ishay eelingsfay? Away eetingmay, ichwhay ehay 
anticipatedway ithway uchsay oyjay, osay angelystray urnedtay otay itternessbay. Utbay Iway 
asway otnay ethay itnessway ofway ishay iefgray, orfay Iway asway ifelesslay andway idday otnay 
ecoverray ymay ensessay orfay away onglay, onglay imetay. 

Isthay asway ethay ommencementcay ofway away ervousnay everfay ichwhay onfinedcay emay orfay 
everalsay onthsmay. Uringday allway atthay imetay Enryhay asway ymay onlyway ursenay. Iway 
afterwardsway earnedlay atthay, owingknay ymay atherfay's advancedway ageway andway unfitnessway 
orfay osay onglay away ourneyjay, andway owhay etchedwray ymay icknesssay ouldway akemay 
Elizabethway, ehay aredspay emthay isthay iefgray ybay oncealingcay ethay extentway ofway ymay 
isorderday. Ehay ewknay atthay Iway ouldcay otnay avehay away oremay indkay andway attentiveway 
ursenay anthay imselfhay; andway, irmfay inway ethay opehay ehay eltfay ofway ymay ecoveryray, ehay 
idday otnay oubtday atthay, insteadway ofway oingday armhay, ehay erformedpay ethay indestkay 
actionway atthay ehay ouldcay owardstay emthay. 

Utbay Iway asway inway ealityray eryvay illway, andway urelysay othingnay utbay ethay unboundedway andway 
unremittingway attentionsway ofway ymay iendfray ouldcay avehay estoredray emay otay ifelay. 
Ethay ormfay ofway ethay onstermay onway omwhay Iway adhay estowedbay existenceway asway oreverfay 
eforebay ymay eyesway, andway Iway avedray incessantlyway oncerningcay imhay. Oubtlessday ymay 
ordsway urprisedsay Enryhay; ehay atway irstfay elievedbay emthay otay ebay ethay anderingsway 
ofway ymay isturbedday imaginationway, utbay ethay ertinacitypay ithway ichwhay Iway 
ontinuallycay ecurredray otay ethay amesay ubjectsay ersuadedpay imhay atthay ymay isorderday 
indeedway owedway itsway originway otay omesay uncommonway andway erribletay eventway. 

Ybay eryvay owslay egreesday, andway ithway equentfray elapsesray atthay alarmedway andway 
ievedgray ymay iendfray, Iway ecoveredray. Iway ememberray ethay irstfay imetay Iway ecamebay 
apablecay ofway observingway outwardway objectsway ithway anyway indkay ofway easureplay, Iway 
erceivedpay atthay ethay allenfay eaveslay adhay isappearedday andway atthay ethay youngway 
udsbay ereway ootingshay orthfay omfray ethay eestray atthay adedshay ymay indowway. Itway asway 
away ivineday ingspray, andway ethay easonsay ontributedcay eatlygray otay ymay 
onvalescencecay. Iway eltfay alsoway entimentssay ofway oyjay andway affectionway eviveray inway 
ymay osombay; ymay oomglay isappearedday, andway inway away ortshay imetay Iway ecamebay asway 
eerfulchay asway eforebay Iway asway attackedway ybay ethay atalfay assionpay. 

"Earestday Ervalclay," exclaimedway Iway, "owhay indkay, owhay eryvay oodgay youway areway otay emay. 
Isthay olewhay interway, insteadway ofway eingbay entspay inway udystay, asway youway omisedpray 
yourselfway, ashay eenbay onsumedcay inway ymay icksay oomray. Owhay allshay Iway everway epayray 
youway? Iway eelfay ethay eatestgray emorseray orfay ethay isappointmentday ofway ichwhay Iway 
avehay eenbay ethay occasionway, utbay youway illway orgivefay emay." 

"Youway illway epayray emay entirelyway ifway youway oday otnay iscomposeday yourselfway, utbay etgay 
ellway asway astfay asway youway ancay; andway incesay youway appearway inway uchsay oodgay iritsspay, Iway 
aymay eakspay otay youway onway oneway ubjectsay, aymay Iway otnay?" 

Iway embledtray. Oneway ubjectsay! Atwhay ouldcay itway ebay? Ouldcay ehay alludeway otay anway 
objectway onway omwhay Iway aredday otnay evenway inkthay? "Omposecay yourselfway," aidsay 
Ervalclay, owhay observedway ymay angechay ofway olourcay, "Iway illway otnay entionmay itway ifway itway 
agitatesway youway; utbay yourway atherfay andway ousincay ouldway ebay eryvay appyhay ifway eythay 
eceivedray away etterlay omfray youway inway yourway ownway andwritinghay. Eythay ardlyhay owknay 
owhay illway youway avehay eenbay andway areway uneasyway atway yourway onglay ilencesay." 

"Isway atthay allway, ymay earday Enryhay? Owhay ouldcay youway upposesay atthay ymay irstfay 
oughtthay ouldway otnay yflay owardstay osethay earday, earday iendsfray omwhay Iway ovelay andway 
owhay areway osay eservingday ofway ymay ovelay?" 

"Ifway isthay isway yourway esentpray empertay, ymay iendfray, youway illway erhapspay ebay adglay otay 
eesay away etterlay atthay ashay eenbay yinglay erehay omesay aysday orfay youway; itway isway omfray 
yourway ousincay, Iway elievebay." 



Apterchay 6 

Ervalclay enthay utpay ethay ollowingfay etterlay intoway ymay andshay. Itway asway omfray ymay 
ownway Elizabethway: 

"Ymay earestday Ousincay, 

"Youway avehay eenbay illway, eryvay illway, andway evenway ethay onstantcay etterslay ofway earday 
indkay Enryhay areway otnay ufficientsay otay eassureray emay onway yourway accountway. Youway areway 
orbiddenfay otay itewray--to oldhay away enpay; yetway oneway ordway omfray youway, earday Ictorvay, 
isway ecessarynay otay almcay ourway apprehensionsway. Orfay away onglay imetay Iway avehay oughtthay 
atthay eachway ostpay ouldway ingbray isthay inelay, andway ymay ersuasionspay avehay 
estrainedray ymay uncleway omfray undertakingway away ourneyjay otay Ingolstadtway. Iway avehay 
eventedpray ishay encounteringway ethay inconveniencesway andway erhapspay angersday ofway osay 
onglay away ourneyjay, yetway owhay oftenway avehay Iway egrettedray otnay eingbay ableway otay 
erformpay itway yselfmay! Iway igurefay otay yselfmay atthay ethay asktay ofway attendingway onway 
yourway ickbedsay ashay evolvedday onway omesay ercenarymay oldway ursenay, owhay ouldcay evernay 
uessgay yourway ishesway ornay inistermay otay emthay ithway ethay arecay andway affectionway ofway 
yourway oorpay ousincay. Yetway atthay isway overway ownay: Ervalclay iteswray atthay indeedway 
youway areway ettinggay etterbay. Iway eagerlyway opehay atthay youway illway onfirmcay isthay 
intelligenceway oonsay inway yourway ownway andwritinghay. 

"Etgay ellway--and eturnray otay usway. Youway illway indfay away appyhay, eerfulchay omehay andway 
iendsfray owhay ovelay youway earlyday. Yourway atherfay's ealthhay isway igorousvay, andway ehay 
asksway utbay otay eesay youway, utbay otay ebay assuredway atthay youway areway ellway; andway otnay away 
arecay illway everway oudclay ishay enevolentbay ountenancecay. Owhay easedplay youway ouldway 
ebay otay emarkray ethay improvementway ofway ourway Ernestway! Ehay isway ownay ixteensay andway ullfay 
ofway activityway andway iritspay. Ehay isway esirousday otay ebay away uetray Isssway andway otay enterway 
intoway oreignfay ervicesay, utbay eway annotcay artpay ithway imhay, atway eastlay untilway ishay 
elderway otherbray eturnsray otay usway. Ymay uncleway isway otnay easedplay ithway ethay ideaway ofway 
away ilitarymay areercay inway away istantday ountrycay, utbay Ernestway evernay adhay yourway 
owerspay ofway applicationway. Ehay ookslay uponway udystay asway anway odiousway etterfay; ishay 
imetay isway entspay inway ethay openway airway, imbingclay ethay illshay orway owingray onway ethay 
akelay. Iway earfay atthay ehay illway ecomebay anway idlerway unlessway eway yieldway ethay ointpay 
andway ermitpay imhay otay enterway onway ethay ofessionpray ichwhay ehay ashay electedsay. 

"Ittlelay alterationway, exceptway ethay owthgray ofway ourway earday ildrenchay, ashay akentay 
aceplay incesay youway eftlay usway. Ethay ueblay akelay andway owsnay-clad ountainsmay--they 
evernay angechay; andway Iway inkthay ourway acidplay omehay andway ourway ontentedcay eartshay areway 
egulatedray ybay ethay amesay immutableway awslay. Ymay iflingtray occupationsway aketay upway 
ymay imetay andway amuseway emay, andway Iway amway ewardedray orfay anyway exertionsway ybay eeingsay 
onenay utbay appyhay, indkay acesfay aroundway emay. Incesay youway eftlay usway, utbay oneway 
angechay ashay akentay aceplay inway ourway ittlelay ouseholdhay. Oday youway ememberray onway 
atwhay occasionway Ustinejay Oritzmay enteredway ourway amilyfay? Obablypray youway oday otnay; 
Iway illway elateray erhay istoryhay, ereforethay inway away ewfay ordsway. Adamemay Oritzmay, 
erhay othermay, asway away idowway ithway ourfay ildrenchay, ofway omwhay Ustinejay asway ethay 
irdthay. Isthay irlgay adhay alwaysway eenbay ethay avouritefay ofway erhay atherfay, utbay 
oughthray away angestray erversitypay, erhay othermay ouldcay otnay endureway erhay, andway 
afterway ethay eathday ofway Mway. Oritzmay, eatedtray erhay eryvay illway. Ymay auntway observedway 
isthay, andway enwhay Ustinejay asway elvetway yearsway ofway ageway, evailedpray onway erhay othermay 
otay allowway erhay otay ivelay atway ourway ousehay. Ethay epublicanray institutionsway ofway ourway 
ountrycay avehay oducedpray implersay andway appierhay annersmay anthay osethay ichwhay 
evailpray inway ethay eatgray onarchiesmay atthay urroundsay itway. Encehay erethay isway esslay 
istinctionday etweenbay ethay everalsay assesclay ofway itsway inhabitantsway; andway ethay 
owerlay ordersway, eingbay eithernay osay oorpay ornay osay espisedday, eirthay annersmay areway 
oremay efinedray andway oralmay. Away ervantsay inway Enevagay oesday otnay eanmay ethay amesay 
ingthay asway away ervantsay inway Ancefray andway Englandway. Ustinejay, usthay eceivedray inway 
ourway amilyfay, earnedlay ethay utiesday ofway away ervantsay, away onditioncay ichwhay, inway ourway 
ortunatefay ountrycay, oesday otnay includeway ethay ideaway ofway ignoranceway andway away 
acrificesay ofway ethay ignityday ofway away umanhay eingbay. 

"Ustinejay, youway aymay ememberray, asway away eatgray avouritefay ofway yoursway; andway Iway 
ecollectray youway onceway emarkedray atthay ifway youway ereway inway anway illway umourhay, oneway 
anceglay omfray Ustinejay ouldcay issipateday itway, orfay ethay amesay easonray atthay 
Ariostoway ivesgay oncerningcay ethay eautybay ofway Angelicaway--she ookedlay osay 
ankfray-hearted andway appyhay. Ymay auntway onceivedcay away eatgray attachmentway orfay erhay, 
ybay ichwhay eshay asway inducedway otay ivegay erhay anway educationway uperiorsay otay atthay 
ichwhay eshay adhay atway irstfay intendedway. Isthay enefitbay asway ullyfay epaidray; 
Ustinejay asway ethay ostmay atefulgray ittlelay eaturecray inway ethay orldway: Iway oday otnay 
eanmay atthay eshay ademay anyway ofessionspray Iway evernay eardhay oneway asspay erhay ipslay, utbay 
youway ouldcay eesay ybay erhay eyesway atthay eshay almostway adoredway erhay otectresspray. 
Althoughway erhay ispositionday asway aygay andway inway anymay espectsray inconsiderateway, 
yetway eshay aidpay ethay eatestgray attentionway otay everyway esturegay ofway ymay auntway. Eshay 
oughtthay erhay ethay odelmay ofway allway excellenceway andway endeavouredway otay imitateway erhay 
aseologyphray andway annersmay, osay atthay evenway ownay eshay oftenway emindsray emay ofway erhay. 

"Enwhay ymay earestday auntway iedday everyway oneway asway ootay uchmay occupiedway inway eirthay ownway 
iefgray otay oticenay oorpay Ustinejay, owhay adhay attendedway erhay uringday erhay illnessway 
ithway ethay ostmay anxiousway affectionway. Oorpay Ustinejay asway eryvay illway; utbay otherway 
ialstray ereway eservedray orfay erhay. 

"Oneway ybay oneway, erhay othersbray andway istersay iedday; andway erhay othermay, ithway ethay 
exceptionway ofway erhay eglectednay aughterday, asway eftlay ildlesschay. Ethay 
onsciencecay ofway ethay omanway asway oubledtray; eshay eganbay otay inkthay atthay ethay 
eathsday ofway erhay avouritesfay asway away udgementjay omfray eavenhay otay astisechay erhay 
artialitypay. Eshay asway away Omanray Atholiccay; andway Iway elievebay erhay onfessorcay 
onfirmedcay ethay ideaway ichwhay eshay adhay onceivedcay. Accordinglyway, away ewfay onthsmay 
afterway yourway epartureday orfay Ingolstadtway, Ustinejay asway alledcay omehay ybay erhay 
epentantray othermay. Oorpay irlgay! Eshay eptway enwhay eshay uittedqay ourway ousehay; eshay 
asway uchmay alteredway incesay ethay eathday ofway ymay auntway; iefgray adhay ivengay oftnesssay 
andway away inningway ildnessmay otay erhay annersmay, ichwhay adhay eforebay eenbay emarkableray 
orfay ivacityvay. Ornay asway erhay esidenceray atway erhay othermay's ousehay ofway away aturenay 
otay estoreray erhay aietygay. Ethay oorpay omanway asway eryvay acillatingvay inway erhay 
epentanceray. Eshay ometimessay eggedbay Ustinejay otay orgivefay erhay unkindnessway, 
utbay uchmay oftenerway accusedway erhay ofway avinghay ausedcay ethay eathsday ofway erhay 
othersbray andway istersay. Erpetualpay ettingfray atway engthlay ewthray Adamemay Oritzmay 
intoway away eclineday, ichwhay atway irstfay increasedway erhay irritabilityway, utbay eshay isway 
ownay atway eacepay orfay everway. Eshay iedday onway ethay irstfay approachway ofway oldcay eatherway, 
atway ethay eginningbay ofway isthay astlay interway. Ustinejay ashay ustjay eturnedray otay usway; 
andway Iway assureway youway Iway ovelay erhay enderlytay. Eshay isway eryvay everclay andway entlegay, 
andway extremelyway ettypray; asway Iway entionedmay eforebay, erhay ienmay andway erhay 
expressionway ontinuallycay emindray emay ofway ymay earday auntway. 

"Iway ustmay aysay alsoway away ewfay ordsway otay youway, ymay earday ousincay, ofway ittlelay arlingday 
Illiamway. Iway ishway youway ouldcay eesay imhay; ehay isway eryvay alltay ofway ishay ageway, ithway 
eetsway aughinglay ueblay eyesway, arkday eyelashesway, andway urlingcay airhay. Enwhay ehay 
ilessmay, otway ittlelay implesday appearway onway eachway eekchay, ichwhay areway osyray ithway 
ealthhay. Ehay ashay alreadyway adhay oneway orway otway ittlelay IVESWAY, utbay Ouisalay Ironbay 
isway ishay avouritefay, away ettypray ittlelay irlgay ofway ivefay yearsway ofway ageway. 

"Ownay, earday Ictorvay, Iway areday aysay youway ishway otay ebay indulgedway inway away ittlelay 
ossipgay oncerningcay ethay oodgay eoplepay ofway Enevagay. Ethay ettypray Issmay Ansfieldmay 
ashay alreadyway eceivedray ethay ongratulatorycay isitsvay onway erhay approachingway 
arriagemay ithway away youngway Englishmanway, Ohnjay Elbournemay, Esqway. Erhay uglyway 
istersay, Anonmay, arriedmay Mway. Uvillardday, ethay ichray ankerbay, astlay autumnway. Yourway 
avouritefay oolfellowschay, Ouislay Anoirmay, ashay ufferedsay everalsay isfortunesmay 
incesay ethay epartureday ofway Ervalclay omfray Enevagay. Utbay ehay ashay alreadyway 
ecoveredray ishay iritsspay, andway isway eportedray otay ebay onway ethay ointpay ofway arryingmay away 
ivelylay ettypray Enchwomanfray, Adamemay Averniertay. Eshay isway away idowway, andway uchmay 
olderway anthay Anoirmay; utbay eshay isway eryvay uchmay admiredway, andway away avouritefay ithway 
everybodyway. 

"Iway avehay ittenwray yselfmay intoway etterbay iritsspay, earday ousincay; utbay ymay anxietyway 
eturnsray uponway emay asway Iway oncludecay. Itewray, earestday Ictorvay,--one inelay--one 
ordway illway ebay away essingblay otay usway. Entay ousandthay anksthay otay Enryhay orfay ishay 
indnesskay, ishay affectionway, andway ishay anymay etterslay; eway areway incerelysay 
atefulgray. Adieuway! ymay ousincay; aketay arecay ofway yourway elfsay; andway, Iway entreatway 
youway, itewray! 

"Elizabethway Avenzalay. 

"Enevagay, Archmay 18, 17--." 


"Earday, earday Elizabethway!" Iway exclaimedway, enwhay Iway adhay eadray erhay etterlay: "Iway 
illway itewray instantlyway andway elieveray emthay omfray ethay anxietyway eythay ustmay eelfay." 
Iway otewray, andway isthay exertionway eatlygray atiguedfay emay; utbay ymay onvalescencecay 
adhay ommencedcay, andway oceededpray egularlyray. Inway anotherway ortnightfay Iway asway 
ableway otay eavelay ymay amberchay. 

Oneway ofway ymay irstfay utiesday onway ymay ecoveryray asway otay introduceway Ervalclay otay ethay 
everalsay ofessorspray ofway ethay universityway. Inway oingday isthay, Iway underwentway away 
indkay ofway oughray usageway, illway efittingbay ethay oundsway atthay ymay indmay adhay 
ustainedsay. Everway incesay ethay atalfay ightnay, ethay endway ofway ymay abourslay, andway ethay 
eginningbay ofway ymay isfortunesmay, Iway adhay onceivedcay away iolentvay antipathyway evenway 
otay ethay amenay ofway aturalnay ilosophyphay. Enwhay Iway asway otherwiseway uiteqay estoredray 
otay ealthhay, ethay ightsay ofway away emicalchay instrumentway ouldway enewray allway ethay agonyway 
ofway ymay ervousnay ymptomssay. Enryhay awsay isthay, andway adhay emovedray allway ymay 
apparatusway omfray ymay iewvay. Ehay adhay alsoway angedchay ymay apartmentway; orfay ehay 
erceivedpay atthay Iway adhay acquiredway away islikeday orfay ethay oomray ichwhay adhay 
eviouslypray eenbay ymay aboratorylay. Utbay esethay arescay ofway Ervalclay ereway ademay ofway 
onay availway enwhay Iway isitedvay ethay ofessorspray. Mway. Aldmanway inflictedway orturetay 
enwhay ehay aisedpray, ithway indnesskay andway armthway, ethay astonishingway ogresspray Iway 
adhay ademay inway ethay iencesscay. Ehay oonsay erceivedpay atthay Iway islikedday ethay 
ubjectsay; utbay otnay uessinggay ethay ealray ausecay, ehay attributedway ymay eelingsfay otay 
odestymay, andway angedchay ethay ubjectsay omfray ymay improvementway, otay ethay iencescay 
itselfway, ithway away esireday, asway Iway evidentlyway awsay, ofway awingdray emay outway. Atwhay 
ouldcay Iway oday? Ehay eantmay otay easeplay, andway ehay ormentedtay emay. Iway eltfay asway ifway ehay 
adhay acedplay arefullycay, oneway ybay oneway, inway ymay iewvay osethay instrumentsway ichwhay 
ereway otay ebay afterwardsway usedway inway uttingpay emay otay away owslay andway uelcray eathday. Iway 
ithedwray underway ishay ordsway, yetway aredday otnay exhibitway ethay ainpay Iway eltfay. 
Ervalclay, osewhay eyesway andway eelingsfay ereway alwaysway uickqay inway iscerningday ethay 
ensationssay ofway othersway, eclinedday ethay ubjectsay, allegingway, inway excuseway, ishay 
otaltay ignoranceway; andway ethay onversationcay ooktay away oremay eneralgay urntay. Iway 
ankedthay ymay iendfray omfray ymay earthay, utbay Iway idday otnay eakspay. Iway awsay ainlyplay 
atthay ehay asway urprisedsay, utbay ehay evernay attemptedway otay awdray ymay ecretsay omfray 
emay; andway althoughway Iway ovedlay imhay ithway away ixturemay ofway affectionway andway everenceray 
atthay ewknay onay oundsbay, yetway Iway ouldcay evernay ersuadepay yselfmay otay onfidecay inway 
imhay atthay eventway ichwhay asway osay oftenway esentpray otay ymay ecollectionray, utbay ichwhay 
Iway earedfay ethay etailday otay anotherway ouldway onlyway impressway oremay eeplyday. 

Mway. Empekray asway otnay equallyway ocileday; andway inway ymay onditioncay atway atthay imetay, ofway 
almostway insupportableway ensitivenesssay, ishay arshhay untblay encomiumsway avegay emay 
evenway oremay ainpay anthay ethay enevolentbay approbationway ofway Mway. Aldmanway. "Dway--n 
ethay ellowfay!" iedcray ehay; "ywhay, Mway. Ervalclay, Iway assureway youway ehay ashay outstriptway 
usway allway. Ayway, arestay ifway youway easeplay; utbay itway isway everthelessnay uetray. Away 
youngsterway owhay, utbay away ewfay yearsway agoway, elievedbay inway Orneliuscay Agrippaway asway 
irmlyfay asway inway ethay ospelgay, ashay ownay etsay imselfhay atway ethay eadhay ofway ethay 
universityway; andway ifway ehay isway otnay oonsay ulledpay ownday, eway allshay allway ebay outway ofway 
ountenancecay.--Ay, ayway," ontinuedcay ehay, observingway ymay acefay expressiveway ofway 
ufferingsay, "Mway. Ankensteinfray isway odestmay; anway excellentway ualityqay inway away youngway 
anmay. Youngway enmay ouldshay ebay iffidentday ofway emselvesthay, youway owknay, Mway. 
Ervalclay: Iway asway yselfmay enwhay youngway; utbay atthay earsway outway inway away eryvay ortshay 
imetay." 

Mway. Empekray adhay ownay ommencedcay anway eulogyway onway imselfhay, ichwhay appilyhay urnedtay 
ethay onversationcay omfray away ubjectsay atthay asway osay annoyingway otay emay. 

Ervalclay adhay evernay ympathizedsay inway ymay astestay orfay aturalnay iencescay; andway ishay 
iterarylay ursuitspay ifferedday ollywhay omfray osethay ichwhay adhay occupiedway emay. Ehay 
amecay otay ethay universityway ithway ethay esignday ofway akingmay imselfhay ompletecay 
astermay ofway ethay orientalway anguageslay, andway usthay ehay ouldshay openway away ieldfay orfay 
ethay anplay ofway ifelay ehay adhay arkedmay outway orfay imselfhay. Esolvedray otay ursuepay onay 
ingloriousway areercay, ehay urnedtay ishay eyesway owardtay ethay Eastway, asway affordingway 
opescay orfay ishay iritspay ofway enterpriseway. Ethay Ersianpay, Arabicway, andway Anskritsay 
anguageslay engagedway ishay attentionway, andway Iway asway easilyway inducedway otay enterway onway 
ethay amesay udiesstay. Idlenessway adhay everway eenbay irksomeway otay emay, andway ownay atthay Iway 
ishedway otay yflay omfray eflectionray, andway atedhay ymay ormerfay udiesstay, Iway eltfay 
eatgray eliefray inway eingbay ethay ellowfay-pupil ithway ymay iendfray, andway oundfay otnay 
onlyway instructionway utbay onsolationcay inway ethay orksway ofway ethay orientalistsway. Iway 
idday otnay, ikelay imhay, attemptway away iticalcray owledgeknay ofway eirthay ialectsday, orfay 
Iway idday otnay ontemplatecay akingmay anyway otherway useway ofway emthay anthay emporarytay 
amusementway. Iway eadray erelymay otay understandway eirthay eaningmay, andway eythay ellway 
epaidray ymay abourslay. Eirthay elancholymay isway oothingsay, andway eirthay oyjay 
elevatingway, otay away egreeday Iway evernay experiencedway inway udyingstay ethay authorsway ofway 
anyway otherway ountrycay. Enwhay youway eadray eirthay itingswray, ifelay appearsway otay 
onsistcay inway away armway unsay andway away ardengay ofway osesray,--in ethay ilessmay andway ownsfray 
ofway away airfay enemyway, andway ethay irefay atthay onsumescay yourway ownway earthay. Owhay 
ifferentday omfray ethay anlymay andway eroicalhay oetrypay ofway Eecegray andway Omeray! 

Ummersay assedpay awayway inway esethay occupationsway, andway ymay eturnray otay Enevagay asway 
ixedfay orfay ethay atterlay endway ofway autumnway; utbay eingbay elayedday ybay everalsay 
accidentsway, interway andway owsnay arrivedway, ethay oadsray ereway eemedday impassableway, 
andway ymay ourneyjay asway etardedray untilway ethay ensuingway ingspray. Iway eltfay isthay 
elayday eryvay itterlybay; orfay Iway ongedlay otay eesay ymay ativenay owntay andway ymay elovedbay 
iendsfray. Ymay eturnray adhay onlyway eenbay elayedday osay onglay, omfray anway 
unwillingnessway otay eavelay Ervalclay inway away angestray aceplay, eforebay ehay adhay ecomebay 
acquaintedway ithway anyway ofway itsway inhabitantsway. Ethay interway, oweverhay, asway entspay 
eerfullychay; andway althoughway ethay ingspray asway uncommonlyway atelay, enwhay itway amecay 
itsway eautybay ompensatedcay orfay itsway ilatorinessday. 

Ethay onthmay ofway Aymay adhay alreadyway ommencedcay, andway Iway expectedway ethay etterlay ailyday 
ichwhay asway otay ixfay ethay ateday ofway ymay epartureday, enwhay Enryhay oposedpray away 
edestrianpay ourtay inway ethay environsway ofway Ingolstadtway, atthay Iway ightmay idbay away 
ersonalpay arewellfay otay ethay ountrycay Iway adhay osay onglay inhabitedway. Iway accededway 
ithway easureplay otay isthay opositionpray: Iway asway ondfay ofway exerciseway, andway Ervalclay 
adhay alwaysway eenbay ymay avouritefay ompanioncay inway ethay ambleray ofway isthay aturenay 
atthay Iway adhay akentay amongway ethay enesscay ofway ymay ativenay ountrycay. 

Eway assedpay away ortnightfay inway esethay erambulationspay: ymay ealthhay andway iritsspay 
adhay onglay eenbay estoredray, andway eythay ainedgay additionalway engthstray omfray ethay 
alubrioussay airway Iway eathedbray, ethay aturalnay incidentsway ofway ourway ogresspray, andway 
ethay onversationcay ofway ymay iendfray. Udystay adhay eforebay ecludedsay emay omfray ethay 
intercourseway ofway ymay ellowfay-creatures, andway enderedray emay unsocialway; utbay 
Ervalclay alledcay orthfay ethay etterbay eelingsfay ofway ymay earthay; ehay againway aughttay 
emay otay ovelay ethay aspectway ofway aturenay, andway ethay eerfulchay acesfay ofway ildrenchay. 
Excellentway iendfray! owhay incerelysay youway idday ovelay emay, andway endeavourway otay 
elevateway ymay indmay untilway itway asway onway away evellay ithway yourway ownway. Away elfishsay 
ursuitpay adhay ampedcray andway arrowednay emay, untilway yourway entlenessgay andway 
affectionway armedway andway openedway ymay ensessay; Iway ecamebay ethay amesay appyhay eaturecray 
owhay, away ewfay yearsway agoway, ovedlay andway elovedbay ybay allway, adhay onay orrowsay orway arecay. 
Enwhay appyhay, inanimateway aturenay adhay ethay owerpay ofway estowingbay onway emay ethay ostmay 
elightfulday ensationssay. Away erenesay yskay andway erdantvay ieldsfay illedfay emay ithway 
ecstasyway. Ethay esentpray easonsay asway indeedway ivineday; ethay owersflay ofway ingspray 
oomedblay inway ethay edgeshay, ilewhay osethay ofway ummersay ereway alreadyway inway udbay. Iway 
asway undisturbedway ybay oughtsthay ichwhay uringday ethay ecedingpray yearway adhay essedpray 
uponway emay, otwithstandingnay ymay endeavoursway otay owthray emthay offway, ithway anway 
invincibleway urdenbay. 

Enryhay ejoicedray inway ymay aietygay, andway incerelysay ympathisedsay inway ymay eelingsfay: 
ehay exertedway imselfhay otay amuseway emay, ilewhay ehay expressedway ethay ensationssay atthay 
illedfay ishay oulsay. Ethay esourcesray ofway ishay indmay onway isthay occasionway ereway ulytray 
astonishingway: ishay onversationcay asway ullfay ofway imaginationway; andway eryvay oftenway, 
inway imitationway ofway ethay Ersianpay andway Arabicway iterswray, ehay inventedway alestay ofway 
onderfulway ancyfay andway assionpay. Atway otherway imestay ehay epeatedray ymay avouritefay 
oemspay, orway ewdray emay outway intoway argumentsway, ichwhay ehay upportedsay ithway eatgray 
ingenuityway. Eway eturnedray otay ourway ollegecay onway away Undaysay afternoonway: ethay 
easantspay ereway ancingday, andway everyway oneway eway etmay appearedway aygay andway appyhay. Ymay 
ownway iritsspay ereway ighhay, andway Iway oundedbay alongway ithway eelingsfay ofway unbridledway 
oyjay andway ilarityhay. 



Apterchay 7 

Onway ymay eturnray, Iway oundfay ethay ollowingfay etterlay omfray ymay atherfay:-- 


"Ymay earday Ictorvay, 

"Youway avehay obablypray aitedway impatientlyway orfay away etterlay otay ixfay ethay ateday ofway 
yourway eturnray otay usway; andway Iway asway atway irstfay emptedtay otay itewray onlyway away ewfay 
ineslay, erelymay entioningmay ethay ayday onway ichwhay Iway ouldshay expectway youway. Utbay 
atthay ouldway ebay away uelcray indnesskay, andway Iway areday otnay oday itway. Atwhay ouldway ebay 
yourway urprisesay, ymay onsay, enwhay youway expectedway away appyhay andway adglay elcomeway, otay 
eholdbay, onway ethay ontrarycay, earstay andway etchednesswray? Andway owhay, Ictorvay, ancay 
Iway elateray ourway isfortunemay? Absenceway annotcay avehay enderedray youway allouscay otay 
ourway oysjay andway iefsgray; andway owhay allshay Iway inflictway ainpay onway ymay onglay absentway 
onsay? Iway ishway otay eparepray youway orfay ethay oefulway ewsnay, utbay Iway owknay itway isway 
impossibleway; evenway ownay yourway eyeway imsskay overway ethay agepay otay eeksay ethay ordsway 
ichwhay areway otay onveycay otay youway ethay orriblehay idingstay. 

"Illiamway isway eadday!--that eetsway ildchay, osewhay ilessmay elightedday andway armedway 
ymay earthay, owhay asway osay entlegay, yetway osay aygay! Ictorvay, ehay isway urderedmay! 

"Iway illway otnay attemptway otay onsolecay youway; utbay illway implysay elateray ethay 
ircumstancescay ofway ethay ansactiontray. 

"Astlay Ursdaythay (Aymay 7thay), Iway, ymay iecenay, andway yourway otway othersbray, entway otay 
alkway inway Ainpalaisplay. Ethay eveningway asway armway andway erenesay, andway eway olongedpray 
ourway alkway artherfay anthay usualway. Itway asway alreadyway uskday eforebay eway oughtthay ofway 
eturningray; andway enthay eway iscoveredday atthay Illiamway andway Ernestway, owhay adhay onegay 
onway eforebay, ereway otnay otay ebay oundfay. Eway accordinglyway estedray onway away eatsay untilway 
eythay ouldshay eturnray. Esentlypray Ernestway amecay, andway enquiredway ifway eway adhay eensay 
ishay otherbray; ehay aidsay, atthay ehay adhay eenbay ayingplay ithway imhay, atthay Illiamway 
adhay unray awayway otay idehay imselfhay, andway atthay ehay ainlyvay oughtsay orfay imhay, andway 
afterwardsway aitedway orfay away onglay imetay, utbay atthay ehay idday otnay eturnray. 

"Isthay accountway atherray alarmedway usway, andway eway ontinuedcay otay earchsay orfay imhay 
untilway ightnay ellfay, enwhay Elizabethway onjecturedcay atthay ehay ightmay avehay 
eturnedray otay ethay ousehay. Ehay asway otnay erethay. Eway eturnedray againway, ithway 
orchestay; orfay Iway ouldcay otnay estray, enwhay Iway oughtthay atthay ymay eetsway oybay adhay 
ostlay imselfhay, andway asway exposedway otay allway ethay ampsday andway ewsday ofway ightnay; 
Elizabethway alsoway ufferedsay extremeway anguishway. Aboutway ivefay inway ethay orningmay Iway 
iscoveredday ymay ovelylay oybay, omwhay ethay ightnay eforebay Iway adhay eensay oomingblay andway 
activeway inway ealthhay, etchedstray onway ethay assgray ividlay andway otionlessmay; ethay 
intpray ofway ethay urdermay's ingerfay asway onway ishay ecknay. 

"Ehay asway onveyedcay omehay, andway ethay anguishway atthay asway isiblevay inway ymay 
ountenancecay etrayedbay ethay ecretsay otay Elizabethway. Eshay asway eryvay earnestway otay 
eesay ethay orpsecay. Atway irstfay Iway attemptedway otay eventpray erhay utbay eshay ersistedpay, 
andway enteringway ethay oomray erewhay itway aylay, astilyhay examinedway ethay ecknay ofway ethay 
ictimvay, andway aspingclay erhay andshay exclaimedway, 'Oway Odgay! Iway avehay urderedmay ymay 
arlingday ildchay!' 

"Eshay aintedfay, andway asway estoredray ithway extremeway ifficultyday. Enwhay eshay againway 
ivedlay, itway asway onlyway otay eepway andway ighsay. Eshay oldtay emay, atthay atthay amesay 
eveningway Illiamway adhay easedtay erhay otay etlay imhay earway away eryvay aluablevay 
iniaturemay atthay eshay ossessedpay ofway yourway othermay. Isthay icturepay isway onegay, andway 
asway oubtlessday ethay emptationtay ichwhay urgedway ethay urderermay otay ethay eedday. Eway 
avehay onay acetray ofway imhay atway esentpray, althoughway ourway exertionsway otay iscoverday imhay 
areway unremittedway; utbay eythay illway otnay estoreray ymay elovedbay Illiamway! 

"Omecay, earestday Ictorvay; youway aloneway ancay onsolecay Elizabethway. Eshay eepsway 
ontinuallycay, andway accusesway erselfhay unjustlyway asway ethay ausecay ofway ishay eathday; 
erhay ordsway iercepay ymay earthay. Eway areway allway unhappyway; utbay illway otnay atthay ebay anway 
additionalway otivemay orfay youway, ymay onsay, otay eturnray andway ebay ourway omfortercay? 
Yourway earday othermay! Alasway, Ictorvay! Iway ownay aysay, Ankthay Odgay eshay idday otnay ivelay 
otay itnessway ethay uelcray, iserablemay eathday ofway erhay youngestway arlingday! 

"Omecay, Ictorvay; otnay oodingbray oughtsthay ofway engeancevay againstway ethay assassinway, 
utbay ithway eelingsfay ofway eacepay andway entlenessgay, atthay illway ealhay, insteadway ofway 
esteringfay, ethay oundsway ofway ourway indsmay. Enterway ethay ousehay ofway ourningmay, ymay 
iendfray, utbay ithway indnesskay andway affectionway orfay osethay owhay ovelay youway, andway otnay 
ithway atredhay orfay yourway enemiesway. 

"Yourway affectionateway andway afflictedway atherfay, 
"Alphonseway Ankensteinfray. 



"Enevagay, Aymay 12thay, 17--." 

Ervalclay, owhay adhay atchedway ymay ountenancecay asway Iway eadray isthay etterlay, asway 
urprisedsay otay observeway ethay espairday atthay ucceededsay ethay oyjay Iway atway irstfay 
expressedway onway eceivingray ewnay omfray ymay iendsfray. Iway ewthray ethay etterlay onway ethay 
abletay, andway overedcay ymay acefay ithway ymay andshay. 

"Ymay earday Ankensteinfray," exclaimedway Enryhay, enwhay ehay erceivedpay emay eepway ithway 
itternessbay, "areway youway alwaysway otay ebay unhappyway? Ymay earday iendfray, atwhay ashay 
appenedhay?" 

Iway otionedmay imhay otay aketay upway ethay etterlay, ilewhay Iway alkedway upway andway ownday ethay 
oomray inway ethay extremestway agitationway. Earstay alsoway ushedgay omfray ethay eyesway ofway 
Ervalclay, asway ehay eadray ethay accountway ofway ymay isfortunemay. 

"Iway ancay offerway youway onay onsolationcay, ymay iendfray," aidsay ehay; "yourway isasterday isway 
irreparableway. Atwhay oday youway intendway otay oday?" 

"Otay ogay instantlyway otay Enevagay: omecay ithway emay, Enryhay, otay orderway ethay orseshay." 

Uringday ourway alkway, Ervalclay endeavouredway otay aysay away ewfay ordsway ofway onsolationcay; 
ehay ouldcay onlyway expressway ishay eartfelthay ympathysay. "Oorpay Illiamway!" aidsay ehay, 
"earday ovelylay ildchay, ehay ownay eepsslay ithway ishay angelway othermay! Owhay atthay adhay 
eensay imhay ightbray andway oyousjay inway ishay youngway eautybay, utbay ustmay eepway overway ishay 
untimelyway osslay! Otay ieday osay iserablymay; otay eelfay ethay urderermay's aspgray! Owhay 
uchmay oremay away urderedmay atthay ouldcay estroyday adiantray innocenceway! Oorpay ittlelay 
ellowfay! oneway onlyway onsolationcay avehay eway; ishay iendsfray ournmay andway eepway, utbay 
ehay isway atway estray. Ethay angpay isway overway, ishay ufferingssay areway atway anway endway orfay everway. 
Away odsay overscay ishay entlegay ormfay, andway ehay owsknay onay ainpay. Ehay ancay onay ongerlay 
ebay away ubjectsay orfay itypay; eway ustmay eserveray atthay orfay ishay iserablemay 
urvivorssay." 

Ervalclay okespay usthay asway eway urriedhay oughthray ethay eetsstray; ethay ordsway 
impressedway emselvesthay onway ymay indmay andway Iway ememberedray emthay afterwardsway inway 
olitudesay. Utbay ownay, asway oonsay asway ethay orseshay arrivedway, Iway urriedhay intoway away 
abrioletcay, andway adebay arewellfay otay ymay iendfray. 

Ymay ourneyjay asway eryvay elancholymay. Atway irstfay Iway ishedway otay urryhay onway, orfay Iway 
ongedlay otay onsolecay andway ympathisesay ithway ymay ovedlay andway orrowingsay iendsfray; 
utbay enwhay Iway ewdray earnay ymay ativenay owntay, Iway ackenedslay ymay ogresspray. Iway ouldcay 
ardlyhay ustainsay ethay ultitudemay ofway eelingsfay atthay owdedcray intoway ymay indmay. Iway 
assedpay oughthray enesscay amiliarfay otay ymay youthway, utbay ichwhay Iway adhay otnay eensay 
orfay earlynay ixsay yearsway. Owhay alteredway everyway ingthay ightmay ebay uringday atthay 
imetay! Oneway uddensay andway esolatingday angechay adhay akentay aceplay; utbay away ousandthay 
ittlelay ircumstancescay ightmay avehay ybay egreesday orkedway otherway alterationsway, 
ichwhay, althoughway eythay ereway oneday oremay anquillytray, ightmay otnay ebay ethay esslay 
ecisiveday. Earfay overcameway emay; Iway aredday onay advanceway, eadingdray away ousandthay 
amelessnay evilsway atthay ademay emay embletray, althoughway Iway asway unableway otay efineday 
emthay. Iway emainedray otway aysday atway Ausannelay, inway isthay ainfulpay atestay ofway indmay. 
Iway ontemplatedcay ethay akelay: ethay atersway ereway acidplay; allway aroundway asway almcay; 
andway ethay owysnay ountainsmay, 'ethay alacespay ofway aturenay,' ereway otnay angedchay. Ybay 
egreesday ethay almcay andway eavenlyhay enescay estoredray emay, andway Iway ontinuedcay ymay 
ourneyjay owardstay Enevagay. 

Ethay oadray anray ybay ethay idesay ofway ethay akelay, ichwhay ecamebay arrowernay asway Iway 
approachedway ymay ativenay owntay. Iway iscoveredday oremay istinctlyday ethay ackblay 
idessay ofway Urajay, andway ethay ightbray ummitsay ofway Ontmay Ancblay. Iway eptway ikelay away 
ildchay. "Earday ountainsmay! ymay ownway eautifulbay akelay! owhay oday youway elcomeway yourway 
andererway? Yourway ummitssay areway earclay; ethay yskay andway akelay areway ueblay andway 
acidplay. Isway isthay otay ognosticatepray eacepay, orway otay ockmay atway ymay unhappinessway?" 

Iway earfay, ymay iendfray, atthay Iway allshay enderray yselfmay edioustay ybay ellingdway onway 
esethay eliminarypray ircumstancescay; utbay eythay ereway aysday ofway omparativecay 
appinesshay, andway Iway inkthay ofway emthay ithway easureplay. Ymay ountrycay, ymay elovedbay 
ountrycay! owhay utbay away ativenay ancay elltay ethay elightday Iway ooktay inway againway 
eholdingbay ythay eamsstray, ythay ountainsmay, andway, oremay anthay allway, ythay ovelylay 
akelay! 

Yetway, asway Iway ewdray earernay omehay, iefgray andway earfay againway overcameway emay. Ightnay 
alsoway osedclay aroundway; andway enwhay Iway ouldcay ardlyhay eesay ethay arkday ountainsmay, Iway 
eltfay illstay oremay oomilyglay. Ethay icturepay appearedway away astvay andway imday enescay ofway 
evilway, andway Iway oresawfay obscurelyway atthay Iway asway estinedday otay ecomebay ethay ostmay 
etchedwray ofway umanhay eingsbay. Alasway! Iway ophesiedpray ulytray, andway ailedfay onlyway 
inway oneway inglesay ircumstancecay, atthay inway allway ethay iserymay Iway imaginedway andway 
eadeddray, Iway idday otnay onceivecay ethay undredthhay artpay ofway ethay anguishway Iway asway 
estinedday otay endureway. Itway asway ompletelycay arkday enwhay Iway arrivedway inway ethay 
environsway ofway Enevagay; ethay atesgay ofway ethay owntay ereway alreadyway utshay; andway Iway asway 
obligedway otay asspay ethay ightnay atway Echeronsay, away illagevay atway ethay istanceday ofway 
alfhay away eaguelay omfray ethay itycay. Ethay yskay asway erenesay; andway, asway Iway asway unableway 
otay estray, Iway esolvedray otay isitvay ethay otspay erewhay ymay oorpay Illiamway adhay eenbay 
urderedmay. Asway Iway ouldcay otnay asspay oughthray ethay owntay, Iway asway obligedway otay osscray 
ethay akelay inway away oatbay otay arriveway atway Ainpalaisplay. Uringday isthay ortshay oyagevay 
Iway awsay ethay ightninglay ayingplay onway ethay ummitsay ofway Ontmay Ancblay inway ethay ostmay 
eautifulbay iguresfay. Ethay ormstay appearedway otay approachway apidlyray, andway, onway 
andinglay, Iway ascendedway away owlay illhay, atthay Iway ightmay observeway itsway ogresspray. Itway 
advancedway; ethay eavenshay ereway oudedclay, andway Iway oonsay eltfay ethay ainray omingcay 
owlyslay inway argelay opsdray, utbay itsway iolencevay uicklyqay increasedway. 

Iway uittedqay ymay eatsay, andway alkedway onway, althoughway ethay arknessday andway ormstay 
increasedway everyway inutemay, andway ethay underthay urstbay ithway away errifictay ashcray 
overway ymay eadhay. Itway asway echoedway omfray Alevesay, ethay Urasjay, andway ethay Alpsway ofway 
Avoysay; ividvay ashesflay ofway ightninglay azzledday ymay eyesway, illuminatingway ethay 
akelay, akingmay itway appearway ikelay away astvay eetshay ofway irefay; enthay orfay anway instantway 
everyway ingthay eemedsay ofway away itchypay arknessday, untilway ethay eyeway ecoveredray itselfway 
omfray ethay ecedingpray ashflay. Ethay ormstay, asway isway oftenway ethay asecay inway 
Itzerlandsway, appearedway atway onceway inway ariousvay artspay ofway ethay eavenshay. Ethay 
ostmay iolentvay ormstay unghay exactlyway orthnay ofway ethay owntay, overway ethay artpay ofway ethay 
akelay ichwhay ieslay etweenbay ethay omontorypray ofway Elrivebay andway ethay illagevay ofway 
Opetcay. Anotherway ormstay enlightenedway Urajay ithway aintfay ashesflay; andway anotherway 
arkenedday andway ometimessay isclosedday ethay Olemay, away eakedpay ountainmay otay ethay 
eastway ofway ethay akelay. 

Ilewhay Iway atchedway ethay empesttay, osay eautifulbay yetway errifictay, Iway anderedway onway 
ithway away astyhay epstay. Isthay oblenay arway inway ethay yskay elevatedway ymay iritsspay; Iway 
aspedclay ymay andshay, andway exclaimedway aloudway, "Illiamway, earday angelway! isthay isway 
ythay uneralfay, isthay ythay irgeday!" Asway Iway aidsay esethay ordsway, Iway erceivedpay inway ethay 
oomglay away igurefay ichwhay olestay omfray ehindbay away umpclay ofway eestray earnay emay; Iway 
oodstay ixedfay, azinggay intentlyway: Iway ouldcay otnay ebay istakenmay. Away ashflay ofway 
ightninglay illuminatedway ethay objectway, andway iscoveredday itsway apeshay ainlyplay otay 
emay; itsway iganticgay aturestay, andway ethay eformityday ofway itsway aspectway oremay ideoushay 
anthay elongsbay otay umanityhay, instantlyway informedway emay atthay itway asway ethay etchwray, 
ethay ilthyfay aemonday, otay omwhay Iway adhay ivengay ifelay. Atwhay idday ehay erethay? Ouldcay 
ehay ebay (Iway udderedshay atway ethay onceptioncay) ethay urderermay ofway ymay otherbray? Onay 
oonersay idday atthay ideaway osscray ymay imaginationway, anthay Iway ecamebay onvincedcay ofway 
itsway uthtray; ymay eethtay atteredchay, andway Iway asway orcedfay otay eanlay againstway away eetray 
orfay upportsay. Ethay igurefay assedpay emay uicklyqay, andway Iway ostlay itway inway ethay oomglay. 

Othingnay inway umanhay apeshay ouldcay avehay estroyedday ethay airfay ildchay. EHAY asway ethay 
urderermay! Iway ouldcay otnay oubtday itway. Ethay eremay esencepray ofway ethay ideaway asway anway 
irresistibleway oofpray ofway ethay actfay. Iway oughtthay ofway ursuingpay ethay evilday; utbay 
itway ouldway avehay eenbay inway ainvay, orfay anotherway ashflay iscoveredday imhay otay emay 
anginghay amongway ethay ocksray ofway ethay earlynay erpendicularpay ascentway ofway Ontmay 
Alevesay, away illhay atthay oundsbay Ainpalaisplay onway ethay outhsay. Ehay oonsay eachedray 
ethay ummitsay, andway isappearedday. 

Iway emainedray otionlessmay. Ethay underthay easedcay; utbay ethay ainray illstay 
ontinuedcay, andway ethay enescay asway envelopedway inway anway impenetrableway arknessday. Iway 
evolvedray inway ymay indmay ethay eventsway ichwhay Iway adhay untilway ownay oughtsay otay orgetfay: 
ethay olewhay aintray ofway ymay ogresspray owardtay ethay eationcray; ethay appearanceway ofway 
ethay orksway ofway ymay ownway andshay atway ymay edsidebay; itsway epartureday. Otway yearsway adhay 
ownay earlynay elapsedway incesay ethay ightnay onway ichwhay ehay irstfay eceivedray ifelay; andway 
asway isthay ishay irstfay imecray? Alasway! Iway adhay urnedtay ooselay intoway ethay orldway away 
epravedday etchwray, osewhay elightday asway inway arnagecay andway iserymay; adhay ehay otnay 
urderedmay ymay otherbray? 

Onay oneway ancay onceivecay ethay anguishway Iway ufferedsay uringday ethay emainderray ofway ethay 
ightnay, ichwhay Iway entspay, oldcay andway etway, inway ethay openway airway. Utbay Iway idday otnay 
eelfay ethay inconvenienceway ofway ethay eatherway; ymay imaginationway asway usybay inway 
enesscay ofway evilway andway espairday. Iway onsideredcay ethay eingbay omwhay Iway adhay astcay 
amongway ankindmay, andway endowedway ithway ethay illway andway owerpay otay effectway urposespay 
ofway orrorhay, uchsay asway ethay eedday ichwhay ehay adhay ownay oneday, earlynay inway ethay ightlay 
ofway ymay ownway ampirevay, ymay ownway iritspay etlay ooselay omfray ethay avegray, andway orcedfay 
otay estroyday allway atthay asway earday otay emay. 

Ayday awnedday; andway Iway irectedday ymay epsstay owardstay ethay owntay. Ethay atesgay ereway 
openway, andway Iway astenedhay otay ymay atherfay's ousehay. Ymay irstfay oughtthay asway otay 
iscoverday atwhay Iway ewknay ofway ethay urderermay, andway ausecay instantway ursuitpay otay ebay 
ademay. Utbay Iway ausedpay enwhay Iway eflectedray onway ethay orystay atthay Iway adhay otay elltay. Away 
eingbay omwhay Iway yselfmay adhay ormedfay, andway enduedway ithway ifelay, adhay etmay emay atway 
idnightmay amongway ethay ecipicespray ofway anway inaccessibleway ountainmay. Iway 
ememberedray alsoway ethay ervousnay everfay ithway ichwhay Iway adhay eenbay eizedsay ustjay atway 
ethay imetay atthay Iway atedday ymay eationcray, andway ichwhay ouldway ivegay anway airway ofway 
eliriumday otay away aletay otherwiseway osay utterlyway improbableway. Iway ellway ewknay atthay 
ifway anyway otherway adhay ommunicatedcay uchsay away elationray otay emay, Iway ouldshay avehay 
ookedlay uponway itway asway ethay avingsray ofway insanityway. Esidesbay, ethay angestray aturenay 
ofway ethay animalway ouldway eludeway allway ursuitpay, evenway ifway Iway ereway osay arfay editedcray 
asway otay ersuadepay ymay elativesray otay ommencecay itway. Andway enthay ofway atwhay useway ouldway 
ebay ursuitpay? Owhay ouldcay arrestway away eaturecray apablecay ofway alingscay ethay 
overhangingway idessay ofway Ontmay Alevesay? Esethay eflectionsray eterminedday emay, andway 
Iway esolvedray otay emainray ilentsay. 

Itway asway aboutway ivefay inway ethay orningmay enwhay Iway enteredway ymay atherfay's ousehay. Iway 
oldtay ethay ervantssay otnay otay isturbday ethay amilyfay, andway entway intoway ethay ibrarylay 
otay attendway eirthay usualway ourhay ofway isingray. 

Ixsay yearsway adhay elapsedway, assedpay inway away eamdray utbay orfay oneway indelibleway acetray, 
andway Iway oodstay inway ethay amesay aceplay erewhay Iway adhay astlay embracedway ymay atherfay 
eforebay ymay epartureday orfay Ingolstadtway. Elovedbay andway enerablevay arentpay! Ehay 
illstay emainedray otay emay. Iway azedgay onway ethay icturepay ofway ymay othermay, ichwhay oodstay 
overway ethay antelmay-piece. Itway asway anway istoricalhay ubjectsay, aintedpay atway ymay 
atherfay's esireday, andway epresentedray Arolinecay Eaufortbay inway anway agonyway ofway 
espairday, eelingknay ybay ethay offincay ofway erhay eadday atherfay. Erhay arbgay asway 
usticray, andway erhay eekchay alepay; utbay erethay asway anway airway ofway ignityday andway eautybay, 
atthay ardlyhay ermittedpay ethay entimentsay ofway itypay. Elowbay isthay icturepay asway away 
iniaturemay ofway Illiamway; andway ymay earstay owedflay enwhay Iway ookedlay uponway itway. Ilewhay 
Iway asway usthay engagedway, Ernestway enteredway: ehay adhay eardhay emay arriveway, andway 
astenedhay otay elcomeway emay: "Elcomeway, ymay earestday Ictorvay," aidsay ehay. "Ahway! Iway 
ishway youway adhay omecay eethray onthsmay agoway, andway enthay youway ouldway avehay oundfay usway 
allway oyousjay andway elightedday. Youway omecay otay usway ownay otay areshay away iserymay ichwhay 
othingnay ancay alleviateway; yetway yourway esencepray illway, Iway opehay, eviveray ourway 
atherfay, owhay eemssay inkingsay underway ishay isfortunemay; andway yourway ersuasionspay 
illway induceway oorpay Elizabethway otay easecay erhay ainvay andway ormentingtay 
elfsay-accusations.--Poor Illiamway! ehay asway ourway arlingday andway ourway idepray!" 

Earstay, unrestrainedway, ellfay omfray ymay otherbray's eyesway; away ensesay ofway ortalmay 
agonyway eptcray overway ymay amefray. Eforebay, Iway adhay onlyway imaginedway ethay 
etchednesswray ofway ymay esolatedday omehay; ethay ealityray amecay onway emay asway away ewnay, andway 
away otnay esslay erribletay, isasterday. Iway iedtray otay almcay Ernestway; Iway enquiredway oremay 
inutelymay oncerningcay ymay atherfay, andway erehay Iway amednay ymay ousincay. 

"Eshay ostmay ofway allway," aidsay Ernestway, "equiresray onsolationcay; eshay accusedway 
erselfhay ofway avinghay ausedcay ethay eathday ofway ymay otherbray, andway atthay ademay erhay 
eryvay etchedwray. Utbay incesay ethay urderermay ashay eenbay iscoveredday--" 

"Ethay urderermay iscoveredday! Oodgay Odgay! owhay ancay atthay ebay? owhay ouldcay attemptway 
otay ursuepay imhay? Itway isway impossibleway; oneway ightmay asway ellway ytray otay overtakeway ethay 
indsway, orway onfinecay away ountainmay-stream ithway away awstray. Iway awsay imhay ootay; ehay 
asway eefray astlay ightnay!" 

"Iway oday otnay owknay atwhay youway eanmay," epliedray ymay otherbray, inway accentsway ofway 
onderway, "utbay otay usway ethay iscoveryday eway avehay ademay ompletescay ourway iserymay. Onay 
oneway ouldway elievebay itway atway irstfay; andway evenway ownay Elizabethway illway otnay ebay 
onvincedcay, otwithstandingnay allway ethay evidenceway. Indeedway, owhay ouldway editcray 
atthay Ustinejay Oritzmay, owhay asway osay amiableway, andway ondfay ofway allway ethay amilyfay, 
ouldcay uddenlysay ecomebay osay apablecay ofway osay ightfulfray, osay appallingway away imecray?" 

"Ustinejay Oritzmay! Oorpay, oorpay irlgay, isway eshay ethay accusedway? Utbay itway isway 
ongfullywray; everyway oneway owsknay atthay; onay oneway elievesbay itway, urelysay, Ernestway?" 

"Onay oneway idday atway irstfay; utbay everalsay ircumstancescay amecay outway, atthay avehay 
almostway orcedfay onvictioncay uponway usway; andway erhay ownway ehaviourbay ashay eenbay osay 
onfusedcay, asway otay addway otay ethay evidenceway ofway actsfay away eightway atthay, Iway earfay, 
eaveslay onay opehay orfay oubtday. Utbay eshay illway ebay iedtray odaytay, andway youway illway 
enthay earhay allway." 

Ehay enthay elatedray atthay, ethay orningmay onway ichwhay ethay urdermay ofway oorpay Illiamway 
adhay eenbay iscoveredday, Ustinejay adhay eenbay akentay illway, andway onfinedcay otay erhay 
edbay orfay everalsay aysday. Uringday isthay intervalway, oneway ofway ethay ervantssay, 
appeninghay otay examineway ethay apparelway eshay adhay ornway onway ethay ightnay ofway ethay 
urdermay, adhay iscoveredday inway erhay ocketpay ethay icturepay ofway ymay othermay, ichwhay 
adhay eenbay udgedjay otay ebay ethay emptationtay ofway ethay urderermay. Ethay ervantsay 
instantlyway owedshay itway otay oneway ofway ethay othersway, owhay, ithoutway ayingsay away ordway otay 
anyway ofway ethay amilyfay, entway otay away agistratemay; andway, uponway eirthay epositionday, 
Ustinejay asway apprehendedway. Onway eingbay argedchay ithway ethay actfay, ethay oorpay irlgay 
onfirmedcay ethay uspicionsay inway away eatgray easuremay ybay erhay extremeway onfusioncay ofway 
annermay. 

Isthay asway away angestray aletay, utbay itway idday otnay akeshay ymay aithfay; andway Iway epliedray 
earnestlyway, "Youway areway allway istakenmay; Iway owknay ethay urderermay. Ustinejay, oorpay, 
oodgay Ustinejay, isway innocentway." 

Atway atthay instantway ymay atherfay enteredway. Iway awsay unhappinessway eeplyday impressedway 
onway ishay ountenancecay, utbay ehay endeavouredway otay elcomeway emay eerfullychay; andway, 
afterway eway adhay exchangedway ourway ournfulmay eetinggray, ouldway avehay introducedway 
omesay otherway opictay anthay atthay ofway ourway isasterday, adhay otnay Ernestway exclaimedway, 
"Oodgay Odgay, apapay! Ictorvay ayssay atthay ehay owsknay owhay asway ethay urderermay ofway 
oorpay Illiamway." 

"Eway oday alsoway, unfortunatelyway," epliedray ymay atherfay, "orfay indeedway Iway adhay 
atherray avehay eenbay orfay everway ignorantway anthay avehay iscoveredday osay uchmay 
epravityday andway ungratitudeway inway oneway Iway aluedvay osay ighlyhay." 

"Ymay earday atherfay, youway areway istakenmay; Ustinejay isway innocentway." 

"Ifway eshay isway, Odgay orbidfay atthay eshay ouldshay uffersay asway uiltygay. Eshay isway otay ebay 
iedtray odaytay, andway Iway opehay, Iway incerelysay opehay, atthay eshay illway ebay acquittedway." 

Isthay eechspay almedcay emay. Iway asway irmlyfay onvincedcay inway ymay ownway indmay atthay 
Ustinejay, andway indeedway everyway umanhay eingbay, asway uiltlessgay ofway isthay urdermay. Iway 
adhay onay earfay, ereforethay, atthay anyway ircumstantialcay evidenceway ouldcay ebay 
oughtbray orwardfay ongstray enoughway otay onvictcay erhay. Ymay aletay asway otnay oneway otay 
announceway ubliclypay; itsway astoundingway orrorhay ouldway ebay ookedlay uponway asway 
adnessmay ybay ethay ulgarvay. Idday anyway oneway indeedway existway, exceptway Iway, ethay 
eatorcray, owhay ouldway elievebay, unlessway ishay ensessay onvincedcay imhay, inway ethay 
existenceway ofway ethay ivinglay onumentmay ofway esumptionpray andway ashray ignoranceway 
ichwhay Iway adhay etlay ooselay uponway ethay orldway? 

Eway ereway oonsay oinedjay ybay Elizabethway. Imetay adhay alteredway erhay incesay Iway astlay 
eheldbay erhay; itway adhay endowedway erhay ithway ovelinesslay urpassingsay ethay eautybay ofway 
erhay ildishchay yearsway. Erethay asway ethay amesay andourcay, ethay amesay ivacityvay, utbay 
itway asway alliedway otay anway expressionway oremay ullfay ofway ensibilitysay andway intellectway. 
Eshay elcomedway emay ithway ethay eatestgray affectionway. "Yourway arrivalway, ymay earday 
ousincay," aidsay eshay, "illsfay emay ithway opehay. Youway erhapspay illway indfay omesay 
eansmay otay ustifyjay ymay oorpay uiltlessgay Ustinejay. Alasway! owhay isway afesay, ifway eshay 
ebay onvictedcay ofway imecray? Iway elyray onway erhay innocenceway asway ertainlycay asway Iway oday 
uponway ymay ownway. Ourway isfortunemay isway oublyday ardhay otay usway; eway avehay otnay onlyway 
ostlay atthay ovelylay arlingday oybay, utbay isthay oorpay irlgay, omwhay Iway incerelysay 
ovelay, isway otay ebay orntay awayway ybay evenway away orseway atefay. Ifway eshay isway ondemnedcay, Iway 
evernay allshay owknay oyjay oremay. Utbay eshay illway otnay, Iway amway uresay eshay illway otnay; 
andway enthay Iway allshay ebay appyhay againway, evenway afterway ethay adsay eathday ofway ymay ittlelay 
Illiamway." 

"Eshay isway innocentway, ymay Elizabethway," aidsay Iway, "andway atthay allshay ebay ovedpray; 
earfay othingnay, utbay etlay yourway iritsspay ebay eeredchay ybay ethay assuranceway ofway erhay 
acquittalway." 

"Owhay indkay andway enerousgay youway areway! everyway oneway elseway elievesbay inway erhay uiltgay, 
andway atthay ademay emay etchedwray, orfay Iway ewknay atthay itway asway impossibleway: andway otay 
eesay everyway oneway elseway ejudicedpray inway osay eadlyday away annermay enderedray emay 
opelesshay andway espairingday." Eshay eptway. 

"Earestday iecenay," aidsay ymay atherfay, "ydray yourway earstay. Ifway eshay isway, asway youway 
elievebay, innocentway, elyray onway ethay usticejay ofway ourway awslay, andway ethay activityway 
ithway ichwhay Iway allshay eventpray ethay ightestslay adowshay ofway artialitypay." 



Apterchay 8 

Eway assedpay away ewfay adsay ourshay untilway elevenway oway'clock, enwhay ethay ialtray asway otay 
ommencecay. Ymay atherfay andway ethay estray ofway ethay amilyfay eingbay obligedway otay attendway 
asway itnessesway, Iway accompaniedway emthay otay ethay ourtcay. Uringday ethay olewhay ofway 
isthay etchedwray ockerymay ofway usticejay Iway ufferedsay ivinglay orturetay. Itway asway otay 
ebay ecidedday etherwhay ethay esultray ofway ymay uriositycay andway awlesslay evicesday ouldway 
ausecay ethay eathday ofway otway ofway ymay ellowfay eingsbay: oneway away ilingsmay abebay ullfay ofway 
innocenceway andway oyjay, ethay otherway arfay oremay eadfullydray urderedmay, ithway everyway 
aggravationway ofway infamyway atthay ouldcay akemay ethay urdermay emorablemay inway orrorhay. 
Ustinejay alsoway asway away irlgay ofway eritmay andway ossessedpay ualitiesqay ichwhay omisedpray 
otay enderray erhay ifelay appyhay; ownay allway asway otay ebay obliteratedway inway anway 
ignominiousway avegray, andway Iway ethay ausecay! Away ousandthay imestay atherray ouldway Iway 
avehay onfessedcay yselfmay uiltygay ofway ethay imecray ascribedway otay Ustinejay, utbay Iway 
asway absentway enwhay itway asway ommittedcay, andway uchsay away eclarationday ouldway avehay 
eenbay onsideredcay asway ethay avingsray ofway away admanmay andway ouldway otnay avehay 
exculpatedway erhay owhay ufferedsay oughthray emay. 

Ethay appearanceway ofway Ustinejay asway almcay. Eshay asway esseddray inway ourningmay, andway 
erhay ountenancecay, alwaysway engagingway, asway enderedray, ybay ethay olemnitysay ofway erhay 
eelingsfay, exquisitelyway eautifulbay. Yetway eshay appearedway onfidentcay inway 
innocenceway andway idday otnay embletray, althoughway azedgay onway andway execratedway ybay 
ousandsthay, orfay allway ethay indnesskay ichwhay erhay eautybay ightmay otherwiseway avehay 
excitedway asway obliteratedway inway ethay indsmay ofway ethay ectatorsspay ybay ethay 
imaginationway ofway ethay enormityway eshay asway upposedsay otay avehay ommittedcay. Eshay 
asway anquiltray, yetway erhay anquillitytray asway evidentlyway onstrainedcay; andway asway 
erhay onfusioncay adhay eforebay eenbay adducedway asway away oofpray ofway erhay uiltgay, eshay 
orkedway upway erhay indmay otay anway appearanceway ofway ouragecay. Enwhay eshay enteredway ethay 
ourtcay eshay ewthray erhay eyesway oundray itway andway uicklyqay iscoveredday erewhay eway ereway 
eatedsay. Away eartay eemedsay otay imday erhay eyeway enwhay eshay awsay usway, utbay eshay uicklyqay 
ecoveredray erselfhay, andway away ooklay ofway orrowfulsay affectionway eemedsay otay attestway 
erhay utterway uiltlessnessgay. 

Ethay ialtray eganbay, andway afterway ethay advocateway againstway erhay adhay atedstay ethay 
argechay, everalsay itnessesway ereway alledcay. Everalsay angestray actsfay ombinedcay 
againstway erhay, ichwhay ightmay avehay aggeredstay anyoneway owhay adhay otnay uchsay oofpray 
ofway erhay innocenceway asway Iway adhay. Eshay adhay eenbay outway ethay olewhay ofway ethay ightnay onway 
ichwhay ethay urdermay adhay eenbay ommittedcay andway owardstay orningmay adhay eenbay 
erceivedpay ybay away arketmay-woman otnay arfay omfray ethay otspay erewhay ethay odybay ofway ethay 
urderedmay ildchay adhay eenbay afterwardsway oundfay. Ethay omanway askedway erhay atwhay eshay 
idday erethay, utbay eshay ookedlay eryvay angelystray andway onlyway eturnedray away onfusedcay 
andway unintelligibleway answerway. Eshay eturnedray otay ethay ousehay aboutway eightway 
oway'clock, andway enwhay oneway inquiredway erewhay eshay adhay assedpay ethay ightnay, eshay 
epliedray atthay eshay adhay eenbay ookinglay orfay ethay ildchay andway emandedday earnestlyway 
ifway anythingway adhay eenbay eardhay oncerningcay imhay. Enwhay ownshay ethay odybay, eshay 
ellfay intoway iolentvay ystericshay andway eptkay erhay edbay orfay everalsay aysday. Ethay 
icturepay asway enthay oducedpray ichwhay ethay ervantsay adhay oundfay inway erhay ocketpay; 
andway enwhay Elizabethway, inway away alteringfay oicevay, ovedpray atthay itway asway ethay amesay 
ichwhay, anway ourhay eforebay ethay ildchay adhay eenbay issedmay, eshay adhay acedplay oundray 
ishay ecknay, away urmurmay ofway orrorhay andway indignationway illedfay ethay ourtcay. 

Ustinejay asway alledcay onway orfay erhay efenceday. Asway ethay ialtray adhay oceededpray, erhay 
ountenancecay adhay alteredway. Urprisesay, orrorhay, andway iserymay ereway onglystray 
expressedway. Ometimessay eshay uggledstray ithway erhay earstay, utbay enwhay eshay asway 
esiredday otay eadplay, eshay ollectedcay erhay owerspay andway okespay inway anway audibleway 
althoughway ariablevay oicevay. 

"Odgay owsknay," eshay aidsay, "owhay entirelyway Iway amway innocentway. Utbay Iway oday otnay 
etendpray atthay ymay otestationspray ouldshay acquitway emay; Iway estray ymay innocenceway onway 
away ainplay andway implesay explanationway ofway ethay actsfay ichwhay avehay eenbay adducedway 
againstway emay, andway Iway opehay ethay aracterchay Iway avehay alwaysway ornebay illway inclineway 
ymay udgesjay otay away avourablefay interpretationway erewhay anyway ircumstancecay appearsway 
oubtfulday orway uspicioussay." 

Eshay enthay elatedray atthay, ybay ethay ermissionpay ofway Elizabethway, eshay adhay assedpay 
ethay eveningway ofway ethay ightnay onway ichwhay ethay urdermay adhay eenbay ommittedcay atway ethay 
ousehay ofway anway auntway atway Enechay, away illagevay ituatedsay atway aboutway away eaguelay omfray 
Enevagay. Onway erhay eturnray, atway aboutway inenay oway'clock, eshay etmay away anmay owhay askedway 
erhay ifway eshay adhay eensay anythingway ofway ethay ildchay owhay asway ostlay. Eshay asway 
alarmedway ybay isthay accountway andway assedpay everalsay ourshay inway ookinglay orfay imhay, 
enwhay ethay atesgay ofway Enevagay ereway utshay, andway eshay asway orcedfay otay emainray 
everalsay ourshay ofway ethay ightnay inway away arnbay elongingbay otay away ottagecay, eingbay 
unwillingway otay allcay upway ethay inhabitantsway, otay omwhay eshay asway ellway ownknay. Ostmay 
ofway ethay ightnay eshay entspay erehay atchingway; owardstay orningmay eshay elievedbay atthay 
eshay eptslay orfay away ewfay inutesmay; omesay epsstay isturbedday erhay, andway eshay awokeway. 
Itway asway awnday, andway eshay uittedqay erhay asylumway, atthay eshay ightmay againway endeavourway 
otay indfay ymay otherbray. Ifway eshay adhay onegay earnay ethay otspay erewhay ishay odybay aylay, 
itway asway ithoutway erhay owledgeknay. Atthay eshay adhay eenbay ewilderedbay enwhay 
uestionedqay ybay ethay arketmay-woman asway otnay urprisingsay, incesay eshay adhay assedpay 
away eeplessslay ightnay andway ethay atefay ofway oorpay Illiamway asway yetway uncertainway. 
Oncerningcay ethay icturepay eshay ouldcay ivegay onay accountway. 

"Iway owknay," ontinuedcay ethay unhappyway ictimvay, "owhay eavilyhay andway atallyfay isthay 
oneway ircumstancecay eighsway againstway emay, utbay Iway avehay onay owerpay ofway explainingway
