itway; andway enwhay Iway avehay expressedway ymay utterway ignoranceway, Iway amway onlyway eftlay otay 
onjecturecay oncerningcay ethay obabilitiespray ybay ichwhay itway ightmay avehay eenbay 
acedplay inway ymay ocketpay. Utbay erehay alsoway Iway amway eckedchay. Iway elievebay atthay Iway 
avehay onay enemyway onway earthway, andway onenay urelysay ouldway avehay eenbay osay ickedway asway otay 
estroyday emay antonlyway. Idday ethay urderermay aceplay itway erethay? Iway owknay ofway onay 
opportunityway affordedway imhay orfay osay oingday; orway, ifway Iway adhay, ywhay ouldshay ehay avehay 
olenstay ethay eweljay, otay artpay ithway itway againway osay oonsay? 

"Iway ommitcay ymay ausecay otay ethay usticejay ofway ymay udgesjay, yetway Iway eesay onay oomray orfay 
opehay. Iway egbay ermissionpay otay avehay away ewfay itnessesway examinedway oncerningcay ymay 
aracterchay, andway ifway eirthay estimonytay allshay otnay overweighway ymay upposedsay 
uiltgay, Iway ustmay ebay ondemnedcay, althoughway Iway ouldway edgeplay ymay alvationsay onway ymay 
innocenceway." 

Everalsay itnessesway ereway alledcay owhay adhay ownknay erhay orfay anymay yearsway, andway 
eythay okespay ellway ofway erhay; utbay earfay andway atredhay ofway ethay imecray ofway ichwhay eythay 
upposedsay erhay uiltygay enderedray emthay imoroustay andway unwillingway otay omecay 
orwardfay. Elizabethway awsay evenway isthay astlay esourceray, erhay excellentway 
ispositionsday andway irreproachableway onductcay, aboutway otay ailfay ethay accusedway, 
enwhay, althoughway iolentlyvay agitatedway, eshay esiredday ermissionpay otay addressway 
ethay ourtcay. 

"Iway amway," aidsay eshay, "ethay ousincay ofway ethay unhappyway ildchay owhay asway urderedmay, orway 
atherray ishay istersay, orfay Iway asway educatedway ybay andway avehay ivedlay ithway ishay 
arentspay everway incesay andway evenway onglay eforebay ishay irthbay. Itway aymay ereforethay ebay 
udgedjay indecentway inway emay otay omecay orwardfay onway isthay occasionway, utbay enwhay Iway eesay 
away ellowfay eaturecray aboutway otay erishpay oughthray ethay owardicecay ofway erhay 
etendedpray iendsfray, Iway ishway otay ebay allowedway otay eakspay, atthay Iway aymay aysay atwhay Iway 
owknay ofway erhay aracterchay. Iway amway ellway acquaintedway ithway ethay accusedway. Iway avehay 
ivedlay inway ethay amesay ousehay ithway erhay, atway oneway imetay orfay ivefay andway atway anotherway 
orfay earlynay otway yearsway. Uringday allway atthay eriodpay eshay appearedway otay emay ethay 
ostmay amiableway andway enevolentbay ofway umanhay eaturescray. Eshay ursednay Adamemay 
Ankensteinfray, ymay auntway, inway erhay astlay illnessway, ithway ethay eatestgray affectionway 
andway arecay andway afterwardsway attendedway erhay ownway othermay uringday away edioustay 
illnessway, inway away annermay atthay excitedway ethay admirationway ofway allway owhay ewknay erhay, 
afterway ichwhay eshay againway ivedlay inway ymay uncleway's ousehay, erewhay eshay asway elovedbay 
ybay allway ethay amilyfay. Eshay asway armlyway attachedway otay ethay ildchay owhay isway ownay 
eadday andway actedway owardstay imhay ikelay away ostmay affectionateway othermay. Orfay ymay ownway 
artpay, Iway oday otnay esitatehay otay aysay atthay, otwithstandingnay allway ethay evidenceway 
oducedpray againstway erhay, Iway elievebay andway elyray onway erhay erfectpay innocenceway. Eshay 
adhay onay emptationtay orfay uchsay anway actionway; asway otay ethay aublebay onway ichwhay ethay 
iefchay oofpray estsray, ifway eshay adhay earnestlyway esiredday itway, Iway ouldshay avehay 
illinglyway ivengay itway otay erhay, osay uchmay oday Iway esteemway andway aluevay erhay." 

Away urmurmay ofway approbationway ollowedfay Elizabethway's implesay andway owerfulpay 
appealway, utbay itway asway excitedway ybay erhay enerousgay interferenceway, andway otnay inway 
avourfay ofway oorpay Ustinejay, onway omwhay ethay ublicpay indignationway asway urnedtay ithway 
enewedray iolencevay, argingchay erhay ithway ethay ackestblay ingratitudeway. Eshay 
erselfhay eptway asway Elizabethway okespay, utbay eshay idday otnay answerway. Ymay ownway 
agitationway andway anguishway asway extremeway uringday ethay olewhay ialtray. Iway elievedbay 
inway erhay innocenceway; Iway ewknay itway. Ouldcay ethay emonday owhay adhay (Iway idday otnay orfay away 
inutemay oubtday) urderedmay ymay otherbray alsoway inway ishay ellishhay ortspay avehay 
etrayedbay ethay innocentway otay eathday andway ignominyway? Iway ouldcay otnay ustainsay ethay 
orrorhay ofway ymay ituationsay, andway enwhay Iway erceivedpay atthay ethay opularpay oicevay andway 
ethay ountenancescay ofway ethay udgesjay adhay alreadyway ondemnedcay ymay unhappyway ictimvay, 
Iway ushedray outway ofway ethay ourtcay inway agonyway. Ethay orturestay ofway ethay accusedway idday 
otnay equalway inemay; eshay asway ustainedsay ybay innocenceway, utbay ethay angsfay ofway 
emorseray oretay ymay osombay andway ouldway otnay orgofay eirthay oldhay. 

Iway assedpay away ightnay ofway unmingledway etchednesswray. Inway ethay orningmay Iway entway otay 
ethay ourtcay; ymay ipslay andway oatthray ereway archedpay. Iway aredday otnay askway ethay atalfay 
uestionqay, utbay Iway asway ownknay, andway ethay officerway uessedgay ethay ausecay ofway ymay 
isitvay. Ethay allotsbay adhay eenbay ownthray; eythay ereway allway ackblay, andway Ustinejay 
asway ondemnedcay. 

Iway annotcay etendpray otay escribeday atwhay Iway enthay eltfay. Iway adhay eforebay 
experiencedway ensationssay ofway orrorhay, andway Iway avehay endeavouredway otay estowbay uponway 
emthay adequateway expressionsway, utbay ordsway annotcay onveycay anway ideaway ofway ethay 
earthay-sickening espairday atthay Iway enthay enduredway. Ethay ersonpay otay omwhay Iway 
addressedway yselfmay addedway atthay Ustinejay adhay alreadyway onfessedcay erhay uiltgay. 
"Atthay evidenceway," ehay observedway, "asway ardlyhay equiredray inway osay aringglay away 
asecay, utbay Iway amway adglay ofway itway, andway, indeedway, onenay ofway ourway udgesjay ikelay otay 
ondemncay away iminalcray uponway ircumstantialcay evidenceway, ebay itway everway osay 
ecisiveday." 

Isthay asway angestray andway unexpectedway intelligenceway; atwhay ouldcay itway eanmay? Adhay 
ymay eyesway eceivedday emay? Andway asway Iway eallyray asway admay asway ethay olewhay orldway ouldway 
elievebay emay otay ebay ifway Iway isclosedday ethay objectway ofway ymay uspicionssay? Iway 
astenedhay otay eturnray omehay, andway Elizabethway eagerlyway emandedday ethay esultray. 

"Ymay ousincay," epliedray Iway, "itway isway ecidedday asway youway aymay avehay expectedway; allway 
udgesjay adhay atherray atthay entay innocentway ouldshay uffersay anthay atthay oneway uiltygay 
ouldshay escapeway. Utbay eshay ashay onfessedcay." 

Isthay asway away ireday owblay otay oorpay Elizabethway, owhay adhay eliedray ithway irmnessfay 
uponway Ustinejay's innocenceway. "Alasway!" aidsay eshay. "Owhay allshay Iway everway againway 
elievebay inway umanhay oodnessgay? Ustinejay, omwhay Iway ovedlay andway esteemedway asway ymay 
istersay, owhay ouldcay eshay utpay onway osethay ilessmay ofway innocenceway onlyway otay etraybay? 
Erhay ildmay eyesway eemedsay incapableway ofway anyway everitysay orway uilegay, andway yetway eshay 
ashay ommittedcay away urdermay." 

Oonsay afterway eway eardhay atthay ethay oorpay ictimvay adhay expressedway away esireday otay eesay 
ymay ousincay. Ymay atherfay ishedway erhay otnay otay ogay utbay aidsay atthay ehay eftlay itway otay 
erhay ownway udgmentjay andway eelingsfay otay ecideday. "Yesway," aidsay Elizabethway, "Iway 
illway ogay, althoughway eshay isway uiltygay; andway youway, Ictorvay, allshay accompanyway emay; Iway 
annotcay ogay aloneway." Ethay ideaway ofway isthay isitvay asway orturetay otay emay, yetway Iway 
ouldcay otnay efuseray. Eway enteredway ethay oomyglay isonpray amberchay andway eheldbay 
Ustinejay ittingsay onway omesay awstray atway ethay artherfay endway; erhay andshay ereway 
anacledmay, andway erhay eadhay estedray onway erhay eesknay. Eshay oseray onway eeingsay usway

eetfay ofway Elizabethway, eepingway itterlybay. Ymay ousincay eptway alsoway. 

"Ohway, Ustinejay!" aidsay eshay. "Ywhay idday youway obray emay ofway ymay astlay onsolationcay? 
Iway eliedray onway yourway innocenceway, andway althoughway Iway asway enthay eryvay etchedwray, Iway 
asway otnay osay iserablemay asway Iway amway ownay." 

"Andway oday youway alsoway elievebay atthay Iway amway osay eryvay, eryvay ickedway? Oday youway alsoway

oicevay asway uffocatedsay ithway obssay. 

"Iseray, ymay oorpay irlgay," aidsay Elizabethway; "ywhay oday youway eelknay, ifway youway areway

"Iway idday onfesscay, utbay Iway onfessedcay away ielay. Iway onfessedcay, atthay Iway ightmay 
obtainway absolutionway; utbay ownay atthay alsehoodfay ieslay eavierhay atway ymay earthay anthay 
allway ymay otherway inssay. Ethay Odgay ofway eavenhay orgivefay emay! Everway incesay Iway asway

Inway anway evilway ourhay Iway ubscribedsay otay away ielay; andway ownay onlyway amway Iway ulytray 
iserablemay." 

Eshay ausedpay, eepingway, andway enthay ontinuedcay, "Iway oughtthay ithway orrorhay, ymay

Earday Illiamway! earestday essedblay ildchay! Iway oonsay allshay eesay youway againway inway 
eavenhay, erewhay eway allshay allway ebay appyhay; andway atthay onsolescay emay, oinggay asway Iway 
amway otay uffersay ignominyway andway eathday." 

"Ohway, Ustinejay! Orgivefay emay orfay avinghay orfay oneway omentmay istrustedday youway. 
Ywhay idday youway onfesscay? Utbay oday otnay ournmay, earday irlgay. Oday otnay earfay. Iway 
illway oclaimpray, Iway illway ovepray yourway innocenceway. Iway illway eltmay ethay onystay

Youway, ymay ayfellowplay, ymay ompanioncay, ymay istersay, erishpay onway ethay affoldscay! 
Onay! Onay! Iway evernay ouldcay urvivesay osay orriblehay away isfortunemay." 

Ustinejay ookshay erhay eadhay ournfullymay. "Iway oday otnay earfay otay ieday," eshay aidsay;

Uringday isthay onversationcay Iway adhay etiredray otay away ornercay ofway ethay isonpray oomray, 
erewhay Iway ouldcay oncealcay ethay orridhay anguishway atthay ossessedpay emay. Espairday! 
Owhay aredday alktay ofway atthay? Ethay oorpay ictimvay, owhay onway ethay orrowmay asway otay asspay

eshay awsay owhay itway asway, eshay approachedway emay andway aidsay, "Earday irsay, youway areway eryvay 
indkay otay isitvay emay; youway, Iway opehay, oday otnay elievebay atthay Iway amway uiltygay?" 

Iway ouldcay otnay answerway. "Onay, Ustinejay," aidsay Elizabethway; "ehay isway oremay 
onvincedcay ofway yourway innocenceway anthay Iway asway, orfay evenway enwhay ehay eardhay atthay youway 
adhay onfessedcay, ehay idday otnay editcray itway." 

"Iway ulytray ankthay imhay. Inway esethay astlay omentsmay Iway eelfay ethay incerestsay 
atitudegray owardstay osethay owhay inkthay ofway emay ithway indnesskay. Owhay eetsway isway 
ethay affectionway ofway othersway otay uchsay away etchwray asway Iway amway! Itway emovesray oremay anthay 
alfhay ymay isfortunemay, andway Iway eelfay asway ifway Iway ouldcay ieday inway eacepay ownay atthay ymay 
innocenceway isway acknowledgedway ybay youway, earday adylay, andway yourway ousincay." 

Usthay ethay oorpay ufferersay iedtray otay omfortcay othersway andway erselfhay. Eshay indeedway 
ainedgay ethay esignationray eshay esiredday. Utbay Iway, ethay uetray urderermay, eltfay ethay

onsolationcay. Elizabethway alsoway eptway andway asway unhappyway, utbay ershay alsoway asway

Ustinejay, andway itway asway ithway eatgray ifficultyday atthay Elizabethway ouldcay eartay
