annotcay ivelay inway isthay orldway ofway iserymay." 

Ustinejay assumedway anway airway ofway eerfulnesschay, ilewhay eshay ithway ifficultyday 
epressedray erhay itterbay earstay. Eshay embracedway Elizabethway andway aidsay inway away oicevay 
ofway alfhay-suppressed emotionway, "Arewellfay, eetsway adylay, earestday Elizabethway, 
ymay elovedbay andway onlyway iendfray; aymay eavenhay, inway itsway ountybay, essblay andway 
eservepray youway; aymay isthay ebay ethay astlay isfortunemay atthay youway illway everway 
uffersay! Ivelay, andway ebay appyhay, andway akemay othersway osay." 

Andway onway ethay orrowmay Ustinejay iedday. Elizabethway's earthay-rending eloquenceway 
ailedfay otay ovemay ethay udgesjay omfray eirthay ettledsay onvictioncay inway ethay 
iminalitycray ofway ethay aintlysay ufferersay. Ymay assionatepay andway indignantway 
appealsway ereway ostlay uponway emthay. Andway enwhay Iway eceivedray eirthay oldcay answersway 
andway eardhay ethay arshhay, unfeelingway easoningray ofway esethay enmay, ymay urposedpay 
avowalway iedday awayway onway ymay ipslay. Usthay Iway ightmay oclaimpray yselfmay away admanmay, 
utbay otnay evokeray ethay entencesay assedpay uponway ymay etchedwray ictimvay. Eshay 
erishedpay onway ethay affoldscay asway away urderessmay! 

Omfray ethay orturestay ofway ymay ownway earthay, Iway urnedtay otay ontemplatecay ethay eepday andway 
oicelessvay iefgray ofway ymay Elizabethway. Isthay alsoway asway ymay oingday! Andway ymay 
atherfay's oeway, andway ethay esolationday ofway atthay atelay osay ilingsmay omehay allway asway 
ethay orkway ofway ymay icethray-accursed andshay! Yeway eepway, unhappyway onesway, utbay esethay 
areway otnay yourway astlay earstay! Againway allshay youway aiseray ethay uneralfay ailway, andway 
ethay oundsay ofway yourway amentationslay allshay againway andway againway ebay eardhay! 
Ankensteinfray, yourway onsay, yourway insmankay, yourway earlyway, uchmay-loved iendfray; ehay 
owhay ouldway endspay eachway italvay opdray ofway oodblay orfay yourway akessay, owhay ashay onay 
oughtthay ornay ensesay ofway oyjay exceptway asway itway isway irroredmay alsoway inway yourway earday 
ountenancescay, owhay ouldway illfay ethay airway ithway essingsblay andway endspay ishay ifelay 
inway ervingsay youway--he idsbay youway eepway, otay edshay ountlesscay earstay; appyhay eyondbay 
ishay opeshay, ifway usthay inexorableway atefay ebay atisfiedsay, andway ifway ethay estructionday 
ausepay eforebay ethay eacepay ofway ethay avegray avehay ucceededsay otay yourway adsay ormentstay! 

Usthay okespay ymay opheticpray oulsay, asway, orntay ybay emorseray, orrorhay, andway espairday, 
Iway eheldbay osethay Iway ovedlay endspay ainvay orrowsay uponway ethay avesgray ofway Illiamway andway 
Ustinejay, ethay irstfay aplesshay ictimsvay otay ymay unhallowedway artsway. 



Apterchay 9 

Othingnay isway oremay ainfulpay otay ethay umanhay indmay anthay, afterway ethay eelingsfay avehay 
eenbay orkedway upway ybay away uickqay uccessionsay ofway eventsway, ethay eadday almnesscay ofway 
inactionway andway ertaintycay ichwhay ollowsfay andway eprivesday ethay oulsay othbay ofway opehay 
andway earfay. Ustinejay iedday, eshay estedray, andway Iway asway aliveway. Ethay oodblay owedflay 
eelyfray inway ymay einsvay, utbay away eightway ofway espairday andway emorseray essedpray onway ymay 
earthay ichwhay othingnay ouldcay emoveray. Eepslay edflay omfray ymay eyesway; Iway anderedway 
ikelay anway evilway iritspay, orfay Iway adhay ommittedcay eedsday ofway ischiefmay eyondbay 
escriptionday orriblehay, andway oremay, uchmay oremay (Iway ersuadedpay yselfmay) asway yetway 
ehindbay. Yetway ymay earthay overflowedway ithway indnesskay andway ethay ovelay ofway irtuevay. 
Iway adhay egunbay ifelay ithway enevolentbay intentionsway andway irstedthay orfay ethay omentmay 
enwhay Iway ouldshay utpay emthay inway acticepray andway akemay yselfmay usefulway otay ymay ellowfay 
eingsbay. Ownay allway asway astedblay; insteadway ofway atthay erenitysay ofway onsciencecay 
ichwhay allowedway emay otay ooklay ackbay uponway ethay astpay ithway elfsay-satisfaction, andway 
omfray encethay otay athergay omisepray ofway ewnay opeshay, Iway asway eizedsay ybay emorseray andway 
ethay ensesay ofway uiltgay, ichwhay urriedhay emay awayway otay away ellhay ofway intenseway orturestay 
uchsay asway onay anguagelay ancay escribeday. 

Isthay atestay ofway indmay eyedpray uponway ymay ealthhay, ichwhay adhay erhapspay evernay 
entirelyway ecoveredray omfray ethay irstfay ockshay itway adhay ustainedsay. Iway unnedshay 
ethay acefay ofway anmay; allway oundsay ofway oyjay orway omplacencycay asway orturetay otay emay; 
olitudesay asway ymay onlyway onsolationcay--deep, arkday, eathlikeday olitudesay. 

Ymay atherfay observedway ithway ainpay ethay alterationway erceptiblepay inway ymay 
ispositionday andway abitshay andway endeavouredway ybay argumentsway educedday omfray ethay 
eelingsfay ofway ishay erenesay onsciencecay andway uiltlessgay ifelay otay inspireway emay ithway 
ortitudefay andway awakenway inway emay ethay ouragecay otay ispelday ethay arkday oudclay ichwhay 
oodedbray overway emay. "Oday youway inkthay, Ictorvay," aidsay ehay, "atthay Iway oday otnay 
uffersay alsoway? Onay oneway ouldcay ovelay away ildchay oremay anthay Iway ovedlay yourway 
otherbray"--tears amecay intoway ishay eyesway asway ehay okespay--"but isway itway otnay away utyday 
otay ethay urvivorssay atthay eway ouldshay efrainray omfray augmentingway eirthay 
unhappinessway ybay anway appearanceway ofway immoderateway iefgray? Itway isway alsoway away utyday 
owedway otay yourselfway, orfay excessiveway orrowsay eventspray improvementway orway 
enjoymentway, orway evenway ethay ischargeday ofway ailyday usefulnessway, ithoutway ichwhay onay 
anmay isway itfay orfay ocietysay." 

Isthay adviceway, althoughway oodgay, asway otallytay inapplicableway otay ymay asecay; Iway 
ouldshay avehay eenbay ethay irstfay otay idehay ymay iefgray andway onsolecay ymay iendsfray ifway 
emorseray adhay otnay ingledmay itsway itternessbay, andway errortay itsway alarmway, ithway ymay 
otherway ensationssay. Ownay Iway ouldcay onlyway answerway ymay atherfay ithway away ooklay ofway 
espairday andway endeavourway otay idehay yselfmay omfray ishay iewvay. 

Aboutway isthay imetay eway etiredray otay ourway ousehay atway Elrivebay. Isthay angechay asway 
articularlypay agreeableway otay emay. Ethay uttingshay ofway ethay atesgay egularlyray atway 
entay oway'clock andway ethay impossibilityway ofway emainingray onway ethay akelay afterway atthay 
ourhay adhay enderedray ourway esidenceray ithinway ethay allsway ofway Enevagay eryvay irksomeway 
otay emay. Iway asway ownay eefray. Oftenway, afterway ethay estray ofway ethay amilyfay adhay 
etiredray orfay ethay ightnay, Iway ooktay ethay oatbay andway assedpay anymay ourshay uponway ethay 
aterway. Ometimessay, ithway ymay ailssay etsay, Iway asway arriedcay ybay ethay indway; andway 
ometimessay, afterway owingray intoway ethay iddlemay ofway ethay akelay, Iway eftlay ethay oatbay otay 
ursuepay itsway ownway oursecay andway avegay ayway otay ymay ownway iserablemay eflectionsray. Iway 
asway oftenway emptedtay, enwhay allway asway atway eacepay aroundway emay, andway Iway ethay onlyway 
unquietway ingthay atthay anderedway estlessray inway away enescay osay eautifulbay andway 
eavenlyhay--if Iway exceptway omesay atbay, orway ethay ogsfray, osewhay arshhay andway 
interruptedway oakingcray asway eardhay onlyway enwhay Iway approachedway ethay oreshay--often, 
Iway aysay, Iway asway emptedtay otay ungeplay intoway ethay ilentsay akelay, atthay ethay atersway 
ightmay oseclay overway emay andway ymay alamitiescay oreverfay. Utbay Iway asway estrainedray, 
enwhay Iway oughtthay ofway ethay eroichay andway ufferingsay Elizabethway, omwhay Iway enderlytay 
ovedlay, andway osewhay existenceway asway oundbay upway inway inemay. Iway oughtthay alsoway ofway ymay 
atherfay andway urvivingsay otherbray; ouldshay Iway ybay ymay asebay esertionday eavelay emthay 
exposedway andway unprotectedway otay ethay alicemay ofway ethay iendfay omwhay Iway adhay etlay ooselay 
amongway emthay? 

Atway esethay omentsmay Iway eptway itterlybay andway ishedway atthay eacepay ouldway evisitray ymay 
indmay onlyway atthay Iway ightmay affordway emthay onsolationcay andway appinesshay. Utbay atthay 
ouldcay otnay ebay. Emorseray extinguishedway everyway opehay. Iway adhay eenbay ethay authorway 
ofway unalterableway evilsway, andway Iway ivedlay inway ailyday earfay estlay ethay onstermay omwhay Iway 
adhay eatedcray ouldshay erpetratepay omesay ewnay ickednessway. Iway adhay anway obscureway 
eelingfay atthay allway asway otnay overway andway atthay ehay ouldway illstay ommitcay omesay 
ignalsay imecray, ichwhay ybay itsway enormityway ouldshay almostway effaceway ethay 
ecollectionray ofway ethay astpay. Erethay asway alwaysway opescay orfay earfay osay onglay asway 
anythingway Iway ovedlay emainedray ehindbay. Ymay abhorrenceway ofway isthay iendfay annotcay 
ebay onceivedcay. Enwhay Iway oughtthay ofway imhay Iway ashedgnay ymay eethtay, ymay eyesway ecamebay 
inflamedway, andway Iway ardentlyway ishedway otay extinguishway atthay ifelay ichwhay Iway adhay osay 
oughtlesslythay estowedbay. Enwhay Iway eflectedray onway ishay imescray andway alicemay, ymay 
atredhay andway evengeray urstbay allway oundsbay ofway oderationmay. Iway ouldway avehay ademay away 
ilgrimagepay otay ethay ighesthay eakpay ofway ethay Andesway, ouldcay Iway enwhay erethay avehay 
ecipitatedpray imhay otay eirthay asebay. Iway ishedway otay eesay imhay againway, atthay Iway 
ightmay eakwray ethay utmostway extentway ofway abhorrenceway onway ishay eadhay andway avengeway ethay 
eathsday ofway Illiamway andway Ustinejay. Ourway ousehay asway ethay ousehay ofway ourningmay. Ymay 
atherfay's ealthhay asway eeplyday akenshay ybay ethay orrorhay ofway ethay ecentray eventsway. 
Elizabethway asway adsay andway espondingday; eshay onay ongerlay ooktay elightday inway erhay 
ordinaryway occupationsway; allway easureplay eemedsay otay erhay acrilegesay owardtay ethay 
eadday; eternalway oeway andway earstay eshay enthay oughtthay asway ethay ustjay ibutetray eshay 
ouldshay aypay otay innocenceway osay astedblay andway estroyedday. Eshay asway onay ongerlay 
atthay appyhay eaturecray owhay inway earlierway youthway anderedway ithway emay onway ethay anksbay 
ofway ethay akelay andway alkedtay ithway ecstasyway ofway ourway uturefay ospectspray. Ethay irstfay 
ofway osethay orrowssay ichwhay areway entsay otay eanway usway omfray ethay earthway adhay isitedvay 
erhay, andway itsway immingday influenceway uenchedqay erhay earestday ilessmay. 

"Enwhay Iway eflectray, ymay earday ousincay," aidsay eshay, "onway ethay iserablemay eathday ofway 
Ustinejay Oritzmay, Iway onay ongerlay eesay ethay orldway andway itsway orksway asway eythay eforebay 
appearedway otay emay. Eforebay, Iway ookedlay uponway ethay accountsway ofway icevay andway 
injusticeway atthay Iway eadray inway ooksbay orway eardhay omfray othersway asway alestay ofway ancientway 
aysday orway imaginaryway evilsway; atway eastlay eythay ereway emoteray andway oremay amiliarfay otay 
easonray anthay otay ethay imaginationway; utbay ownay iserymay ashay omecay omehay, andway enmay 
appearway otay emay asway onstersmay irstingthay orfay eachway otherway's oodblay. Yetway Iway amway 
ertainlycay unjustway. Everybodyway elievedbay atthay oorpay irlgay otay ebay uiltygay; andway 
ifway eshay ouldcay avehay ommittedcay ethay imecray orfay ichwhay eshay ufferedsay, assuredlyway 
eshay ouldway avehay eenbay ethay ostmay epravedday ofway umanhay eaturescray. Orfay ethay akesay 
ofway away ewfay ewelsjay, otay avehay urderedmay ethay onsay ofway erhay enefactorbay andway iendfray, 
away ildchay omwhay eshay adhay ursednay omfray itsway irthbay, andway appearedway otay ovelay asway ifway 
itway adhay eenbay erhay ownway! Iway ouldcay otnay onsentcay otay ethay eathday ofway anyway umanhay 
eingbay, utbay ertainlycay Iway ouldshay avehay oughtthay uchsay away eaturecray unfitway otay 
emainray inway ethay ocietysay ofway enmay. Utbay eshay asway innocentway. Iway owknay, Iway eelfay 
eshay asway innocentway; youway areway ofway ethay amesay opinionway, andway atthay onfirmscay emay. 
Alasway! Ictorvay, enwhay alsehoodfay ancay ooklay osay ikelay ethay uthtray, owhay ancay 
assureway emselvesthay ofway ertaincay appinesshay? Iway eelfay asway ifway Iway ereway alkingway onway 
ethay edgeway ofway away ecipicepray, owardstay ichwhay ousandsthay areway owdingcray andway 
endeavouringway otay ungeplay emay intoway ethay abyssway. Illiamway andway Ustinejay ereway 
assassinatedway, andway ethay urderermay escapesway; ehay alksway aboutway ethay orldway eefray, 
andway erhapspay espectedray. Utbay evenway ifway Iway ereway ondemnedcay otay uffersay onway ethay 
affoldscay orfay ethay amesay imescray, Iway ouldway otnay angechay acesplay ithway uchsay away 
etchwray." 

Iway istenedlay otay isthay iscourseday ithway ethay extremestway agonyway. Iway, otnay inway eedday, 
utbay inway effectway, asway ethay uetray urderermay. Elizabethway eadray ymay anguishway inway ymay 
ountenancecay, andway indlykay akingtay ymay andhay, aidsay, "Ymay earestday iendfray, youway 
ustmay almcay yourselfway. Esethay eventsway avehay affectedway emay, Odgay owsknay owhay 
eeplyday; utbay Iway amway otnay osay etchedwray asway youway areway. Erethay isway anway expressionway ofway 
espairday, andway ometimessay ofway evengeray, inway yourway ountenancecay atthay akesmay emay 
embletray. Earday Ictorvay, anishbay esethay arkday assionspay. Ememberray ethay 
iendsfray aroundway youway, owhay entrecay allway eirthay opeshay inway youway. Avehay eway ostlay 
ethay owerpay ofway enderingray youway appyhay? Ahway! Ilewhay eway ovelay, ilewhay eway areway 
uetray otay eachway otherway, erehay inway isthay andlay ofway eacepay andway eautybay, yourway ativenay 
ountrycay, eway aymay eapray everyway anquiltray essingblay--what ancay isturbday ourway 
eacepay?" 

Andway ouldcay otnay uchsay ordsway omfray erhay omwhay Iway ondlyfay izedpray eforebay everyway 
otherway iftgay ofway ortunefay ufficesay otay asechay awayway ethay iendfay atthay urkedlay inway ymay 
earthay? Evenway asway eshay okespay Iway ewdray earnay otay erhay, asway ifway inway errortay, estlay atway 
atthay eryvay omentmay ethay estroyerday adhay eenbay earnay otay obray emay ofway erhay. 

Usthay otnay ethay endernesstay ofway iendshipfray, ornay ethay eautybay ofway earthway, ornay ofway 
eavenhay, ouldcay edeemray ymay oulsay omfray oeway; ethay eryvay accentsway ofway ovelay ereway 
ineffectualway. Iway asway encompassedway ybay away oudclay ichwhay onay eneficialbay 
influenceway ouldcay enetratepay. Ethay oundedway eerday aggingdray itsway aintingfay 
imbslay otay omesay untroddenway akebray, erethay otay azegay uponway ethay arrowway ichwhay adhay 
iercedpay itway, andway otay ieday, asway utbay away ypetay ofway emay. 

Ometimessay Iway ouldcay opecay ithway ethay ullensay espairday atthay overwhelmedway emay, utbay 
ometimessay ethay irlwindwhay assionspay ofway ymay oulsay ovedray emay otay eeksay, ybay odilybay 
exerciseway andway ybay angechay ofway aceplay, omesay eliefray omfray ymay intolerableway 
ensationssay. Itway asway uringday anway accessway ofway isthay indkay atthay Iway uddenlysay eftlay 
ymay omehay, andway endingbay ymay epsstay owardstay ethay earnay Alpineway alleysvay, oughtsay 
inway ethay agnificencemay, ethay eternityway ofway uchsay enesscay, otay orgetfay yselfmay andway 
ymay ephemeralway, ecausebay umanhay, orrowssay. Ymay anderingsway ereway irectedday 
owardstay ethay alleyvay ofway Amounixchay. Iway adhay isitedvay itway equentlyfray uringday ymay 
oyhoodbay. Ixsay yearsway adhay assedpay incesay enthay: _Iway_ asway away eckwray, utbay oughtnay 
adhay angedchay inway osethay avagesay andway enduringway enesscay. 

Iway erformedpay ethay irstfay artpay ofway ymay ourneyjay onway orsebackhay. Iway afterwardsway 
iredhay away ulemay, asway ethay oremay uresay-footed andway eastlay iablelay otay eceiveray 
injuryway onway esethay uggedray oadsray. Ethay eatherway asway inefay; itway asway aboutway ethay 
iddlemay ofway ethay onthmay ofway Augustway, earlynay otway onthsmay afterway ethay eathday ofway 
Ustinejay, atthay iserablemay epochway omfray ichwhay Iway atedday allway ymay oeway. Ethay 
eightway uponway ymay iritspay asway ensiblysay ightenedlay asway Iway ungedplay yetway eeperday inway 
ethay avineray ofway Arveway. Ethay immenseway ountainsmay andway ecipicespray atthay overhungway 
emay onway everyway idesay, ethay oundsay ofway ethay iverray agingray amongway ethay ocksray, andway 
ethay ashingday ofway ethay aterfallsway aroundway okespay ofway away owerpay ightymay asway 
Omnipotenceway--and Iway easedcay otay earfay orway otay endbay eforebay anyway eingbay esslay 
almightyway anthay atthay ichwhay adhay eatedcray andway uledray ethay elementsway, erehay 
isplayedday inway eirthay ostmay errifictay uisegay. Illstay, asway Iway ascendedway igherhay, 
ethay alleyvay assumedway away oremay agnificentmay andway astonishingway aracterchay. 
Uinedray astlescay anginghay onway ethay ecipicespray ofway inypay ountainsmay, ethay 
impetuousway Arveway, andway ottagescay everyway erehay andway erethay eepingpay orthfay omfray 
amongway ethay eestray ormedfay away enescay ofway ingularsay eautybay. Utbay itway asway 
augmentedway andway enderedray ublimesay ybay ethay ightymay Alpsway, osewhay itewhay andway 
iningshay yramidspay andway omesday oweredtay aboveway allway, asway elongingbay otay anotherway 
earthway, ethay abitationshay ofway anotherway aceray ofway eingsbay. 

Iway assedpay ethay idgebray ofway Elissierpay, erewhay ethay avineray, ichwhay ethay iverray 
ormsfay, openedway eforebay emay, andway Iway eganbay otay ascendway ethay ountainmay atthay 
overhangsway itway. Oonsay afterway, Iway enteredway ethay alleyvay ofway Amounixchay. Isthay 
alleyvay isway oremay onderfulway andway ublimesay, utbay otnay osay eautifulbay andway 
icturesquepay asway atthay ofway Ervoxsay, oughthray ichwhay Iway adhay ustjay assedpay. Ethay 
ighhay andway owysnay ountainsmay ereway itsway immediateway oundariesbay, utbay Iway awsay onay 
oremay uinedray astlescay andway ertilefay ieldsfay. Immenseway aciersglay approachedway 
ethay oadray; Iway eardhay ethay umblingray underthay ofway ethay allingfay avalancheway andway 
arkedmay ethay okesmay ofway itsway assagepay. Ontmay Ancblay, ethay upremesay andway 
agnificentmay Ontmay Ancblay, aisedray itselfway omfray ethay urroundingsay aiguillesway, 
andway itsway emendoustray omeday overlookedway ethay alleyvay. 

Away inglingtay onglay-lost ensesay ofway easureplay oftenway amecay acrossway emay uringday isthay 
ourneyjay. Omesay urntay inway ethay oadray, omesay ewnay objectway uddenlysay erceivedpay andway 
ecognizedray, emindedray emay ofway aysday onegay ybay, andway ereway associatedway ithway ethay 
ightheartedlay aietygay ofway oyhoodbay. Ethay eryvay indsway isperedwhay inway oothingsay 
accentsway, andway aternalmay Aturenay adebay emay eepway onay oremay. Enthay againway ethay 
indlykay influenceway easedcay otay actway--I oundfay yselfmay etteredfay againway otay iefgray 
andway indulgingway inway allway ethay iserymay ofway eflectionray. Enthay Iway urredspay onway ymay 
animalway, ivingstray osay otay orgetfay ethay orldway, ymay earsfay, andway oremay anthay allway, 
yselfmay--or, inway away oremay esperateday ashionfay, Iway alightedway andway ewthray yselfmay onway 
ethay assgray, eighedway ownday ybay orrorhay andway espairday. 

Atway engthlay Iway arrivedway atway ethay illagevay ofway Amounixchay. Exhaustionway ucceededsay 
otay ethay extremeway atiguefay othbay ofway odybay andway ofway indmay ichwhay Iway adhay enduredway. 
Orfay away ortshay acespay ofway imetay Iway emainedray atway ethay indowway atchingway ethay allidpay 
ightningslay atthay ayedplay aboveway Ontmay Ancblay andway isteninglay otay ethay ushingray ofway 
ethay Arveway, ichwhay ursuedpay itsway oisynay ayway eneathbay. Ethay amesay ullinglay oundssay 
actedway asway away ullabylay otay ymay ootay eenkay ensationssay; enwhay Iway acedplay ymay eadhay 
uponway ymay illowpay, eepslay eptcray overway emay; Iway eltfay itway asway itway amecay andway essedblay 
ethay ivergay ofway oblivionway. 



Apterchay 10 

Iway entspay ethay ollowingfay ayday oamingray oughthray ethay alleyvay. Iway oodstay esidebay 
ethay ourcessay ofway ethay Arveironway, ichwhay aketay eirthay iseray inway away acierglay, atthay 
ithway owslay acepay isway advancingway ownday omfray ethay ummitsay ofway ethay illshay otay 
arricadebay ethay alleyvay. Ethay abruptway idessay ofway astvay ountainsmay ereway eforebay 
emay; ethay icyway allway ofway ethay acierglay overhungway emay; away ewfay atteredshay inespay ereway 
atteredscay aroundway; andway ethay olemnsay ilencesay ofway isthay oriousglay 
esencepray-chamber ofway imperialway aturenay asway okenbray onlyway ybay ethay awlingbray 
avesway orway ethay allfay ofway omesay astvay agmentfray, ethay underthay oundsay ofway ethay 
avalancheway orway ethay ackingcray, everberatedray alongway ethay ountainsmay, ofway ethay 
accumulatedway iceway, ichwhay, oughthray ethay ilentsay orkingway ofway immutableway awslay, 
asway everway andway anonway entray andway orntay, asway ifway itway adhay eenbay utbay away aythingplay inway 
eirthay andshay. Esethay ublimesay andway agnificentmay enesscay affordedway emay ethay 
eatestgray onsolationcay atthay Iway asway apablecay ofway eceivingray. Eythay elevatedway emay 
omfray allway ittlenesslay ofway eelingfay, andway althoughway eythay idday otnay emoveray ymay 
iefgray, eythay ubduedsay andway anquillizedtray itway. Inway omesay egreeday, alsoway, eythay 
ivertedday ymay indmay omfray ethay oughtsthay overway ichwhay itway adhay oodedbray orfay ethay 
astlay onthmay. Iway etiredray otay estray atway ightnay; ymay umbersslay, asway itway ereway, 
aitedway onway andway inisteredmay otay ybay ethay assemblanceway ofway andgray apesshay ichwhay Iway 
adhay ontemplatedcay uringday ethay ayday. Eythay ongregatedcay oundray emay; ethay 
unstainedway owysnay ountainmay-top, ethay itteringglay innaclepay, ethay inepay oodsway, 
andway aggedray arebay avineray, ethay eagleway, oaringsay amidstway ethay oudsclay--they allway 
atheredgay oundray emay andway adebay emay ebay atway eacepay. 

Erewhay adhay eythay edflay enwhay ethay extnay orningmay Iway awokeway? Allway ofway 
oulsay-inspiriting edflay ithway eepslay, andway arkday elancholymay oudedclay everyway 
oughtthay. Ethay ainray asway ouringpay inway orrentstay, andway ickthay istsmay idhay ethay 
ummitssay ofway ethay ountainsmay, osay atthay Iway evenway awsay otnay ethay acesfay ofway osethay 
ightymay iendsfray. Illstay Iway ouldway enetratepay eirthay istymay eilvay andway eeksay emthay 
inway eirthay oudyclay etreatsray. Atwhay ereway ainray andway ormstay otay emay? Ymay ulemay asway 
oughtbray otay ethay oorday, andway Iway esolvedray otay ascendway otay ethay ummitsay ofway 
Ontanvertmay. Iway ememberedray ethay effectway atthay ethay iewvay ofway ethay emendoustray 
andway everway-moving acierglay adhay oducedpray uponway ymay indmay enwhay Iway irstfay awsay itway. 
Itway adhay enthay illedfay emay ithway away ublimesay ecstasyway atthay avegay ingsway otay ethay 
oulsay andway allowedway itway otay oarsay omfray ethay obscureway orldway otay ightlay andway oyjay. 
Ethay ightsay ofway ethay awfulway andway ajesticmay inway aturenay adhay indeedway alwaysway ethay 
effectway ofway olemnizingsay ymay indmay andway ausingcay emay otay orgetfay ethay assingpay 
arescay ofway ifelay. Iway eterminedday otay ogay ithoutway away uidegay, orfay Iway asway ellway 
acquaintedway ithway ethay athpay, andway ethay esencepray ofway anotherway ouldway estroyday ethay 
olitarysay andeurgray ofway ethay enescay. 

Ethay ascentway isway ecipitouspray, utbay ethay athpay isway utcay intoway ontinualcay andway ortshay 
indingsway, ichwhay enableway youway otay urmountsay ethay erpendicularitypay ofway ethay 
ountainmay. Itway isway away enescay errificallytay esolateday. Inway away ousandthay otsspay 
ethay acestray ofway ethay interway avalancheway aymay ebay erceivedpay, erewhay eestray ielay 
okenbray andway ewedstray onway ethay oundgray, omesay entirelyway estroyedday, othersway entbay, 
eaninglay uponway ethay uttingjay ocksray ofway ethay ountainmay orway ansverselytray uponway 
otherway eestray. Ethay athpay, asway youway ascendway igherhay, isway intersectedway ybay avinesray 
ofway owsnay, ownday ichwhay onesstay ontinuallycay ollray omfray aboveway; oneway ofway emthay isway 
articularlypay angerousday, asway ethay ightestslay oundsay, uchsay asway evenway eakingspay 
inway away oudlay oicevay, oducespray away oncussioncay ofway airway ufficientsay otay awdray 
estructionday uponway ethay eadhay ofway ethay eakerspay. Ethay inespay areway otnay alltay orway 
uxuriantlay, utbay eythay areway ombresay andway addway anway airway ofway everitysay otay ethay enescay. 
Iway ookedlay onway ethay alleyvay eneathbay; astvay istsmay ereway isingray omfray ethay iversray 
ichwhay anray oughthray itway andway urlingcay inway ickthay eathswray aroundway ethay oppositeway 
ountainsmay, osewhay ummitssay ereway idhay inway ethay uniformway oudsclay, ilewhay ainray 
ouredpay omfray ethay arkday yskay andway addedway otay ethay elancholymay impressionway Iway 
eceivedray omfray ethay objectsway aroundway emay. Alasway! Ywhay oesday anmay oastbay ofway 
ensibilitiessay uperiorsay otay osethay apparentway inway ethay utebray; itway onlyway endersray 
emthay oremay ecessarynay eingsbay. Ifway ourway impulsesway ereway onfinedcay otay ungerhay, 
irstthay, andway esireday, eway ightmay ebay earlynay eefray; utbay ownay eway areway ovedmay ybay 
everyway indway atthay owsblay andway away ancechay ordway orway enescay atthay atthay ordway aymay 
onveycay otay usway. 


Eway estray; away eamdray ashay owerpay otay oisonpay eepslay. 
Eway iseray; oneway andway'ring oughtthay ollutespay ethay ayday. 
Eway eelfay, onceivecay, orway easonray; aughlay orway eepway, 
Embraceway ondfay oeway, orway astcay ourway arescay awayway; 
Itway isway ethay amesay: orfay, ebay itway oyjay orway orrowsay, 
Ethay athpay ofway itsway epartureday illstay isway eefray. 
Anmay's yesterdayway aymay enay'er ebay ikelay ishay orrowmay; 
Oughtnay aymay endureway utbay utabilitymay! 


Itway asway earlynay oonnay enwhay Iway arrivedway atway ethay optay ofway ethay ascentway. Orfay omesay 
imetay Iway atsay uponway ethay ockray atthay overlooksway ethay easay ofway iceway. Away istmay overedcay 
othbay atthay andway ethay urroundingsay ountainsmay. Esentlypray away eezebray issipatedday 
ethay oudclay, andway Iway escendedday uponway ethay acierglay. Ethay urfacesay isway eryvay 
unevenway, isingray ikelay ethay avesway ofway away oubledtray easay, escendingday owlay, andway 
interspersedway ybay iftsray atthay inksay eepday. Ethay ieldfay ofway iceway isway almostway away 
eaguelay inway idthway, utbay Iway entspay earlynay otway ourshay inway ossingcray itway. Ethay 
oppositeway ountainmay isway away arebay erpendicularpay ockray. Omfray ethay idesay erewhay Iway 
ownay oodstay Ontanvertmay asway exactlyway oppositeway, atway ethay istanceday ofway away eaguelay; 
andway aboveway itway oseray Ontmay Ancblay, inway awfulway ajestymay. Iway emainedray inway away ecessray 
ofway ethay ockray, azinggay onway isthay onderfulway andway upendousstay enescay. Ethay easay, 
orway atherray ethay astvay iverray ofway iceway, oundway amongway itsway ependentday ountainsmay, 
osewhay aerialway ummitssay unghay overway itsway ecessesray. Eirthay icyway andway itteringglay 
eakspay oneshay inway ethay unlightsay overway ethay oudsclay. Ymay earthay, ichwhay asway 
eforebay orrowfulsay, ownay elledsway ithway omethingsay ikelay oyjay; Iway exclaimedway, 
"Anderingway iritsspay, ifway indeedway yeway anderway, andway oday otnay estray inway yourway arrownay 
edsbay, allowway emay isthay aintfay appinesshay, orway aketay emay, asway yourway ompanioncay, 
awayway omfray ethay oysjay ofway ifelay." 

Asway Iway aidsay isthay Iway uddenlysay eheldbay ethay igurefay ofway away anmay, atway omesay istanceday, 
advancingway owardstay emay ithway uperhumansay eedspay. Ehay oundedbay overway ethay 
evicescray inway ethay iceway, amongway ichwhay Iway adhay alkedway ithway autioncay; ishay 
aturestay, alsoway, asway ehay approachedway, eemedsay otay exceedway atthay ofway anmay. Iway asway 
oubledtray; away istmay amecay overway ymay eyesway, andway Iway eltfay away aintnessfay eizesay emay, 
utbay Iway asway uicklyqay estoredray ybay ethay oldcay alegay ofway ethay ountainsmay. Iway 
erceivedpay, asway ethay apeshay amecay earernay (ightsay emendoustray andway abhorredway!) 
atthay itway asway ethay etchwray omwhay Iway adhay eatedcray. Iway embledtray ithway ageray andway 
orrorhay, esolvingray otay aitway ishay approachway andway enthay oseclay ithway imhay inway 
ortalmay ombatcay. Ehay approachedway; ishay ountenancecay espokebay itterbay anguishway, 
ombinedcay ithway isdainday andway alignitymay, ilewhay itsway unearthlyway uglinessway 
enderedray itway almostway ootay orriblehay orfay umanhay eyesway. Utbay Iway arcelyscay 
observedway isthay; ageray andway atredhay adhay atway irstfay eprivedday emay ofway utteranceway, 
andway Iway ecoveredray onlyway otay overwhelmway imhay ithway ordsway expressiveway ofway uriousfay 
etestationday andway ontemptcay. 

"Evilday," Iway exclaimedway, "oday youway areday approachway emay? Andway oday otnay youway earfay 
ethay iercefay engeancevay ofway ymay armway eakedwray onway yourway iserablemay eadhay? Egonebay, 
ilevay insectway! Orway atherray, aystay, atthay Iway aymay ampletray youway otay ustday! Andway, 
ohway! Atthay Iway ouldcay, ithway ethay extinctionway ofway yourway iserablemay existenceway, 
estoreray osethay ictimsvay omwhay youway avehay osay iabolicallyday urderedmay!" 

"Iway expectedway isthay eceptionray," aidsay ethay aemonday. "Allway enmay atehay ethay 
etchedwray; owhay, enthay, ustmay Iway ebay atedhay, owhay amway iserablemay eyondbay allway 
ivinglay ingsthay! Yetway youway, ymay eatorcray, etestday andway urnspay emay, ythay eaturecray, 
otay omwhay outhay artway oundbay ybay iestay onlyway issolubleday ybay ethay annihilationway ofway 
oneway ofway usway. Youway urposepay otay illkay emay. Owhay areday youway ortspay usthay ithway ifelay? 
Oday yourway utyday owardstay emay, andway Iway illway oday inemay owardstay youway andway ethay estray ofway 
ankindmay. Ifway youway illway omplycay ithway ymay onditionscay, Iway illway eavelay emthay andway 
youway atway eacepay; utbay ifway youway efuseray, Iway illway utglay ethay awmay ofway eathday, untilway itway 
ebay atiatedsay ithway ethay oodblay ofway yourway emainingray iendsfray." 

"Abhorredway onstermay! Iendfay atthay outhay artway! Ethay orturestay ofway ellhay areway ootay 
ildmay away engeancevay orfay ythay imescray. Etchedwray evilday! Youway eproachray emay ithway 
yourway eationcray, omecay onway, enthay, atthay Iway aymay extinguishway ethay arkspay ichwhay Iway 
osay egligentlynay estowedbay." 

Ymay ageray asway ithoutway oundsbay; Iway angspray onway imhay, impelledway ybay allway ethay 
eelingsfay ichwhay ancay armway oneway eingbay againstway ethay existenceway ofway anotherway. 

Ehay easilyway eludedway emay andway aidsay, 

"Ebay almcay! Iway entreatway youway otay earhay emay eforebay youway ivegay entvay otay yourway atredhay 
onway ymay evotedday eadhay. Avehay Iway otnay ufferedsay enoughway, atthay youway eeksay otay 
increaseway ymay iserymay? Ifelay, althoughway itway aymay onlyway ebay anway accumulationway ofway 
anguishway, isway earday otay emay, andway Iway illway efendday itway. Ememberray, outhay asthay ademay 
emay oremay owerfulpay anthay yselfthay; ymay eighthay isway uperiorsay otay inethay, ymay 
ointsjay oremay upplesay. Utbay Iway illway otnay ebay emptedtay otay etsay yselfmay inway 
oppositionway otay eethay. Iway amway ythay eaturecray, andway Iway illway ebay evenway ildmay andway 
ocileday otay ymay aturalnay ordlay andway ingkay ifway outhay iltway alsoway erformpay ythay artpay, 
ethay ichwhay outhay owestway emay. Ohway, Ankensteinfray, ebay otnay equitableway otay everyway 
otherway andway ampletray uponway emay aloneway, otay omwhay ythay usticejay, andway evenway ythay 
emencyclay andway affectionway, isway ostmay ueday. Ememberray atthay Iway amway ythay eaturecray; 
Iway oughtway otay ebay ythay Adamway, utbay Iway amway atherray ethay allenfay angelway, omwhay outhay 
ivestdray omfray oyjay orfay onay isdeedmay. Everywhereway Iway eesay issblay, omfray ichwhay Iway 
aloneway amway irrevocablyway excludedway. Iway asway enevolentbay andway oodgay; iserymay ademay 
emay away iendfay. Akemay emay appyhay, andway Iway allshay againway ebay irtuousvay." 

"Egonebay! Iway illway otnay earhay youway. Erethay ancay ebay onay ommunitycay etweenbay youway 
andway emay; eway areway enemiesway. Egonebay, orway etlay usway ytray ourway engthstray inway away ightfay, 
inway ichwhay oneway ustmay allfay." 

"Owhay ancay Iway ovemay eethay? Illway onay entreatiesway ausecay eethay otay urntay away 
avourablefay eyeway uponway ythay eaturecray, owhay imploresway ythay oodnessgay andway 
ompassioncay? Elievebay emay, Ankensteinfray, Iway asway enevolentbay; ymay oulsay owedglay 
ithway ovelay andway umanityhay; utbay amway Iway otnay aloneway, iserablymay aloneway? Youway, ymay 
eatorcray, abhorway emay; atwhay opehay ancay Iway athergay omfray yourway ellowfay eaturescray, 
owhay oweway emay othingnay? Eythay urnspay andway atehay emay. Ethay esertday ountainsmay andway 
earydray aciersglay areway ymay efugeray. Iway avehay anderedway erehay anymay aysday; ethay 
avescay ofway iceway, ichwhay Iway onlyway oday otnay earfay, areway away ellingdway otay emay, andway ethay 
onlyway oneway ichwhay anmay oesday otnay udgegray. Esethay eakblay iesskay Iway ailhay, orfay eythay 
areway inderkay otay emay anthay yourway ellowfay eingsbay. Ifway ethay ultitudemay ofway ankindmay 
ewknay ofway ymay existenceway, eythay ouldway oday asway youway oday, andway armway emselvesthay orfay 
ymay estructionday. Allshay Iway otnay enthay atehay emthay owhay abhorway emay? Iway illway eepkay 
onay ermstay ithway ymay enemiesway. Iway amway iserablemay, andway eythay allshay areshay ymay 
etchednesswray. Yetway itway isway inway yourway owerpay otay ecompenseray emay, andway eliverday 
emthay omfray anway evilway ichwhay itway onlyway emainsray orfay youway otay akemay osay eatgray, atthay 
otnay onlyway youway andway yourway amilyfay, utbay ousandsthay ofway othersway, allshay ebay 
allowedsway upway inway ethay irlwindswhay ofway itsway ageray. Etlay yourway ompassioncay ebay 
ovedmay, andway oday otnay isdainday emay. Istenlay otay ymay aletay; enwhay youway avehay eardhay 
atthay, abandonway orway ommiseratecay emay, asway youway allshay udgejay atthay Iway eserveday. 
Utbay earhay emay. Ethay uiltygay areway allowedway, ybay umanhay awslay, oodyblay asway eythay 
areway, otay eakspay inway eirthay ownway efenceday eforebay eythay areway ondemnedcay. Istenlay 
otay emay, Ankensteinfray. Youway accuseway emay ofway urdermay, andway yetway youway ouldway, ithway 
away atisfiedsay onsciencecay, estroyday yourway ownway eaturecray. Ohway, aisepray ethay 
eternalway usticejay ofway anmay! Yetway Iway askway youway otnay otay arespay emay; istenlay otay emay, 
andway enthay, ifway youway ancay, andway ifway youway illway, estroyday ethay orkway ofway yourway andshay." 

"Ywhay oday youway allcay otay ymay emembranceray," Iway ejoinedray, "ircumstancescay ofway 
ichwhay Iway uddershay otay eflectray, atthay Iway avehay eenbay ethay iserablemay originway andway 
authorway? Ursedcay ebay ethay ayday, abhorredway evilday, inway ichwhay youway irstfay awsay 
ightlay! Ursedcay (althoughway Iway ursecay yselfmay) ebay ethay andshay atthay ormedfay youway! 
Youway avehay ademay emay etchedwray eyondbay expressionway. Youway avehay eftlay emay onay owerpay 
otay onsidercay etherwhay Iway amway ustjay otay youway orway otnay. Egonebay! Elieveray emay omfray 
ethay ightsay ofway yourway etestedday ormfay." 

"Usthay Iway elieveray eethay, ymay eatorcray," ehay aidsay, andway acedplay ishay atedhay andshay 
eforebay ymay eyesway, ichwhay Iway ungflay omfray emay ithway iolencevay; "usthay Iway aketay omfray 
eethay away ightsay ichwhay youway abhorway. Illstay outhay anstcay istenlay otay emay andway antgray 
emay ythay ompassioncay. Ybay ethay irtuesvay atthay Iway onceway ossessedpay, Iway emandday isthay 
omfray youway. Earhay ymay aletay; itway isway onglay andway angestray, andway ethay emperaturetay ofway 
isthay aceplay isway otnay ittingfay otay yourway inefay ensationssay; omecay otay ethay uthay uponway 
ethay ountainmay. Ethay unsay isway yetway ighhay inway ethay eavenshay; eforebay itway escendsday 
otay idehay itselfway ehindbay yourway owysnay ecipicespray andway illuminateway anotherway 
orldway, youway illway avehay eardhay ymay orystay andway ancay ecideday. Onway youway itway estsray, 
etherwhay Iway uitqay oreverfay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofway anmay andway eadlay away armlesshay 
ifelay, orway ecomebay ethay ourgescay ofway yourway ellowfay eaturescray andway ethay authorway ofway 
yourway ownway eedyspay uinray." 

Asway ehay aidsay isthay ehay edlay ethay ayway acrossway ethay iceway; Iway ollowedfay. Ymay earthay 
asway ullfay, andway Iway idday otnay answerway imhay, utbay asway Iway oceededpray, Iway eighedway ethay 
ariousvay argumentsway atthay ehay adhay usedway andway eterminedday atway eastlay otay istenlay otay 
ishay aletay. Iway asway artlypay urgedway ybay uriositycay, andway ompassioncay onfirmedcay ymay 
esolutionray. Iway adhay ithertohay upposedsay imhay otay ebay ethay urderermay ofway ymay 
otherbray, andway Iway eagerlyway oughtsay away onfirmationcay orway enialday ofway isthay opinionway. 
Orfay ethay irstfay imetay, alsoway, Iway eltfay atwhay ethay utiesday ofway away eatorcray owardstay 
ishay eaturecray ereway, andway atthay Iway oughtway otay enderray imhay appyhay eforebay Iway 
omplainedcay ofway ishay ickednessway. Esethay otivesmay urgedway emay otay omplycay ithway 
ishay emandday. Eway ossedcray ethay iceway, ereforethay, andway ascendedway ethay oppositeway 
ockray. Ethay airway asway oldcay, andway ethay ainray againway eganbay otay escendday; eway 
enteredway ethay uthay, ethay iendfay ithway anway airway ofway exultationway, Iway ithway away eavyhay 
earthay andway epressedday iritsspay. Utbay Iway onsentedcay otay istenlay, andway eatingsay 
yselfmay ybay ethay irefay ichwhay ymay odiousway ompanioncay adhay ightedlay, ehay usthay eganbay 
ishay aletay. 



Apterchay 11 

"Itway isway ithway onsiderablecay ifficultyday atthay Iway ememberray ethay originalway eraway ofway 
ymay eingbay; allway ethay eventsway ofway atthay eriodpay appearway onfusedcay andway indistinctway. 
Away angestray ultiplicitymay ofway ensationssay eizedsay emay, andway Iway awsay, eltfay, eardhay, 
andway eltsmay atway ethay amesay imetay; andway itway asway, indeedway, away onglay imetay eforebay Iway 
earnedlay otay istinguishday etweenbay ethay operationsway ofway ymay ariousvay ensessay. Ybay 
egreesday, Iway ememberray, away ongerstray ightlay essedpray uponway ymay ervesnay, osay atthay Iway 
asway obligedway otay utshay ymay eyesway. Arknessday enthay amecay overway emay andway oubledtray 
emay, utbay ardlyhay adhay Iway eltfay isthay enwhay, ybay openingway ymay eyesway, asway Iway ownay 
upposesay, ethay ightlay ouredpay inway uponway emay againway. Iway alkedway andway, Iway elievebay, 
escendedday, utbay Iway esentlypray oundfay away eatgray alterationway inway ymay ensationssay. 
Eforebay, arkday andway opaqueway odiesbay adhay urroundedsay emay, imperviousway otay ymay 
ouchtay orway ightsay; utbay Iway ownay oundfay atthay Iway ouldcay anderway onway atway ibertylay, ithway 
onay obstaclesway ichwhay Iway ouldcay otnay eitherway urmountsay orway avoidway. Ethay ightlay 
ecamebay oremay andway oremay oppressiveway otay emay, andway ethay eathay earyingway emay asway Iway 
alkedway, Iway oughtsay away aceplay erewhay Iway ouldcay eceiveray adeshay. Isthay asway ethay 
orestfay earnay Ingolstadtway; andway erehay Iway aylay ybay ethay idesay ofway away ookbray estingray 
omfray ymay atiguefay, untilway Iway eltfay ormentedtay ybay ungerhay andway irstthay. Isthay 
ousedray emay omfray ymay earlynay ormantday atestay, andway Iway ateway omesay erriesbay ichwhay Iway 
oundfay anginghay onway ethay eestray orway yinglay onway ethay oundgray. Iway akedslay ymay irstthay 
atway ethay ookbray, andway enthay yinglay ownday, asway overcomeway ybay eepslay. 

"Itway asway arkday enwhay Iway awokeway; Iway eltfay oldcay alsoway, andway alfhay ightenedfray, asway itway 
ereway, instinctivelyway, indingfay yselfmay osay esolateday. Eforebay Iway adhay uittedqay 
yourway apartmentway, onway away ensationsay ofway oldcay, Iway adhay overedcay yselfmay ithway omesay 
othesclay, utbay esethay ereway insufficientway otay ecuresay emay omfray ethay ewsday ofway 
ightnay. Iway asway away oorpay, elplesshay, iserablemay etchwray; Iway ewknay, andway ouldcay 
istinguishday, othingnay; utbay eelingfay ainpay invadeway emay onway allway idessay, Iway atsay 
ownday andway eptway. 

"Oonsay away entlegay ightlay olestay overway ethay eavenshay andway avegay emay away ensationsay ofway 
easureplay. Iway artedstay upway andway eheldbay away adiantray ormfay iseray omfray amongway ethay 
eestray. [Ethay oonmay] Iway azedgay ithway away indkay ofway onderway. Itway ovedmay owlyslay, 
utbay itway enlightenedway ymay athpay, andway Iway againway entway outway inway earchsay ofway erriesbay. 
Iway asway illstay oldcay enwhay underway oneway ofway ethay eestray Iway oundfay away ugehay oakclay, ithway 
ichwhay Iway overedcay yselfmay, andway atsay ownday uponway ethay oundgray. Onay istinctday 
ideasway occupiedway ymay indmay; allway asway onfusedcay. Iway eltfay ightlay, andway ungerhay, 
andway irstthay, andway arknessday; innumerableway oundssay angray inway ymay earsway, andway onway 
allway idessay ariousvay entsscay alutedsay emay; ethay onlyway objectway atthay Iway ouldcay 
istinguishday asway ethay ightbray oonmay, andway Iway ixedfay ymay eyesway onway atthay ithway 
easureplay. 

"Everalsay angeschay ofway ayday andway ightnay assedpay, andway ethay orbway ofway ightnay adhay 
eatlygray essenedlay, enwhay Iway eganbay otay istinguishday ymay ensationssay omfray eachway 
otherway. Iway aduallygray awsay ainlyplay ethay earclay eamstray atthay uppliedsay emay ithway 
inkdray andway ethay eestray atthay adedshay emay ithway eirthay oliagefay. Iway asway elightedday 
enwhay Iway irstfay iscoveredday atthay away easantplay oundsay, ichwhay oftenway alutedsay ymay 
earsway, oceededpray omfray ethay oatsthray ofway ethay ittlelay ingedway animalsway owhay adhay 
oftenway interceptedway ethay ightlay omfray ymay eyesway. Iway eganbay alsoway otay observeway, 
ithway eatergray accuracyway, ethay ormsfay atthay urroundedsay emay andway otay erceivepay ethay 
oundariesbay ofway ethay adiantray oofray ofway ightlay ichwhay anopiedcay emay. Ometimessay Iway 
iedtray otay imitateway ethay easantplay ongssay ofway ethay irdsbay utbay asway unableway. 
Ometimessay Iway ishedway otay expressway ymay ensationssay inway ymay ownway odemay, utbay ethay 
uncouthway andway inarticulateway oundssay ichwhay okebray omfray emay ightenedfray emay intoway 
ilencesay againway. 

"Ethay oonmay adhay isappearedday omfray ethay ightnay, andway againway, ithway away essenedlay 
ormfay, owedshay itselfway, ilewhay Iway illstay emainedray inway ethay orestfay. Ymay 
ensationssay adhay ybay isthay imetay ecomebay istinctday, andway ymay indmay eceivedray everyway 
ayday additionalway ideasway. Ymay eyesway ecamebay accustomedway otay ethay ightlay andway otay 
erceivepay objectsway inway eirthay ightray ormsfay; Iway istinguishedday ethay insectway omfray 
ethay erbhay, andway ybay egreesday, oneway erbhay omfray anotherway. Iway oundfay atthay ethay 
arrowspay utteredway onenay utbay arshhay otesnay, ilstwhay osethay ofway ethay ackbirdblay andway 
ushthray ereway eetsway andway enticingway. 

"Oneway ayday, enwhay Iway asway oppressedway ybay oldcay, Iway oundfay away irefay ichwhay adhay eenbay 
eftlay ybay omesay anderingway eggarsbay, andway asway overcomeway ithway elightday atway ethay 
armthway Iway experiencedway omfray itway. Inway ymay oyjay Iway ustthray ymay andhay intoway ethay ivelay 
embersway, utbay uicklyqay ewdray itway outway againway ithway away ycray ofway ainpay. Owhay angestray, 
Iway oughtthay, atthay ethay amesay ausecay ouldshay oducepray uchsay oppositeway effectsway! Iway 
examinedway ethay aterialsmay ofway ethay irefay, andway otay ymay oyjay oundfay itway otay ebay 
omposedcay ofway oodway. Iway uicklyqay ollectedcay omesay anchesbray, utbay eythay ereway etway 
andway ouldway otnay urnbay. Iway asway ainedpay atway isthay andway atsay illstay atchingway ethay 
operationway ofway ethay irefay. Ethay etway oodway ichwhay Iway adhay acedplay earnay ethay eathay 
ieddray andway itselfway ecamebay inflamedway. Iway eflectedray onway isthay, andway ybay ouchingtay 
ethay ariousvay anchesbray, Iway iscoveredday ethay ausecay andway usiedbay yselfmay inway 
ollectingcay away eatgray uantityqay ofway oodway, atthay Iway ightmay ydray itway andway avehay away 
entifulplay upplysay ofway irefay. Enwhay ightnay amecay onway andway oughtbray eepslay ithway 
itway, Iway asway inway ethay eatestgray earfay estlay ymay irefay ouldshay ebay extinguishedway. Iway 
overedcay itway arefullycay ithway ydray oodway andway eaveslay andway acedplay etway anchesbray 
uponway itway; andway enthay, eadingspray ymay oakclay, Iway aylay onway ethay oundgray andway anksay 
intoway eepslay. 

"Itway asway orningmay enwhay Iway awokeway, andway ymay irstfay arecay asway otay isitvay ethay irefay. 
Iway uncoveredway itway, andway away entlegay eezebray uicklyqay annedfay itway intoway away ameflay. Iway 
observedway isthay alsoway andway ontrivedcay away anfay ofway anchesbray, ichwhay ousedray ethay 
embersway enwhay eythay ereway earlynay extinguishedway. Enwhay ightnay amecay againway Iway 
oundfay, ithway easureplay, atthay ethay irefay avegay ightlay asway ellway asway eathay andway atthay 
ethay iscoveryday ofway isthay elementway asway usefulway otay emay inway ymay oodfay, orfay Iway oundfay 
omesay ofway ethay offalsway atthay ethay avellerstray adhay eftlay adhay eenbay oastedray, andway 
astedtay uchmay oremay avourysay anthay ethay erriesbay Iway atheredgay omfray ethay eestray. Iway 
iedtray, ereforethay, otay essdray ymay oodfay inway ethay amesay annermay, acingplay itway onway 
ethay ivelay embersway. Iway oundfay atthay ethay erriesbay ereway oiledspay ybay isthay 
operationway, andway ethay utsnay andway ootsray uchmay improvedway. 

"Oodfay, oweverhay, ecamebay arcescay, andway Iway oftenway entspay ethay olewhay ayday 
earchingsay inway ainvay orfay away ewfay acornsway otay assuageway ethay angspay ofway ungerhay. Enwhay 
Iway oundfay isthay, Iway esolvedray otay uitqay ethay aceplay atthay Iway adhay ithertohay 
inhabitedway, otay eeksay orfay oneway erewhay ethay ewfay antsway Iway experiencedway ouldway ebay 
oremay easilyway atisfiedsay. Inway isthay emigrationway Iway exceedinglyway amentedlay ethay 
osslay ofway ethay irefay ichwhay Iway adhay obtainedway oughthray accidentway andway ewknay otnay owhay 
otay eproduceray itway. Iway avegay everalsay ourshay otay ethay erioussay onsiderationcay ofway 
isthay ifficultyday, utbay Iway asway obligedway otay elinquishray allway attemptway otay upplysay 
itway, andway appingwray yselfmay upway inway ymay oakclay, Iway uckstray acrossway ethay oodway 
owardstay ethay ettingsay unsay. Iway assedpay eethray aysday inway esethay amblesray andway atway 
engthlay iscoveredday ethay openway ountrycay. Away eatgray allfay ofway owsnay adhay akentay 
aceplay ethay ightnay eforebay, andway ethay ieldsfay ereway ofway oneway uniformway itewhay; ethay 
appearanceway asway isconsolateday, andway Iway oundfay ymay eetfay illedchay ybay ethay oldcay 
ampday ubstancesay atthay overedcay ethay oundgray. 

"Itway asway aboutway evensay inway ethay orningmay, andway Iway ongedlay otay obtainway oodfay andway 
eltershay; atway engthlay Iway erceivedpay away allsmay uthay, onway away isingray oundgray, ichwhay 
adhay oubtlessday eenbay uiltbay orfay ethay onveniencecay ofway omesay epherdshay. Isthay 
asway away ewnay ightsay otay emay, andway Iway examinedway ethay ucturestray ithway eatgray 
uriositycay. Indingfay ethay oorday openway, Iway enteredway. Anway oldway anmay atsay inway itway, 
earnay away irefay, overway ichwhay ehay asway eparingpray ishay eakfastbray. Ehay urnedtay onway 
earinghay away oisenay, andway erceivingpay emay, iekedshray oudlylay, andway uittingqay ethay 
uthay, anray acrossway ethay ieldsfay ithway away eedspay ofway ichwhay ishay ebilitatedday ormfay 
ardlyhay appearedway apablecay. Ishay appearanceway, ifferentday omfray anyway Iway adhay everway 
eforebay eensay, andway ishay ightflay omewhatsay urprisedsay emay. Utbay Iway asway enchantedway 
ybay ethay appearanceway ofway ethay uthay; erehay ethay owsnay andway ainray ouldcay otnay 
enetratepay; ethay oundgray asway ydray; andway itway esentedpray otay emay enthay asway exquisiteway 
andway ivineday away etreatray asway Andemoniumpay appearedway otay ethay emonsday ofway ellhay 
afterway eirthay ufferingssay inway ethay akelay ofway irefay. Iway eedilygray evouredday ethay 
emnantsray ofway ethay epherdshay's eakfastbray, ichwhay onsistedcay ofway eadbray, eesechay, 
ilkmay, andway ineway; ethay atterlay, oweverhay, Iway idday otnay ikelay. Enthay, overcomeway ybay 
atiguefay, Iway aylay ownday amongway omesay awstray andway ellfay asleepway. 

"Itway asway oonnay enwhay Iway awokeway, andway alluredway ybay ethay armthway ofway ethay unsay, ichwhay 
oneshay ightlybray onway ethay itewhay oundgray, Iway eterminedday otay ecommenceray ymay 
avelstray; andway, epositingday ethay emainsray ofway ethay easantpay's eakfastbray inway away 
alletway Iway oundfay, Iway oceededpray acrossway ethay ieldsfay orfay everalsay ourshay, untilway 
atway unsetsay Iway arrivedway atway away illagevay. Owhay iraculousmay idday isthay appearway! Ethay 
utshay, ethay eaternay ottagescay, andway atelystay ouseshay engagedway ymay admirationway ybay 
urnstay. Ethay egetablesvay inway ethay ardensgay, ethay ilkmay andway eesechay atthay Iway awsay 
acedplay atway ethay indowsway ofway omesay ofway ethay ottagescay, alluredway ymay appetiteway. Oneway 
ofway ethay estbay ofway esethay Iway enteredway, utbay Iway adhay ardlyhay acedplay ymay ootfay ithinway 
ethay oorday eforebay ethay ildrenchay iekedshray, andway oneway ofway ethay omenway aintedfay. 
Ethay olewhay illagevay asway ousedray; omesay edflay, omesay attackedway emay, untilway, 
ievouslygray uisedbray ybay onesstay andway anymay otherway indskay ofway issilemay eaponsway, Iway 
escapedway otay ethay openway ountrycay andway earfullyfay ooktay efugeray inway away owlay ovelhay, 
uiteqay arebay, andway akingmay away etchedwray appearanceway afterway ethay alacespay Iway adhay 
eheldbay inway ethay illagevay. Isthay ovelhay oweverhay, oinedjay away ottagecay ofway away eatnay 
andway easantplay appearanceway, utbay afterway ymay atelay earlyday oughtbay experienceway, Iway 
aredday otnay enterway itway. Ymay aceplay ofway efugeray asway onstructedcay ofway oodway, utbay osay 
owlay atthay Iway ouldcay ithway ifficultyday itsay uprightway inway itway. Onay oodway, oweverhay, 
asway acedplay onway ethay earthway, ichwhay ormedfay ethay oorflay, utbay itway asway ydray; andway 
althoughway ethay indway enteredway itway ybay innumerableway inkschay, Iway oundfay itway anway 
agreeableway asylumway omfray ethay owsnay andway ainray. 

"Erehay, enthay, Iway etreatedray andway aylay ownday appyhay otay avehay oundfay away eltershay, 
oweverhay iserablemay, omfray ethay inclemencyway ofway ethay easonsay, andway illstay oremay 
omfray ethay arbaritybay ofway anmay. Asway oonsay asway orningmay awnedday Iway eptcray omfray ymay 
ennelkay, atthay Iway ightmay iewvay ethay adjacentway ottagecay andway iscoverday ifway Iway ouldcay 
emainray inway ethay abitationhay Iway adhay oundfay. Itway asway ituatedsay againstway ethay ackbay 
ofway ethay ottagecay andway urroundedsay onway ethay idessay ichwhay ereway exposedway ybay away igpay 
ystay andway away earclay oolpay ofway aterway. Oneway artpay asway openway, andway ybay atthay Iway adhay 
eptcray inway; utbay ownay Iway overedcay everyway evicecray ybay ichwhay Iway ightmay ebay erceivedpay 
ithway onesstay andway oodway, yetway inway uchsay away annermay atthay Iway ightmay ovemay emthay onway 
occasionway otay asspay outway; allway ethay ightlay Iway enjoyedway amecay oughthray ethay ystay, andway 
atthay asway ufficientsay orfay emay. 

"Avinghay usthay arrangedway ymay ellingdway andway arpetedcay itway ithway eanclay awstray, Iway 
etiredray, orfay Iway awsay ethay igurefay ofway away anmay atway away istanceday, andway Iway ememberedray 
ootay ellway ymay eatmenttray ethay ightnay eforebay otay usttray yselfmay inway ishay owerpay. Iway 
adhay irstfay, oweverhay, ovidedpray orfay ymay ustenancesay orfay atthay ayday ybay away oaflay 
ofway oarsecay eadbray, ichwhay Iway urloinedpay, andway away upcay ithway ichwhay Iway ouldcay inkdray 
oremay onvenientlycay anthay omfray ymay andhay ofway ethay urepay aterway ichwhay owedflay ybay 
ymay etreatray. Ethay oorflay asway away ittlelay aisedray, osay atthay itway asway eptkay 
erfectlypay ydray, andway ybay itsway icinityvay otay ethay imneychay ofway ethay ottagecay itway asway 
olerablytay armway. 

"Eingbay usthay ovidedpray, Iway esolvedray otay esideray inway isthay ovelhay untilway 
omethingsay ouldshay occurway ichwhay ightmay alterway ymay eterminationday. Itway asway 
indeedway away aradisepay omparedcay otay ethay eakblay orestfay, ymay ormerfay esidenceray, 
ethay ainray-dropping anchesbray, andway ankday earthway. Iway ateway ymay eakfastbray ithway 
easureplay andway asway aboutway otay emoveray away ankplay otay ocurepray yselfmay away ittlelay 
aterway enwhay Iway eardhay away epstay, andway ookinglay oughthray away allsmay inkchay, Iway eheldbay 
away youngway eaturecray, ithway away ailpay onway erhay eadhay, assingpay eforebay ymay ovelhay. Ethay 
irlgay asway youngway andway ofway entlegay emeanourday, unlikeway atwhay Iway avehay incesay oundfay 
ottagerscay andway armhousefay ervantssay otay ebay. Yetway eshay asway eanlymay esseddray, away 
oarsecay ueblay etticoatpay andway away inenlay acketjay eingbay erhay onlyway arbgay; erhay airfay 
airhay asway aitedplay utbay otnay adornedway: eshay ookedlay atientpay yetway adsay. Iway ostlay 
ightsay ofway erhay, andway inway aboutway away uarterqay ofway anway ourhay eshay eturnedray earingbay 
ethay ailpay, ichwhay asway ownay artlypay illedfay ithway ilkmay. Asway eshay alkedway alongway, 
eeminglysay incommodedway ybay ethay urdenbay, away youngway anmay etmay erhay, osewhay 
ountenancecay expressedway away eeperday espondenceday. Utteringway away ewfay oundssay ithway 
anway airway ofway elancholymay, ehay ooktay ethay ailpay omfray erhay eadhay andway orebay itway otay ethay 
ottagecay imselfhay. Eshay ollowedfay, andway eythay isappearedday. Esentlypray Iway awsay 
ethay youngway anmay againway, ithway omesay oolstay inway ishay andhay, osscray ethay ieldfay 
ehindbay ethay ottagecay; andway ethay irlgay asway alsoway usiedbay, ometimessay inway ethay 
ousehay andway ometimessay inway ethay yardway. 

"Onway examiningway ymay ellingdway, Iway oundfay atthay oneway ofway ethay indowsway ofway ethay 
ottagecay adhay ormerlyfay occupiedway away artpay ofway itway, utbay ethay anespay adhay eenbay 
illedfay upway ithway oodway. Inway oneway ofway esethay asway away allsmay andway almostway 
imperceptibleway inkchay oughthray ichwhay ethay eyeway ouldcay ustjay enetratepay. 
Oughthray isthay evicecray away allsmay oomray asway isiblevay, itewashedwhay andway eanclay 
utbay eryvay arebay ofway urniturefay. Inway oneway ornercay, earnay away allsmay irefay, atsay anway 
oldway anmay, eaninglay ishay eadhay onway ishay andshay inway away isconsolateday attitudeway. Ethay 
youngway irlgay asway occupiedway inway arrangingway ethay ottagecay; utbay esentlypray eshay 
ooktay omethingsay outway ofway away awerdray, ichwhay employedway erhay andshay, andway eshay atsay 
ownday esidebay ethay oldway anmay, owhay, akingtay upway anway instrumentway, eganbay otay ayplay 
andway otay oducepray oundssay eetersway anthay ethay oicevay ofway ethay ushthray orway ethay 
ightingalenay. Itway asway away ovelylay ightsay, evenway otay emay, oorpay etchwray owhay adhay 
evernay eheldbay aughtway eautifulbay eforebay. Ethay ilversay airhay andway enevolentbay 
ountenancecay ofway ethay agedway ottagercay onway ymay everenceray, ilewhay ethay entlegay 
annersmay ofway ethay irlgay enticedway ymay ovelay. Ehay ayedplay away eetsway ournfulmay airway 
ichwhay Iway erceivedpay ewdray earstay omfray ethay eyesway ofway ishay amiableway ompanioncay, ofway 
ichwhay ethay oldway anmay ooktay onay oticenay, untilway eshay obbedsay audiblyway; ehay enthay 
onouncedpray away ewfay oundssay, andway ethay airfay eaturecray, eavinglay erhay orkway, eltknay 
atway ishay eetfay. Ehay aisedray erhay andway iledsmay ithway uchsay indnesskay andway affectionway 
atthay Iway eltfay ensationssay ofway away eculiarpay andway overpoweringway aturenay; eythay ereway 
away ixturemay ofway ainpay andway easureplay, uchsay asway Iway adhay evernay eforebay experiencedway, 
eitherway omfray ungerhay orway oldcay, armthway orway oodfay; andway Iway ithdrewway omfray ethay 
indowway, unableway otay earbay esethay emotionsway. 

"Oonsay afterway isthay ethay youngway anmay eturnedray, earingbay onway ishay ouldersshay away 
oadlay ofway oodway. Ethay irlgay etmay imhay atway ethay oorday, elpedhay otay elieveray imhay ofway 
ishay urdenbay, andway akingtay omesay ofway ethay uelfay intoway ethay ottagecay, acedplay itway onway 
ethay irefay; enthay eshay andway ethay youthway entway apartway intoway away ooknay ofway ethay ottagecay, 
andway ehay owedshay erhay away argelay oaflay andway away iecepay ofway eesechay. Eshay eemedsay 
easedplay andway entway intoway ethay ardengay orfay omesay ootsray andway antsplay, ichwhay eshay 
acedplay inway aterway, andway enthay uponway ethay irefay. Eshay afterwardsway ontinuedcay erhay 
orkway, ilstwhay ethay youngway anmay entway intoway ethay ardengay andway appearedway usilybay 
employedway inway iggingday andway ullingpay upway ootsray. Afterway ehay adhay eenbay employedway 
usthay aboutway anway ourhay, ethay youngway omanway oinedjay imhay andway eythay enteredway ethay 
ottagecay ogethertay. 

"Ethay oldway anmay adhay, inway ethay eantimemay, eenbay ensivepay, utbay onway ethay appearanceway 
ofway ishay ompanionscay ehay assumedway away oremay eerfulchay airway, andway eythay atsay ownday otay 
eatway. Ethay ealmay asway uicklyqay ispatchedday. Ethay youngway omanway asway againway 
occupiedway inway arrangingway ethay ottagecay, ethay oldway anmay alkedway eforebay ethay 
ottagecay inway ethay unsay orfay away ewfay inutesmay, eaninglay onway ethay armway ofway ethay youthway. 
Othingnay ouldcay exceedway inway eautybay ethay ontrastcay etweenbay esethay otway excellentway 
eaturescray. Oneway asway oldway, ithway ilversay airshay andway away ountenancecay eamingbay 
ithway enevolencebay andway ovelay; ethay youngerway asway ightslay andway acefulgray inway ishay 
igurefay, andway ishay eaturesfay ereway ouldedmay ithway ethay inestfay ymmetrysay, yetway ishay 
eyesway andway attitudeway expressedway ethay utmostway adnesssay andway espondencyday. Ethay 
oldway anmay eturnedray otay ethay ottagecay, andway ethay youthway, ithway oolstay ifferentday 
omfray osethay ehay adhay usedway inway ethay orningmay, irectedday ishay epsstay acrossway ethay 
ieldsfay. 

"Ightnay uicklyqay utshay inway, utbay otay ymay extremeway onderway, Iway oundfay atthay ethay 
ottagerscay adhay away eansmay ofway olongingpray ightlay ybay ethay useway ofway aperstay, andway asway 
elightedday otay indfay atthay ethay ettingsay ofway ethay unsay idday otnay utpay anway endway otay ethay 
easureplay Iway experiencedway inway atchingway ymay umanhay eighboursnay. Inway ethay eveningway 
ethay youngway irlgay andway erhay ompanioncay ereway employedway inway ariousvay occupationsway 
ichwhay Iway idday otnay understandway; andway ethay oldway anmay againway ooktay upway ethay 
instrumentway ichwhay oducedpray ethay ivineday oundssay atthay adhay enchantedway emay inway 
ethay orningmay. Osay oonsay asway ehay adhay inishedfay, ethay youthway eganbay, otnay otay ayplay, 
utbay otay utterway oundssay atthay ereway onotonousmay, andway eithernay esemblingray ethay 
armonyhay ofway ethay oldway anmay's instrumentway ornay ethay ongssay ofway ethay irdsbay; Iway incesay 
oundfay atthay ehay eadray aloudway, utbay atway atthay imetay Iway ewknay othingnay ofway ethay 
iencescay ofway ordsway orway etterslay. 

"Ethay amilyfay, afterway avinghay eenbay usthay occupiedway orfay away ortshay imetay, 
extinguishedway eirthay ightslay andway etiredray, asway Iway onjecturedcay, otay estray." 



Apterchay 12 

"Iway aylay onway ymay awstray, utbay Iway ouldcay otnay eepslay. Iway oughtthay ofway ethay 
occurrencesway ofway ethay ayday. Atwhay ieflychay uckstray emay asway ethay entlegay annersmay 
ofway esethay eoplepay, andway Iway ongedlay otay oinjay emthay, utbay aredday otnay. Iway 
ememberedray ootay ellway ethay eatmenttray Iway adhay ufferedsay ethay ightnay eforebay omfray 
ethay arbarousbay illagersvay, andway esolvedray, ateverwhay oursecay ofway onductcay Iway 
ightmay ereafterhay inkthay itway ightray otay ursuepay, atthay orfay ethay esentpray Iway ouldway 
emainray uietlyqay inway ymay ovelhay, atchingway andway endeavouringway otay iscoverday ethay 
otivesmay ichwhay influencedway eirthay actionsway. 

"Ethay ottagerscay aroseway ethay extnay orningmay eforebay ethay unsay. Ethay youngway omanway 
arrangedway ethay ottagecay andway eparedpray ethay oodfay, andway ethay youthway epartedday 
afterway ethay irstfay ealmay. 

"Isthay ayday asway assedpay inway ethay amesay outineray asway atthay ichwhay ecededpray itway. 
Ethay youngway anmay asway onstantlycay employedway outway ofway oorsday, andway ethay irlgay inway 
ariousvay aboriouslay occupationsway ithinway. Ethay oldway anmay, omwhay Iway oonsay 
erceivedpay otay ebay indblay, employedway ishay eisurelay ourshay onway ishay instrumentway orway 
inway ontemplationcay. Othingnay ouldcay exceedway ethay ovelay andway espectray ichwhay ethay 
youngerway ottagerscay exhibitedway owardstay eirthay enerablevay ompanioncay. Eythay 
erformedpay owardstay imhay everyway ittlelay officeway ofway affectionway andway utyday ithway 
entlenessgay, andway ehay ewardedray emthay ybay ishay enevolentbay ilessmay. 

"Eythay ereway otnay entirelyway appyhay. Ethay youngway anmay andway ishay ompanioncay oftenway 
entway apartway andway appearedway otay eepway. Iway awsay onay ausecay orfay eirthay unhappinessway, 
utbay Iway asway eeplyday affectedway ybay itway. Ifway uchsay ovelylay eaturescray ereway 
iserablemay, itway asway esslay angestray atthay Iway, anway imperfectway andway olitarysay eingbay, 
ouldshay ebay etchedwray. Yetway ywhay ereway esethay entlegay eingsbay unhappyway? Eythay 
ossessedpay away elightfulday ousehay (orfay uchsay itway asway inway ymay eyesway) andway everyway 
uxurylay; eythay adhay away irefay otay armway emthay enwhay illchay andway eliciousday iandsvay 
enwhay ungryhay; eythay ereway esseddray inway excellentway othesclay; andway, illstay oremay, 
eythay enjoyedway oneway anotherway's ompanycay andway eechspay, interchangingway eachway ayday 
ookslay ofway affectionway andway indnesskay. Atwhay idday eirthay earstay implyway? Idday eythay 
eallyray expressway ainpay? Iway asway atway irstfay unableway otay olvesay esethay uestionsqay, 
utbay erpetualpay attentionway andway imetay explainedway otay emay anymay appearancesway ichwhay 
ereway atway irstfay enigmaticway. 

"Away onsiderablecay eriodpay elapsedway eforebay Iway iscoveredday oneway ofway ethay ausescay ofway 
ethay uneasinessway ofway isthay amiableway amilyfay: itway asway overtypay, andway eythay 
ufferedsay atthay evilway inway away eryvay istressingday egreeday. Eirthay ourishmentnay 
onsistedcay entirelyway ofway ethay egetablesvay ofway eirthay ardengay andway ethay ilkmay ofway 
oneway owcay, ichwhay avegay eryvay ittlelay uringday ethay interway, enwhay itsway astersmay 
ouldcay arcelyscay ocurepray oodfay otay upportsay itway. Eythay oftenway, Iway elievebay, 
ufferedsay ethay angspay ofway ungerhay eryvay oignantlypay, especiallyway ethay otway 
youngerway ottagerscay, orfay everalsay imestay eythay acedplay oodfay eforebay ethay oldway 
anmay enwhay eythay eservedray onenay orfay emselvesthay. 

"Isthay aittray ofway indnesskay ovedmay emay ensiblysay. Iway adhay eenbay accustomedway, 
uringday ethay ightnay, otay ealstay away artpay ofway eirthay orestay orfay ymay ownway 
onsumptioncay, utbay enwhay Iway oundfay atthay inway oingday isthay Iway inflictedway ainpay onway 
ethay ottagerscay, Iway abstainedway andway atisfiedsay yselfmay ithway erriesbay, utsnay, andway 
ootsray ichwhay Iway atheredgay omfray away eighbouringnay oodway. 

"Iway iscoveredday alsoway anotherway eansmay oughthray ichwhay Iway asway enabledway otay assistway 
eirthay abourslay. Iway oundfay atthay ethay youthway entspay away eatgray artpay ofway eachway ayday 
inway ollectingcay oodway orfay ethay amilyfay irefay, andway uringday ethay ightnay Iway oftenway 
ooktay ishay oolstay, ethay useway ofway ichwhay Iway uicklyqay iscoveredday, andway oughtbray omehay 
iringfay ufficientsay orfay ethay onsumptioncay ofway everalsay aysday. 

"Iway ememberray, ethay irstfay imetay atthay Iway idday isthay, ethay youngway omanway, enwhay eshay 
openedway ethay oorday inway ethay orningmay, appearedway eatlygray astonishedway onway eeingsay away 
eatgray ilepay ofway oodway onway ethay outsideway. Eshay utteredway omesay ordsway inway away oudlay 
oicevay, andway ethay youthway oinedjay erhay, owhay alsoway expressedway urprisesay. Iway 
observedway, ithway easureplay, atthay ehay idday otnay ogay otay ethay orestfay atthay ayday, utbay 
entspay itway inway epairingray ethay ottagecay andway ultivatingcay ethay ardengay. 

"Ybay egreesday Iway ademay away iscoveryday ofway illstay eatergray omentmay. Iway oundfay atthay 
esethay eoplepay ossessedpay away ethodmay ofway ommunicatingcay eirthay experienceway andway 
eelingsfay otay oneway anotherway ybay articulateway oundssay. Iway erceivedpay atthay ethay 
ordsway eythay okespay ometimessay oducedpray easureplay orway ainpay, ilessmay orway 
adnesssay, inway ethay indsmay andway ountenancescay ofway ethay earershay. Isthay asway indeedway 
away odlikegay iencescay, andway Iway ardentlyway esiredday otay ecomebay acquaintedway ithway itway. 
Utbay Iway asway affledbay inway everyway attemptway Iway ademay orfay isthay urposepay. Eirthay 
onunciationpray asway uickqay, andway ethay ordsway eythay utteredway, otnay avinghay anyway 
apparentway onnectioncay ithway isiblevay objectsway, Iway asway unableway otay iscoverday anyway 
ueclay ybay ichwhay Iway ouldcay unravelway ethay ysterymay ofway eirthay eferenceray. Ybay eatgray 
applicationway, oweverhay, andway afterway avinghay emainedray uringday ethay acespay ofway 
everalsay evolutionsray ofway ethay oonmay inway ymay ovelhay, Iway iscoveredday ethay amesnay 
atthay ereway ivengay otay omesay ofway ethay ostmay amiliarfay objectsway ofway iscourseday; Iway 
earnedlay andway appliedway ethay ordsway, 'irefay,' 'ilkmay,' 'eadbray,' andway 'oodway.' Iway 
earnedlay alsoway ethay amesnay ofway ethay ottagerscay emselvesthay. Ethay youthway andway ishay 
ompanioncay adhay eachway ofway emthay everalsay amesnay, utbay ethay oldway anmay adhay onlyway oneway, 
ichwhay asway 'atherfay.' Ethay irlgay asway alledcay 'istersay' orway 'Agathaway,' andway ethay 
youthway 'Elixfay,' 'otherbray,' orway 'onsay.' Iway annotcay escribeday ethay elightday Iway 
eltfay enwhay Iway earnedlay ethay ideasway appropriatedway otay eachway ofway esethay oundssay andway 
asway ableway otay onouncepray emthay. Iway istinguishedday everalsay otherway ordsway 
ithoutway eingbay ableway asway yetway otay understandway orway applyway emthay, uchsay asway 'oodgay,' 
'earestday,' 'unhappyway.' 

"Iway entspay ethay interway inway isthay annermay. Ethay entlegay annersmay andway eautybay ofway 
ethay ottagerscay eatlygray endearedway emthay otay emay; enwhay eythay ereway unhappyway, Iway 
eltfay epressedday; enwhay eythay ejoicedray, Iway ympathizedsay inway eirthay oysjay. Iway awsay 
ewfay umanhay eingsbay esidesbay emthay, andway ifway anyway otherway appenedhay otay enterway ethay 
ottagecay, eirthay arshhay annersmay andway uderay aitgay onlyway enhancedway otay emay ethay 
uperiorsay accomplishmentsway ofway ymay iendsfray. Ethay oldway anmay, Iway ouldcay erceivepay, 
oftenway endeavouredway otay encourageway ishay ildrenchay, asway ometimessay Iway oundfay atthay 
ehay alledcay emthay, otay astcay offway eirthay elancholymay. Ehay ouldway alktay inway away 
eerfulchay accentway, ithway anway expressionway ofway oodnessgay atthay estowedbay easureplay 
evenway uponway emay. Agathaway istenedlay ithway espectray, erhay eyesway ometimessay illedfay 
ithway earstay, ichwhay eshay endeavouredway otay ipeway awayway unperceivedway; utbay Iway 
enerallygay oundfay atthay erhay ountenancecay andway onetay ereway oremay eerfulchay afterway 
avinghay istenedlay otay ethay exhortationsway ofway erhay atherfay. Itway asway otnay usthay 
ithway Elixfay. Ehay asway alwaysway ethay addestsay ofway ethay oupgray, andway evenway otay ymay 
unpractisedway ensessay, ehay appearedway otay avehay ufferedsay oremay eeplyday anthay ishay 
iendsfray. Utbay ifway ishay ountenancecay asway oremay orrowfulsay, ishay oicevay asway oremay 
eerfulchay anthay atthay ofway ishay istersay, especiallyway enwhay ehay addressedway ethay oldway 
anmay. 

"Iway ouldcay entionmay innumerableway instancesway ichwhay, althoughway ightslay, arkedmay 
ethay ispositionsday ofway esethay amiableway ottagerscay. Inway ethay idstmay ofway overtypay 
andway antway, Elixfay arriedcay ithway easureplay otay ishay istersay ethay irstfay ittlelay 
itewhay owerflay atthay eepedpay outway omfray eneathbay ethay owysnay oundgray. Earlyway inway 
ethay orningmay, eforebay eshay adhay isenray, ehay earedclay awayway ethay owsnay atthay 
obstructedway erhay athpay otay ethay ilkmay-house, ewdray aterway omfray ethay ellway, andway 
oughtbray ethay oodway omfray ethay outhouseway, erewhay, otay ishay erpetualpay 
astonishmentway, ehay oundfay ishay orestay alwaysway eplenishedray ybay anway invisibleway 
andhay. Inway ethay ayday, Iway elievebay, ehay orkedway ometimessay orfay away eighbouringnay 
armerfay, ecausebay ehay oftenway entway orthfay andway idday otnay eturnray untilway innerday, 
yetway oughtbray onay oodway ithway imhay. Atway otherway imestay ehay orkedway inway ethay ardengay, 
utbay asway erethay asway ittlelay otay oday inway ethay ostyfray easonsay, ehay eadray otay ethay oldway 
anmay andway Agathaway. 

"Isthay eadingray adhay uzzledpay emay extremelyway atway irstfay, utbay ybay egreesday Iway 
iscoveredday atthay ehay utteredway anymay ofway ethay amesay oundssay enwhay ehay eadray asway enwhay 
ehay alkedtay. Iway onjecturedcay, ereforethay, atthay ehay oundfay onway ethay aperpay ignssay 
orfay eechspay ichwhay ehay understoodway, andway Iway ardentlyway ongedlay otay omprehendcay 
esethay alsoway; utbay owhay asway atthay ossiblepay enwhay Iway idday otnay evenway understandway 
ethay oundssay orfay ichwhay eythay oodstay asway ignssay? Iway improvedway, oweverhay, 
ensiblysay inway isthay iencescay, utbay otnay ufficientlysay otay ollowfay upway anyway indkay ofway 
onversationcay, althoughway Iway appliedway ymay olewhay indmay otay ethay endeavourway, orfay Iway 
easilyway erceivedpay atthay, althoughway Iway eagerlyway ongedlay otay iscoverday yselfmay otay 
ethay ottagerscay, Iway oughtway otnay otay akemay ethay attemptway untilway Iway adhay irstfay ecomebay 
astermay ofway eirthay anguagelay, ichwhay owledgeknay ightmay enableway emay otay akemay emthay 
overlookway ethay eformityday ofway ymay igurefay, orfay ithway isthay alsoway ethay ontrastcay 
erpetuallypay esentedpray otay ymay eyesway adhay ademay emay acquaintedway. 

"Iway adhay admiredway ethay erfectpay ormsfay ofway ymay ottagerscay--their acegray, eautybay, 
andway elicateday omplexionscay; utbay owhay asway Iway errifiedtay enwhay Iway iewedvay yselfmay 
inway away ansparenttray oolpay! Atway irstfay Iway artedstay ackbay, unableway otay elievebay atthay 
itway asway indeedway Iway owhay asway eflectedray inway ethay irrormay; andway enwhay Iway ecamebay 
ullyfay onvincedcay atthay Iway asway inway ealityray ethay onstermay atthay Iway amway, Iway asway 
illedfay ithway ethay itterestbay ensationssay ofway espondenceday andway ortificationmay. 
Alasway! Iway idday otnay yetway entirelyway owknay ethay atalfay effectsway ofway isthay iserablemay 
eformityday. 

"Asway ethay unsay ecamebay armerway andway ethay ightlay ofway ayday ongerlay, ethay owsnay 
anishedvay, andway Iway eheldbay ethay arebay eestray andway ethay ackblay earthway. Omfray isthay 
imetay Elixfay asway oremay employedway, andway ethay earthay-moving indicationsway ofway 
impendingway aminefay isappearedday. Eirthay oodfay, asway Iway afterwardsway oundfay, asway 
oarsecay, utbay itway asway olesomewhay; andway eythay ocuredpray away ufficiencysay ofway itway. 
Everalsay ewnay indskay ofway antsplay angspray upway inway ethay ardengay, ichwhay eythay 
esseddray; andway esethay ignssay ofway omfortcay increasedway ailyday asway ethay easonsay 
advancedway. 

"Ethay oldway anmay, eaninglay onway ishay onsay, alkedway eachway ayday atway oonnay, enwhay itway idday 
otnay ainray, asway Iway oundfay itway asway alledcay enwhay ethay eavenshay ouredpay orthfay itsway 
atersway. Isthay equentlyfray ooktay aceplay, utbay away ighhay indway uicklyqay ieddray ethay 
earthway, andway ethay easonsay ecamebay arfay oremay easantplay anthay itway adhay eenbay. 

"Ymay odemay ofway ifelay inway ymay ovelhay asway uniformway. Uringday ethay orningmay Iway 
attendedway ethay otionsmay ofway ethay ottagerscay, andway enwhay eythay ereway ispersedday inway 
ariousvay occupationsway, Iway eptslay; ethay emainderray ofway ethay ayday asway entspay inway 
observingway ymay iendsfray. Enwhay eythay adhay etiredray otay estray, ifway erethay asway anyway 
oonmay orway ethay ightnay asway arstay-light, Iway entway intoway ethay oodsway andway ollectedcay 
ymay ownway oodfay andway uelfay orfay ethay ottagecay. Enwhay Iway eturnedray, asway oftenway asway itway 
asway ecessarynay, Iway earedclay eirthay athpay omfray ethay owsnay andway erformedpay osethay 
officesway atthay Iway adhay eensay oneday ybay Elixfay. Iway afterwardsway oundfay atthay esethay 
abourslay, erformedpay ybay anway invisibleway andhay, eatlygray astonishedway emthay; andway 
onceway orway icetway Iway eardhay emthay, onway esethay occasionsway, utterway ethay ordsway 'oodgay 
iritspay,' 'onderfulway'; utbay Iway idday otnay enthay understandway ethay ignificationsay 
ofway esethay ermstay. 

"Ymay oughtsthay ownay ecamebay oremay activeway, andway Iway ongedlay otay iscoverday ethay 
otivesmay andway eelingsfay ofway esethay ovelylay eaturescray; Iway asway inquisitiveway otay 
owknay ywhay Elixfay appearedway osay iserablemay andway Agathaway osay adsay. Iway oughtthay 
(oolishfay etchwray!) atthay itway ightmay ebay inway ymay owerpay otay estoreray appinesshay otay 
esethay eservingday eoplepay. Enwhay Iway eptslay orway asway absentway, ethay ormsfay ofway ethay 
enerablevay indblay atherfay, ethay entlegay Agathaway, andway ethay excellentway Elixfay 
ittedflay eforebay emay. Iway ookedlay uponway emthay asway uperiorsay eingsbay owhay ouldway ebay 
ethay arbitersway ofway ymay uturefay estinyday. Iway ormedfay inway ymay imaginationway away 
ousandthay icturespay ofway esentingpray yselfmay otay emthay, andway eirthay eceptionray ofway 
emay. Iway imaginedway atthay eythay ouldway ebay isgustedday, untilway, ybay ymay entlegay 
emeanourday andway onciliatingcay ordsway, Iway ouldshay irstfay inway eirthay avourfay andway 
afterwardsway eirthay ovelay. 

"Esethay oughtsthay exhilaratedway emay andway edlay emay otay applyway ithway eshfray ardourway otay 
ethay acquiringway ethay artway ofway anguagelay. Ymay organsway ereway indeedway arshhay, utbay 
upplesay; andway althoughway ymay oicevay asway eryvay unlikeway ethay oftsay usicmay ofway eirthay 
onestay, yetway Iway onouncedpray uchsay ordsway asway Iway understoodway ithway olerabletay easeway. 
Itway asway asway ethay assway andway ethay aplay-dog; yetway urelysay ethay entlegay assway osewhay 
intentionsway ereway affectionateway, althoughway ishay annersmay ereway uderay, eservedday 
etterbay eatmenttray anthay owsblay andway execrationway. 

"Ethay easantplay owersshay andway enialgay armthway ofway ingspray eatlygray alteredway ethay 
aspectway ofway ethay earthway. Enmay owhay eforebay isthay angechay eemedsay otay avehay eenbay 
idhay inway avescay ispersedday emselvesthay andway ereway employedway inway ariousvay artsway ofway 
ultivationcay. Ethay irdsbay angsay inway oremay eerfulchay otesnay, andway ethay eaveslay 
eganbay otay udbay orthfay onway ethay eestray. Appyhay, appyhay earthway! Itfay abitationhay 
orfay odsgay, ichwhay, osay ortshay away imetay eforebay, asway eakblay, ampday, andway 
unwholesomeway. Ymay iritsspay ereway elevatedway ybay ethay enchantingway appearanceway ofway 
aturenay; ethay astpay asway ottedblay omfray ymay emorymay, ethay esentpray asway anquiltray, 
andway ethay uturefay ildedgay ybay ightbray aysray ofway opehay andway anticipationsway ofway oyjay." 



Apterchay 13 

"Iway ownay astenhay otay ethay oremay ovingmay artpay ofway ymay orystay. Iway allshay elateray 
eventsway atthay impressedway emay ithway eelingsfay ichwhay, omfray atwhay Iway adhay eenbay,

"Ingspray advancedway apidlyray; ethay eatherway ecamebay inefay andway ethay iesskay

ensessay ereway atifiedgray andway efreshedray ybay away ousandthay entsscay ofway elightday andway

"Everyway onversationcay ofway ethay ottagerscay ownay openedway ewnay ondersway otay emay. 
Ilewhay Iway istenedlay otay ethay instructionsway ichwhay Elixfay estowedbay uponway ethay
