Apterchay 14 

"Omesay imetay elapsedway eforebay Iway earnedlay ethay istoryhay ofway ymay iendsfray. Itway asway 
oneway ichwhay ouldcay otnay ailfay otay impressway itselfway eeplyday onway ymay indmay, unfoldingway 
asway itway idday away umbernay ofway ircumstancescay, eachway interestingway andway onderfulway otay 
oneway osay utterlyway inexperiencedway asway Iway asway. 

"Ethay amenay ofway ethay oldway anmay asway Eday Aceylay. Ehay asway escendedday omfray away oodgay 
amilyfay inway Ancefray, erewhay ehay adhay ivedlay orfay anymay yearsway inway affluenceway, 
espectedray ybay ishay uperiorssay andway elovedbay ybay ishay equalsway. Ishay onsay asway edbray

"Ethay atherfay ofway Afiesay adhay eenbay ethay ausecay ofway eirthay uinray. Ehay asway away 
Urkishtay erchantmay andway adhay inhabitedway Arispay orfay anymay yearsway, enwhay, orfay omesay

"Elixfay adhay accidentallyway eenbay esentpray atway ethay ialtray; ishay orrorhay andway

amazedway andway elightedday, endeavouredway otay indlekay ethay ealzay ofway ishay elivererday

erhay atherfay andway owhay ybay erhay esturesgay expressedway erhay ivelylay atitudegray, ethay

away easuretray ichwhay ouldway ullyfay ewardray ishay oiltay andway azardhay. 

"Ethay Urktay uicklyqay erceivedpay ethay impressionway atthay ishay aughterday adhay ademay 
onway ethay earthay ofway Elixfay andway endeavouredway otay ecuresay imhay oremay entirelyway inway 
ishay interestsway ybay ethay omisepray ofway erhay andhay inway arriagemay osay oonsay asway ehay 
ouldshay ebay onveyedcay otay away aceplay ofway afetysay. Elixfay asway ootay elicateday otay 
acceptway isthay offerway, yetway ehay ookedlay orwardfay otay ethay obabilitypray ofway ethay 
eventway asway otay ethay onsummationcay ofway ishay appinesshay. 

"Uringday ethay ensuingway aysday, ilewhay ethay eparationspray ereway oinggay orwardfay orfay 
ethay escapeway ofway ethay erchantmay, ethay ealzay ofway Elixfay asway armedway ybay everalsay 
etterslay atthay ehay eceivedray omfray isthay ovelylay irlgay, owhay oundfay eansmay otay 
expressway erhay oughtsthay inway ethay anguagelay ofway erhay overlay ybay ethay aidway ofway anway oldway

ethay ostmay ardentway ermstay orfay ishay intendedway ervicessay owardstay erhay arentpay, andway 
atway ethay amesay imetay eshay entlygay eploredday erhay ownway atefay. 

"Iway avehay opiescay ofway esethay etterslay, orfay Iway oundfay eansmay, uringday ymay esidenceray 
inway ethay ovelhay, otay ocurepray ethay implementsway ofway itingwray; andway ethay etterslay 
ereway oftenway inway ethay andshay ofway Elixfay orway Agathaway. Eforebay Iway epartday Iway illway 
ivegay emthay otay youway; eythay illway ovepray ethay uthtray ofway ymay aletay; utbay atway esentpray, 
asway ethay unsay isway alreadyway arfay eclinedday, Iway allshay onlyway avehay imetay otay epeatray 
ethay ubstancesay ofway emthay otay youway. 

"Afiesay elatedray atthay erhay othermay asway away Istianchray Arabway, eizedsay andway ademay away 
aveslay ybay ethay Urkstay; ecommendedray ybay erhay eautybay, eshay adhay onway ethay earthay ofway

"Ethay ayday orfay ethay executionway ofway ethay Urktay asway ixedfay, utbay onway ethay ightnay

"Ethay overnmentgay ofway Ancefray ereway eatlygray enragedway atway ethay escapeway ofway eirthay

"Eshay arrivedway inway afetysay atway away owntay aboutway entytway eagueslay omfray ethay ottagecay

Apterchay 15 

"Uchsay asway ethay istoryhay ofway ymay elovedbay ottagerscay. Itway impressedway emay eeplyday. 
Iway earnedlay, omfray ethay iewsvay ofway ocialsay ifelay ichwhay itway evelopedday, otay admireway

"Asway Iway eadray, oweverhay, Iway appliedway uchmay ersonallypay otay ymay ownway eelingsfay andway 
onditioncay. Iway oundfay yselfmay imilarsay yetway atway ethay amesay imetay angelystray

asway away istenerlay. Iway ympathizedsay ithway andway artlypay understoodway emthay, utbay Iway

'Ethay athpay ofway ymay epartureday asway eefray,' andway erethay asway onenay otay amentlay ymay

"Ethay olumevay ofway Utarchplay's Iveslay ichwhay Iway ossessedpay ontainedcay ethay

"Utbay Aradisepay Ostlay excitedway ifferentday andway arfay eeperday emotionsway. Iway eadray

Anymay imestay Iway onsideredcay Atansay asway ethay itterfay emblemway ofway ymay onditioncay, orfay 
oftenway, ikelay imhay, enwhay Iway iewedvay ethay issblay ofway ymay otectorspray, ethay itterbay

"Anotherway ircumstancecay engthenedstray andway onfirmedcay esethay eelingsfay. Oonsay

ethay essdray ichwhay Iway adhay akentay omfray yourway aboratorylay. Atway irstfay Iway adhay 
eglectednay emthay, utbay ownay atthay Iway asway ableway otay ecipherday ethay aracterschay inway

inutelymay escribedday inway esethay aperspay everyway epstay youway ooktay inway ethay ogresspray

Everythingway isway elatedray inway emthay ichwhay earsbay eferenceray otay ymay accursedway

Ywhay idday youway ormfay away onstermay osay ideoushay atthay evenway YOUWAY urnedtay omfray emay inway

eryvay esemblanceray. Atansay adhay ishay ompanionscay, ellowfay evilsday, otay admireway 
andway encourageway imhay, utbay Iway amway olitarysay andway abhorredway.' 

"Esethay ereway ethay eflectionsray ofway ymay ourshay ofway espondencyday andway olitudesay;

ostponedpay isthay attemptway orfay omesay onthsmay ongerlay, orfay ethay importanceway

Esidesbay, Iway oundfay atthay ymay understandingway improvedway osay uchmay ithway everyway 
ayday's experienceway atthay Iway asway unwillingway otay ommencecay isthay undertakingway 
untilway away ewfay oremay onthsmay ouldshay avehay addedway otay ymay agacitysay. 

"Everalsay angeschay, inway ethay eantimemay, ooktay aceplay inway ethay ottagecay. Ethay 
esencepray ofway Afiesay iffusedday appinesshay amongway itsway inhabitantsway, andway Iway alsoway 
oundfay atthay away eatergray egreeday ofway entyplay eignedray erethay. Elixfay andway Agathaway 
entspay oremay imetay inway amusementway andway onversationcay, andway ereway assistedway inway 
eirthay abourslay ybay ervantssay. Eythay idday otnay appearway ichray, utbay eythay ereway 
ontentedcay andway appyhay; eirthay eelingsfay ereway erenesay andway eacefulpay, ilewhay 
inemay ecamebay everyway ayday oremay umultuoustay. Increaseway ofway owledgeknay onlyway 
iscoveredday otay emay oremay earlyclay atwhay away etchedwray outcastway Iway asway. Iway 
erishedchay opehay, itway isway uetray, utbay itway anishedvay enwhay Iway eheldbay ymay ersonpay 
eflectedray inway aterway orway ymay adowshay inway ethay oonshinemay, evenway asway atthay ailfray 
imageway andway atthay inconstantway adeshay. 

"Iway endeavouredway otay ushcray esethay earsfay andway otay ortifyfay yselfmay orfay ethay ialtray 
ichwhay inway away ewfay onthsmay Iway esolvedray otay undergoway; andway ometimessay Iway allowedway ymay 
oughtsthay, uncheckedway ybay easonray, otay ambleray inway ethay ieldsfay ofway Aradisepay, andway 
aredday otay ancyfay amiableway andway ovelylay eaturescray ympathizingsay ithway ymay 
eelingsfay andway eeringchay ymay oomglay; eirthay angelicway ountenancescay eathedbray 
ilessmay ofway onsolationcay. Utbay itway asway allway away eamdray; onay Eveway oothedsay ymay 
orrowssay ornay aredshay ymay oughtsthay; Iway asway aloneway. Iway ememberedray Adamway's 
upplicationsay otay ishay Eatorcray. Utbay erewhay asway inemay? Ehay adhay abandonedway emay, 
andway inway ethay itternessbay ofway ymay earthay Iway ursedcay imhay. 

"Autumnway assedpay usthay. Iway awsay, ithway urprisesay andway iefgray, ethay eaveslay ecayday 
andway allfay, andway aturenay againway assumeway ethay arrenbay andway eakblay appearanceway itway 
adhay ornway enwhay Iway irstfay eheldbay ethay oodsway andway ethay ovelylay oonmay. Yetway Iway idday 
otnay eedhay ethay eaknessblay ofway ethay eatherway; Iway asway etterbay ittedfay ybay ymay 
onformationcay orfay ethay enduranceway ofway oldcay anthay eathay. Utbay ymay iefchay 
elightsday ereway ethay ightsay ofway ethay owersflay, ethay irdsbay, andway allway ethay aygay 
apparelway ofway ummersay; enwhay osethay esertedday emay, Iway urnedtay ithway oremay attentionway 
owardstay ethay ottagerscay. Eirthay appinesshay asway otnay ecreasedday ybay ethay 
absenceway ofway ummersay. Eythay ovedlay andway ympathizedsay ithway oneway anotherway; andway 
eirthay oysjay, ependingday onway eachway otherway, ereway otnay interruptedway ybay ethay 
asualtiescay atthay ooktay aceplay aroundway emthay. Ethay oremay Iway awsay ofway emthay, ethay 
eatergray ecamebay ymay esireday otay aimclay eirthay otectionpray andway indnesskay; ymay 
earthay yearnedway otay ebay ownknay andway ovedlay ybay esethay amiableway eaturescray; otay eesay 
eirthay eetsway ookslay irectedday owardstay emay ithway affectionway asway ethay utmostway 
imitlay ofway ymay ambitionway. Iway aredday otnay inkthay atthay eythay ouldway urntay emthay omfray 
emay ithway isdainday andway orrorhay. Ethay oorpay atthay oppedstay atway eirthay oorday ereway 
evernay ivendray awayway. Iway askedway, itway isway uetray, orfay eatergray easurestray anthay away 
ittlelay oodfay orway estray: Iway equiredray indnesskay andway ympathysay; utbay Iway idday otnay 
elievebay yselfmay utterlyway unworthyway ofway itway. 

"Ethay interway advancedway, andway anway entireway evolutionray ofway ethay easonssay adhay akentay 
aceplay incesay Iway awokeway intoway ifelay. Ymay attentionway atway isthay imetay asway olelysay 
irectedday owardstay ymay anplay ofway introducingway yselfmay intoway ethay ottagecay ofway ymay 
otectorspray. Iway evolvedray anymay ojectspray, utbay atthay onway ichwhay Iway inallyfay 
ixedfay asway otay enterway ethay ellingdway enwhay ethay indblay oldway anmay ouldshay ebay aloneway. 
Iway adhay agacitysay enoughway otay iscoverday atthay ethay unnaturalway ideousnesshay ofway ymay 
ersonpay asway ethay iefchay objectway ofway orrorhay ithway osethay owhay adhay ormerlyfay 
eheldbay emay. Ymay oicevay, althoughway arshhay, adhay othingnay erribletay inway itway; Iway 
oughtthay, ereforethay, atthay ifway inway ethay absenceway ofway ishay ildrenchay Iway ouldcay aingay 
ethay oodgay illway andway ediationmay ofway ethay oldway Eday Aceylay, Iway ightmay ybay ishay eansmay 
ebay oleratedtay ybay ymay youngerway otectorspray. 

"Oneway ayday, enwhay ethay unsay oneshay onway ethay edray eaveslay atthay ewedstray ethay oundgray 
andway iffusedday eerfulnesschay, althoughway itway eniedday armthway, Afiesay, Agathaway, 
andway Elixfay epartedday onway away onglay ountrycay alkway, andway ethay oldway anmay, atway ishay ownway 
esireday, asway eftlay aloneway inway ethay ottagecay. Enwhay ishay ildrenchay adhay epartedday, 
ehay ooktay upway ishay uitargay andway ayedplay everalsay ournfulmay utbay eetsway airsway, oremay 
eetsway andway ournfulmay anthay Iway adhay everway eardhay imhay ayplay eforebay. Atway irstfay ishay 
ountenancecay asway illuminatedway ithway easureplay, utbay asway ehay ontinuedcay, 
oughtfulnessthay andway adnesssay ucceededsay; atway engthlay, ayinglay asideway ethay 
instrumentway, ehay atsay absorbedway inway eflectionray. 

"Ymay earthay eatbay uickqay; isthay asway ethay ourhay andway omentmay ofway ialtray, ichwhay 
ouldway ecideday ymay opeshay orway ealizeray ymay earsfay. Ethay ervantssay ereway onegay otay away 
eighbouringnay airfay. Allway asway ilentsay inway andway aroundway ethay ottagecay; itway asway anway 
excellentway opportunityway; yetway, enwhay Iway oceededpray otay executeway ymay anplay, ymay 
imbslay ailedfay emay andway Iway anksay otay ethay oundgray. Againway Iway oseray, andway exertingway 
allway ethay irmnessfay ofway ichwhay Iway asway astermay, emovedray ethay anksplay ichwhay Iway adhay 
acedplay eforebay ymay ovelhay otay oncealcay ymay etreatray. Ethay eshfray airway evivedray 
emay, andway ithway enewedray eterminationday Iway approachedway ethay oorday ofway eirthay 
ottagecay. 

"Iway ockedknay. 'Owhay isway erethay?' aidsay ethay oldway anmay. 'Omecay inway.' 

"Iway enteredway. 'Ardonpay isthay intrusionway,' aidsay Iway; 'Iway amway away avellertray inway antway 
ofway away ittlelay estray; youway ouldway eatlygray obligeway emay ifway youway ouldway allowway emay otay 
emainray away ewfay inutesmay eforebay ethay irefay.' 

"'Enterway,' aidsay Eday Aceylay, 'andway Iway illway ytray inway atwhay annermay Iway ancay otay 
elieveray yourway antsway; utbay, unfortunatelyway, ymay ildrenchay areway omfray omehay, andway 
asway Iway amway indblay, Iway amway afraidway Iway allshay indfay itway ifficultday otay ocurepray oodfay 
orfay youway.' 

"'Oday otnay oubletray yourselfway, ymay indkay osthay; Iway avehay oodfay; itway isway armthway andway 
estray onlyway atthay Iway eednay.' 

"Iway atsay ownday, andway away ilencesay ensuedway. Iway ewknay atthay everyway inutemay asway 
eciouspray otay emay, yetway Iway emainedray irresoluteway inway atwhay annermay otay ommencecay 
ethay interviewway, enwhay ethay oldway anmay addressedway emay. 'Ybay yourway anguagelay, 
angerstray, Iway upposesay youway areway ymay ountrymancay; areway youway Enchfray?' 

"'Onay; utbay Iway asway educatedway ybay away Enchfray amilyfay andway understandway atthay 
anguagelay onlyway. Iway amway ownay oinggay otay aimclay ethay otectionpray ofway omesay iendsfray, 
omwhay Iway incerelysay ovelay, andway ofway osewhay avourfay Iway avehay omesay opeshay.' 

"'Areway eythay Ermansgay?' 

"'Onay, eythay areway Enchfray. Utbay etlay usway angechay ethay ubjectsay. Iway amway anway 
unfortunateway andway esertedday eaturecray, Iway ooklay aroundway andway Iway avehay onay elationray 
orway iendfray uponway earthway. Esethay amiableway eoplepay otay omwhay Iway ogay avehay evernay 
eensay emay andway owknay ittlelay ofway emay. Iway amway ullfay ofway earsfay, orfay ifway Iway ailfay 
erethay, Iway amway anway outcastway inway ethay orldway oreverfay.' 

"'Oday otnay espairday. Otay ebay iendlessfray isway indeedway otay ebay unfortunateway, utbay 
ethay eartshay ofway enmay, enwhay unprejudicedway ybay anyway obviousway elfsay-interest, areway 
ullfay ofway otherlybray ovelay andway aritychay. Elyray, ereforethay, onway yourway opeshay; 
andway ifway esethay iendsfray areway oodgay andway amiableway, oday otnay espairday.' 

"'Eythay areway indkay--they areway ethay ostmay excellentway eaturescray inway ethay orldway; 
utbay, unfortunatelyway, eythay areway ejudicedpray againstway emay. Iway avehay oodgay 
ispositionsday; ymay ifelay ashay eenbay ithertohay armlesshay andway inway omesay egreeday 
eneficialbay; utbay away atalfay ejudicepray oudsclay eirthay eyesway, andway erewhay eythay 
oughtway otay eesay away eelingfay andway indkay iendfray, eythay eholdbay onlyway away etestableday 
onstermay.' 

"'Atthay isway indeedway unfortunateway; utbay ifway youway areway eallyray amelessblay, annotcay 
youway undeceiveway emthay?' 

"'Iway amway aboutway otay undertakeway atthay asktay; andway itway isway onway atthay accountway atthay Iway 
eelfay osay anymay overwhelmingway errorstay. Iway enderlytay ovelay esethay iendsfray; Iway 
avehay, unknownway otay emthay, eenbay orfay anymay onthsmay inway ethay abitshay ofway ailyday 
indnesskay owardstay emthay; utbay eythay elievebay atthay Iway ishway otay injureway emthay, andway 
itway isway atthay ejudicepray ichwhay Iway ishway otay overcomeway.' 

"'Erewhay oday esethay iendsfray esideray?' 

"'Earnay isthay otspay.' 

"Ethay oldway anmay ausedpay andway enthay ontinuedcay, 'Ifway youway illway unreservedlyway 
onfidecay otay emay ethay articularspay ofway yourway aletay, Iway erhapspay aymay ebay ofway useway inway 
undeceivingway emthay. Iway amway indblay andway annotcay udgejay ofway yourway ountenancecay, utbay 
erethay isway omethingsay inway yourway ordsway ichwhay ersuadespay emay atthay youway areway 
inceresay. Iway amway oorpay andway anway exileway, utbay itway illway affordway emay uetray easureplay 
otay ebay inway anyway ayway erviceablesay otay away umanhay eaturecray.' 

"'Excellentway anmay! Iway ankthay youway andway acceptway yourway enerousgay offerway. Youway 
aiseray emay omfray ethay ustday ybay isthay indnesskay; andway Iway usttray atthay, ybay yourway aidway, 
Iway allshay otnay ebay ivendray omfray ethay ocietysay andway ympathysay ofway yourway ellowfay 
eaturescray.' 

"'Eavenhay orbidfay! Evenway ifway youway ereway eallyray iminalcray, orfay atthay ancay onlyway 
ivedray youway otay esperationday, andway otnay instigateway youway otay irtuevay. Iway alsoway amway 
unfortunateway; Iway andway ymay amilyfay avehay eenbay ondemnedcay, althoughway innocentway; 
udgejay, ereforethay, ifway Iway oday otnay eelfay orfay yourway isfortunesmay.' 

"'Owhay ancay Iway ankthay youway, ymay estbay andway onlyway enefactorbay? Omfray yourway ipslay 
irstfay avehay Iway eardhay ethay oicevay ofway indnesskay irectedday owardstay emay; Iway allshay 
ebay oreverfay atefulgray; andway yourway esentpray umanityhay assuresway emay ofway uccesssay 
ithway osethay iendsfray omwhay Iway amway onway ethay ointpay ofway eetingmay.' 

"'Aymay Iway owknay ethay amesnay andway esidenceray ofway osethay iendsfray?' 

"Iway ausedpay. Isthay, Iway oughtthay, asway ethay omentmay ofway ecisionday, ichwhay asway otay 
obray emay ofway orway estowbay appinesshay onway emay oreverfay. Iway uggledstray ainlyvay orfay 
irmnessfay ufficientsay otay answerway imhay, utbay ethay effortway estroyedday allway ymay 
emainingray engthstray; Iway anksay onway ethay airchay andway obbedsay aloudway. Atway atthay 
omentmay Iway eardhay ethay epsstay ofway ymay youngerway otectorspray. Iway adhay otnay away omentmay 
otay oselay, utbay eizingsay ethay andhay ofway ethay oldway anmay, Iway iedcray, 'Ownay isway ethay 
imetay! Avesay andway otectpray emay! Youway andway yourway amilyfay areway ethay iendsfray omwhay Iway 
eeksay. Oday otnay youway esertday emay inway ethay ourhay ofway ialtray!' 

"'Eatgray Odgay!' exclaimedway ethay oldway anmay. 'Owhay areway youway?' 

"Atway atthay instantway ethay ottagecay oorday asway openedway, andway Elixfay, Afiesay, andway 
Agathaway enteredway. Owhay ancay escribeday eirthay orrorhay andway onsternationcay onway 
eholdingbay emay? Agathaway aintedfay, andway Afiesay, unableway otay attendway otay erhay 
iendfray, ushedray outway ofway ethay ottagecay. Elixfay artedday orwardfay, andway ithway 
upernaturalsay orcefay oretay emay omfray ishay atherfay, otay osewhay eesknay Iway ungclay, inway 
away ansporttray ofway uryfay, ehay ashedday emay otay ethay oundgray andway uckstray emay iolentlyvay 
ithway away ickstay. Iway ouldcay avehay orntay imhay imblay omfray imblay, asway ethay ionlay endsray 
ethay antelopeway. Utbay ymay earthay anksay ithinway emay asway ithway itterbay icknesssay, andway 
Iway efrainedray. Iway awsay imhay onway ethay ointpay ofway epeatingray ishay owblay, enwhay, 
overcomeway ybay ainpay andway anguishway, Iway uittedqay ethay ottagecay, andway inway ethay eneralgay 
umulttay escapedway unperceivedway otay ymay ovelhay." 



Apterchay 16 

"Ursedcay, ursedcay eatorcray! Ywhay idday Iway ivelay? Ywhay, inway atthay instantway, idday Iway 
otnay extinguishway ethay arkspay ofway existenceway ichwhay youway adhay osay antonlyway 
estowedbay? Iway owknay otnay; espairday adhay otnay yetway akentay ossessionpay ofway emay; ymay 
eelingsfay ereway osethay ofway ageray andway evengeray. Iway ouldcay ithway easureplay avehay 
estroyedday ethay ottagecay andway itsway inhabitantsway andway avehay uttedglay yselfmay ithway 
eirthay ieksshray andway iserymay. 

"Enwhay ightnay amecay Iway uittedqay ymay etreatray andway anderedway inway ethay oodway; andway 
ownay, onay ongerlay estrainedray ybay ethay earfay ofway iscoveryday, Iway avegay entvay otay ymay 
anguishway inway earfulfay owlingshay. Iway asway ikelay away ildway eastbay atthay adhay okenbray 
ethay oilstay, estroyingday ethay objectsway atthay obstructedway emay andway angingray 
oughthray ethay oodway ithway away agstay-like iftnesssway. Ohway! Atwhay away iserablemay 
ightnay Iway assedpay! Ethay oldcay arsstay oneshay inway ockerymay, andway ethay arebay eestray 
avedway eirthay anchesbray aboveway emay; ownay andway enthay ethay eetsway oicevay ofway away irdbay 
urstbay orthfay amidstway ethay universalway illnessstay. Allway, avesay Iway, ereway atway estray 
orway inway enjoymentway; Iway, ikelay ethay archway-fiend, orebay away ellhay ithinway emay, andway 
indingfay yselfmay unsympathizedway ithway, ishedway otay eartay upway ethay eestray, eadspray 
avochay andway estructionday aroundway emay, andway enthay otay avehay atsay ownday andway enjoyedway 
ethay uinray. 

"Utbay isthay asway away uxurylay ofway ensationsay atthay ouldcay otnay endureway; Iway ecamebay 
atiguedfay ithway excessway ofway odilybay exertionway andway anksay onway ethay ampday assgray inway 
ethay icksay impotenceway ofway espairday. Erethay asway onenay amongway ethay yriadsmay ofway enmay 
atthay existedway owhay ouldway itypay orway assistway emay; andway ouldshay Iway eelfay indnesskay 
owardstay ymay enemiesway? Onay; omfray atthay omentmay Iway eclaredday everlastingway arway 
againstway ethay eciesspay, andway oremay anthay allway, againstway imhay owhay adhay ormedfay emay 
andway entsay emay orthfay otay isthay insupportableway iserymay. 

"Ethay unsay oseray; Iway eardhay ethay oicesvay ofway enmay andway ewknay atthay itway asway 
impossibleway otay eturnray otay ymay etreatray uringday atthay ayday. Accordinglyway Iway idhay 
yselfmay inway omesay ickthay underwoodway, eterminingday otay evoteday ethay ensuingway ourshay 
otay eflectionray onway ymay ituationsay. 

"Ethay easantplay unshinesay andway ethay urepay airway ofway ayday estoredray emay otay omesay 
egreeday ofway anquillitytray; andway enwhay Iway onsideredcay atwhay adhay assedpay atway ethay 
ottagecay, Iway ouldcay otnay elphay elievingbay atthay Iway adhay eenbay ootay astyhay inway ymay 
onclusionscay. Iway adhay ertainlycay actedway imprudentlyway. Itway asway apparentway atthay 
ymay onversationcay adhay interestedway ethay atherfay inway ymay ehalfbay, andway Iway asway away 
oolfay inway avinghay exposedway ymay ersonpay otay ethay orrorhay ofway ishay ildrenchay. Iway 
oughtway otay avehay amiliarizedfay ethay oldway Eday Aceylay otay emay, andway ybay egreesday otay 
avehay iscoveredday yselfmay otay ethay estray ofway ishay amilyfay, enwhay eythay ouldshay avehay 
eenbay eparedpray orfay ymay approachway. Utbay Iway idday otnay elievebay ymay errorsway otay ebay 
irretrievableway, andway afterway uchmay onsiderationcay Iway esolvedray otay eturnray otay ethay 
ottagecay, eeksay ethay oldway anmay, andway ybay ymay epresentationsray inway imhay otay ymay 
artypay. 

"Esethay oughtsthay almedcay emay, andway inway ethay afternoonway Iway anksay intoway away ofoundpray 
eepslay; utbay ethay everfay ofway ymay oodblay idday otnay allowway emay otay ebay isitedvay ybay 
eacefulpay eamsdray. Ethay orriblehay enescay ofway ethay ecedingpray ayday asway oreverfay 
actingway eforebay ymay eyesway; ethay emalesfay ereway yingflay andway ethay enragedway Elixfay 
earingtay emay omfray ishay atherfay's eetfay. Iway awokeway exhaustedway, andway indingfay atthay 
itway asway alreadyway ightnay, Iway eptcray orthfay omfray ymay idinghay-place, andway entway inway 
earchsay ofway oodfay. 

"Enwhay ymay ungerhay asway appeasedway, Iway irectedday ymay epsstay owardstay ethay 
ellway-known athpay atthay onductedcay otay ethay ottagecay. Allway erethay asway atway eacepay. 
Iway eptcray intoway ymay ovelhay andway emainedray inway ilentsay expectationway ofway ethay 
accustomedway ourhay enwhay ethay amilyfay aroseway. Atthay ourhay assedpay, ethay unsay 
ountedmay ighhay inway ethay eavenshay, utbay ethay ottagerscay idday otnay appearway. Iway 
embledtray iolentlyvay, apprehendingway omesay eadfuldray isfortunemay. Ethay insideway 
ofway ethay ottagecay asway arkday, andway Iway eardhay onay otionmay; Iway annotcay escribeday ethay 
agonyway ofway isthay uspensesay. 

"Esentlypray otway ountrymencay assedpay ybay, utbay ausingpay earnay ethay ottagecay, eythay 
enteredway intoway onversationcay, usingway iolentvay esticulationsgay; utbay Iway idday otnay 
understandway atwhay eythay aidsay, asway eythay okespay ethay anguagelay ofway ethay ountrycay, 
ichwhay ifferedday omfray atthay ofway ymay otectorspray. Oonsay afterway, oweverhay, Elixfay 
approachedway ithway anotherway anmay; Iway asway urprisedsay, asway Iway ewknay atthay ehay adhay otnay 
uittedqay ethay ottagecay atthay orningmay, andway aitedway anxiouslyway otay iscoverday omfray 
ishay iscourseday ethay eaningmay ofway esethay unusualway appearancesway. 

"'Oday youway onsidercay,' aidsay ishay ompanioncay otay imhay, 'atthay youway illway ebay 
obligedway otay aypay eethray onthsmay' entray andway otay oselay ethay oducepray ofway yourway 
ardengay? Iway oday otnay ishway otay aketay anyway unfairway advantageway, andway Iway egbay 
ereforethay atthay youway illway aketay omesay aysday otay onsidercay ofway yourway 
eterminationday.' 

"'Itway isway utterlyway uselessway,' epliedray Elixfay; 'eway ancay evernay againway inhabitway 
yourway ottagecay. Ethay ifelay ofway ymay atherfay isway inway ethay eatestgray angerday, owingway 
otay ethay eadfuldray ircumstancecay atthay Iway avehay elatedray. Ymay ifeway andway ymay 
istersay illway evernay ecoverray omfray eirthay orrorhay. Iway entreatway youway otnay otay 
easonray ithway emay anyway oremay. Aketay ossessionpay ofway yourway enementtay andway etlay emay 
yflay omfray isthay aceplay.' 

"Elixfay embledtray iolentlyvay asway ehay aidsay isthay. Ehay andway ishay ompanioncay 
enteredway ethay ottagecay, inway ichwhay eythay emainedray orfay away ewfay inutesmay, andway enthay 
epartedday. Iway evernay awsay anyway ofway ethay amilyfay ofway Eday Aceylay oremay. 

"Iway ontinuedcay orfay ethay emainderray ofway ethay ayday inway ymay ovelhay inway away atestay ofway 
utterway andway upidstay espairday. Ymay otectorspray adhay epartedday andway adhay okenbray 
ethay onlyway inklay atthay eldhay emay otay ethay orldway. Orfay ethay irstfay imetay ethay 
eelingsfay ofway evengeray andway atredhay illedfay ymay osombay, andway Iway idday otnay ivestray otay 
ontrolcay emthay, utbay allowingway yselfmay otay ebay ornebay awayway ybay ethay eamstray, Iway 
entbay ymay indmay owardstay injuryway andway eathday. Enwhay Iway oughtthay ofway ymay iendsfray, 
ofway ethay ildmay oicevay ofway Eday Aceylay, ethay entlegay eyesway ofway Agathaway, andway ethay 
exquisiteway eautybay ofway ethay Arabianway, esethay oughtsthay anishedvay andway away ushgay ofway 
earstay omewhatsay oothedsay emay. Utbay againway enwhay Iway eflectedray atthay eythay adhay 
urnedspay andway esertedday emay, angerway eturnedray, away ageray ofway angerway, andway unableway otay 
injureway anythingway umanhay, Iway urnedtay ymay uryfay owardstay inanimateway objectsway. Asway 
ightnay advancedway Iway acedplay away arietyvay ofway ombustiblescay aroundway ethay ottagecay, 
andway afterway avinghay estroyedday everyway estigevay ofway ultivationcay inway ethay ardengay, 
Iway aitedway ithway orcedfay impatienceway untilway ethay oonmay adhay unksay otay ommencecay ymay 
operationsway. 

"Asway ethay ightnay advancedway, away iercefay indway aroseway omfray ethay oodsway andway uicklyqay 
ispersedday ethay oudsclay atthay adhay oiteredlay inway ethay eavenshay; ethay astblay oretay 
alongway ikelay away ightymay avalancheway andway oducedpray away indkay ofway insanityway inway ymay 
iritsspay atthay urstbay allway oundsbay ofway easonray andway eflectionray. Iway ightedlay ethay 
ydray anchbray ofway away eetray andway ancedday ithway uryfay aroundway ethay evotedday ottagecay, 
ymay eyesway illstay ixedfay onway ethay esternway orizonhay, ethay edgeway ofway ichwhay ethay oonmay 
earlynay ouchedtay. Away artpay ofway itsway orbway asway atway engthlay idhay, andway Iway avedway ymay 
andbray; itway anksay, andway ithway away oudlay eamscray Iway iredfay ethay awstray, andway eathhay, 
andway ushesbay, ichwhay Iway adhay ollectedcay. Ethay indway annedfay ethay irefay, andway ethay 
ottagecay asway uicklyqay envelopedway ybay ethay amesflay, ichwhay ungclay otay itway andway 
ickedlay itway ithway eirthay orkedfay andway estroyingday onguestay. 

"Asway oonsay asway Iway asway onvincedcay atthay onay assistanceway ouldcay avesay anyway artpay ofway 
ethay abitationhay, Iway uittedqay ethay enescay andway oughtsay orfay efugeray inway ethay oodsway. 

"Andway ownay, ithway ethay orldway eforebay emay, itherwhay ouldshay Iway endbay ymay epsstay? Iway 
esolvedray otay yflay arfay omfray ethay enescay ofway ymay isfortunesmay; utbay otay emay, atedhay 
andway espisedday, everyway ountrycay ustmay ebay equallyway orriblehay. Atway engthlay ethay 
oughtthay ofway youway ossedcray ymay indmay. Iway earnedlay omfray yourway aperspay atthay youway 
ereway ymay atherfay, ymay eatorcray; andway otay omwhay ouldcay Iway applyway ithway oremay itnessfay 
anthay otay imhay owhay adhay ivengay emay ifelay? Amongway ethay essonslay atthay Elixfay adhay 
estowedbay uponway Afiesay, eographygay adhay otnay eenbay omittedway; Iway adhay earnedlay omfray 
esethay ethay elativeray ituationssay ofway ethay ifferentday ountriescay ofway ethay earthway. 
Youway adhay entionedmay Enevagay asway ethay amenay ofway yourway ativenay owntay, andway owardstay 
isthay aceplay Iway esolvedray otay oceedpray. 

"Utbay owhay asway Iway otay irectday yselfmay? Iway ewknay atthay Iway ustmay aveltray inway away 
outhwesterlysay irectionday otay eachray ymay estinationday, utbay ethay unsay asway ymay 
onlyway uidegay. Iway idday otnay owknay ethay amesnay ofway ethay ownstay atthay Iway asway otay asspay 
oughthray, ornay ouldcay Iway askway informationway omfray away inglesay umanhay eingbay; utbay Iway 
idday otnay espairday. Omfray youway onlyway ouldcay Iway opehay orfay uccoursay, althoughway 
owardstay youway Iway eltfay onay entimentsay utbay atthay ofway atredhay. Unfeelingway, 
eartlesshay eatorcray! Youway adhay endowedway emay ithway erceptionspay andway assionspay 
andway enthay astcay emay abroadway anway objectway orfay ethay ornscay andway orrorhay ofway ankindmay. 
Utbay onway youway onlyway adhay Iway anyway aimclay orfay itypay andway edressray, andway omfray youway Iway 
eterminedday otay eeksay atthay usticejay ichwhay Iway ainlyvay attemptedway otay aingay omfray 
anyway otherway eingbay atthay oreway ethay umanhay ormfay. 

"Ymay avelstray ereway onglay andway ethay ufferingssay Iway enduredway intenseway. Itway asway 
atelay inway autumnway enwhay Iway uittedqay ethay istrictday erewhay Iway adhay osay onglay esidedray. 
Iway avelledtray onlyway atway ightnay, earfulfay ofway encounteringway ethay isagevay ofway away 
umanhay eingbay. Aturenay ecayedday aroundway emay, andway ethay unsay ecamebay eatlesshay; 
ainray andway owsnay ouredpay aroundway emay; ightymay iversray ereway ozenfray; ethay urfacesay 
ofway ethay earthway asway ardhay andway illchay, andway arebay, andway Iway oundfay onay eltershay. Ohway, 
earthway! Owhay oftenway idday Iway imprecateway ursescay onway ethay ausecay ofway ymay eingbay! Ethay 
ildnessmay ofway ymay aturenay adhay edflay, andway allway ithinway emay asway urnedtay otay allgay 
andway itternessbay. Ethay earernay Iway approachedway otay yourway abitationhay, ethay oremay 
eeplyday idday Iway eelfay ethay iritspay ofway evengeray enkindledway inway ymay earthay. Owsnay 
ellfay, andway ethay atersway ereway ardenedhay, utbay Iway estedray otnay. Away ewfay incidentsway 
ownay andway enthay irectedday emay, andway Iway ossessedpay away apmay ofway ethay ountrycay; utbay Iway 
oftenway anderedway ideway omfray ymay athpay. Ethay agonyway ofway ymay eelingsfay allowedway emay 
onay espiteray; onay incidentway occurredway omfray ichwhay ymay ageray andway iserymay ouldcay 
otnay extractway itsway oodfay; utbay away ircumstancecay atthay appenedhay enwhay Iway arrivedway 
onway ethay onfinescay ofway Itzerlandsway, enwhay ethay unsay adhay ecoveredray itsway armthway 
andway ethay earthway againway eganbay otay ooklay eengray, onfirmedcay inway anway especialway 
annermay ethay itternessbay andway orrorhay ofway ymay eelingsfay. 

"Iway enerallygay estedray uringday ethay ayday andway avelledtray onlyway enwhay Iway asway 
ecuredsay ybay ightnay omfray ethay iewvay ofway anmay. Oneway orningmay, oweverhay, indingfay 
atthay ymay athpay aylay oughthray away eepday oodway, Iway enturedvay otay ontinuecay ymay ourneyjay 
afterway ethay unsay adhay isenray; ethay ayday, ichwhay asway oneway ofway ethay irstfay ofway ingspray, 
eeredchay evenway emay ybay ethay ovelinesslay ofway itsway unshinesay andway ethay alminessbay ofway 
ethay airway. Iway eltfay emotionsway ofway entlenessgay andway easureplay, atthay adhay onglay 
appearedway eadday, eviveray ithinway emay. Alfhay urprisedsay ybay ethay oveltynay ofway 
esethay ensationssay, Iway allowedway yselfmay otay ebay ornebay awayway ybay emthay, andway 
orgettingfay ymay olitudesay andway eformityday, aredday otay ebay appyhay. Oftsay earstay 
againway edewedbay ymay eekschay, andway Iway evenway aisedray ymay umidhay eyesway ithway 
ankfulnessthay owardstay ethay essedblay unsay, ichwhay estowedbay uchsay oyjay uponway emay. 

"Iway ontinuedcay otay indway amongway ethay athspay ofway ethay oodway, untilway Iway amecay otay itsway 
oundarybay, ichwhay asway irtedskay ybay away eepday andway apidray iverray, intoway ichwhay anymay 
ofway ethay eestray entbay eirthay anchesbray, ownay uddingbay ithway ethay eshfray ingspray. 
Erehay Iway ausedpay, otnay exactlyway owingknay atwhay athpay otay ursuepay, enwhay Iway eardhay 
ethay oundsay ofway oicesvay, atthay inducedway emay otay oncealcay yselfmay underway ethay adeshay 
ofway away ypresscay. Iway asway arcelyscay idhay enwhay away youngway irlgay amecay unningray 
owardstay ethay otspay erewhay Iway asway oncealedcay, aughinglay, asway ifway eshay anray omfray 
omeonesay inway ortspay. Eshay ontinuedcay erhay oursecay alongway ethay ecipitouspray idessay 
ofway ethay iverray, enwhay uddenlysay erhay ootfay ippedslay, andway eshay ellfay intoway ethay 
apidray eamstray. Iway ushedray omfray ymay idinghay-place andway ithway extremeway abourlay, 
omfray ethay orcefay ofway ethay urrentcay, avedsay erhay andway aggeddray erhay otay oreshay. Eshay 
asway enselesssay, andway Iway endeavouredway ybay everyway eansmay inway ymay owerpay otay estoreray 
animationway, enwhay Iway asway uddenlysay interruptedway ybay ethay approachway ofway away usticray, 
owhay asway obablypray ethay ersonpay omfray omwhay eshay adhay ayfullyplay edflay. Onway 
eeingsay emay, ehay artedday owardstay emay, andway earingtay ethay irlgay omfray ymay armsway, 
astenedhay owardstay ethay eeperday artspay ofway ethay oodway. Iway ollowedfay eedilyspay, Iway 
ardlyhay ewknay ywhay; utbay enwhay ethay anmay awsay emay awdray earnay, ehay aimedway away ungay, 
ichwhay ehay arriedcay, atway ymay odybay andway iredfay. Iway anksay otay ethay oundgray, andway ymay 
injurerway, ithway increasedway iftnesssway, escapedway intoway ethay oodway. 

"Isthay asway enthay ethay ewardray ofway ymay enevolencebay! Iway adhay avedsay away umanhay eingbay 
omfray estructionday, andway asway away ecompenseray Iway ownay ithedwray underway ethay iserablemay 
ainpay ofway away oundway ichwhay atteredshay ethay eshflay andway onebay. Ethay eelingsfay ofway 
indnesskay andway entlenessgay ichwhay Iway adhay entertainedway utbay away ewfay omentsmay 
eforebay avegay aceplay otay ellishhay ageray andway ashinggnay ofway eethtay. Inflamedway ybay 
ainpay, Iway owedvay eternalway atredhay andway engeancevay otay allway ankindmay. Utbay ethay 
agonyway ofway ymay oundway overcameway emay; ymay ulsespay ausedpay, andway Iway aintedfay. 

"Orfay omesay eeksway Iway edlay away iserablemay ifelay inway ethay oodsway, endeavouringway otay 
urecay ethay oundway ichwhay Iway adhay eceivedray. Ethay allbay adhay enteredway ymay ouldershay, 
andway Iway ewknay otnay etherwhay itway adhay emainedray erethay orway assedpay oughthray; atway anyway 
ateray Iway adhay onay eansmay ofway extractingway itway. Ymay ufferingssay ereway augmentedway 
alsoway ybay ethay oppressiveway ensesay ofway ethay injusticeway andway ingratitudeway ofway eirthay 
inflictionway. Ymay ailyday owsvay oseray orfay evengeray--a eepday andway eadlyday evengeray, 
uchsay asway ouldway aloneway ompensatecay orfay ethay outragesway andway anguishway Iway adhay 
enduredway. 

"Afterway omesay eeksway ymay oundway ealedhay, andway Iway ontinuedcay ymay ourneyjay. Ethay 
abourslay Iway enduredway ereway onay ongerlay otay ebay alleviatedway ybay ethay ightbray unsay orway 
entlegay eezesbray ofway ingspray; allway oyjay asway utbay away ockerymay ichwhay insultedway ymay 
esolateday atestay andway ademay emay eelfay oremay ainfullypay atthay Iway asway otnay ademay orfay 
ethay enjoymentway ofway easureplay. 

"Utbay ymay oilstay ownay ewdray earnay away oseclay, andway inway otway onthsmay omfray isthay imetay Iway 
eachedray ethay environsway ofway Enevagay. 

"Itway asway eveningway enwhay Iway arrivedway, andway Iway etiredray otay away idinghay-place amongway 
ethay ieldsfay atthay urroundsay itway otay editatemay inway atwhay annermay Iway ouldshay applyway 
otay youway. Iway asway oppressedway ybay atiguefay andway ungerhay andway arfay ootay unhappyway otay 
enjoyway ethay entlegay eezesbray ofway eveningway orway ethay ospectpray ofway ethay unsay ettingsay 
ehindbay ethay upendousstay ountainsmay ofway Urajay. 

"Atway isthay imetay away ightslay eepslay elievedray emay omfray ethay ainpay ofway eflectionray, 
ichwhay asway isturbedday ybay ethay approachway ofway away eautifulbay ildchay, owhay amecay 
unningray intoway ethay ecessray Iway adhay osenchay, ithway allway ethay ortivenessspay ofway 
infancyway. Uddenlysay, asway Iway azedgay onway imhay, anway ideaway eizedsay emay atthay isthay 
ittlelay eaturecray asway unprejudicedway andway adhay ivedlay ootay ortshay away imetay otay avehay 
imbibedway away orrorhay ofway eformityday. Ifway, ereforethay, Iway ouldcay eizesay imhay andway 
educateway imhay asway ymay ompanioncay andway iendfray, Iway ouldshay otnay ebay osay esolateday inway 
isthay eopledpay earthway. 

"Urgedway ybay isthay impulseway, Iway eizedsay onway ethay oybay asway ehay assedpay andway ewdray imhay 
owardstay emay. Asway oonsay asway ehay eheldbay ymay ormfay, ehay acedplay ishay andshay eforebay 
ishay eyesway andway utteredway away illshray eamscray; Iway ewdray ishay andhay orciblyfay omfray ishay 
acefay andway aidsay, 'Ildchay, atwhay isway ethay eaningmay ofway isthay? Iway oday otnay intendway otay 
urthay youway; istenlay otay emay.' 

"Ehay uggledstray iolentlyvay. 'Etlay emay ogay,' ehay iedcray; 'onstermay! Uglyway 
etchwray! Youway ishway otay eatway emay andway eartay emay otay iecespay. Youway areway anway ogreway. 
Etlay emay ogay, orway Iway illway elltay ymay apapay.' 

"'Oybay, youway illway evernay eesay yourway atherfay againway; youway ustmay omecay ithway emay.' 

"'Ideoushay onstermay! Etlay emay ogay. Ymay apapay isway away yndicsay--he isway Mway. 
Ankensteinfray--he illway unishpay youway. Youway areday otnay eepkay emay.' 

"'Ankensteinfray! youway elongbay enthay otay ymay enemyway--to imhay owardstay omwhay Iway avehay 
ornsway eternalway evengeray; youway allshay ebay ymay irstfay ictimvay.' 

"Ethay ildchay illstay uggledstray andway oadedlay emay ithway epithetsway ichwhay arriedcay 
espairday otay ymay earthay; Iway aspedgray ishay oatthray otay ilencesay imhay, andway inway away 
omentmay ehay aylay eadday atway ymay eetfay. 

"Iway azedgay onway ymay ictimvay, andway ymay earthay elledsway ithway exultationway andway ellishhay 
iumphtray; appingclay ymay andshay, Iway exclaimedway, 'Iway ootay ancay eatecray esolationday; 
ymay enemyway isway otnay invulnerableway; isthay eathday illway arrycay espairday otay imhay, andway 
away ousandthay otherway iseriesmay allshay ormenttay andway estroyday imhay.' 

"Asway Iway ixedfay ymay eyesway onway ethay ildchay, Iway awsay omethingsay itteringglay onway ishay 
eastbray. Iway ooktay itway; itway asway away ortraitpay ofway away ostmay ovelylay omanway. Inway itespay 
ofway ymay alignitymay, itway oftenedsay andway attractedway emay. Orfay away ewfay omentsmay Iway 
azedgay ithway elightday onway erhay arkday eyesway, ingedfray ybay eepday asheslay, andway erhay 
ovelylay ipslay; utbay esentlypray ymay ageray eturnedray; Iway ememberedray atthay Iway asway 
oreverfay eprivedday ofway ethay elightsday atthay uchsay eautifulbay eaturescray ouldcay 
estowbay andway atthay eshay osewhay esemblanceray Iway ontemplatedcay ouldway, inway 
egardingray emay, avehay angedchay atthay airway ofway ivineday enignitybay otay oneway 
expressiveway ofway isgustday andway affrightway. 

"Ancay youway onderway atthay uchsay oughtsthay ansportedtray emay ithway ageray? Iway onlyway 
onderway atthay atway atthay omentmay, insteadway ofway entingvay ymay ensationssay inway 
exclamationsway andway agonyway, Iway idday otnay ushray amongway ankindmay andway erishpay inway ethay 
attemptway otay estroyday emthay. 

"Ilewhay Iway asway overcomeway ybay esethay eelingsfay, Iway eftlay ethay otspay erewhay Iway adhay 
ommittedcay ethay urdermay, andway eekingsay away oremay ecludedsay idinghay-place, Iway 
enteredway away arnbay ichwhay adhay appearedway otay emay otay ebay emptyway. Away omanway asway 
eepingslay onway omesay awstray; eshay asway youngway, otnay indeedway osay eautifulbay asway erhay 
osewhay ortraitpay Iway eldhay, utbay ofway anway agreeableway aspectway andway oomingblay inway ethay 
ovelinesslay ofway youthway andway ealthhay. Erehay, Iway oughtthay, isway oneway ofway osethay osewhay 
oyjay-imparting ilessmay areway estowedbay onway allway utbay emay. Andway enthay Iway entbay overway 
erhay andway isperedwhay, 'Awakeway, airestfay, ythay overlay isway earnay--he owhay ouldway 
ivegay ishay ifelay utbay otay obtainway oneway ooklay ofway affectionway omfray inethay eyesway; ymay 
elovedbay, awakeway!' 

"Ethay eeperslay irredstay; away illthray ofway errortay anray oughthray emay. Ouldshay eshay 
indeedway awakeway, andway eesay emay, andway ursecay emay, andway enounceday ethay urderermay? Usthay 
ouldway eshay assuredlyway actway ifway erhay arkenedday eyesway openedway andway eshay eheldbay emay. 
Ethay oughtthay asway adnessmay; itway irredstay ethay iendfay ithinway emay--not Iway, utbay 
eshay, allshay uffersay; ethay urdermay Iway avehay ommittedcay ecausebay Iway amway oreverfay 
obbedray ofway allway atthay eshay ouldcay ivegay emay, eshay allshay atoneway. Ethay imecray adhay 
itsway ourcesay inway erhay; ebay ershay ethay unishmentpay! Anksthay otay ethay essonslay ofway 
Elixfay andway ethay anguinarysay awslay ofway anmay, Iway adhay earnedlay ownay otay orkway 
ischiefmay. Iway entbay overway erhay andway acedplay ethay ortraitpay ecurelysay inway oneway ofway 
ethay oldsfay ofway erhay essdray. Eshay ovedmay againway, andway Iway edflay. 

"Orfay omesay aysday Iway auntedhay ethay otspay erewhay esethay enesscay adhay akentay aceplay, 
ometimessay ishingway otay eesay youway, ometimessay esolvedray otay uitqay ethay orldway andway 
itsway iseriesmay oreverfay. Atway engthlay Iway anderedway owardstay esethay ountainsmay, 
andway avehay angedray oughthray eirthay immenseway ecessesray, onsumedcay ybay away urningbay 
assionpay ichwhay youway aloneway ancay atifygray. Eway aymay otnay artpay untilway youway avehay 
omisedpray otay omplycay ithway ymay equisitionray. Iway amway aloneway andway iserablemay; anmay 
illway otnay associateway ithway emay; utbay oneway asway eformedday andway orriblehay asway yselfmay 
ouldway otnay enyday erselfhay otay emay. Ymay ompanioncay ustmay ebay ofway ethay amesay eciesspay 
andway avehay ethay amesay efectsday. Isthay eingbay youway ustmay eatecray." 



Apterchay 17 

Ethay eingbay inishedfay eakingspay andway ixedfay ishay ookslay uponway emay inway ethay 
expectationway ofway away eplyray. Utbay Iway asway ewilderedbay, erplexedpay, andway unableway otay 
arrangeway ymay ideasway ufficientlysay otay understandway ethay ullfay extentway ofway ishay 
opositionpray. Ehay ontinuedcay, 

"Youway ustmay eatecray away emalefay orfay emay ithway omwhay Iway ancay ivelay inway ethay 
interchangeway ofway osethay ympathiessay ecessarynay orfay ymay eingbay. Isthay youway aloneway 
ancay oday, andway Iway emandday itway ofway youway asway away ightray ichwhay youway ustmay otnay efuseray otay 
oncedecay." 

Ethay atterlay artpay ofway ishay aletay adhay indledkay anewway inway emay ethay angerway atthay adhay 
iedday awayway ilewhay ehay arratednay ishay eacefulpay ifelay amongway ethay ottagerscay, andway 
asway ehay aidsay isthay Iway ouldcay onay ongerlay uppresssay ethay ageray atthay urnedbay ithinway 
emay. 

"Iway oday efuseray itway," Iway epliedray; "andway onay orturetay allshay everway extortway away 
onsentcay omfray emay. Youway aymay enderray emay ethay ostmay iserablemay ofway enmay, utbay youway 
allshay evernay akemay emay asebay inway ymay ownway eyesway. Allshay Iway eatecray anotherway ikelay 
yourselfway, osewhay ointjay ickednessway ightmay esolateday ethay orldway. Egonebay! Iway 
avehay answeredway youway; youway aymay orturetay emay, utbay Iway illway evernay onsentcay." 

"Youway areway inway ethay ongwray," epliedray ethay iendfay; "andway insteadway ofway eateningthray, 
Iway amway ontentcay otay easonray ithway youway. Iway amway aliciousmay ecausebay Iway amway 
iserablemay. Amway Iway otnay unnedshay andway atedhay ybay allway ankindmay? Youway, ymay 
eatorcray, ouldway eartay emay otay iecespay andway iumphtray; ememberray atthay, andway elltay 
emay ywhay Iway ouldshay itypay anmay oremay anthay ehay itiespay emay? Youway ouldway otnay allcay itway 
urdermay ifway youway ouldcay ecipitatepray emay intoway oneway ofway osethay iceway-rifts andway 
estroyday ymay amefray, ethay orkway ofway yourway ownway andshay. Allshay Iway espectray anmay enwhay 
ehay ondemnscay emay? Etlay imhay ivelay ithway emay inway ethay interchangeway ofway indnesskay, 
andway insteadway ofway injuryway Iway ouldway estowbay everyway enefitbay uponway imhay ithway earstay 
ofway atitudegray atway ishay acceptanceway. Utbay atthay annotcay ebay; ethay umanhay ensessay 
areway insurmountableway arriersbay otay ourway unionway. Yetway inemay allshay otnay ebay ethay 
ubmissionsay ofway abjectway averyslay. Iway illway evengeray ymay injuriesway; ifway Iway annotcay 
inspireway ovelay, Iway illway ausecay earfay, andway ieflychay owardstay youway ymay archway-enemy, 
ecausebay ymay eatorcray, oday Iway earsway inextinguishableway atredhay. Avehay away arecay; Iway 
illway orkway atway yourway estructionday, ornay inishfay untilway Iway esolateday yourway earthay, 
osay atthay youway allshay ursecay ethay ourhay ofway yourway irthbay." 

Away iendishfay ageray animatedway imhay asway ehay aidsay isthay; ishay acefay asway inkledwray 
intoway ontortionscay ootay orriblehay orfay umanhay eyesway otay eholdbay; utbay esentlypray 
ehay almedcay imselfhay andway oceededpray-- 

"Iway intendedway otay easonray. Isthay assionpay isway etrimentalday otay emay, orfay youway oday 
otnay eflectray atthay YOUWAY areway ethay ausecay ofway itsway excessway. Ifway anyway eingbay eltfay 
emotionsway ofway enevolencebay owardstay emay, Iway ouldshay eturnray emthay away undredhay andway 
away undredfoldhay; orfay atthay oneway eaturecray's akesay Iway ouldway akemay eacepay ithway ethay 
olewhay indkay! Utbay Iway ownay indulgeway inway eamsdray ofway issblay atthay annotcay ebay 
ealizedray. Atwhay Iway askway ofway youway isway easonableray andway oderatemay; Iway emandday away 
eaturecray ofway anotherway exsay, utbay asway ideoushay asway yselfmay; ethay atificationgray isway 
allsmay, utbay itway isway allway atthay Iway ancay eceiveray, andway itway allshay ontentcay emay. Itway 
isway uetray, eway allshay ebay onstersmay, utcay offway omfray allway ethay orldway; utbay onway atthay 
accountway eway allshay ebay oremay attachedway otay oneway anotherway. Ourway iveslay illway otnay 
ebay appyhay, utbay eythay illway ebay armlesshay andway eefray omfray ethay iserymay Iway ownay 
eelfay. Ohway! Ymay eatorcray, akemay emay appyhay; etlay emay eelfay atitudegray owardstay 
youway orfay oneway enefitbay! Etlay emay eesay atthay Iway exciteway ethay ympathysay ofway omesay 
existingway ingthay; oday otnay enyday emay ymay equestray!" 

Iway asway ovedmay. Iway udderedshay enwhay Iway oughtthay ofway ethay ossiblepay onsequencescay 
ofway ymay onsentcay, utbay Iway eltfay atthay erethay asway omesay usticejay inway ishay argumentway. 
Ishay aletay andway ethay eelingsfay ehay ownay expressedway ovedpray imhay otay ebay away eaturecray 
ofway inefay ensationssay, andway idday Iway otnay asway ishay akermay oweway imhay allway ethay ortionpay 
ofway appinesshay atthay itway asway inway ymay owerpay otay estowbay? Ehay awsay ymay angechay ofway 
eelingfay andway ontinuedcay, 

"Ifway youway onsentcay, eithernay youway ornay anyway otherway umanhay eingbay allshay everway eesay 
usway againway; Iway illway ogay otay ethay astvay ildsway ofway Outhsay Americaway. Ymay oodfay isway otnay 
atthay ofway anmay; Iway oday otnay estroyday ethay amblay andway ethay idkay otay utglay ymay appetiteway; 
acornsway andway erriesbay affordway emay ufficientsay ourishmentnay. Ymay ompanioncay illway 
ebay ofway ethay amesay aturenay asway yselfmay andway illway ebay ontentcay ithway ethay amesay arefay. 
Eway allshay akemay ourway edbay ofway ieddray eaveslay; ethay unsay illway ineshay onway usway asway onway 
anmay andway illway ipenray ourway oodfay. Ethay icturepay Iway esentpray otay youway isway eacefulpay 
andway umanhay, andway youway ustmay eelfay atthay youway ouldcay enyday itway onlyway inway ethay 
antonnessway ofway owerpay andway ueltycray. Itilesspay asway youway avehay eenbay owardstay emay, 
Iway ownay eesay ompassioncay inway yourway eyesway; etlay emay eizesay ethay avourablefay omentmay 
andway ersuadepay youway otay omisepray atwhay Iway osay ardentlyway esireday." 

"Youway oposepray," epliedray Iway, "otay yflay omfray ethay abitationshay ofway anmay, otay elldway 
inway osethay ildsway erewhay ethay eastsbay ofway ethay ieldfay illway ebay yourway onlyway 
ompanionscay. Owhay ancay youway, owhay onglay orfay ethay ovelay andway ympathysay ofway anmay, 
erseverepay inway isthay exileway? Youway illway eturnray andway againway eeksay eirthay 
indnesskay, andway youway illway eetmay ithway eirthay etestationday; yourway evilway assionspay 
illway ebay enewedray, andway youway illway enthay avehay away ompanioncay otay aidway youway inway ethay 
asktay ofway estructionday. Isthay aymay otnay ebay; easecay otay argueway ethay ointpay, orfay Iway 
annotcay onsentcay." 

"Owhay inconstantway areway yourway eelingsfay! Utbay away omentmay agoway youway ereway ovedmay ybay 
ymay epresentationsray, andway ywhay oday youway againway ardenhay yourselfway otay ymay 
omplaintscay? Iway earsway otay youway, ybay ethay earthway ichwhay Iway inhabitway, andway ybay youway 
atthay ademay emay, atthay ithway ethay ompanioncay youway estowbay Iway illway uitqay ethay 
eighbourhoodnay ofway anmay andway elldway, asway itway aymay ancechay, inway ethay ostmay avagesay ofway 
acesplay. Ymay evilway assionspay illway avehay edflay, orfay Iway allshay eetmay ithway 
ympathysay! Ymay ifelay illway owflay uietlyqay awayway, andway inway ymay yingday omentsmay Iway 
allshay otnay ursecay ymay akermay." 

Ishay ordsway adhay away angestray effectway uponway emay. Iway ompassionatedcay imhay andway 
ometimessay eltfay away ishway otay onsolecay imhay, utbay enwhay Iway ookedlay uponway imhay, enwhay 
Iway awsay ethay ilthyfay assmay atthay ovedmay andway alkedtay, ymay earthay ickenedsay andway ymay 
eelingsfay ereway alteredway otay osethay ofway orrorhay andway atredhay. Iway iedtray otay iflestay 
esethay ensationssay; Iway oughtthay atthay asway Iway ouldcay otnay ympathizesay ithway imhay, Iway 
adhay onay ightray otay ithholdway omfray imhay ethay allsmay ortionpay ofway appinesshay ichwhay 
asway yetway inway ymay owerpay otay estowbay. 

"Youway earsway," Iway aidsay, "otay ebay armlesshay; utbay avehay youway otnay alreadyway ownshay away 
egreeday ofway alicemay atthay ouldshay easonablyray akemay emay istrustday youway? Aymay otnay 
evenway isthay ebay away eintfay atthay illway increaseway yourway iumphtray ybay affordingway away 
iderway opescay orfay yourway evengeray?" 

"Owhay isway isthay? Iway ustmay otnay ebay ifledtray ithway, andway Iway emandday anway answerway. Ifway 
Iway avehay onay iestay andway onay affectionsway, atredhay andway icevay ustmay ebay ymay ortionpay; 
ethay ovelay ofway anotherway illway estroyday ethay ausecay ofway ymay imescray, andway Iway allshay 
ecomebay away ingthay ofway osewhay existenceway everyoneway illway ebay ignorantway. Ymay icesvay 
areway ethay ildrenchay ofway away orcedfay olitudesay atthay Iway abhorway, andway ymay irtuesvay illway 
ecessarilynay ariseway enwhay Iway ivelay inway ommunioncay ithway anway equalway. Iway allshay eelfay 
ethay affectionsway ofway away ensitivesay eingbay andway ecomebay inkedlay otay ethay ainchay ofway 
existenceway andway eventsway omfray ichwhay Iway amway ownay excludedway." 

Iway ausedpay omesay imetay otay eflectray onway allway ehay adhay elatedray andway ethay ariousvay 
argumentsway ichwhay ehay adhay employedway. Iway oughtthay ofway ethay omisepray ofway irtuesvay 
ichwhay ehay adhay isplayedday onway ethay openingway ofway ishay existenceway andway ethay 
ubsequentsay ightblay ofway allway indlykay eelingfay ybay ethay oathinglay andway ornscay ichwhay 
ishay otectorspray adhay anifestedmay owardstay imhay. Ishay owerpay andway eatsthray ereway 
otnay omittedway inway ymay alculationscay; away eaturecray owhay ouldcay existway inway ethay iceway 
avescay ofway ethay aciersglay andway idehay imselfhay omfray ursuitpay amongway ethay idgesray ofway 
inaccessibleway ecipicespray asway away eingbay ossessingpay acultiesfay itway ouldway ebay 
ainvay otay opecay ithway. Afterway away onglay ausepay ofway eflectionray Iway oncludedcay atthay 
ethay usticejay ueday othbay otay imhay andway ymay ellowfay eaturescray emandedday ofway emay atthay 
Iway ouldshay omplycay ithway ishay equestray. Urningtay otay imhay, ereforethay, Iway aidsay, 

"Iway onsentcay otay yourway emandday, onway yourway olemnsay oathway otay uitqay Europeway oreverfay, 
andway everyway otherway aceplay inway ethay eighbourhoodnay ofway anmay, asway oonsay asway Iway allshay 
eliverday intoway yourway andshay away emalefay owhay illway accompanyway youway inway yourway exileway." 

"Iway earsway," ehay iedcray, "ybay ethay unsay, andway ybay ethay ueblay yskay ofway eavenhay, andway ybay 
ethay irefay ofway ovelay atthay urnsbay ymay earthay, atthay ifway youway antgray ymay ayerpray, 
ilewhay eythay existway youway allshay evernay eholdbay emay againway. Epartday otay yourway omehay 
andway ommencecay yourway abourslay; Iway allshay atchway eirthay ogresspray ithway 
unutterableway anxietyway; andway earfay otnay utbay atthay enwhay youway areway eadyray Iway allshay 
appearway." 

Ayingsay isthay, ehay uddenlysay uittedqay emay, earfulfay, erhapspay, ofway anyway angechay inway 
ymay entimentssay. Iway awsay imhay escendday ethay ountainmay ithway eatergray eedspay anthay 
ethay ightflay ofway anway eagleway, andway uicklyqay ostlay amongway ethay undulationsway ofway ethay 
easay ofway iceway. 

Ishay aletay adhay occupiedway ethay olewhay ayday, andway ethay unsay asway uponway ethay ergevay ofway 
ethay orizonhay enwhay ehay epartedday. Iway ewknay atthay Iway oughtway otay astenhay ymay escentday 
owardstay ethay alleyvay, asway Iway ouldshay oonsay ebay encompassedway inway arknessday; utbay ymay 
earthay asway eavyhay, andway ymay epsstay owslay. Ethay abourlay ofway indingway amongway ethay 
ittlelay athspay ofway ethay ountainmay andway ixingfay ymay eetfay irmlyfay asway Iway advancedway 
erplexedpay emay, occupiedway asway Iway asway ybay ethay emotionsway ichwhay ethay occurrencesway 
ofway ethay ayday adhay oducedpray. Ightnay asway arfay advancedway enwhay Iway amecay otay ethay 
alfwayhay estingray-place andway eatedsay yselfmay esidebay ethay ountainfay. Ethay arsstay 
oneshay atway intervalsway asway ethay oudsclay assedpay omfray overway emthay; ethay arkday inespay 
oseray eforebay emay, andway everyway erehay andway erethay away okenbray eetray aylay onway ethay 
oundgray; itway asway away enescay ofway onderfulway olemnitysay andway irredstay angestray 
oughtsthay ithinway emay. Iway eptway itterlybay, andway aspingclay ymay andshay inway agonyway, Iway 
exclaimedway, "Ohway! Arsstay andway oudsclay andway indsway, yeway areway allway aboutway otay ockmay 
emay; ifway yeway eallyray itypay emay, ushcray ensationsay andway emorymay; etlay emay ecomebay asway 
oughtnay; utbay ifway otnay, epartday, epartday, andway eavelay emay inway arknessday." 

Esethay ereway ildway andway iserablemay oughtsthay, utbay Iway annotcay escribeday otay youway 
owhay ethay eternalway inklingtway ofway ethay arsstay eighedway uponway emay andway owhay Iway 
istenedlay otay everyway astblay ofway indway asway ifway itway ereway away ullday uglyway irocsay onway itsway 
ayway otay onsumecay emay. 

Orningmay awnedday eforebay Iway arrivedway atway ethay illagevay ofway Amounixchay; Iway ooktay onay 
estray, utbay eturnedray immediatelyway otay Enevagay. Evenway inway ymay ownway earthay Iway ouldcay 
ivegay onay expressionway otay ymay ensationssay--they eighedway onway emay ithway away 
ountainmay's eightway andway eirthay excessway estroyedday ymay agonyway eneathbay emthay. 
Usthay Iway eturnedray omehay, andway enteringway ethay ousehay, esentedpray yselfmay otay ethay 
amilyfay. Ymay aggardhay andway ildway appearanceway awokeway intenseway alarmway, utbay Iway 
answeredway onay uestionqay, arcelyscay idday Iway eakspay. Iway eltfay asway ifway Iway ereway acedplay 
underway away anbay--as ifway Iway adhay onay ightray otay aimclay eirthay ympathiessay--as ifway 
evernay oremay ightmay Iway enjoyway ompanionshipcay ithway emthay. Yetway evenway usthay Iway 
ovedlay emthay otay adorationway; andway otay avesay emthay, Iway esolvedray otay edicateday 
yselfmay otay ymay ostmay abhorredway asktay. Ethay ospectpray ofway uchsay anway occupationway 
ademay everyway otherway ircumstancecay ofway existenceway asspay eforebay emay ikelay away eamdray, 
andway atthay oughtthay onlyway adhay otay emay ethay ealityray ofway ifelay. 



Apterchay 18 

Ayday afterway ayday, eekway afterway eekway, assedpay awayway onway ymay eturnray otay Enevagay; andway 
Iway ouldcay otnay ollectcay ethay ouragecay otay ecommenceray ymay orkway. Iway earedfay ethay 
engeancevay ofway ethay isappointedday iendfay, yetway Iway asway unableway otay overcomeway ymay 
epugnanceray otay ethay asktay ichwhay asway enjoinedway emay. Iway oundfay atthay Iway ouldcay otnay 
omposecay away emalefay ithoutway againway evotingday everalsay onthsmay otay ofoundpray 
udystay andway aboriouslay isquisitionday. Iway adhay eardhay ofway omesay iscoveriesday 
avinghay eenbay ademay ybay anway Englishway ilosopherphay, ethay owledgeknay ofway ichwhay asway 
aterialmay otay ymay uccesssay, andway Iway ometimessay oughtthay ofway obtainingway ymay 
atherfay's onsentcay otay isitvay Englandway orfay isthay urposepay; utbay Iway ungclay otay 
everyway etencepray ofway elayday andway ankshray omfray akingtay ethay irstfay epstay inway anway 
undertakingway osewhay immediateway ecessitynay eganbay otay appearway esslay absoluteway otay 
emay. Away angechay indeedway adhay akentay aceplay inway emay; ymay ealthhay, ichwhay adhay 
ithertohay eclinedday, asway ownay uchmay estoredray; andway ymay iritsspay, enwhay 
uncheckedway ybay ethay emorymay ofway ymay unhappyway omisepray, oseray oportionablypray. Ymay 
atherfay awsay isthay angechay ithway easureplay, andway ehay urnedtay ishay oughtsthay 
owardstay ethay estbay ethodmay ofway eradicatingway ethay emainsray ofway ymay elancholymay, 
ichwhay everyway ownay andway enthay ouldway eturnray ybay itsfay, andway ithway away evouringday 
acknessblay overcastway ethay approachingway unshinesay. Atway esethay omentsmay Iway ooktay 
efugeray inway ethay ostmay erfectpay olitudesay. Iway assedpay olewhay aysday onway ethay akelay 
aloneway inway away ittlelay oatbay, atchingway ethay oudsclay andway isteninglay otay ethay 
ipplingray ofway ethay avesway, ilentsay andway istlesslay. Utbay ethay eshfray airway andway 
ightbray unsay eldomsay ailedfay otay estoreray emay otay omesay egreeday ofway omposurecay, andway 
onway ymay eturnray Iway etmay ethay alutationssay ofway ymay iendsfray ithway away eadierray ilesmay 
andway away oremay eerfulchay earthay. 

Itway asway afterway ymay eturnray omfray oneway ofway esethay amblesray atthay ymay atherfay, 
allingcay emay asideway, usthay addressedway emay, 

"Iway amway appyhay otay emarkray, ymay earday onsay, atthay youway avehay esumedray yourway ormerfay 
easuresplay andway eemsay otay ebay eturningray otay yourselfway. Andway yetway youway areway illstay 
unhappyway andway illstay avoidway ourway ocietysay. Orfay omesay imetay Iway asway ostlay inway 
onjecturecay asway otay ethay ausecay ofway isthay, utbay yesterdayway anway ideaway uckstray emay, 
andway ifway itway isway ellway oundedfay, Iway onjurecay youway otay avowway itway. Eserveray onway uchsay away 
ointpay ouldway ebay otnay onlyway uselessway, utbay awdray ownday ebletray iserymay onway usway allway." 

Iway embledtray iolentlyvay atway ishay exordiumway, andway ymay atherfay ontinuedcay--"I 
onfesscay, ymay onsay, atthay Iway avehay alwaysway ookedlay orwardfay otay yourway arriagemay 
ithway ourway earday Elizabethway asway ethay ietay ofway ourway omesticday omfortcay andway ethay aystay 
ofway ymay ecliningday yearsway. Youway ereway attachedway otay eachway otherway omfray yourway 
earliestway infancyway; youway udiedstay ogethertay, andway appearedway, inway ispositionsday 
andway astestay, entirelyway uitedsay otay oneway anotherway. Utbay osay indblay isway ethay 
experienceway ofway anmay atthay atwhay Iway onceivedcay otay ebay ethay estbay assistantsway otay ymay 
anplay aymay avehay entirelyway estroyedday itway. Youway, erhapspay, egardray erhay asway yourway 
istersay, ithoutway anyway ishway atthay eshay ightmay ecomebay yourway ifeway. Aynay, youway aymay 
avehay etmay ithway anotherway omwhay youway aymay ovelay; andway onsideringcay yourselfway asway 
oundbay inway onourhay otay Elizabethway, isthay ugglestray aymay occasionway ethay oignantpay 
iserymay ichwhay youway appearway otay eelfay." 

"Ymay earday atherfay, eassureray yourselfway. Iway ovelay ymay ousincay enderlytay andway 
incerelysay. Iway evernay awsay anyway omanway owhay excitedway, asway Elizabethway oesday, ymay 
armestway admirationway andway affectionway. Ymay uturefay opeshay andway ospectspray areway 
entirelyway oundbay upway inway ethay expectationway ofway ourway unionway." 

"Ethay expressionway ofway yourway entimentssay ofway isthay ubjectsay, ymay earday Ictorvay, 
ivesgay emay oremay easureplay anthay Iway avehay orfay omesay imetay experiencedway. Ifway youway 
eelfay usthay, eway allshay assuredlyway ebay appyhay, oweverhay esentpray eventsway aymay astcay 
away oomglay overway usway. Utbay itway isway isthay oomglay ichwhay appearsway otay avehay akentay osay 
ongstray away oldhay ofway yourway indmay atthay Iway ishway otay issipateday. Elltay emay, 
ereforethay, etherwhay youway objectway otay anway immediateway olemnizationsay ofway ethay 
arriagemay. Eway avehay eenbay unfortunateway, andway ecentray eventsway avehay awndray usway 
omfray atthay everydayway anquillitytray efittingbay ymay yearsway andway infirmitiesway. Youway 
areway youngerway; yetway Iway oday otnay upposesay, ossessedpay asway youway areway ofway away ompetentcay 
ortunefay, atthay anway earlyway arriagemay ouldway atway allway interfereway ithway anyway uturefay 
ansplay ofway onourhay andway utilityway atthay youway aymay avehay ormedfay. Oday otnay upposesay, 
oweverhay, atthay Iway ishway otay ictateday appinesshay otay youway orway atthay away elayday onway 
yourway artpay ouldway ausecay emay anyway erioussay uneasinessway. Interpretway ymay ordsway 
ithway andourcay andway answerway emay, Iway onjurecay youway, ithway onfidencecay andway 
inceritysay." 

Iway istenedlay otay ymay atherfay inway ilencesay andway emainedray orfay omesay imetay incapableway 
ofway offeringway anyway eplyray. Iway evolvedray apidlyray inway ymay indmay away ultitudemay ofway 
oughtsthay andway endeavouredway otay arriveway atway omesay onclusioncay. Alasway! Otay emay 
ethay ideaway ofway anway immediateway unionway ithway ymay Elizabethway asway oneway ofway orrorhay andway 
ismayday. Iway asway oundbay ybay away olemnsay omisepray ichwhay Iway adhay otnay yetway ulfilledfay 
andway aredday otnay eakbray, orway ifway Iway idday, atwhay anifoldmay iseriesmay ightmay otnay 
impendway overway emay andway ymay evotedday amilyfay! Ouldcay Iway enterway intoway away estivalfay 
ithway isthay eadlyday eightway yetway anginghay oundray ymay ecknay andway owingbay emay otay ethay 
oundgray? Iway ustmay erformpay ymay engagementway andway etlay ethay onstermay epartday ithway 
ishay atemay eforebay Iway allowedway yselfmay otay enjoyway ethay elightday ofway away unionway omfray 
ichwhay Iway expectedway eacepay. 

Iway ememberedray alsoway ethay ecessitynay imposedway uponway emay ofway eitherway ourneyingjay otay 
Englandway orway enteringway intoway away onglay orrespondencecay ithway osethay ilosophersphay 
ofway atthay ountrycay osewhay owledgeknay andway iscoveriesday ereway ofway indispensableway 
useway otay emay inway ymay esentpray undertakingway. Ethay atterlay ethodmay ofway obtainingway 
ethay esiredday intelligenceway asway ilatoryday andway unsatisfactoryway; esidesbay, Iway 
adhay anway insurmountableway aversionway otay ethay ideaway ofway engagingway yselfmay inway ymay 
oathsomelay asktay inway ymay atherfay's ousehay ilewhay inway abitshay ofway amiliarfay 
intercourseway ithway osethay Iway ovedlay. Iway ewknay atthay away ousandthay earfulfay 
accidentsway ightmay occurway, ethay ightestslay ofway ichwhay ouldway iscloseday away aletay otay 
illthray allway onnectedcay ithway emay ithway orrorhay. Iway asway awareway alsoway atthay Iway 
ouldshay oftenway oselay allway elfsay-command, allway apacitycay ofway idinghay ethay 
arrowinghay ensationssay atthay ouldway ossesspay emay uringday ethay ogresspray ofway ymay 
unearthlyway occupationway. Iway ustmay absentway yselfmay omfray allway Iway ovedlay ilewhay usthay 
employedway. Onceway ommencedcay, itway ouldway uicklyqay ebay achievedway, andway Iway ightmay ebay 
estoredray otay ymay amilyfay inway eacepay andway appinesshay. Ymay omisepray ulfilledfay, 
ethay onstermay ouldway epartday oreverfay. Orway (osay ymay ondfay ancyfay imagedway) omesay 
accidentway ightmay eanwhilemay occurway otay estroyday imhay andway utpay anway endway otay ymay 
averyslay oreverfay. 

Esethay eelingsfay ictatedday ymay answerway otay ymay atherfay. Iway expressedway away ishway otay 
isitvay Englandway, utbay oncealingcay ethay uetray easonsray ofway isthay equestray, Iway 
othedclay ymay esiresday underway away uisegay ichwhay excitedway onay uspicionsay, ilewhay Iway 
urgedway ymay esireday ithway anway earnestnessway atthay easilyway inducedway ymay atherfay otay 
omplycay. Afterway osay onglay away eriodpay ofway anway absorbingway elancholymay atthay 
esembledray adnessmay inway itsway intensityway andway effectsway, ehay asway adglay otay indfay 
atthay Iway asway apablecay ofway akingtay easureplay inway ethay ideaway ofway uchsay away ourneyjay, 
andway ehay opedhay atthay angechay ofway enescay andway ariedvay amusementway ouldway, eforebay ymay 
eturnray, avehay estoredray emay entirelyway otay yselfmay. 

Ethay urationday ofway ymay absenceway asway eftlay otay ymay ownway oicechay; away ewfay onthsmay, orway 
atway ostmay away yearway, asway ethay eriodpay ontemplatedcay. Oneway aternalpay indkay 
ecautionpray ehay adhay akentay otay ensureway ymay avinghay away ompanioncay. Ithoutway 
eviouslypray ommunicatingcay ithway emay, ehay adhay, inway oncertcay ithway Elizabethway, 
arrangedway atthay Ervalclay ouldshay oinjay emay atway Asbourgstray. Isthay interferedway 
ithway ethay olitudesay Iway ovetedcay orfay ethay osecutionpray ofway ymay asktay; yetway atway ethay 
ommencementcay ofway ymay ourneyjay ethay esencepray ofway ymay iendfray ouldcay inway onay ayway ebay 
anway impedimentway, andway ulytray Iway ejoicedray atthay usthay Iway ouldshay ebay avedsay anymay 
ourshay ofway onelylay, addeningmay eflectionray. Aynay, Enryhay ightmay andstay etweenbay 
emay andway ethay intrusionway ofway ymay oefay. Ifway Iway ereway aloneway, ouldway ehay otnay atway imestay 
orcefay ishay abhorredway esencepray onway emay otay emindray emay ofway ymay asktay orway otay 
ontemplatecay itsway ogresspray? 

Otay Englandway, ereforethay, Iway asway oundbay, andway itway asway understoodway atthay ymay unionway 
ithway Elizabethway ouldshay aketay aceplay immediatelyway onway ymay eturnray. Ymay atherfay's 
ageway enderedray imhay extremelyway averseway otay elayday. Orfay yselfmay, erethay asway oneway 
ewardray Iway omisedpray yselfmay omfray ymay etestedday oilstay--one onsolationcay orfay ymay 
unparalleledway ufferingssay; itway asway ethay ospectpray ofway atthay ayday enwhay, 
enfranchisedway omfray ymay iserablemay averyslay, Iway ightmay aimclay Elizabethway andway 
orgetfay ethay astpay inway ymay unionway ithway erhay. 

Iway ownay ademay arrangementsway orfay ymay ourneyjay, utbay oneway eelingfay auntedhay emay 
ichwhay illedfay emay ithway earfay andway agitationway. Uringday ymay absenceway Iway ouldshay 
eavelay ymay iendsfray unconsciousway ofway ethay existenceway ofway eirthay enemyway andway 
unprotectedway omfray ishay attacksway, exasperatedway asway ehay ightmay ebay ybay ymay 
epartureday. Utbay ehay adhay omisedpray otay ollowfay emay ereverwhay Iway ightmay ogay, andway 
ouldway ehay otnay accompanyway emay otay Englandway? Isthay imaginationway asway eadfuldray inway 
itselfway, utbay oothingsay inasmuchway asway itway upposedsay ethay afetysay ofway ymay iendsfray. 
Iway asway agonizedway ithway ethay ideaway ofway ethay ossibilitypay atthay ethay everseray ofway 
isthay ightmay appenhay. Utbay oughthray ethay olewhay eriodpay uringday ichwhay Iway asway ethay 
aveslay ofway ymay eaturecray Iway allowedway yselfmay otay ebay overnedgay ybay ethay impulsesway ofway 
ethay omentmay; andway ymay esentpray ensationssay onglystray intimatedway atthay ethay iendfay 
ouldway ollowfay emay andway exemptway ymay amilyfay omfray ethay angerday ofway ishay 
achinationsmay. 

Itway asway inway ethay atterlay endway ofway Eptembersay atthay Iway againway uittedqay ymay ativenay 
ountrycay. Ymay ourneyjay adhay eenbay ymay ownway uggestionsay, andway Elizabethway 
ereforethay acquiescedway, utbay eshay asway illedfay ithway isquietday atway ethay ideaway ofway 
ymay ufferingsay, awayway omfray erhay, ethay inroadsway ofway iserymay andway iefgray. Itway adhay 
eenbay erhay arecay ichwhay ovidedpray emay away ompanioncay inway Ervalclay--and yetway away anmay 
isway indblay otay away ousandthay inutemay ircumstancescay ichwhay allcay orthfay away omanway's 
eduloussay attentionway. Eshay ongedlay otay idbay emay astenhay ymay eturnray; away ousandthay 
onflictingcay emotionsway enderedray erhay utemay asway eshay adebay emay away earfultay, ilentsay 
arewellfay. 

Iway ewthray yselfmay intoway ethay arriagecay atthay asway otay onveycay emay awayway, ardlyhay 
owingknay itherwhay Iway asway oinggay, andway arelesscay ofway atwhay asway assingpay aroundway. 
Iway ememberedray onlyway, andway itway asway ithway away itterbay anguishway atthay Iway eflectedray onway 
itway, otay orderway atthay ymay emicalchay instrumentsway ouldshay ebay ackedpay otay ogay ithway 
emay. Illedfay ithway earydray imaginationsway, Iway assedpay oughthray anymay eautifulbay 
andway ajesticmay enesscay, utbay ymay eyesway ereway ixedfay andway unobservingway. Iway ouldcay 
onlyway inkthay ofway ethay ournebay ofway ymay avelstray andway ethay orkway ichwhay asway otay occupyway 
emay ilstwhay eythay enduredway. 

Afterway omesay aysday entspay inway istlesslay indolenceway, uringday ichwhay Iway aversedtray

Ervalclay. Ehay amecay. Alasway, owhay eatgray asway ethay ontrastcay etweenbay usway! Ehay 
asway aliveway otay everyway ewnay enescay, oyfuljay enwhay ehay awsay ethay eautiesbay ofway ethay 
ettingsay unsay, andway oremay appyhay enwhay ehay eheldbay itway iseray andway ecommenceray away ewnay

youway espondingday andway orrowfulsay!" Inway uthtray, Iway asway occupiedway ybay oomyglay 
oughtsthay andway eithernay awsay ethay escentday ofway ethay eveningway arstay ornay ethay oldengay

Eway adhay agreedway otay escendday ethay Inerhay inway away oatbay omfray Asbourgstray otay

oyagevay eway assedpay anymay illowyway islandsway andway awsay everalsay eautifulbay ownstay. 
Eway ayedstay away ayday atway Annheimmay, andway onway ethay ifthfay omfray ourway epartureday omfray

Enryhay? Ehay eltfay asway ifway ehay adhay eenbay ansportedtray otay airyfay-land andway enjoyedway

anthay osethay owhay ilepay ethay acierglay orway etireray otay ethay inaccessibleway eakspay ofway 
ethay ountainsmay ofway ourway ownway ountrycay." Ervalclay! Elovedbay iendfray! Evenway ownay 
itway elightsday emay otay ecordray yourway ordsway andway otay elldway onway ethay aisepray ofway ichwhay

Ethay eneryscay ofway externalway aturenay, ichwhay othersway egardray onlyway ithway 
admirationway, ehay ovedlay ithway ardourway:-- 


----Ethay oundingsay ataractcay 
Auntedhay imhay ikelay away assionpay: ethay alltay ockray, 
Ethay ountainmay, andway ethay eepday andway oomyglay oodway, 
Eirthay olourscay andway eirthay ormsfay, ereway enthay otay imhay 
Anway appetiteway; away eelingfay, andway away ovelay, 
Atthay adhay onay eednay ofway away emoterray armchay, 
Ybay oughtthay uppliedsay, orway anyway interestway 
Unborrowway'd omfray ethay eyeway. 

[Ordsworthway's "Interntay Abbeyway".] 


Andway erewhay oesday ehay ownay existway? Isway isthay entlegay andway ovelylay eingbay ostlay 
oreverfay? Ashay isthay indmay, osay epleteray ithway ideasway, imaginationsway ancifulfay 
andway agnificentmay, ichwhay ormedfay away orldway, osewhay existenceway ependedday onway ethay

eamingbay ithway eautybay, ashay ecayedday, utbay yourway iritspay illstay isitsvay andway 
onsolescay yourway unhappyway iendfray.

Eyondbay Olognecay eway escendedday otay ethay ainsplay ofway Ollandhay; andway eway esolvedray

Apterchay 19

Utbay ehay oundfay atthay away avellertray's ifelay isway oneway atthay includesway uchmay ainpay

Eway adhay arcelyscay isitedvay ethay ariousvay akeslay ofway Umberlandcay andway Estmorlandway 
andway onceivedcay anway affectionway orfay omesay ofway ethay inhabitantsway enwhay ethay eriodpay 
ofway ourway appointmentway ithway ourway Otchscay iendfray approachedway, andway eway eftlay emthay 
otay aveltray onway. Orfay ymay ownway artpay Iway asway otnay orrysay. Iway adhay ownay eglectednay ymay

isappointmentday. Ehay ightmay emainray inway Itzerlandsway andway eakwray ishay engeancevay 
onway ymay elativesray. Isthay ideaway ursuedpay emay andway ormentedtay emay atway everyway omentmay

eadray andway ascertainway ymay atefay. Ometimessay Iway oughtthay atthay ethay iendfay 
ollowedfay emay andway ightmay expediteway ymay emissnessray ybay urderingmay ymay ompanioncay. 
Enwhay esethay oughtsthay ossessedpay emay, Iway ouldway otnay uitqay Enryhay orfay away omentmay, 
utbay ollowedfay imhay asway ishay adowshay, otay otectpray imhay omfray ethay anciedfay ageray ofway 
ishay estroyerday. Iway eltfay asway ifway Iway adhay ommittedcay omesay eatgray imecray, ethay 
onsciousnesscay ofway ichwhay auntedhay emay. Iway asway uiltlessgay, utbay Iway adhay indeedway 
awndray ownday away orriblehay ursecay uponway ymay eadhay, asway ortalmay asway atthay ofway imecray. 

Iway isitedvay Edinburghway ithway anguidlay eyesway andway indmay; andway yetway atthay itycay ightmay 
avehay interestedway ethay ostmay unfortunateway eingbay. Ervalclay idday otnay ikelay itway osay 
ellway asway Oxfordway, orfay ethay antiquityway ofway ethay atterlay itycay asway oremay easingplay 
otay imhay. Utbay ethay eautybay andway egularityray ofway ethay ewnay owntay ofway Edinburghway, 
itsway omanticray astlecay andway itsway environsway, ethay ostmay elightfulday inway ethay orldway, 
Arthurway's Eatsay, Stay. Ernardbay's Ellway, andway ethay Entlandpay Illshay ompensatedcay 
imhay orfay ethay angechay andway illedfay imhay ithway eerfulnesschay andway admirationway. Utbay 
Iway asway impatientway otay arriveway atway ethay erminationtay ofway ymay ourneyjay. 

Eway eftlay Edinburghway inway away eekway, assingpay oughthray Ouparcay, Stay. Andrewway's, andway 
alongway ethay anksbay ofway ethay Aytay, otay Erthpay, erewhay ourway iendfray expectedway usway. 
Utbay Iway asway inway onay oodmay otay aughlay andway alktay ithway angersstray orway enterway intoway 
eirthay eelingsfay orway ansplay ithway ethay oodgay umourhay expectedway omfray away uestgay; andway 
accordinglyway Iway oldtay Ervalclay atthay Iway ishedway otay akemay ethay ourtay ofway Otlandscay 
aloneway. "Oday youway," aidsay Iway, "enjoyway yourselfway, andway etlay isthay ebay ourway 
endezvousray. Iway aymay ebay absentway away onthmay orway otway; utbay oday otnay interfereway ithway 
ymay otionsmay, Iway entreatway youway; eavelay emay otay eacepay andway olitudesay orfay away ortshay 
imetay; andway enwhay Iway eturnray, Iway opehay itway illway ebay ithway away ighterlay earthay, oremay 
ongenialcay otay yourway ownway empertay." 

Enryhay ishedway otay issuadeday emay, utbay eeingsay emay entbay onway isthay anplay, easedcay otay 
emonstrateray. Ehay entreatedway emay otay itewray oftenway. "Iway adhay atherray ebay ithway 
youway," ehay aidsay, "inway yourway olitarysay amblesray, anthay ithway esethay Otchscay 
eoplepay, omwhay Iway oday otnay owknay; astenhay, enthay, ymay earday iendfray, otay eturnray, 
atthay Iway aymay againway eelfay yselfmay omewhatsay atway omehay, ichwhay Iway annotcay oday inway 
yourway absenceway." 

Avinghay artedpay omfray ymay iendfray, Iway eterminedday otay isitvay omesay emoteray otspay ofway 
Otlandscay andway inishfay ymay orkway inway olitudesay. Iway idday otnay oubtday utbay atthay ethay 
onstermay ollowedfay emay andway ouldway iscoverday imselfhay otay emay enwhay Iway ouldshay avehay 
inishedfay, atthay ehay ightmay eceiveray ishay ompanioncay. Ithway isthay esolutionray Iway 
aversedtray ethay orthernnay ighlandshay andway ixedfay onway oneway ofway ethay emotestray ofway 
ethay Orkneysway asway ethay enescay ofway ymay abourslay. Itway asway away aceplay ittedfay orfay uchsay 
away orkway, eingbay ardlyhay oremay anthay away ockray osewhay ighhay idessay ereway ontinuallycay
