eatenbay uponway ybay ethay avesway. Ethay oilsay asway arrenbay, arcelyscay affordingway 
asturepay orfay away ewfay iserablemay owscay, andway oatmealway orfay itsway inhabitantsway, 
ichwhay onsistedcay ofway ivefay ersonspay, osewhay auntgay andway aggyscray imbslay avegay 
okenstay ofway eirthay iserablemay arefay. Egetablesvay andway eadbray, enwhay eythay 
indulgedway inway uchsay uxurieslay, andway evenway eshfray aterway, asway otay ebay ocuredpray 
omfray ethay ainlandmay, ichwhay asway aboutway ivefay ilesmay istantday. 

Onway ethay olewhay islandway erethay ereway utbay eethray iserablemay utshay, andway oneway ofway 
esethay asway acantvay enwhay Iway arrivedway. Isthay Iway iredhay. Itway ontainedcay utbay otway 
oomsray, andway esethay exhibitedway allway ethay ualidnesssqay ofway ethay ostmay iserablemay 
enurypay. Ethay atchthay adhay allenfay inway, ethay allsway ereway unplasteredway, andway ethay 
oorday asway offway itsway ingeshay. Iway orderedway itway otay ebay epairedray, oughtbay omesay 
urniturefay, andway ooktay ossessionpay, anway incidentway ichwhay ouldway oubtlessday avehay 
occasionedway omesay urprisesay adhay otnay allway ethay ensessay ofway ethay ottagerscay eenbay 
enumbedbay ybay antway andway ualidsqay overtypay. Asway itway asway, Iway ivedlay ungazedway atway 
andway unmolestedway, ardlyhay ankedthay orfay ethay ittancepay ofway oodfay andway othesclay 
ichwhay Iway avegay, osay uchmay oesday ufferingsay untblay evenway ethay oarsestcay ensationssay 
ofway enmay. 

Inway isthay etreatray Iway evotedday ethay orningmay otay abourlay; utbay inway ethay eveningway, 
enwhay ethay eatherway ermittedpay, Iway alkedway onway ethay onystay eachbay ofway ethay easay otay 
istenlay otay ethay avesway asway eythay oaredray andway ashedday atway ymay eetfay. Itway asway away 
onotonousmay yetway everway-changing enescay. Iway oughtthay ofway Itzerlandsway; itway asway 
arfay ifferentday omfray isthay esolateday andway appallingway andscapelay. Itsway illshay 
areway overedcay ithway inesvay, andway itsway ottagescay areway atteredscay icklythay inway ethay 
ainsplay. Itsway airfay akeslay eflectray away ueblay andway entlegay yskay, andway enwhay 
oubledtray ybay ethay indsway, eirthay umulttay isway utbay asway ethay ayplay ofway away ivelylay 
infantway enwhay omparedcay otay ethay oaringsray ofway ethay iantgay oceanway. 

Inway isthay annermay Iway istributedday ymay occupationsway enwhay Iway irstfay arrivedway, utbay 
asway Iway oceededpray inway ymay abourlay, itway ecamebay everyway ayday oremay orriblehay andway 
irksomeway otay emay. Ometimessay Iway ouldcay otnay evailpray onway yselfmay otay enterway ymay 
aboratorylay orfay everalsay aysday, andway atway otherway imestay Iway oiledtay ayday andway ightnay 
inway orderway otay ompletecay ymay orkway. Itway asway, indeedway, away ilthyfay ocesspray inway 
ichwhay Iway asway engagedway. Uringday ymay irstfay experimentway, away indkay ofway 
enthusiasticway enzyfray adhay indedblay emay otay ethay orrorhay ofway ymay employmentway; ymay 
indmay asway intentlyway ixedfay onway ethay onsummationcay ofway ymay abourlay, andway ymay eyesway 
ereway utshay otay ethay orrorhay ofway ymay oceedingspray. Utbay ownay Iway entway otay itway inway 
oldcay oodblay, andway ymay earthay oftenway ickenedsay atway ethay orkway ofway ymay andshay. 

Usthay ituatedsay, employedway inway ethay ostmay etestableday occupationway, immersedway inway 
away olitudesay erewhay othingnay ouldcay orfay anway instantway allcay ymay attentionway omfray 
ethay actualway enescay inway ichwhay Iway asway engagedway, ymay iritsspay ecamebay unequalway; Iway 
ewgray estlessray andway ervousnay. Everyway omentmay Iway earedfay otay eetmay ymay 
ersecutorpay. Ometimessay Iway atsay ithway ymay eyesway ixedfay onway ethay oundgray, earingfay 
otay aiseray emthay estlay eythay ouldshay encounterway ethay objectway ichwhay Iway osay uchmay 
eadeddray otay eholdbay. Iway earedfay otay anderway omfray ethay ightsay ofway ymay ellowfay 
eaturescray estlay enwhay aloneway ehay ouldshay omecay otay aimclay ishay ompanioncay. 

Inway ethay eanmay imetay Iway orkedway onway, andway ymay abourlay asway alreadyway onsiderablycay 
advancedway. Iway ookedlay owardstay itsway ompletioncay ithway away emuloustray andway eagerway 
opehay, ichwhay Iway aredday otnay usttray yselfmay otay uestionqay utbay ichwhay asway 
intermixedway ithway obscureway orebodingsfay ofway evilway atthay ademay ymay earthay ickensay 
inway ymay osombay. 



Apterchay 20 

Iway atsay oneway eveningway inway ymay aboratorylay; ethay unsay adhay etsay, andway ethay oonmay asway 
ustjay isingray omfray ethay easay; Iway adhay otnay ufficientsay ightlay orfay ymay employmentway, 
andway Iway emainedray idleway, inway away ausepay ofway onsiderationcay ofway etherwhay Iway ouldshay 
eavelay ymay abourlay orfay ethay ightnay orway astenhay itsway onclusioncay ybay anway 
unremittingway attentionway otay itway. Asway Iway atsay, away aintray ofway eflectionray occurredway 
otay emay ichwhay edlay emay otay onsidercay ethay effectsway ofway atwhay Iway asway ownay oingday. 
Eethray yearsway eforebay, Iway asway engagedway inway ethay amesay annermay andway adhay eatedcray away 
iendfay osewhay unparalleledway arbaritybay adhay esolatedday ymay earthay andway illedfay itway 
oreverfay ithway ethay itterestbay emorseray. Iway asway ownay aboutway otay ormfay anotherway 
eingbay ofway osewhay ispositionsday Iway asway alikeway ignorantway; eshay ightmay ecomebay entay 
ousandthay imestay oremay alignantmay anthay erhay atemay andway elightday, orfay itsway ownway 
akesay, inway urdermay andway etchednesswray. Ehay adhay ornsway otay uitqay ethay 
eighbourhoodnay ofway anmay andway idehay imselfhay inway esertsday, utbay eshay adhay otnay; andway 
eshay, owhay inway allway obabilitypray asway otay ecomebay away inkingthay andway easoningray 
animalway, ightmay efuseray otay omplycay ithway away ompactcay ademay eforebay erhay eationcray. 
Eythay ightmay evenway atehay eachway otherway; ethay eaturecray owhay alreadyway ivedlay oathedlay 
ishay ownway eformityday, andway ightmay ehay otnay onceivecay away eatergray abhorrenceway orfay 
itway enwhay itway amecay eforebay ishay eyesway inway ethay emalefay ormfay? Eshay alsoway ightmay 
urntay ithway isgustday omfray imhay otay ethay uperiorsay eautybay ofway anmay; eshay ightmay 
uitqay imhay, andway ehay ebay againway aloneway, exasperatedway ybay ethay eshfray ovocationpray 
ofway eingbay esertedday ybay oneway ofway ishay ownway eciesspay. Evenway ifway eythay ereway otay 
eavelay Europeway andway inhabitway ethay esertsday ofway ethay ewnay orldway, yetway oneway ofway ethay 
irstfay esultsray ofway osethay ympathiessay orfay ichwhay ethay aemonday irstedthay ouldway 
ebay ildrenchay, andway away aceray ofway evilsday ouldway ebay opagatedpray uponway ethay earthway 
owhay ightmay akemay ethay eryvay existenceway ofway ethay eciesspay ofway anmay away onditioncay 
ecariouspray andway ullfay ofway errortay. Adhay Iway ightray, orfay ymay ownway enefitbay, otay 
inflictway isthay ursecay uponway everlastingway enerationsgay? Iway adhay eforebay eenbay 
ovedmay ybay ethay ophismssay ofway ethay eingbay Iway adhay eatedcray; Iway adhay eenbay uckstray 
enselesssay ybay ishay iendishfay eatsthray; utbay ownay, orfay ethay irstfay imetay, ethay 
ickednessway ofway ymay omisepray urstbay uponway emay; Iway udderedshay otay inkthay atthay 
uturefay agesway ightmay ursecay emay asway eirthay estpay, osewhay elfishnesssay adhay otnay 
esitatedhay otay uybay itsway ownway eacepay atway ethay icepray, erhapspay, ofway ethay existenceway 
ofway ethay olewhay umanhay aceray. 

Iway embledtray andway ymay earthay ailedfay ithinway emay, enwhay, onway ookinglay upway, Iway awsay ybay 
ethay ightlay ofway ethay oonmay ethay aemonday atway ethay asementcay. Away astlyghay ingray 
inkledwray ishay ipslay asway ehay azedgay onway emay, erewhay Iway atsay ulfillingfay ethay asktay 
ichwhay ehay adhay allottedway otay emay. Yesway, ehay adhay ollowedfay emay inway ymay avelstray; ehay 
adhay oiteredlay inway orestsfay, idhay imselfhay inway avescay, orway akentay efugeray inway ideway 
andway esertday eathshay; andway ehay ownay amecay otay arkmay ymay ogresspray andway aimclay ethay 
ulfilmentfay ofway ymay omisepray. 

Asway Iway ookedlay onway imhay, ishay ountenancecay expressedway ethay utmostway extentway ofway 
alicemay andway eacherytray. Iway oughtthay ithway away ensationsay ofway adnessmay onway ymay 
omisepray ofway eatingcray anotherway ikelay otay imhay, andway emblingtray ithway assionpay, 
oretay otay iecespay ethay ingthay onway ichwhay Iway asway engagedway. Ethay etchwray awsay emay 
estroyday ethay eaturecray onway osewhay uturefay existenceway ehay ependedday orfay 
appinesshay, andway ithway away owlhay ofway evilishday espairday andway evengeray, ithdrewway. 

Iway eftlay ethay oomray, andway ockinglay ethay oorday, ademay away olemnsay owvay inway ymay ownway 
earthay evernay otay esumeray ymay abourslay; andway enthay, ithway emblingtray epsstay, Iway 
oughtsay ymay ownway apartmentway. Iway asway aloneway; onenay ereway earnay emay otay issipateday 
ethay oomglay andway elieveray emay omfray ethay ickeningsay oppressionway ofway ethay ostmay 
erribletay everiesray. 

Everalsay ourshay assedpay, andway Iway emainedray earnay ymay indowway azinggay onway ethay easay; 
itway asway almostway otionlessmay, orfay ethay indsway ereway ushedhay, andway allway aturenay 
eposedray underway ethay eyeway ofway ethay uietqay oonmay. Away ewfay ishingfay esselsvay aloneway 
eckedspay ethay aterway, andway ownay andway enthay ethay entlegay eezebray aftedway ethay oundsay 
ofway oicesvay asway ethay ishermenfay alledcay otay oneway anotherway. Iway eltfay ethay ilencesay, 
althoughway Iway asway ardlyhay onsciouscay ofway itsway extremeway ofunditypray, untilway ymay earway 
asway uddenlysay arrestedway ybay ethay addlingpay ofway oarsway earnay ethay oreshay, andway away 
ersonpay andedlay oseclay otay ymay ousehay. 

Inway away ewfay inutesmay afterway, Iway eardhay ethay eakingcray ofway ymay oorday, asway ifway omesay oneway 
endeavouredway otay openway itway oftlysay. Iway embledtray omfray eadhay otay ootfay; Iway eltfay away 
esentimentpray ofway owhay itway asway andway ishedway otay ouseray oneway ofway ethay easantspay owhay 
eltdway inway away ottagecay otnay arfay omfray inemay; utbay Iway asway overcomeway ybay ethay 
ensationsay ofway elplessnesshay, osay oftenway eltfay inway ightfulfray eamsdray, enwhay youway 
inway ainvay endeavourway otay yflay omfray anway impendingway angerday, andway asway ootedray otay 
ethay otspay. Esentlypray Iway eardhay ethay oundsay ofway ootstepsfay alongway ethay assagepay; 
ethay oorday openedway, andway ethay etchwray omwhay Iway eadeddray appearedway. 

Uttingshay ethay oorday, ehay approachedway emay andway aidsay inway away otheredsmay oicevay, "Youway 
avehay estroyedday ethay orkway ichwhay youway eganbay; atwhay isway itway atthay youway intendway? 
Oday youway areday otay eakbray yourway omisepray? Iway avehay enduredway oiltay andway iserymay; Iway 
eftlay Itzerlandsway ithway youway; Iway eptcray alongway ethay oresshay ofway ethay Inerhay, amongway 
itsway illowway islandsway andway overway ethay ummitssay ofway itsway illshay. Iway avehay eltdway 
anymay onthsmay inway ethay eathshay ofway Englandway andway amongway ethay esertsday ofway Otlandscay. 
Iway avehay enduredway incalculableway atiguefay, andway oldcay, andway ungerhay; oday youway areday 
estroyday ymay opeshay?" 

"Egonebay! Iway oday eakbray ymay omisepray; evernay illway Iway eatecray anotherway ikelay 
yourselfway, equalway inway eformityday andway ickednessway." 

"Aveslay, Iway eforebay easonedray ithway youway, utbay youway avehay ovedpray yourselfway 
unworthyway ofway ymay ondescensioncay. Ememberray atthay Iway avehay owerpay; youway elievebay 
yourselfway iserablemay, utbay Iway ancay akemay youway osay etchedwray atthay ethay ightlay ofway 
ayday illway ebay atefulhay otay youway. Youway areway ymay eatorcray, utbay Iway amway yourway astermay; 
obeyway!" 

"Ethay ourhay ofway ymay irresolutionway isway astpay, andway ethay eriodpay ofway yourway owerpay isway 
arrivedway. Yourway eatsthray annotcay ovemay emay otay oday anway actway ofway ickednessway; utbay 
eythay onfirmcay emay inway away eterminationday ofway otnay eatingcray youway away ompanioncay inway 
icevay. Allshay Iway, inway oolcay oodblay, etsay ooselay uponway ethay earthway away aemonday osewhay 
elightday isway inway eathday andway etchednesswray? Egonebay! Iway amway irmfay, andway yourway 
ordsway illway onlyway exasperateway ymay ageray." 

Ethay onstermay awsay ymay eterminationday inway ymay acefay andway ashedgnay ishay eethtay inway 
ethay impotenceway ofway angerway. "Allshay eachway anmay," iedcray ehay, "indfay away ifeway orfay 
ishay osombay, andway eachway eastbay avehay ishay atemay, andway Iway ebay aloneway? Iway adhay 
eelingsfay ofway affectionway, andway eythay ereway equitedray ybay etestationday andway ornscay. 
Anmay! Youway aymay atehay, utbay ewarebay! Yourway ourshay illway asspay inway eaddray andway 
iserymay, andway oonsay ethay oltbay illway allfay ichwhay ustmay avishray omfray youway yourway 
appinesshay oreverfay. Areway youway otay ebay appyhay ilewhay Iway ovelgray inway ethay intensityway 
ofway ymay etchednesswray? Youway ancay astblay ymay otherway assionspay, utbay evengeray 
emainsray--revenge, enceforthhay earerday anthay ightlay orway oodfay! Iway aymay ieday, utbay 
irstfay youway, ymay yranttay andway ormentortay, allshay ursecay ethay unsay atthay azesgay onway 
yourway iserymay. Ewarebay, orfay Iway amway earlessfay andway ereforethay owerfulpay. Iway illway 
atchway ithway ethay ilinessway ofway away akesnay, atthay Iway aymay ingstay ithway itsway enomvay. 
Anmay, youway allshay epentray ofway ethay injuriesway youway inflictway." 

"Evilday, easecay; andway oday otnay oisonpay ethay airway ithway esethay oundssay ofway alicemay. 
Iway avehay eclaredday ymay esolutionray otay youway, andway Iway amway onay owardcay otay endbay 
eneathbay ordsway. Eavelay emay; Iway amway inexorableway." 

"Itway isway ellway. Iway ogay; utbay ememberray, Iway allshay ebay ithway youway onway yourway 
eddingway-night." 

Iway artedstay orwardfay andway exclaimedway, "Illainvay! Eforebay youway ignsay ymay 
eathday-warrant, ebay uresay atthay youway areway yourselfway afesay." 

Iway ouldway avehay eizedsay imhay, utbay ehay eludedway emay andway uittedqay ethay ousehay ithway 
ecipitationpray. Inway away ewfay omentsmay Iway awsay imhay inway ishay oatbay, ichwhay otshay 
acrossway ethay atersway ithway anway arrowyway iftnesssway andway asway oonsay ostlay amidstway ethay 
avesway. 

Allway asway againway ilentsay, utbay ishay ordsway angray inway ymay earsway. Iway urnedbay ithway 
ageray otay ursuepay ethay urderermay ofway ymay eacepay andway ecipitatepray imhay intoway ethay 
oceanway. Iway alkedway upway andway ownday ymay oomray astilyhay andway erturbedpay, ilewhay ymay 
imaginationway onjuredcay upway away ousandthay imagesway otay ormenttay andway ingstay emay. Ywhay 
adhay Iway otnay ollowedfay imhay andway osedclay ithway imhay inway ortalmay ifestray? Utbay Iway adhay 
ufferedsay imhay otay epartday, andway ehay adhay irectedday ishay oursecay owardstay ethay 
ainlandmay. Iway udderedshay otay inkthay owhay ightmay ebay ethay extnay ictimvay acrificedsay 
otay ishay insatiateway evengeray. Andway enthay Iway oughtthay againway ofway ishay ordsway--"I 
ILLWAY EBAY ITHWAY YOUWAY ONWAY YOURWAY EDDINGWAY-NIGHT." Atthay, enthay, asway ethay eriodpay 
ixedfay orfay ethay ulfilmentfay ofway ymay estinyday. Inway atthay ourhay Iway ouldshay ieday andway 
atway onceway atisfysay andway extinguishway ishay alicemay. Ethay ospectpray idday otnay ovemay 
emay otay earfay; yetway enwhay Iway oughtthay ofway ymay elovedbay Elizabethway, ofway erhay earstay 
andway endlessway orrowsay, enwhay eshay ouldshay indfay erhay overlay osay arbarouslybay 
atchedsnay omfray erhay, earstay, ethay irstfay Iway adhay edshay orfay anymay onthsmay, 
eamedstray omfray ymay eyesway, andway Iway esolvedray otnay otay allfay eforebay ymay enemyway 
ithoutway away itterbay ugglestray. 

Ethay ightnay assedpay awayway, andway ethay unsay oseray omfray ethay oceanway; ymay eelingsfay 
ecamebay almercay, ifway itway aymay ebay alledcay almnesscay enwhay ethay iolencevay ofway ageray 
inkssay intoway ethay epthsday ofway espairday. Iway eftlay ethay ousehay, ethay orridhay enescay 
ofway ethay astlay ightnay's ontentioncay, andway alkedway onway ethay eachbay ofway ethay easay, 
ichwhay Iway almostway egardedray asway anway insuperableway arrierbay etweenbay emay andway ymay 
ellowfay eaturescray; aynay, away ishway atthay uchsay ouldshay ovepray ethay actfay olestay 
acrossway emay. 

Iway esiredday atthay Iway ightmay asspay ymay ifelay onway atthay arrenbay ockray, earilyway, itway isway 
uetray, utbay uninterruptedway ybay anyway uddensay ockshay ofway iserymay. Ifway Iway eturnedray, 
itway asway otay ebay acrificedsay orway otay eesay osethay omwhay Iway ostmay ovedlay ieday underway ethay 
aspgray ofway away aemonday omwhay Iway adhay yselfmay eatedcray. 

Iway alkedway aboutway ethay isleway ikelay away estlessray ectrespay, eparatedsay omfray allway itway 
ovedlay andway iserablemay inway ethay eparationsay. Enwhay itway ecamebay oonnay, andway ethay 
unsay oseray igherhay, Iway aylay ownday onway ethay assgray andway asway overpoweredway ybay away eepday 
eepslay. Iway adhay eenbay awakeway ethay olewhay ofway ethay ecedingpray ightnay, ymay ervesnay 
ereway agitatedway, andway ymay eyesway inflamedway ybay atchingway andway iserymay. Ethay eepslay 
intoway ichwhay Iway ownay anksay efreshedray emay; andway enwhay Iway awokeway, Iway againway eltfay asway 
ifway Iway elongedbay otay away aceray ofway umanhay eingsbay ikelay yselfmay, andway Iway eganbay otay 
eflectray uponway atwhay adhay assedpay ithway eatergray omposurecay; yetway illstay ethay 
ordsway ofway ethay iendfay angray inway ymay earsway ikelay away eathday-knell; eythay appearedway 
ikelay away eamdray, yetway istinctday andway oppressiveway asway away ealityray. 

Ethay unsay adhay arfay escendedday, andway Iway illstay atsay onway ethay oreshay, atisfyingsay ymay 
appetiteway, ichwhay adhay ecomebay avenousray, ithway anway oatenway akecay, enwhay Iway awsay away 
ishingfay-boat andlay oseclay otay emay, andway oneway ofway ethay enmay oughtbray emay away acketpay; 
itway ontainedcay etterslay omfray Enevagay, andway oneway omfray Ervalclay entreatingway emay otay 
oinjay imhay. Ehay aidsay atthay ehay asway earingway awayway ishay imetay uitlesslyfray erewhay 
ehay asway, atthay etterslay omfray ethay iendsfray ehay adhay ormedfay inway Ondonlay esiredday 
ishay eturnray otay ompletecay ethay egotiationnay eythay adhay enteredway intoway orfay ishay 
Indianway enterpriseway. Ehay ouldcay otnay anyway ongerlay elayday ishay epartureday; utbay asway 
ishay ourneyjay otay Ondonlay ightmay ebay ollowedfay, evenway oonersay anthay ehay ownay 
onjecturedcay, ybay ishay ongerlay oyagevay, ehay entreatedway emay otay estowbay asway uchmay ofway 
ymay ocietysay onway imhay asway Iway ouldcay arespay. Ehay esoughtbay emay, ereforethay, otay 
eavelay ymay olitarysay isleway andway otay eetmay imhay atway Erthpay, atthay eway ightmay oceedpray 
outhwardssay ogethertay. Isthay etterlay inway away egreeday ecalledray emay otay ifelay, andway 
Iway eterminedday otay uitqay ymay islandway atway ethay expirationway ofway otway aysday. Yetway, 
eforebay Iway epartedday, erethay asway away asktay otay erformpay, onway ichwhay Iway udderedshay otay 
eflectray; Iway ustmay ackpay upway ymay emicalchay instrumentsway, andway orfay atthay urposepay Iway 
ustmay enterway ethay oomray ichwhay adhay eenbay ethay enescay ofway ymay odiousway orkway, andway Iway 
ustmay andlehay osethay utensilsway ethay ightsay ofway ichwhay asway ickeningsay otay emay. Ethay 
extnay orningmay, atway aybreakday, Iway ummonedsay ufficientsay ouragecay andway unlockedway 
ethay oorday ofway ymay aboratorylay. Ethay emainsray ofway ethay alfhay-finished eaturecray, 
omwhay Iway adhay estroyedday, aylay atteredscay onway ethay oorflay, andway Iway almostway eltfay asway 
ifway Iway adhay angledmay ethay ivinglay eshflay ofway away umanhay eingbay. Iway ausedpay otay 
ollectcay yselfmay andway enthay enteredway ethay amberchay. Ithway emblingtray andhay Iway 
onveyedcay ethay instrumentsway outway ofway ethay oomray, utbay Iway eflectedray atthay Iway oughtway 
otnay otay eavelay ethay elicsray ofway ymay orkway otay exciteway ethay orrorhay andway uspicionsay 
ofway ethay easantspay; andway Iway accordinglyway utpay emthay intoway away asketbay, ithway away eatgray 
uantityqay ofway onesstay, andway ayinglay emthay upway, eterminedday otay owthray emthay intoway 
ethay easay atthay eryvay ightnay; andway inway ethay eantimemay Iway atsay uponway ethay eachbay, 
employedway inway eaningclay andway arrangingway ymay emicalchay apparatusway. 

Othingnay ouldcay ebay oremay ompletecay anthay ethay alterationway atthay adhay akentay aceplay 
inway ymay eelingsfay incesay ethay ightnay ofway ethay appearanceway ofway ethay aemonday. Iway adhay 
eforebay egardedray ymay omisepray ithway away oomyglay espairday asway away ingthay atthay, ithway 
ateverwhay onsequencescay, ustmay ebay ulfilledfay; utbay Iway ownay eltfay asway ifway away ilmfay 
adhay eenbay akentay omfray eforebay ymay eyesway andway atthay Iway orfay ethay irstfay imetay awsay 
earlyclay. Ethay ideaway ofway enewingray ymay abourslay idday otnay orfay oneway instantway occurway 
otay emay; ethay eatthray Iway adhay eardhay eighedway onway ymay oughtsthay, utbay Iway idday otnay 
eflectray atthay away oluntaryvay actway ofway inemay ouldcay avertway itway. Iway adhay esolvedray inway 
ymay ownway indmay atthay otay eatecray anotherway ikelay ethay iendfay Iway adhay irstfay ademay 
ouldway ebay anway actway ofway ethay asestbay andway ostmay atrociousway elfishnesssay, andway Iway 
anishedbay omfray ymay indmay everyway oughtthay atthay ouldcay eadlay otay away ifferentday 
onclusioncay. 

Etweenbay otway andway eethray inway ethay orningmay ethay oonmay oseray; andway Iway enthay, uttingpay 
ymay asketbay aboardway away ittlelay iffskay, ailedsay outway aboutway ourfay ilesmay omfray ethay 
oreshay. Ethay enescay asway erfectlypay olitarysay; away ewfay oatsbay ereway eturningray 
owardstay andlay, utbay Iway ailedsay awayway omfray emthay. Iway eltfay asway ifway Iway asway aboutway 
ethay ommissioncay ofway away eadfuldray imecray andway avoidedway ithway udderingshay anxietyway 
anyway encounterway ithway ymay ellowfay eaturescray. Atway oneway imetay ethay oonmay, ichwhay 
adhay eforebay eenbay earclay, asway uddenlysay overspreadway ybay away ickthay oudclay, andway Iway 
ooktay advantageway ofway ethay omentmay ofway arknessday andway astcay ymay asketbay intoway ethay 
easay; Iway istenedlay otay ethay urglinggay oundsay asway itway anksay andway enthay ailedsay awayway 
omfray ethay otspay. Ethay yskay ecamebay oudedclay, utbay ethay airway asway urepay, althoughway 
illedchay ybay ethay ortheastnay eezebray atthay asway enthay isingray. Utbay itway efreshedray 
emay andway illedfay emay ithway uchsay agreeableway ensationssay atthay Iway esolvedray otay 
olongpray ymay aystay onway ethay aterway, andway ixingfay ethay udderray inway away irectday 
ositionpay, etchedstray yselfmay atway ethay ottombay ofway ethay oatbay. Oudsclay idhay ethay 
oonmay, everythingway asway obscureway, andway Iway eardhay onlyway ethay oundsay ofway ethay oatbay asway 
itsway eelkay utcay oughthray ethay avesway; ethay urmurmay ulledlay emay, andway inway away ortshay 
imetay Iway eptslay oundlysay. Iway oday otnay owknay owhay onglay Iway emainedray inway isthay 
ituationsay, utbay enwhay Iway awokeway Iway oundfay atthay ethay unsay adhay alreadyway ountedmay 
onsiderablycay. Ethay indway asway ighhay, andway ethay avesway ontinuallycay eatenedthray 
ethay afetysay ofway ymay ittlelay iffskay. Iway oundfay atthay ethay indway asway ortheastnay andway 
ustmay avehay ivendray emay arfay omfray ethay oastcay omfray ichwhay Iway adhay embarkedway. Iway 
endeavouredway otay angechay ymay oursecay utbay uicklyqay oundfay atthay ifway Iway againway ademay 
ethay attemptway ethay oatbay ouldway ebay instantlyway illedfay ithway aterway. Usthay 
ituatedsay, ymay onlyway esourceray asway otay ivedray eforebay ethay indway. Iway onfesscay 
atthay Iway eltfay away ewfay ensationssay ofway errortay. Iway adhay onay ompasscay ithway emay andway 
asway osay enderlyslay acquaintedway ithway ethay eographygay ofway isthay artpay ofway ethay 
orldway atthay ethay unsay asway ofway ittlelay enefitbay otay emay. Iway ightmay ebay ivendray intoway 
ethay ideway Atlanticway andway eelfay allway ethay orturestay ofway arvationstay orway ebay 
allowedsway upway inway ethay immeasurableway atersway atthay oaredray andway uffetedbay aroundway 
emay. Iway adhay alreadyway eenbay outway anymay ourshay andway eltfay ethay ormenttay ofway away 
urningbay irstthay, away eludepray otay ymay otherway ufferingssay. Iway ookedlay onway ethay 
eavenshay, ichwhay ereway overedcay ybay oudsclay atthay ewflay eforebay ethay indway, onlyway 
otay ebay eplacedray ybay othersway; Iway ookedlay uponway ethay easay; itway asway otay ebay ymay avegray. 
"Iendfay," Iway exclaimedway, "yourway asktay isway alreadyway ulfilledfay!" Iway oughtthay ofway 
Elizabethway, ofway ymay atherfay, andway ofway Ervalclay--all eftlay ehindbay, onway omwhay ethay 
onstermay ightmay atisfysay ishay anguinarysay andway ercilessmay assionspay. Isthay ideaway 
ungedplay emay intoway away everieray osay espairingday andway ightfulfray atthay evenway ownay, 
enwhay ethay enescay isway onway ethay ointpay ofway osingclay eforebay emay oreverfay, Iway uddershay 
otay eflectray onway itway. 

Omesay ourshay assedpay usthay; utbay ybay egreesday, asway ethay unsay eclinedday owardstay ethay 
orizonhay, ethay indway iedday awayway intoway away entlegay eezebray andway ethay easay ecamebay 
eefray omfray eakersbray. Utbay esethay avegay aceplay otay away eavyhay ellsway; Iway eltfay icksay 
andway ardlyhay ableway otay oldhay ethay udderray, enwhay uddenlysay Iway awsay away inelay ofway ighhay 
andlay owardstay ethay outhsay. 

Almostway entspay, asway Iway asway, ybay atiguefay andway ethay eadfuldray uspensesay Iway enduredway 
orfay everalsay ourshay, isthay uddensay ertaintycay ofway ifelay ushedray ikelay away oodflay ofway 
armway oyjay otay ymay earthay, andway earstay ushedgay omfray ymay eyesway. 

Owhay utablemay areway ourway eelingsfay, andway owhay angestray isway atthay ingingclay ovelay eway 
avehay ofway ifelay evenway inway ethay excessway ofway iserymay! Iway onstructedcay anotherway ailsay 
ithway away artpay ofway ymay essdray andway eagerlyway eeredstay ymay oursecay owardstay ethay andlay. 
Itway adhay away ildway andway ockyray appearanceway, utbay asway Iway approachedway earernay Iway easilyway 
erceivedpay ethay acestray ofway ultivationcay. Iway awsay esselsvay earnay ethay oreshay andway 
oundfay yselfmay uddenlysay ansportedtray ackbay otay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofway 
ivilizedcay anmay. Iway arefullycay acedtray ethay indingsway ofway ethay andlay andway ailedhay 
away eeplestay ichwhay Iway atway engthlay awsay issuingway omfray ehindbay away allsmay omontorypray. 
Asway Iway asway inway away atestay ofway extremeway ebilityday, Iway esolvedray otay ailsay irectlyday 
owardstay ethay owntay, asway away aceplay erewhay Iway ouldcay ostmay easilyway ocurepray 
ourishmentnay. Ortunatelyfay Iway adhay oneymay ithway emay. 

Asway Iway urnedtay ethay omontorypray Iway erceivedpay away allsmay eatnay owntay andway away oodgay 
arbourhay, ichwhay Iway enteredway, ymay earthay oundingbay ithway oyjay atway ymay unexpectedway 
escapeway. 

Asway Iway asway occupiedway inway ixingfay ethay oatbay andway arrangingway ethay ailssay, everalsay 
eoplepay owdedcray owardstay ethay otspay. Eythay eemedsay uchmay urprisedsay atway ymay 
appearanceway, utbay insteadway ofway offeringway emay anyway assistanceway, isperedwhay 
ogethertay ithway esturesgay atthay atway anyway otherway imetay ightmay avehay oducedpray inway emay 
away ightslay ensationsay ofway alarmway. Asway itway asway, Iway erelymay emarkedray atthay eythay 
okespay Englishway, andway Iway ereforethay addressedway emthay inway atthay anguagelay. "Ymay 
oodgay iendsfray," aidsay Iway, "illway youway ebay osay indkay asway otay elltay emay ethay amenay ofway 
isthay owntay andway informway emay erewhay Iway amway?" 

"Youway illway owknay atthay oonsay enoughway," epliedray away anmay ithway away oarsehay oicevay. 
"Aybemay youway areway omecay otay away aceplay atthay illway otnay ovepray uchmay otay yourway astetay, 
utbay youway illway otnay ebay onsultedcay asway otay yourway uartersqay, Iway omisepray youway." 

Iway asway exceedinglyway urprisedsay onway eceivingray osay uderay anway answerway omfray away 
angerstray, andway Iway asway alsoway isconcertedday onway erceivingpay ethay owningfray andway 
angryway ountenancescay ofway ishay ompanionscay. "Ywhay oday youway answerway emay osay 
oughlyray?" Iway epliedray. "Urelysay itway isway otnay ethay ustomcay ofway Englishmenway otay 
eceiveray angersstray osay inhospitablyway." 

"Iway oday otnay owknay," aidsay ethay anmay, "atwhay ethay ustomcay ofway ethay Englishway aymay ebay, 
utbay itway isway ethay ustomcay ofway ethay Irishway otay atehay illainsvay." Ilewhay isthay angestray 
ialogueday ontinuedcay, Iway erceivedpay ethay owdcray apidlyray increaseway. Eirthay 
acesfay expressedway away ixturemay ofway uriositycay andway angerway, ichwhay annoyedway andway inway 
omesay egreeday alarmedway emay. 

Iway inquiredway ethay ayway otay ethay innway, utbay onay oneway epliedray. Iway enthay ovedmay 
orwardfay, andway away urmuringmay oundsay aroseway omfray ethay owdcray asway eythay ollowedfay 
andway urroundedsay emay, enwhay anway illway-looking anmay approachingway appedtay emay onway ethay 
ouldershay andway aidsay, "Omecay, irsay, youway ustmay ollowfay emay otay Mray. Irwinkay's otay 
ivegay anway accountway ofway yourselfway." 

"Owhay isway Mray. Irwinkay? Ywhay amway Iway otay ivegay anway accountway ofway yselfmay? Isway otnay 
isthay away eefray ountrycay?" 

"Ayway, irsay, eefray enoughway orfay onesthay olksfay. Mray. Irwinkay isway away agistratemay, 
andway youway areway otay ivegay anway accountway ofway ethay eathday ofway away entlemangay owhay asway 
oundfay urderedmay erehay astlay ightnay." 

Isthay answerway artledstay emay, utbay Iway esentlypray ecoveredray yselfmay. Iway asway 
innocentway; atthay ouldcay easilyway ebay ovedpray; accordinglyway Iway ollowedfay ymay 
onductorcay inway ilencesay andway asway edlay otay oneway ofway ethay estbay ouseshay inway ethay owntay. 
Iway asway eadyray otay inksay omfray atiguefay andway ungerhay, utbay eingbay urroundedsay ybay away 
owdcray, Iway oughtthay itway oliticpay otay ouseray allway ymay engthstray, atthay onay ysicalphay 
ebilityday ightmay ebay onstruedcay intoway apprehensionway orway onsciouscay uiltgay. 
Ittlelay idday Iway enthay expectway ethay alamitycay atthay asway inway away ewfay omentsmay otay 
overwhelmway emay andway extinguishway inway orrorhay andway espairday allway earfay ofway ignominyway 
orway eathday. Iway ustmay ausepay erehay, orfay itway equiresray allway ymay ortitudefay otay ecallray 
ethay emorymay ofway ethay ightfulfray eventsway ichwhay Iway amway aboutway otay elateray, inway 
operpray etailday, otay ymay ecollectionray. 



Apterchay 21 

Iway asway oonsay introducedway intoway ethay esencepray ofway ethay agistratemay, anway oldway 
enevolentbay anmay ithway almcay andway ildmay annersmay. Ehay ookedlay uponway emay, oweverhay, 
ithway omesay egreeday ofway everitysay, andway enthay, urningtay owardstay ymay onductorscay, 
ehay askedway owhay appearedway asway itnessesway onway isthay occasionway. 

Aboutway alfhay away ozenday enmay amecay orwardfay; andway, oneway eingbay electedsay ybay ethay 
agistratemay, ehay eposedday atthay ehay adhay eenbay outway ishingfay ethay ightnay eforebay 
ithway ishay onsay andway otherbray-in-law, Anielday Ugentnay, enwhay, aboutway entay 
oway'clock, eythay observedway away ongstray ortherlynay astblay isingray, andway eythay 
accordinglyway utpay inway orfay ortpay. Itway asway away eryvay arkday ightnay, asway ethay oonmay adhay 
otnay yetway isenray; eythay idday otnay andlay atway ethay arbourhay, utbay, asway eythay adhay eenbay 
accustomedway, atway away eekcray aboutway otway ilesmay elowbay. Ehay alkedway onway irstfay, 
arryingcay away artpay ofway ethay ishingfay ackletay, andway ishay ompanionscay ollowedfay imhay 
atway omesay istanceday. 

Asway ehay asway oceedingpray alongway ethay andssay, ehay uckstray ishay ootfay againstway 
omethingsay andway ellfay atway ishay engthlay onway ethay oundgray. Ishay ompanionscay amecay upway 
otay assistway imhay, andway ybay ethay ightlay ofway eirthay anternlay eythay oundfay atthay ehay adhay 
allenfay onway ethay odybay ofway away anmay, owhay asway otay allway appearanceway eadday. Eirthay 
irstfay uppositionsay asway atthay itway asway ethay orpsecay ofway omesay ersonpay owhay adhay 
eenbay owneddray andway asway ownthray onway oreshay ybay ethay avesway, utbay onway examinationway 
eythay oundfay atthay ethay othesclay ereway otnay etway andway evenway atthay ethay odybay asway otnay 
enthay oldcay. Eythay instantlyway arriedcay itway otay ethay ottagecay ofway anway oldway omanway 
earnay ethay otspay andway endeavouredway, utbay inway ainvay, otay estoreray itway otay ifelay. Itway 
appearedway otay ebay away andsomehay youngway anmay, aboutway ivefay andway entytway yearsway ofway 
ageway. Ehay adhay apparentlyway eenbay angledstray, orfay erethay asway onay ignsay ofway anyway 
iolencevay exceptway ethay ackblay arkmay ofway ingersfay onway ishay ecknay. 

Ethay irstfay artpay ofway isthay epositionday idday otnay inway ethay eastlay interestway emay, utbay 
enwhay ethay arkmay ofway ethay ingersfay asway entionedmay Iway ememberedray ethay urdermay ofway 
ymay otherbray andway eltfay yselfmay extremelyway agitatedway; ymay imbslay embledtray, andway away 
istmay amecay overway ymay eyesway, ichwhay obligedway emay otay eanlay onway away airchay orfay 
upportsay. Ethay agistratemay observedway emay ithway away eenkay eyeway andway ofway oursecay ewdray 
anway unfavourableway auguryway omfray ymay annermay. 

Ethay onsay onfirmedcay ishay atherfay's accountway, utbay enwhay Anielday Ugentnay asway 
alledcay ehay oresway ositivelypay atthay ustjay eforebay ethay allfay ofway ishay ompanioncay, 
ehay awsay away oatbay, ithway away inglesay anmay inway itway, atway away ortshay istanceday omfray ethay 
oreshay; andway asway arfay asway ehay ouldcay udgejay ybay ethay ightlay ofway away ewfay arsstay, itway asway 
ethay amesay oatbay inway ichwhay Iway adhay ustjay andedlay. Away omanway eposedday atthay eshay 
ivedlay earnay ethay eachbay andway asway andingstay atway ethay oorday ofway erhay ottagecay, 
aitingway orfay ethay eturnray ofway ethay ishermenfay, aboutway anway ourhay eforebay eshay eardhay 
ofway ethay iscoveryday ofway ethay odybay, enwhay eshay awsay away oatbay ithway onlyway oneway anmay inway 
itway ushpay offway omfray atthay artpay ofway ethay oreshay erewhay ethay orpsecay asway afterwardsway 
oundfay. 

Anotherway omanway onfirmedcay ethay accountway ofway ethay ishermenfay avinghay oughtbray ethay 
odybay intoway erhay ousehay; itway asway otnay oldcay. Eythay utpay itway intoway away edbay andway 
ubbedray itway, andway Anielday entway otay ethay owntay orfay anway apothecaryway, utbay ifelay asway 
uiteqay onegay. 

Everalsay otherway enmay ereway examinedway oncerningcay ymay andinglay, andway eythay agreedway 
atthay, ithway ethay ongstray orthnay indway atthay adhay arisenway uringday ethay ightnay, itway 
asway eryvay obablepray atthay Iway adhay eatenbay aboutway orfay anymay ourshay andway adhay eenbay 
obligedway otay eturnray earlynay otay ethay amesay otspay omfray ichwhay Iway adhay epartedday. 
Esidesbay, eythay observedway atthay itway appearedway atthay Iway adhay oughtbray ethay odybay 
omfray anotherway aceplay, andway itway asway ikelylay atthay asway Iway idday otnay appearway otay owknay 
ethay oreshay, Iway ightmay avehay utpay intoway ethay arbourhay ignorantway ofway ethay istanceday 
ofway ethay owntay ofway ---- omfray ethay aceplay erewhay Iway adhay epositedday ethay orpsecay. 

Mray. Irwinkay, onway earinghay isthay evidenceway, esiredday atthay Iway ouldshay ebay akentay 
intoway ethay oomray erewhay ethay odybay aylay orfay intermentway, atthay itway ightmay ebay 
observedway atwhay effectway ethay ightsay ofway itway ouldway oducepray uponway emay. Isthay ideaway 
asway obablypray uggestedsay ybay ethay extremeway agitationway Iway adhay exhibitedway enwhay 
ethay odemay ofway ethay urdermay adhay eenbay escribedday. Iway asway accordinglyway 
onductedcay, ybay ethay agistratemay andway everalsay otherway ersonspay, otay ethay innway. Iway 
ouldcay otnay elphay eingbay uckstray ybay ethay angestray oincidencescay atthay adhay akentay 
aceplay uringday isthay eventfulway ightnay; utbay, owingknay atthay Iway adhay eenbay 
onversingcay ithway everalsay ersonspay inway ethay islandway Iway adhay inhabitedway aboutway ethay 
imetay atthay ethay odybay adhay eenbay oundfay, Iway asway erfectlypay anquiltray asway otay ethay 
onsequencescay ofway ethay affairway. Iway enteredway ethay oomray erewhay ethay orpsecay aylay 
andway asway edlay upway otay ethay offincay. Owhay ancay Iway escribeday ymay ensationssay onway 
eholdingbay itway? Iway eelfay yetway archedpay ithway orrorhay, ornay ancay Iway eflectray onway 
atthay erribletay omentmay ithoutway udderingshay andway agonyway. Ethay examinationway, 
ethay esencepray ofway ethay agistratemay andway itnessesway, assedpay ikelay away eamdray omfray 
ymay emorymay enwhay Iway awsay ethay ifelesslay ormfay ofway Enryhay Ervalclay etchedstray 
eforebay emay. Iway aspedgay orfay eathbray, andway owingthray yselfmay onway ethay odybay, Iway 
exclaimedway, "Avehay ymay urderousmay achinationsmay eprivedday youway alsoway, ymay 
earestday Enryhay, ofway ifelay? Otway Iway avehay alreadyway estroyedday; otherway ictimsvay 
awaitway eirthay estinyday; utbay youway, Ervalclay, ymay iendfray, ymay enefactorbay--" 

Ethay umanhay amefray ouldcay onay ongerlay upportsay ethay agoniesway atthay Iway enduredway, andway 
Iway asway arriedcay outway ofway ethay oomray inway ongstray onvulsionscay. Away everfay ucceededsay 
otay isthay. Iway aylay orfay otway onthsmay onway ethay ointpay ofway eathday; ymay avingsray, asway Iway 
afterwardsway eardhay, ereway ightfulfray; Iway alledcay yselfmay ethay urderermay ofway 
Illiamway, ofway Ustinejay, andway ofway Ervalclay. Ometimessay Iway entreatedway ymay 
attendantsway otay assistway emay inway ethay estructionday ofway ethay iendfay ybay omwhay Iway asway 
ormentedtay; andway atway othersway Iway eltfay ethay ingersfay ofway ethay onstermay alreadyway 
aspinggray ymay ecknay, andway eamedscray aloudway ithway agonyway andway errortay. 
Ortunatelyfay, asway Iway okespay ymay ativenay anguagelay, Mray. Irwinkay aloneway understoodway 
emay; utbay ymay esturesgay andway itterbay iescray ereway ufficientsay otay affrightway ethay 
otherway itnessesway. Ywhay idday Iway otnay ieday? Oremay iserablemay anthay anmay everway asway 
eforebay, ywhay idday Iway otnay inksay intoway orgetfulnessfay andway estray? Eathday atchessnay 
awayway anymay oomingblay ildrenchay, ethay onlyway opeshay ofway eirthay otingday arentspay; 
owhay anymay idesbray andway youthfulway overslay avehay eenbay oneway ayday inway ethay oomblay ofway 
ealthhay andway opehay, andway ethay extnay away eypray orfay ormsway andway ethay ecayday ofway ethay 
ombtay! Ofway atwhay aterialsmay asway Iway ademay atthay Iway ouldcay usthay esistray osay anymay 
ocksshay, ichwhay, ikelay ethay urningtay ofway ethay eelwhay, ontinuallycay enewedray ethay 
orturetay? 

Utbay Iway asway oomedday otay ivelay andway inway otway onthsmay oundfay yselfmay asway awakingway omfray 
away eamdray, inway away isonpray, etchedstray onway away etchedwray edbay, urroundedsay ybay 
ailersjay, urnkeystay, oltsbay, andway allway ethay iserablemay apparatusway ofway away ungeonday. 
Itway asway orningmay, Iway ememberray, enwhay Iway usthay awokeway otay understandingway; Iway adhay 
orgottenfay ethay articularspay ofway atwhay adhay appenedhay andway onlyway eltfay asway ifway omesay 
eatgray isfortunemay adhay uddenlysay overwhelmedway emay; utbay enwhay Iway ookedlay aroundway 
andway awsay ethay arredbay indowsway andway ethay ualidnesssqay ofway ethay oomray inway ichwhay Iway 
asway, allway ashedflay acrossway ymay emorymay andway Iway oanedgray itterlybay. 

Isthay oundsay isturbedday anway oldway omanway owhay asway eepingslay inway away airchay esidebay 
emay. Eshay asway away iredhay ursenay, ethay ifeway ofway oneway ofway ethay urnkeystay, andway erhay 
ountenancecay expressedway allway osethay adbay ualitiesqay ichwhay oftenway aracterizechay 
atthay assclay. Ethay ineslay ofway erhay acefay ereway ardhay andway uderay, ikelay atthay ofway 
ersonspay accustomedway otay eesay ithoutway ympathizingsay inway ightssay ofway iserymay. Erhay 
onetay expressedway erhay entireway indifferenceway; eshay addressedway emay inway Englishway, 
andway ethay oicevay uckstray emay asway oneway atthay Iway adhay eardhay uringday ymay ufferingssay. 
"Areway youway etterbay ownay, irsay?" aidsay eshay. 

Iway epliedray inway ethay amesay anguagelay, ithway away eeblefay oicevay, "Iway elievebay Iway amway; 
utbay ifway itway ebay allway uetray, ifway indeedway Iway idday otnay eamdray, Iway amway orrysay atthay Iway amway 
illstay aliveway otay eelfay isthay iserymay andway orrorhay." 

"Orfay atthay attermay," epliedray ethay oldway omanway, "ifway youway eanmay aboutway ethay 
entlemangay youway urderedmay, Iway elievebay atthay itway ereway etterbay orfay youway ifway youway 
ereway eadday, orfay Iway ancyfay itway illway ogay ardhay ithway youway! Oweverhay, atthay's onenay 
ofway ymay usinessbay; Iway amway entsay otay ursenay youway andway etgay youway ellway; Iway oday ymay utyday 
ithway away afesay onsciencecay; itway ereway ellway ifway everybodyway idday ethay amesay." 

Iway urnedtay ithway oathinglay omfray ethay omanway owhay ouldcay utterway osay unfeelingway away 
eechspay otay away ersonpay ustjay avedsay, onway ethay eryvay edgeway ofway eathday; utbay Iway eltfay 
anguidlay andway unableway otay eflectray onway allway atthay adhay assedpay. Ethay olewhay eriessay 
ofway ymay ifelay appearedway otay emay asway away eamdray; Iway ometimessay oubtedday ifway indeedway itway 
ereway allway uetray, orfay itway evernay esentedpray itselfway otay ymay indmay ithway ethay orcefay 
ofway ealityray. 

Asway ethay imagesway atthay oatedflay eforebay emay ecamebay oremay istinctday, Iway ewgray 
everishfay; away arknessday essedpray aroundway emay; onay oneway asway earnay emay owhay oothedsay 
emay ithway ethay entlegay oicevay ofway ovelay; onay earday andhay upportedsay emay. Ethay 
ysicianphay amecay andway escribedpray edicinesmay, andway ethay oldway omanway eparedpray 
emthay orfay emay; utbay utterway arelessnesscay asway isiblevay inway ethay irstfay, andway ethay 
expressionway ofway utalitybray asway onglystray arkedmay inway ethay isagevay ofway ethay 
econdsay. Owhay ouldcay ebay interestedway inway ethay atefay ofway away urderermay utbay ethay 
angmanhay owhay ouldway aingay ishay eefay? 

Esethay ereway ymay irstfay eflectionsray, utbay Iway oonsay earnedlay atthay Mray. Irwinkay adhay 
ownshay emay extremeway indnesskay. Ehay adhay ausedcay ethay estbay oomray inway ethay isonpray 
otay ebay eparedpray orfay emay (etchedwray indeedway asway ethay estbay); andway itway asway ehay owhay 
adhay ovidedpray away ysicianphay andway away ursenay. Itway isway uetray, ehay eldomsay amecay otay 
eesay emay, orfay althoughway ehay ardentlyway esiredday otay elieveray ethay ufferingssay ofway 
everyway umanhay eaturecray, ehay idday otnay ishway otay ebay esentpray atway ethay agoniesway andway 
iserablemay avingsray ofway away urderermay. Ehay amecay, ereforethay, ometimessay otay eesay 
atthay Iway asway otnay eglectednay, utbay ishay isitsvay ereway ortshay andway ithway onglay 
intervalsway. Oneway ayday, ilewhay Iway asway aduallygray ecoveringray, Iway asway eatedsay inway 
away airchay, ymay eyesway alfhay openway andway ymay eekschay ividlay ikelay osethay inway eathday. Iway 
asway overcomeway ybay oomglay andway iserymay andway oftenway eflectedray Iway adhay etterbay eeksay 
eathday anthay esireday otay emainray inway away orldway ichwhay otay emay asway epleteray ithway 
etchednesswray. Atway oneway imetay Iway onsideredcay etherwhay Iway ouldshay otnay eclareday 
yselfmay uiltygay andway uffersay ethay enaltypay ofway ethay awlay, esslay innocentway anthay 
oorpay Ustinejay adhay eenbay. Uchsay ereway ymay oughtsthay enwhay ethay oorday ofway ymay 
apartmentway asway openedway andway Mray. Irwinkay enteredway. Ishay ountenancecay expressedway 
ympathysay andway ompassioncay; ehay ewdray away airchay oseclay otay inemay andway addressedway emay 
inway Enchfray, "Iway earfay atthay isthay aceplay isway eryvay ockingshay otay youway; ancay Iway oday 
anythingway otay akemay youway oremay omfortablecay?" 

"Iway ankthay youway, utbay allway atthay youway entionmay isway othingnay otay emay; onway ethay olewhay 
earthway erethay isway onay omfortcay ichwhay Iway amway apablecay ofway eceivingray." 

"Iway owknay atthay ethay ympathysay ofway away angerstray ancay ebay utbay ofway ittlelay eliefray otay 
oneway ornebay ownday asway youway areway ybay osay angestray away isfortunemay. Utbay youway illway, Iway 
opehay, oonsay uitqay isthay elancholymay abodeway, orfay oubtlessday evidenceway ancay 
easilyway ebay oughtbray otay eefray youway omfray ethay iminalcray argechay." 

"Atthay isway ymay eastlay oncerncay; Iway amway, ybay away oursecay ofway angestray eventsway, ecomebay 
ethay ostmay iserablemay ofway ortalsmay. Ersecutedpay andway orturedtay asway Iway amway andway 
avehay eenbay, ancay eathday ebay anyway evilway otay emay?" 

"Othingnay indeedway ouldcay ebay oremay unfortunateway andway agonizingway anthay ethay 
angestray anceschay atthay avehay atelylay occurredway. Youway ereway ownthray, ybay omesay 
urprisingsay accidentway, onway isthay oreshay, enownedray orfay itsway ospitalityhay, 
eizedsay immediatelyway, andway argedchay ithway urdermay. Ethay irstfay ightsay atthay asway 
esentedpray otay yourway eyesway asway ethay odybay ofway yourway iendfray, urderedmay inway osay 
unaccountableway away annermay andway acedplay, asway itway ereway, ybay omesay iendfay acrossway 
yourway athpay." 

Asway Mray. Irwinkay aidsay isthay, otwithstandingnay ethay agitationway Iway enduredway onway 
isthay etrospectray ofway ymay ufferingssay, Iway alsoway eltfay onsiderablecay urprisesay atway 
ethay owledgeknay ehay eemedsay otay ossesspay oncerningcay emay. Iway upposesay omesay 
astonishmentway asway exhibitedway inway ymay ountenancecay, orfay Mray. Irwinkay astenedhay 
otay aysay, "Immediatelyway uponway yourway eingbay akentay illway, allway ethay aperspay atthay 
ereway onway yourway ersonpay ereway oughtbray emay, andway Iway examinedway emthay atthay Iway ightmay 
iscoverday omesay acetray ybay ichwhay Iway ouldcay endsay otay yourway elationsray anway accountway 
ofway yourway isfortunemay andway illnessway. Iway oundfay everalsay etterslay, andway, amongway 
othersway, oneway ichwhay Iway iscoveredday omfray itsway ommencementcay otay ebay omfray yourway 
atherfay. Iway instantlyway otewray otay Enevagay; earlynay otway onthsmay avehay elapsedway 
incesay ethay epartureday ofway ymay etterlay. Utbay youway areway illway; evenway ownay youway 
embletray; youway areway unfitway orfay agitationway ofway anyway indkay." 

"Isthay uspensesay isway away ousandthay imestay orseway anthay ethay ostmay orriblehay eventway; 
elltay emay atwhay ewnay enescay ofway eathday ashay eenbay actedway, andway osewhay urdermay Iway amway 
ownay otay amentlay?" 

"Yourway amilyfay isway erfectlypay ellway," aidsay Mray. Irwinkay ithway entlenessgay; "andway 
omeonesay, away iendfray, isway omecay otay isitvay youway." 

Iway owknay otnay ybay atwhay ainchay ofway oughtthay ethay ideaway esentedpray itselfway, utbay itway 
instantlyway artedday intoway ymay indmay atthay ethay urderermay adhay omecay otay ockmay atway ymay 
iserymay andway aunttay emay ithway ethay eathday ofway Ervalclay, asway away ewnay incitementway orfay 
emay otay omplycay ithway ishay ellishhay esiresday. Iway utpay ymay andhay eforebay ymay eyesway, 
andway iedcray outway inway agonyway, "Ohway! Aketay imhay awayway! Iway annotcay eesay imhay; orfay 
Odgay's akesay, oday otnay etlay imhay enterway!" 

Mray. Irwinkay egardedray emay ithway away oubledtray ountenancecay. Ehay ouldcay otnay elphay 
egardingray ymay exclamationway asway away esumptionpray ofway ymay uiltgay andway aidsay inway 
atherray away everesay onetay, "Iway ouldshay avehay oughtthay, youngway anmay, atthay ethay 
esencepray ofway yourway atherfay ouldway avehay eenbay elcomeway insteadway ofway inspiringway 
uchsay iolentvay epugnanceray." 

"Ymay atherfay!" iedcray Iway, ilewhay everyway eaturefay andway everyway usclemay asway elaxedray 
omfray anguishway otay easureplay. "Isway ymay atherfay indeedway omecay? Owhay indkay, owhay 
eryvay indkay! Utbay erewhay isway ehay, ywhay oesday ehay otnay astenhay otay emay?" 

Ymay angechay ofway annermay urprisedsay andway easedplay ethay agistratemay; erhapspay ehay 
oughtthay atthay ymay ormerfay exclamationway asway away omentarymay eturnray ofway eliriumday, 
andway ownay ehay instantlyway esumedray ishay ormerfay enevolencebay. Ehay oseray andway 
uittedqay ethay oomray ithway ymay ursenay, andway inway away omentmay ymay atherfay enteredway itway. 

Othingnay, atway isthay omentmay, ouldcay avehay ivengay emay eatergray easureplay anthay ethay 
arrivalway ofway ymay atherfay. Iway etchedstray outway ymay andhay otay imhay andway iedcray, "Areway 
youway, enthay, afesay--and Elizabethway--and Ernestway?" Ymay atherfay almedcay emay ithway 
assurancesway ofway eirthay elfareway andway endeavouredway, ybay ellingdway onway esethay 
ubjectssay osay interestingway otay ymay earthay, otay aiseray ymay espondingday iritsspay; 
utbay ehay oonsay eltfay atthay away isonpray annotcay ebay ethay abodeway ofway eerfulnesschay. 

"Atwhay away aceplay isway isthay atthay youway inhabitway, ymay onsay!" aidsay ehay, ookinglay 
ournfullymay atway ethay arredbay indowsway andway etchedwray appearanceway ofway ethay oomray. 
"Youway avelledtray otay eeksay appinesshay, utbay away atalityfay eemssay otay ursuepay youway. 
Andway oorpay Ervalclay--" 

Ethay amenay ofway ymay unfortunateway andway urderedmay iendfray asway anway agitationway ootay 
eatgray otay ebay enduredway inway ymay eakway atestay; Iway edshay earstay. "Alasway! Yesway, ymay 
atherfay," epliedray Iway; "omesay estinyday ofway ethay ostmay orriblehay indkay angshay overway 
emay, andway Iway ustmay ivelay otay ulfilfay itway, orway urelysay Iway ouldshay avehay iedday onway ethay 
offincay ofway Enryhay." 

Eway ereway otnay allowedway otay onversecay orfay anyway engthlay ofway imetay, orfay ethay 
ecariouspray atestay ofway ymay ealthhay enderedray everyway ecautionpray ecessarynay atthay 
ouldcay ensureway anquillitytray. Mray. Irwinkay amecay inway andway insistedway atthay ymay 
engthstray ouldshay otnay ebay exhaustedway ybay ootay uchmay exertionway. Utbay ethay 
appearanceway ofway ymay atherfay asway otay emay ikelay atthay ofway ymay oodgay angelway, andway Iway 
aduallygray ecoveredray ymay ealthhay. 

Asway ymay icknesssay uittedqay emay, Iway asway absorbedway ybay away oomyglay andway ackblay 
elancholymay atthay othingnay ouldcay issipateday. Ethay imageway ofway Ervalclay asway 
oreverfay eforebay emay, astlyghay andway urderedmay. Oremay anthay onceway ethay agitationway 
intoway ichwhay esethay eflectionsray ewthray emay ademay ymay iendsfray eaddray away angerousday 
elapseray. Alasway! Ywhay idday eythay eservepray osay iserablemay andway etestedday away 
ifelay? Itway asway urelysay atthay Iway ightmay ulfilfay ymay estinyday, ichwhay isway ownay 
awingdray otay away oseclay. Oonsay, ohway, eryvay oonsay, illway eathday extinguishway esethay 
obbingsthray andway elieveray emay omfray ethay ightymay eightway ofway anguishway atthay earsbay 
emay otay ethay ustday; andway, inway executingway ethay awardway ofway usticejay, Iway allshay alsoway 
inksay otay estray. Enthay ethay appearanceway ofway eathday asway istantday, althoughway ethay 
ishway asway everway esentpray otay ymay oughtsthay; andway Iway oftenway atsay orfay ourshay 
otionlessmay andway eechlessspay, ishingway orfay omesay ightymay evolutionray atthay 
ightmay urybay emay andway ymay estroyerday inway itsway uinsray. 

Ethay easonsay ofway ethay assizesway approachedway. Iway adhay alreadyway eenbay eethray onthsmay 
inway isonpray, andway althoughway Iway asway illstay eakway andway inway ontinualcay angerday ofway away 
elapseray, Iway asway obligedway otay aveltray earlynay away undredhay ilesmay otay ethay ountrycay 
owntay erewhay ethay ourtcay asway eldhay. Mray. Irwinkay argedchay imselfhay ithway everyway 
arecay ofway ollectingcay itnessesway andway arrangingway ymay efenceday. Iway asway aredspay 
ethay isgraceday ofway appearingway ubliclypay asway away iminalcray, asway ethay asecay asway otnay 
oughtbray eforebay ethay ourtcay atthay ecidesday onway ifelay andway eathday. Ethay andgray 
uryjay ejectedray ethay illbay, onway itsway eingbay ovedpray atthay Iway asway onway ethay Orkneyway 
Islandsway atway ethay ourhay ethay odybay ofway ymay iendfray asway oundfay; andway away ortnightfay 
afterway ymay emovalray Iway asway iberatedlay omfray isonpray. 

Ymay atherfay asway enrapturedway onway indingfay emay eedfray omfray ethay exationsvay ofway away 
iminalcray argechay, atthay Iway asway againway allowedway otay eathebray ethay eshfray 
atmosphereway andway ermittedpay otay eturnray otay ymay ativenay ountrycay. Iway idday otnay 
articipatepay inway esethay eelingsfay, orfay otay emay ethay allsway ofway away ungeonday orway away 
alacepay ereway alikeway atefulhay. Ethay upcay ofway ifelay asway oisonedpay oreverfay, andway 
althoughway ethay unsay oneshay uponway emay, asway uponway ethay appyhay andway aygay ofway earthay, Iway 
awsay aroundway emay othingnay utbay away enseday andway ightfulfray arknessday, enetratedpay ybay 
onay ightlay utbay ethay immerglay ofway otway eyesway atthay aredglay uponway emay. Ometimessay 
eythay ereway ethay expressiveway eyesway ofway Enryhay, anguishinglay inway eathday, ethay arkday 
orbsway earlynay overedcay ybay ethay idslay andway ethay onglay ackblay asheslay atthay ingedfray 
emthay; ometimessay itway asway ethay ateryway, oudedclay eyesway ofway ethay onstermay, asway Iway 
irstfay awsay emthay inway ymay amberchay atway Ingolstadtway. 

Ymay atherfay iedtray otay awakenway inway emay ethay eelingsfay ofway affectionway. Ehay alkedtay 
ofway Enevagay, ichwhay Iway ouldshay oonsay isitvay, ofway Elizabethway andway Ernestway; utbay 
esethay ordsway onlyway ewdray eepday oansgray omfray emay. Ometimessay, indeedway, Iway eltfay away 
ishway orfay appinesshay andway oughtthay ithway elancholymay elightday ofway ymay elovedbay 
ousincay orway ongedlay, ithway away evouringday aladiemay uday ayspay, otay eesay onceway oremay 
ethay ueblay akelay andway apidray Onerhay, atthay adhay eenbay osay earday otay emay inway earlyway 
ildhoodchay; utbay ymay eneralgay atestay ofway eelingfay asway away orportay inway ichwhay away 
isonpray asway asway elcomeway away esidenceray asway ethay ivinestday enescay inway aturenay; andway 
esethay itsfay ereway eldomsay interruptedway utbay ybay aroxysmspay ofway anguishway andway 
espairday. Atway esethay omentsmay Iway oftenway endeavouredway otay utpay anway endway otay ethay 
existenceway Iway oathedlay, andway itway equiredray unceasingway attendanceway andway igilancevay 
otay estrainray emay omfray ommittingcay omesay eadfuldray actway ofway iolencevay. 

Yetway oneway utyday emainedray otay emay, ethay ecollectionray ofway ichwhay inallyfay 
iumphedtray overway ymay elfishsay espairday. Itway asway ecessarynay atthay Iway ouldshay 
eturnray ithoutway elayday otay Enevagay, erethay otay atchway overway ethay iveslay ofway osethay 
Iway osay ondlyfay ovedlay andway otay ielay inway aitway orfay ethay urderermay, atthay ifway anyway 
ancechay edlay emay otay ethay aceplay ofway ishay oncealmentcay, orway ifway ehay aredday againway otay 
astblay emay ybay ishay esencepray, Iway ightmay, ithway unfailingway aimway, utpay anway endway otay 
ethay existenceway ofway ethay onstrousmay imageway ichwhay Iway adhay enduedway ithway ethay 
ockerymay ofway away oulsay illstay oremay onstrousmay. Ymay atherfay illstay esiredday otay 
elayday ourway epartureday, earfulfay atthay Iway ouldcay otnay ustainsay ethay atiguesfay ofway away 
ourneyjay, orfay Iway asway away atteredshay eckwray--the adowshay ofway away umanhay eingbay. Ymay 
engthstray asway onegay. Iway asway away eremay eletonskay, andway everfay ightnay andway ayday 
eyedpray uponway ymay astedway amefray. Illstay, asway Iway urgedway ourway eavinglay Irelandway 
ithway uchsay inquietudeway andway impatienceway, ymay atherfay oughtthay itway estbay otay 
yieldway. Eway ooktay ourway assagepay onway oardbay away esselvay oundbay orfay Avrehay-de-Grace 
andway ailedsay ithway away airfay indway omfray ethay Irishway oresshay. Itway asway idnightmay. Iway 
aylay onway ethay eckday ookinglay atway ethay arsstay andway isteninglay otay ethay ashingday ofway 
ethay avesway. Iway ailedhay ethay arknessday atthay utshay Irelandway omfray ymay ightsay, andway 
ymay ulsepay eatbay ithway away everishfay oyjay enwhay Iway eflectedray atthay Iway ouldshay oonsay 
eesay Enevagay. Ethay astpay appearedway otay emay inway ethay ightlay ofway away ightfulfray eamdray; 
yetway ethay esselvay inway ichwhay Iway asway, ethay indway atthay ewblay emay omfray ethay etestedday 
oreshay ofway Irelandway, andway ethay easay ichwhay urroundedsay emay oldtay emay ootay orciblyfay 
atthay Iway asway eceivedday ybay onay isionvay andway atthay Ervalclay, ymay iendfray andway 
earestday ompanioncay, adhay allenfay away ictimvay otay emay andway ethay onstermay ofway ymay 
eationcray. Iway epassedray, inway ymay emorymay, ymay olewhay ifelay--my uietqay appinesshay 
ilewhay esidingray ithway ymay amilyfay inway Enevagay, ethay eathday ofway ymay othermay, andway ymay 
epartureday orfay Ingolstadtway. Iway ememberedray, udderingshay, ethay admay enthusiasmway 
atthay urriedhay emay onway otay ethay eationcray ofway ymay ideoushay enemyway, andway Iway alledcay otay 
indmay ethay ightnay inway ichwhay ehay irstfay ivedlay. Iway asway unableway otay ursuepay ethay 
aintray ofway oughtthay; away ousandthay eelingsfay essedpray uponway emay, andway Iway eptway 
itterlybay. Everway incesay ymay ecoveryray omfray ethay everfay Iway adhay eenbay inway ethay 
ustomcay ofway akingtay everyway ightnay away allsmay uantityqay ofway audanumlay, orfay itway asway 
ybay eansmay ofway isthay ugdray onlyway atthay Iway asway enabledway otay aingay ethay estray 
ecessarynay orfay ethay eservationpray ofway ifelay. Oppressedway ybay ethay ecollectionray 
ofway ymay ariousvay isfortunesmay, Iway ownay allowedsway oubleday ymay usualway uantityqay andway 
oonsay eptslay ofoundlypray. Utbay eepslay idday otnay affordway emay espiteray omfray 
oughtthay andway iserymay; ymay eamsdray esentedpray away ousandthay objectsway atthay aredscay 
emay. Owardstay orningmay Iway asway ossessedpay ybay away indkay ofway ightmarenay; Iway eltfay ethay 
iendfay's aspgray inway ymay ecknay andway ouldcay otnay eefray yselfmay omfray itway; oansgray andway 
iescray angray inway ymay earsway. Ymay atherfay, owhay asway atchingway overway emay, erceivingpay 
ymay estlessnessray, awokeway emay; ethay ashingday avesway ereway aroundway, ethay oudyclay 
yskay aboveway, ethay iendfay asway otnay erehay: away ensesay ofway ecuritysay, away eelingfay atthay 
away ucetray asway establishedway etweenbay ethay esentpray ourhay andway ethay irresistibleway, 
isastrousday uturefay impartedway otay emay away indkay ofway almcay orgetfulnessfay, ofway ichwhay 
ethay umanhay indmay isway ybay itsway ucturestray eculiarlypay usceptiblesay. 



Apterchay 22 

Ethay oyagevay amecay otay anway endway. Eway andedlay, andway oceededpray otay Arispay. Iway oonsay 
oundfay atthay Iway adhay overtaxedway ymay engthstray andway atthay Iway ustmay eposeray eforebay Iway 
ouldcay ontinuecay ymay ourneyjay. Ymay atherfay's arecay andway attentionsway ereway 
indefatigableway, utbay ehay idday otnay owknay ethay originway ofway ymay ufferingssay andway 
oughtsay erroneousway ethodsmay otay emedyray ethay incurableway illway. Ehay ishedway emay otay 
eeksay amusementway inway ocietysay. Iway abhorredway ethay acefay ofway anmay. Ohway, otnay 
abhorredway! Eythay ereway ymay ethrenbray, ymay ellowfay eingsbay, andway Iway eltfay 
attractedway evenway otay ethay ostmay epulsiveray amongway emthay, asway otay eaturescray ofway anway 
angelicway aturenay andway elestialcay echanismmay. Utbay Iway eltfay atthay Iway adhay onay ightray 
otay areshay eirthay intercourseway. Iway adhay unchainedway anway enemyway amongway emthay osewhay 
oyjay itway asway otay edshay eirthay oodblay andway otay evelray inway eirthay oansgray. Owhay eythay 
ouldway, eachway andway allway, abhorway emay andway unthay emay omfray ethay orldway idday eythay owknay 
ymay unhallowedway actsway andway ethay imescray ichwhay adhay eirthay ourcesay inway emay! 

Ymay atherfay yieldedway atway engthlay otay ymay esireday otay avoidway ocietysay andway ovestray ybay 
ariousvay argumentsway otay anishbay ymay espairday. Ometimessay ehay oughtthay atthay Iway 
eltfay eeplyday ethay egradationday ofway eingbay obligedway otay answerway away argechay ofway 
urdermay, andway ehay endeavouredway otay ovepray otay emay ethay utilityfay ofway idepray. 

"Alasway! Ymay atherfay," aidsay Iway, "owhay ittlelay oday youway owknay emay. Umanhay eingsbay, 
eirthay eelingsfay andway assionspay, ouldway indeedway ebay egradedday ifway uchsay away etchwray 
asway Iway eltfay idepray. Ustinejay, oorpay unhappyway Ustinejay, asway asway innocentway asway Iway, 
andway eshay ufferedsay ethay amesay argechay; eshay iedday orfay itway; andway Iway amway ethay ausecay 
ofway isthay--I urderedmay erhay. Illiamway, Ustinejay, andway Enryhay--they allway iedday ybay 
ymay andshay." 

Ymay atherfay adhay oftenway, uringday ymay imprisonmentway, eardhay emay akemay ethay amesay 
assertionway; enwhay Iway usthay accusedway yselfmay, ehay ometimessay eemedsay otay esireday anway 
explanationway, andway atway othersway ehay appearedway otay onsidercay itway asway ethay offspringway 
ofway eliriumday, andway atthay, uringday ymay illnessway, omesay ideaway ofway isthay indkay adhay 
esentedpray itselfway otay ymay imaginationway, ethay emembranceray ofway ichwhay Iway 
eservedpray inway ymay onvalescencecay. 

Iway avoidedway explanationway andway aintainedmay away ontinualcay ilencesay oncerningcay ethay 
etchwray Iway adhay eatedcray. Iway adhay away ersuasionpay atthay Iway ouldshay ebay upposedsay 
admay, andway isthay inway itselfway ouldway oreverfay avehay ainedchay ymay onguetay. Utbay, 
esidesbay, Iway ouldcay otnay ingbray yselfmay otay iscloseday away ecretsay ichwhay ouldway illfay 
ymay earerhay ithway onsternationcay andway akemay earfay andway unnaturalway orrorhay ethay 
inmatesway ofway ishay eastbray. Iway eckedchay, ereforethay, ymay impatientway irstthay orfay 
ympathysay andway asway ilentsay enwhay Iway ouldway avehay ivengay ethay orldway otay avehay 
onfidedcay ethay atalfay ecretsay. Yetway, illstay, ordsway ikelay osethay Iway avehay 
ecordedray ouldway urstbay uncontrollablyway omfray emay. Iway ouldcay offerway onay 
explanationway ofway emthay, utbay eirthay uthtray inway artpay elievedray ethay urdenbay ofway ymay 
ysteriousmay oeway. Uponway isthay occasionway ymay atherfay aidsay, ithway anway expressionway 
ofway unboundedway onderway, "Ymay earestday Ictorvay, atwhay infatuationway isway isthay? Ymay 
earday onsay, Iway entreatway youway evernay otay akemay uchsay anway assertionway againway." 

"Iway amway otnay admay," Iway iedcray energeticallyway; "ethay unsay andway ethay eavenshay, owhay 
avehay iewedvay ymay operationsway, ancay earbay itnessway ofway ymay uthtray. Iway amway ethay 
assassinway ofway osethay ostmay innocentway ictimsvay; eythay iedday ybay ymay achinationsmay. 
Away ousandthay imestay ouldway Iway avehay edshay ymay ownway oodblay, opdray ybay opdray, otay avehay 
avedsay eirthay iveslay; utbay Iway ouldcay otnay, ymay atherfay, indeedway Iway ouldcay otnay 
acrificesay ethay olewhay umanhay aceray." 

Ethay onclusioncay ofway isthay eechspay onvincedcay ymay atherfay atthay ymay ideasway ereway 
erangedday, andway ehay instantlyway angedchay ethay ubjectsay ofway ourway onversationcay andway 
endeavouredway otay alterway ethay oursecay ofway ymay oughtsthay. Ehay ishedway asway uchmay asway 
ossiblepay otay obliterateway ethay emorymay ofway ethay enesscay atthay adhay akentay aceplay inway 
Irelandway andway evernay alludedway otay emthay orway ufferedsay emay otay eakspay ofway ymay 
isfortunesmay. 

Asway imetay assedpay awayway Iway ecamebay oremay almcay; iserymay adhay erhay ellingdway inway ymay 
earthay, utbay Iway onay ongerlay alkedtay inway ethay amesay incoherentway annermay ofway ymay ownway 
imescray; ufficientsay orfay emay asway ethay onsciousnesscay ofway emthay. Ybay ethay utmostway 
elfsay-violence Iway urbedcay ethay imperiousway oicevay ofway etchednesswray, ichwhay 
ometimessay esiredday otay eclareday itselfway otay ethay olewhay orldway, andway ymay annersmay 
ereway almercay andway oremay omposedcay anthay eythay adhay everway eenbay incesay ymay ourneyjay 
otay ethay easay ofway iceway. Away ewfay aysday eforebay eway eftlay Arispay onway ourway ayway otay 
Itzerlandsway, Iway eceivedray ethay ollowingfay etterlay omfray Elizabethway: 


"Ymay earday Iendfray, 

"Itway avegay emay ethay eatestgray easureplay otay eceiveray away etterlay omfray ymay uncleway 
atedday atway Arispay; youway areway onay ongerlay atway away ormidablefay istanceday, andway Iway aymay 
opehay otay eesay youway inway esslay anthay away ortnightfay. Ymay oorpay ousincay, owhay uchmay youway 
ustmay avehay ufferedsay! Iway expectway otay eesay youway ookinglay evenway oremay illway anthay 
enwhay youway uittedqay Enevagay. Isthay interway ashay eenbay assedpay ostmay iserablymay, 
orturedtay asway Iway avehay eenbay ybay anxiousway uspensesay; yetway Iway opehay otay eesay eacepay inway 
yourway ountenancecay andway otay indfay atthay yourway earthay isway otnay otallytay oidvay ofway 
omfortcay andway anquillitytray. 

"Yetway Iway earfay atthay ethay amesay eelingsfay ownay existway atthay ademay youway osay iserablemay 
away yearway agoway, evenway erhapspay augmentedway ybay imetay. Iway ouldway otnay isturbday youway atway 
isthay eriodpay, enwhay osay anymay isfortunesmay eighway uponway youway, utbay away 
onversationcay atthay Iway adhay ithway ymay uncleway eviouspray otay ishay epartureday endersray 
omesay explanationway ecessarynay eforebay eway eetmay. Explanationway! Youway aymay 
ossiblypay aysay, Atwhay ancay Elizabethway avehay otay explainway? Ifway youway eallyray aysay 
isthay, ymay uestionsqay areway answeredway andway allway ymay oubtsday atisfiedsay. Utbay youway 
areway istantday omfray emay, andway itway isway ossiblepay atthay youway aymay eaddray andway yetway ebay 
easedplay ithway isthay explanationway; andway inway away obabilitypray ofway isthay eingbay ethay 
asecay, Iway areday otnay anyway ongerlay ostponepay itingwray atwhay, uringday yourway absenceway, 
Iway avehay oftenway ishedway otay expressway otay youway utbay avehay evernay adhay ethay ouragecay otay 
eginbay. 

"Youway ellway owknay, Ictorvay, atthay ourway unionway adhay eenbay ethay avouritefay anplay ofway 
yourway arentspay everway incesay ourway infancyway. Eway ereway oldtay isthay enwhay youngway, andway 
aughttay otay ooklay orwardfay otay itway asway anway eventway atthay ouldway ertainlycay aketay 
aceplay. Eway ereway affectionateway ayfellowsplay uringday ildhoodchay, andway, Iway 
elievebay, earday andway aluedvay iendsfray otay oneway anotherway asway eway ewgray olderway. Utbay 
asway otherbray andway istersay oftenway entertainway away ivelylay affectionway owardstay eachway 
otherway ithoutway esiringday away oremay intimateway unionway, aymay otnay uchsay alsoway ebay ourway 
asecay? Elltay emay, earestday Ictorvay. Answerway emay, Iway onjurecay youway ybay ourway utualmay 
appinesshay, ithway implesay uthtray--Do youway otnay ovelay anotherway? 

"Youway avehay avelledtray; youway avehay entspay everalsay yearsway ofway yourway ifelay atway 
Ingolstadtway; andway Iway onfesscay otay youway, ymay iendfray, atthay enwhay Iway awsay youway astlay 
autumnway osay unhappyway, yingflay otay olitudesay omfray ethay ocietysay ofway everyway 
eaturecray, Iway ouldcay otnay elphay upposingsay atthay youway ightmay egretray ourway 
onnectioncay andway elievebay yourselfway oundbay inway onourhay otay ulfilfay ethay ishesway ofway 
yourway arentspay, althoughway eythay opposedway emselvesthay otay yourway inclinationsway. 
Utbay isthay isway alsefay easoningray. Iway onfesscay otay youway, ymay iendfray, atthay Iway ovelay 
youway andway atthay inway ymay airyway eamsdray ofway uturityfay youway avehay eenbay ymay onstantcay 
iendfray andway ompanioncay. Utbay itway isway yourway appinesshay Iway esireday asway ellway asway ymay 
ownway enwhay Iway eclareday otay youway atthay ourway arriagemay ouldway enderray emay eternallyway 
iserablemay unlessway itway ereway ethay ictateday ofway yourway ownway eefray oicechay. Evenway ownay 
Iway eepway otay inkthay atthay, ornebay ownday asway youway areway ybay ethay uellestcray 
isfortunesmay, youway aymay iflestay, ybay ethay ordway 'onourhay,' allway opehay ofway atthay 
ovelay andway appinesshay ichwhay ouldway aloneway estoreray youway otay yourselfway. Iway, owhay 
avehay osay isinterestedday anway affectionway orfay youway, aymay increaseway yourway iseriesmay 
enfoldtay ybay eingbay anway obstacleway otay yourway ishesway. Ahway! Ictorvay, ebay assuredway 
atthay yourway ousincay andway aymateplay ashay ootay inceresay away ovelay orfay youway otnay otay ebay 
ademay iserablemay ybay isthay uppositionsay. Ebay appyhay, ymay iendfray; andway ifway youway 
obeyway emay inway isthay oneway equestray, emainray atisfiedsay atthay othingnay onway earthway 
illway avehay ethay owerpay otay interruptway ymay anquillitytray. 

"Oday otnay etlay isthay etterlay isturbday youway; oday otnay answerway omorrowtay, orway ethay 
extnay ayday, orway evenway untilway youway omecay, ifway itway illway ivegay youway ainpay. Ymay uncleway 
illway endsay emay ewsnay ofway yourway ealthhay, andway ifway Iway eesay utbay oneway ilesmay onway yourway 
ipslay enwhay eway eetmay, occasionedway ybay isthay orway anyway otherway exertionway ofway inemay, Iway 
allshay eednay onay otherway appinesshay. 

"Elizabethway Avenzalay 


"Enevagay, Aymay 18thay, 17--" 


Isthay etterlay evivedray inway ymay emorymay atwhay Iway adhay eforebay orgottenfay, ethay 
eatthray ofway ethay iendfay--"I ILLWAY EBAY ITHWAY YOUWAY ONWAY YOURWAY EDDINGWAY-NIGHT!" Uchsay 
asway ymay entencesay, andway onway atthay ightnay ouldway ethay aemonday employway everyway artway otay 
estroyday emay andway eartay emay omfray ethay impseglay ofway appinesshay ichwhay omisedpray 
artlypay otay onsolecay ymay ufferingssay. Onway atthay ightnay ehay adhay eterminedday otay 
onsummatecay ishay imescray ybay ymay eathday. Ellway, ebay itway osay; away eadlyday ugglestray 
ouldway enthay assuredlyway aketay aceplay, inway ichwhay ifway ehay ereway ictoriousvay Iway 
ouldshay ebay atway eacepay andway ishay owerpay overway emay ebay atway anway endway. Ifway ehay ereway 
anquishedvay, Iway ouldshay ebay away eefray anmay. Alasway! Atwhay eedomfray? Uchsay asway ethay 
easantpay enjoysway enwhay ishay amilyfay avehay eenbay assacredmay eforebay ishay eyesway, ishay 
ottagecay urntbay, ishay andslay aidlay asteway, andway ehay isway urnedtay adriftway, omelesshay, 
ennilesspay, andway aloneway, utbay eefray. Uchsay ouldway ebay ymay ibertylay exceptway atthay inway 
ymay Elizabethway Iway ossessedpay away easuretray, alasway, alancedbay ybay osethay orrorshay ofway 
emorseray andway uiltgay ichwhay ouldway ursuepay emay untilway eathday. 

Eetsway andway elovedbay Elizabethway! Iway eadray andway ereadray erhay etterlay, andway omesay 
oftenedsay eelingsfay olestay intoway ymay earthay andway aredday otay isperwhay aradisiacalpay 
eamsdray ofway ovelay andway oyjay; utbay ethay appleway asway alreadyway eatenway, andway ethay 
angelway's armway aredbay otay ivedray emay omfray allway opehay. Yetway Iway ouldway ieday otay akemay 
erhay appyhay. Ifway ethay onstermay executedway ishay eatthray, eathday asway inevitableway; 
yetway, againway, Iway onsideredcay etherwhay ymay arriagemay ouldway astenhay ymay atefay. Ymay 
estructionday ightmay indeedway arriveway away ewfay onthsmay oonersay, utbay ifway ymay orturertay 
ouldshay uspectsay atthay Iway ostponedpay itway, influencedway ybay ishay enacesmay, ehay ouldway 
urelysay indfay otherway andway erhapspay oremay eadfuldray eansmay ofway evengeray. 

Ehay adhay owedvay OTAY EBAY ITHWAY EMAY ONWAY YMAY EDDINGWAY-NIGHT, yetway ehay idday otnay onsidercay 
atthay eatthray asway indingbay imhay otay eacepay inway ethay eantimemay, orfay asway ifway otay owshay 
emay atthay ehay asway otnay yetway atiatedsay ithway oodblay, ehay adhay urderedmay Ervalclay 
immediatelyway afterway ethay enunciationway ofway ishay eatsthray. Iway esolvedray, 
ereforethay, atthay ifway ymay immediateway unionway ithway ymay ousincay ouldway onducecay 
eitherway otay ershay orway ymay atherfay's appinesshay, ymay adversaryway's esignsday againstway 
ymay ifelay ouldshay otnay etardray itway away inglesay ourhay. 

Inway isthay atestay ofway indmay Iway otewray otay Elizabethway. Ymay etterlay asway almcay andway 
affectionateway. "Iway earfay, ymay elovedbay irlgay," Iway aidsay, "ittlelay appinesshay 
emainsray orfay usway onway earthway; yetway allway atthay Iway aymay oneway ayday enjoyway isway entredcay inway 
youway. Asechay awayway yourway idleway earsfay; otay youway aloneway oday Iway onsecratecay ymay ifelay 
andway ymay endeavoursway orfay ontentmentcay. Iway avehay oneway ecretsay, Elizabethway, away 
eadfuldray oneway; enwhay evealedray otay youway, itway illway illchay yourway amefray ithway 
orrorhay, andway enthay, arfay omfray eingbay urprisedsay atway ymay iserymay, youway illway onlyway 
onderway atthay Iway urvivesay atwhay Iway avehay enduredway. Iway illway onfidecay isthay aletay ofway 
iserymay andway errortay otay youway ethay ayday afterway ourway arriagemay allshay aketay aceplay, 
orfay, ymay eetsway ousincay, erethay ustmay ebay erfectpay onfidencecay etweenbay usway. Utbay 
untilway enthay, Iway onjurecay youway, oday otnay entionmay orway alludeway otay itway. Isthay Iway ostmay 
earnestlyway entreatway, andway Iway owknay youway illway omplycay." 

Inway aboutway away eekway afterway ethay arrivalway ofway Elizabethway's etterlay eway eturnedray otay 
Enevagay. Ethay eetsway irlgay elcomedway emay ithway armway affectionway, yetway earstay ereway 
inway erhay eyesway asway eshay eheldbay ymay emaciatedway amefray andway everishfay eekschay. Iway 
awsay away angechay inway erhay alsoway. Eshay asway innerthay andway adhay ostlay uchmay ofway atthay 
eavenlyhay ivacityvay atthay adhay eforebay armedchay emay; utbay erhay entlenessgay andway 
oftsay ookslay ofway ompassioncay ademay erhay away oremay itfay ompanioncay orfay oneway astedblay 
andway iserablemay asway Iway asway. Ethay anquillitytray ichwhay Iway ownay enjoyedway idday otnay 
endureway. Emorymay oughtbray adnessmay ithway itway, andway enwhay Iway oughtthay ofway atwhay adhay 
assedpay, away ealray insanityway ossessedpay emay; ometimessay Iway asway uriousfay andway urntbay 
ithway ageray, ometimessay owlay andway espondentday. Iway eithernay okespay ornay ookedlay atway 
anyoneway, utbay atsay otionlessmay, ewilderedbay ybay ethay ultitudemay ofway iseriesmay 
atthay overcameway emay. 

Elizabethway aloneway adhay ethay owerpay otay awdray emay omfray esethay itsfay; erhay entlegay 
oicevay ouldway oothesay emay enwhay ansportedtray ybay assionpay andway inspireway emay ithway 
umanhay eelingsfay enwhay unksay inway orportay. Eshay eptway ithway emay andway orfay emay. Enwhay 
easonray eturnedray, eshay ouldway emonstrateray andway endeavourway otay inspireway emay ithway 
esignationray. Ahway! Itway isway ellway orfay ethay unfortunateway otay ebay esignedray, utbay 
orfay ethay uiltygay erethay isway onay eacepay. Ethay agoniesway ofway emorseray oisonpay ethay 
uxurylay erethay isway otherwiseway ometimessay oundfay inway indulgingway ethay excessway ofway 
iefgray. Oonsay afterway ymay arrivalway ymay atherfay okespay ofway ymay immediateway arriagemay 
ithway Elizabethway. Iway emainedray ilentsay. 

"Avehay youway, enthay, omesay otherway attachmentway?" 

"Onenay onway earthway. Iway ovelay Elizabethway andway ooklay orwardfay otay ourway unionway ithway 
elightday. Etlay ethay ayday ereforethay ebay ixedfay; andway onway itway Iway illway onsecratecay 
yselfmay, inway ifelay orway eathday, otay ethay appinesshay ofway ymay ousincay." 

"Ymay earday Ictorvay, oday otnay eakspay usthay. Eavyhay isfortunesmay avehay efallenbay 
usway, utbay etlay usway onlyway ingclay oserclay otay atwhay emainsray andway ansfertray ourway ovelay 
orfay osethay omwhay eway avehay ostlay otay osethay owhay yetway ivelay. Ourway irclecay illway ebay 
allsmay utbay oundbay oseclay ybay ethay iestay ofway affectionway andway utualmay isfortunemay. 
Andway enwhay imetay allshay avehay oftenedsay yourway espairday, ewnay andway earday objectsway ofway 
arecay illway ebay ornbay otay eplaceray osethay ofway omwhay eway avehay eenbay osay uellycray 
eprivedday." 

Uchsay ereway ethay essonslay ofway ymay atherfay. Utbay otay emay ethay emembranceray ofway ethay 
eatthray eturnedray; ornay ancay youway onderway atthay, omnipotentway asway ethay iendfay adhay 
yetway eenbay inway ishay eedsday ofway oodblay, Iway ouldshay almostway egardray imhay asway 
invincibleway, andway atthay enwhay ehay adhay onouncedpray ethay ordsway "Iway ALLSHAY EBAY ITHWAY 
YOUWAY ONWAY YOURWAY EDDINGWAY-NIGHT," Iway ouldshay egardray ethay eatenedthray atefay asway
