unavoidableway. Utbay eathday asway onay evilway otay emay ifway ethay osslay ofway Elizabethway ereway 
alancedbay ithway itway, andway Iway ereforethay, ithway away ontentedcay andway evenway eerfulchay 
ountenancecay, agreedway ithway ymay atherfay atthay ifway ymay ousincay ouldway onsentcay, ethay 
eremonycay ouldshay aketay aceplay inway entay aysday, andway usthay utpay, asway Iway imaginedway, 
ethay ealsay otay ymay atefay. 

Eatgray Odgay! Ifway orfay oneway instantway Iway adhay oughtthay atwhay ightmay ebay ethay ellishhay 
intentionway ofway ymay iendishfay adversaryway, Iway ouldway atherray avehay anishedbay yselfmay 
oreverfay omfray ymay ativenay ountrycay andway anderedway away iendlessfray outcastway overway 
ethay earthway anthay avehay onsentedcay otay isthay iserablemay arriagemay. Utbay, asway ifway 
ossessedpay ofway agicmay owerspay, ethay onstermay adhay indedblay emay otay ishay ealray 
intentionsway; andway enwhay Iway oughtthay atthay Iway adhay eparedpray onlyway ymay ownway eathday, Iway 
astenedhay atthay ofway away arfay earerday ictimvay. 

Asway ethay eriodpay ixedfay orfay ourway arriagemay ewdray earernay, etherwhay omfray 
owardicecay orway away opheticpray eelingfay, Iway eltfay ymay earthay inksay ithinway emay. Utbay 
Iway oncealedcay ymay eelingsfay ybay anway appearanceway ofway ilarityhay atthay oughtbray 
ilessmay andway oyjay otay ethay ountenancecay ofway ymay atherfay, utbay ardlyhay eceivedday ethay 
everway-watchful andway icernay eyeway ofway Elizabethway. Eshay ookedlay orwardfay otay ourway 
unionway ithway acidplay ontentmentcay, otnay unmingledway ithway away ittlelay earfay, ichwhay 
astpay isfortunesmay adhay impressedway, atthay atwhay ownay appearedway ertaincay andway 
angibletay appinesshay ightmay oonsay issipateday intoway anway airyway eamdray andway eavelay onay 
acetray utbay eepday andway everlastingway egretray. Eparationspray ereway ademay orfay ethay 
eventway, ongratulatorycay isitsvay ereway eceivedray, andway allway oreway away ilingsmay 
appearanceway. Iway utshay upway, asway ellway asway Iway ouldcay, inway ymay ownway earthay ethay anxietyway 
atthay eyedpray erethay andway enteredway ithway eemingsay earnestnessway intoway ethay ansplay 
ofway ymay atherfay, althoughway eythay ightmay onlyway ervesay asway ethay ecorationsday ofway ymay 
agedytray. Oughthray ymay atherfay's exertionsway away artpay ofway ethay inheritanceway ofway 
Elizabethway adhay eenbay estoredray otay erhay ybay ethay Austrianway overnmentgay. Away allsmay 
ossessionpay onway ethay oresshay ofway Omocay elongedbay otay erhay. Itway asway agreedway atthay, 
immediatelyway afterway ourway unionway, eway ouldshay oceedpray otay Illavay Avenzalay andway 
endspay ourway irstfay aysday ofway appinesshay esidebay ethay eautifulbay akelay earnay ichwhay 
itway oodstay. 

Inway ethay eantimemay Iway ooktay everyway ecautionpray otay efendday ymay ersonpay inway asecay ethay 
iendfay ouldshay openlyway attackway emay. Iway arriedcay istolspay andway away aggerday 
onstantlycay aboutway emay andway asway everway onway ethay atchway otay eventpray artificeway, andway 
ybay esethay eansmay ainedgay away eatergray egreeday ofway anquillitytray. Indeedway, asway ethay 
eriodpay approachedway, ethay eatthray appearedway oremay asway away elusionday, otnay otay ebay 
egardedray asway orthyway otay isturbday ymay eacepay, ilewhay ethay appinesshay Iway opedhay orfay 
inway ymay arriagemay oreway away eatergray appearanceway ofway ertaintycay asway ethay ayday ixedfay 
orfay itsway olemnizationsay ewdray earernay andway Iway eardhay itway ontinuallycay okenspay ofway 
asway anway occurrenceway ichwhay onay accidentway ouldcay ossiblypay eventpray. 

Elizabethway eemedsay appyhay; ymay anquiltray emeanourday ontributedcay eatlygray otay 
almcay erhay indmay. Utbay onway ethay ayday atthay asway otay ulfilfay ymay ishesway andway ymay 
estinyday, eshay asway elancholymay, andway away esentimentpray ofway evilway ervadedpay erhay; 
andway erhapspay alsoway eshay oughtthay ofway ethay eadfuldray ecretsay ichwhay Iway adhay 
omisedpray otay evealray otay erhay onway ethay ollowingfay ayday. Ymay atherfay asway inway ethay 
eantimemay overjoyedway andway inway ethay ustlebay ofway eparationpray onlyway ecognizedray inway 
ethay elancholymay ofway ishay iecenay ethay iffidenceday ofway away idebray. 

Afterway ethay eremonycay asway erformedpay away argelay artypay assembledway atway ymay 
atherfay's, utbay itway asway agreedway atthay Elizabethway andway Iway ouldshay ommencecay ourway 
ourneyjay ybay aterway, eepingslay atthay ightnay atway Evianway andway ontinuingcay ourway 
oyagevay onway ethay ollowingfay ayday. Ethay ayday asway airfay, ethay indway avourablefay; 
allway iledsmay onway ourway uptialnay embarkationway. 

Osethay ereway ethay astlay omentsmay ofway ymay ifelay uringday ichwhay Iway enjoyedway ethay 
eelingfay ofway appinesshay. Eway assedpay apidlyray alongway; ethay unsay asway othay, utbay eway 
ereway elteredshay omfray itsway aysray ybay away indkay ofway anopycay ilewhay eway enjoyedway ethay 
eautybay ofway ethay enescay, ometimessay onway oneway idesay ofway ethay akelay, erewhay eway awsay 
Ontmay Alevesay, ethay easantplay anksbay ofway Ontalegremay, andway atway away istanceday, 
urmountingsay allway, ethay eautifulbay Ontmay Ancblay andway ethay assemblageway ofway owysnay 
ountainsmay atthay inway ainvay endeavourway otay emulateway erhay; ometimessay oastingcay ethay 
oppositeway anksbay, eway awsay ethay ightymay Urajay opposingway itsway arkday idesay otay ethay 
ambitionway atthay ouldway uitqay itsway ativenay ountrycay, andway anway almostway 
insurmountableway arrierbay otay ethay invaderway owhay ouldshay ishway otay enslaveway itway. 

Iway ooktay ethay andhay ofway Elizabethway. "Youway areway orrowfulsay, ymay ovelay. Ahway! Ifway 
youway ewknay atwhay Iway avehay ufferedsay andway atwhay Iway aymay yetway endureway, youway ouldway 
endeavourway otay etlay emay astetay ethay uietqay andway eedomfray omfray espairday atthay isthay 
oneway ayday atway eastlay ermitspay emay otay enjoyway." 

"Ebay appyhay, ymay earday Ictorvay," epliedray Elizabethway; "erethay isway, Iway opehay, 
othingnay otay istressday youway; andway ebay assuredway atthay ifway away ivelylay oyjay isway otnay 
aintedpay inway ymay acefay, ymay earthay isway ontentedcay. Omethingsay isperswhay otay emay 
otnay otay ependday ootay uchmay onway ethay ospectpray atthay isway openedway eforebay usway, utbay Iway 
illway otnay istenlay otay uchsay away inistersay oicevay. Observeway owhay astfay eway ovemay 
alongway andway owhay ethay oudsclay, ichwhay ometimessay obscureway andway ometimessay iseray 
aboveway ethay omeday ofway Ontmay Ancblay, enderray isthay enescay ofway eautybay illstay oremay 
interestingway. Ooklay alsoway atway ethay innumerableway ishfay atthay areway immingsway inway 
ethay earclay atersway, erewhay eway ancay istinguishday everyway ebblepay atthay ieslay atway 
ethay ottombay. Atwhay away ivineday ayday! Owhay appyhay andway erenesay allway aturenay 
appearsway!" 

Usthay Elizabethway endeavouredway otay ivertday erhay oughtsthay andway inemay omfray allway 
eflectionray uponway elancholymay ubjectssay. Utbay erhay empertay asway uctuatingflay; 
oyjay orfay away ewfay instantsway oneshay inway erhay eyesway, utbay itway ontinuallycay avegay aceplay 
otay istractionday andway everieray. 

Ethay unsay anksay owerlay inway ethay eavenshay; eway assedpay ethay iverray Ancedray andway 
observedway itsway athpay oughthray ethay asmschay ofway ethay igherhay andway ethay ensglay ofway ethay 
owerlay illshay. Ethay Alpsway erehay omecay oserclay otay ethay akelay, andway eway approachedway 
ethay amphitheatreway ofway ountainsmay ichwhay ormsfay itsway easternway oundarybay. Ethay 
irespay ofway Evianway oneshay underway ethay oodsway atthay urroundedsay itway andway ethay angeray 
ofway ountainmay aboveway ountainmay ybay ichwhay itway asway overhungway. 

Ethay indway, ichwhay adhay ithertohay arriedcay usway alongway ithway amazingway apidityray, 
anksay atway unsetsay otay away ightlay eezebray; ethay oftsay airway ustjay uffledray ethay aterway 
andway ausedcay away easantplay otionmay amongway ethay eestray asway eway approachedway ethay 
oreshay, omfray ichwhay itway aftedway ethay ostmay elightfulday entscay ofway owersflay andway 
ayhay. Ethay unsay anksay eneathbay ethay orizonhay asway eway andedlay, andway asway Iway ouchedtay 
ethay oreshay Iway eltfay osethay arescay andway earsfay eviveray ichwhay oonsay ereway otay aspclay 
emay andway ingclay otay emay oreverfay. 



Apterchay 23 

Itway asway eightway oway'clock enwhay eway andedlay; eway alkedway orfay away ortshay imetay onway ethay 
oreshay, enjoyingway ethay ansitorytray ightlay, andway enthay etiredray otay ethay innway andway 
ontemplatedcay ethay ovelylay enescay ofway atersway, oodsway, andway ountainsmay, obscuredway 
inway arknessday, yetway illstay isplayingday eirthay ackblay outlinesway. 

Ethay indway, ichwhay adhay allenfay inway ethay outhsay, ownay oseray ithway eatgray iolencevay 
inway ethay estway. Ethay oonmay adhay eachedray erhay ummitsay inway ethay eavenshay andway asway 
eginningbay otay escendday; ethay oudsclay eptsway acrossway itway iftersway anthay ethay 
ightflay ofway ethay ulturevay andway immedday erhay aysray, ilewhay ethay akelay eflectedray ethay 
enescay ofway ethay usybay eavenshay, enderedray illstay usierbay ybay ethay estlessray avesway 
atthay ereway eginningbay otay iseray. Uddenlysay away eavyhay ormstay ofway ainray escendedday. 

Iway adhay eenbay almcay uringday ethay ayday, utbay osay oonsay asway ightnay obscuredway ethay 
apesshay ofway objectsway, away ousandthay earsfay aroseway inway ymay indmay. Iway asway anxiousway 
andway atchfulway, ilewhay ymay ightray andhay aspedgray away istolpay ichwhay asway iddenhay inway 
ymay osombay; everyway oundsay errifiedtay emay, utbay Iway esolvedray atthay Iway ouldway ellsay ymay 
ifelay earlyday andway otnay inkshray omfray ethay onflictcay untilway ymay ownway ifelay orway atthay 
ofway ymay adversaryway asway extinguishedway. Elizabethway observedway ymay agitationway orfay 
omesay imetay inway imidtay andway earfulfay ilencesay, utbay erethay asway omethingsay inway ymay 
anceglay ichwhay ommunicatedcay errortay otay erhay, andway emblingtray, eshay askedway, 
"Atwhay isway itway atthay agitatesway youway, ymay earday Ictorvay? Atwhay isway itway youway earfay?" 

"Ohway! Eacepay, eacepay, ymay ovelay," epliedray Iway; "isthay ightnay, andway allway illway ebay 
afesay; utbay isthay ightnay isway eadfuldray, eryvay eadfuldray." 

Iway assedpay anway ourhay inway isthay atestay ofway indmay, enwhay uddenlysay Iway eflectedray owhay 
earfulfay ethay ombatcay ichwhay Iway omentarilymay expectedway ouldway ebay otay ymay ifeway, 
andway Iway earnestlyway entreatedway erhay otay etireray, esolvingray otnay otay oinjay erhay 
untilway Iway adhay obtainedway omesay owledgeknay asway otay ethay ituationsay ofway ymay enemyway. 

Eshay eftlay emay, andway Iway ontinuedcay omesay imetay alkingway upway andway ownday ethay assagespay 
ofway ethay ousehay andway inspectingway everyway ornercay atthay ightmay affordway away etreatray otay 
ymay adversaryway. Utbay Iway iscoveredday onay acetray ofway imhay andway asway eginningbay otay 
onjecturecay atthay omesay ortunatefay ancechay adhay intervenedway otay eventpray ethay 
executionway ofway ishay enacesmay enwhay uddenlysay Iway eardhay away illshray andway eadfuldray 
eamscray. Itway amecay omfray ethay oomray intoway ichwhay Elizabethway adhay etiredray. Asway Iway 
eardhay itway, ethay olewhay uthtray ushedray intoway ymay indmay, ymay armsway oppeddray, ethay 
otionmay ofway everyway usclemay andway ibrefay asway uspendedsay; Iway ouldcay eelfay ethay oodblay 
icklingtray inway ymay einsvay andway inglingtay inway ethay extremitiesway ofway ymay imbslay. Isthay 
atestay astedlay utbay orfay anway instantway; ethay eamscray asway epeatedray, andway Iway ushedray 
intoway ethay oomray. Eatgray Odgay! Ywhay idday Iway otnay enthay expireway! Ywhay amway Iway erehay 
otay elateray ethay estructionday ofway ethay estbay opehay andway ethay urestpay eaturecray onway 
earthway? Eshay asway erethay, ifelesslay andway inanimateway, ownthray acrossway ethay edbay, 
erhay eadhay anginghay ownday andway erhay alepay andway istortedday eaturesfay alfhay overedcay 
ybay erhay airhay. Everywhereway Iway urntay Iway eesay ethay amesay igurefay--her oodlessblay 
armsway andway elaxedray ormfay ungflay ybay ethay urderermay onway itsway idalbray ierbay. Ouldcay 
Iway eholdbay isthay andway ivelay? Alasway! Ifelay isway obstinateway andway ingsclay osestclay 
erewhay itway isway ostmay atedhay. Orfay away omentmay onlyway idday Iway oselay ecollectionray; Iway 
ellfay enselesssay onway ethay oundgray. 

Enwhay Iway ecoveredray Iway oundfay yselfmay urroundedsay ybay ethay eoplepay ofway ethay innway; 
eirthay ountenancescay expressedway away eathlessbray errortay, utbay ethay orrorhay ofway 
othersway appearedway onlyway asway away ockerymay, away adowshay ofway ethay eelingsfay atthay 
oppressedway emay. Iway escapedway omfray emthay otay ethay oomray erewhay aylay ethay odybay ofway 
Elizabethway, ymay ovelay, ymay ifeway, osay atelylay ivinglay, osay earday, osay orthyway. Eshay 
adhay eenbay ovedmay omfray ethay osturepay inway ichwhay Iway adhay irstfay eheldbay erhay, andway 
ownay, asway eshay aylay, erhay eadhay uponway erhay armway andway away andkerchiefhay ownthray acrossway 
erhay acefay andway ecknay, Iway ightmay avehay upposedsay erhay asleepway. Iway ushedray owardstay 
erhay andway embracedway erhay ithway ardourway, utbay ethay eadlyday anguorlay andway oldnesscay 
ofway ethay imbslay oldtay emay atthay atwhay Iway ownay eldhay inway ymay armsway adhay easedcay otay ebay 
ethay Elizabethway omwhay Iway adhay ovedlay andway erishedchay. Ethay urderousmay arkmay ofway 
ethay iendfay's aspgray asway onway erhay ecknay, andway ethay eathbray adhay easedcay otay issueway 
omfray erhay ipslay. Ilewhay Iway illstay unghay overway erhay inway ethay agonyway ofway espairday, Iway 
appenedhay otay ooklay upway. Ethay indowsway ofway ethay oomray adhay eforebay eenbay arkenedday, 
andway Iway eltfay away indkay ofway anicpay onway eeingsay ethay alepay yellowway ightlay ofway ethay oonmay 
illuminateway ethay amberchay. Ethay uttersshay adhay eenbay ownthray ackbay, andway ithway away 
ensationsay ofway orrorhay otnay otay ebay escribedday, Iway awsay atway ethay openway indowway away 
igurefay ethay ostmay ideoushay andway abhorredway. Away ingray asway onway ethay acefay ofway ethay 
onstermay; ehay eemedsay otay eerjay, asway ithway ishay iendishfay ingerfay ehay ointedpay 
owardstay ethay orpsecay ofway ymay ifeway. Iway ushedray owardstay ethay indowway, andway 
awingdray away istolpay omfray ymay osombay, iredfay; utbay ehay eludedway emay, eapedlay omfray 
ishay ationstay, andway unningray ithway ethay iftnesssway ofway ightninglay, ungedplay intoway 
ethay akelay. 

Ethay eportray ofway ethay istolpay oughtbray away owdcray intoway ethay oomray. Iway ointedpay otay 
ethay otspay erewhay ehay adhay isappearedday, andway eway ollowedfay ethay acktray ithway 
oatsbay; etsnay ereway astcay, utbay inway ainvay. Afterway assingpay everalsay ourshay, eway 
eturnedray opelesshay, ostmay ofway ymay ompanionscay elievingbay itway otay avehay eenbay away 
ormfay onjuredcay upway ybay ymay ancyfay. Afterway avinghay andedlay, eythay oceededpray otay 
earchsay ethay ountrycay, artiespay oinggay inway ifferentday irectionsday amongway ethay 
oodsway andway inesvay. 

Iway attemptedway otay accompanyway emthay andway oceededpray away ortshay istanceday omfray ethay 
ousehay, utbay ymay eadhay irledwhay oundray, ymay epsstay ereway ikelay osethay ofway away unkendray 
anmay, Iway ellfay atway astlay inway away atestay ofway utterway exhaustionway; away ilmfay overedcay ymay 
eyesway, andway ymay inskay asway archedpay ithway ethay eathay ofway everfay. Inway isthay atestay Iway 
asway arriedcay ackbay andway acedplay onway away edbay, ardlyhay onsciouscay ofway atwhay adhay 
appenedhay; ymay eyesway anderedway oundray ethay oomray asway ifway otay eeksay omethingsay atthay 
Iway adhay ostlay. 

Afterway anway intervalway Iway aroseway, andway asway ifway ybay instinctway, awledcray intoway ethay oomray 
erewhay ethay orpsecay ofway ymay elovedbay aylay. Erethay ereway omenway eepingway aroundway; Iway 
unghay overway itway andway oinedjay ymay adsay earstay otay eirsthay; allway isthay imetay onay 
istinctday ideaway esentedpray itselfway otay ymay indmay, utbay ymay oughtsthay ambledray otay 
ariousvay ubjectssay, eflectingray onfusedlycay onway ymay isfortunesmay andway eirthay 
ausecay. Iway asway ewilderedbay, inway away oudclay ofway onderway andway orrorhay. Ethay eathday 
ofway Illiamway, ethay executionway ofway Ustinejay, ethay urdermay ofway Ervalclay, andway astlylay 
ofway ymay ifeway; evenway atway atthay omentmay Iway ewknay otnay atthay ymay onlyway emainingray 
iendsfray ereway afesay omfray ethay alignitymay ofway ethay iendfay; ymay atherfay evenway ownay 
ightmay ebay ithingwray underway ishay aspgray, andway Ernestway ightmay ebay eadday atway ishay 
eetfay. Isthay ideaway ademay emay uddershay andway ecalledray emay otay actionway. Iway artedstay 
upway andway esolvedray otay eturnray otay Enevagay ithway allway ossiblepay eedspay. 

Erethay ereway onay orseshay otay ebay ocuredpray, andway Iway ustmay eturnray ybay ethay akelay; utbay 
ethay indway asway unfavourableway, andway ethay ainray ellfay inway orrentstay. Oweverhay, itway 
asway ardlyhay orningmay, andway Iway ightmay easonablyray opehay otay arriveway ybay ightnay. Iway 
iredhay enmay otay owray andway ooktay anway oarway yselfmay, orfay Iway adhay alwaysway experiencedway 
eliefray omfray entalmay ormenttay inway odilybay exerciseway. Utbay ethay overflowingway 
iserymay Iway ownay eltfay, andway ethay excessway ofway agitationway atthay Iway enduredway enderedray 
emay incapableway ofway anyway exertionway. Iway ewthray ownday ethay oarway, andway eaninglay ymay 
eadhay uponway ymay andshay, avegay ayway otay everyway oomyglay ideaway atthay aroseway. Ifway Iway 
ookedlay upway, Iway awsay enesscay ichwhay ereway amiliarfay otay emay inway ymay appierhay imetay 
andway ichwhay Iway adhay ontemplatedcay utbay ethay ayday eforebay inway ethay ompanycay ofway erhay 
owhay asway ownay utbay away adowshay andway away ecollectionray. Earstay eamedstray omfray ymay 
eyesway. Ethay ainray adhay easedcay orfay away omentmay, andway Iway awsay ethay ishfay ayplay inway ethay 
atersway asway eythay adhay oneday away ewfay ourshay eforebay; eythay adhay enthay eenbay observedway 
ybay Elizabethway. Othingnay isway osay ainfulpay otay ethay umanhay indmay asway away eatgray andway 
uddensay angechay. Ethay unsay ightmay ineshay orway ethay oudsclay ightmay owerlay, utbay 
othingnay ouldcay appearway otay emay asway itway adhay oneday ethay ayday eforebay. Away iendfay adhay 
atchedsnay omfray emay everyway opehay ofway uturefay appinesshay; onay eaturecray adhay everway 
eenbay osay iserablemay asway Iway asway; osay ightfulfray anway eventway isway inglesay inway ethay 
istoryhay ofway anmay. Utbay ywhay ouldshay Iway elldway uponway ethay incidentsway atthay ollowedfay 
isthay astlay overwhelmingway eventway? Inemay ashay eenbay away aletay ofway orrorshay; Iway avehay 
eachedray eirthay acmeway, andway atwhay Iway ustmay ownay elateray ancay utbay ebay edioustay otay 
youway. Owknay atthay, oneway ybay oneway, ymay iendsfray ereway atchedsnay awayway; Iway asway eftlay 
esolateday. Ymay ownway engthstray isway exhaustedway, andway Iway ustmay elltay, inway away ewfay 
ordsway, atwhay emainsray ofway ymay ideoushay arrationnay. Iway arrivedway atway Enevagay. Ymay 
atherfay andway Ernestway yetway ivedlay, utbay ethay ormerfay unksay underway ethay idingstay atthay 
Iway orebay. Iway eesay imhay ownay, excellentway andway enerablevay oldway anmay! Ishay eyesway 
anderedway inway acancyvay, orfay eythay adhay ostlay eirthay armchay andway eirthay 
elightday--his Elizabethway, ishay oremay anthay aughterday, omwhay ehay otedday onway ithway 
allway atthay affectionway ichwhay away anmay eelsfay, owhay inway ethay eclineday ofway ifelay, 
avinghay ewfay affectionsway, ingsclay oremay earnestlyway otay osethay atthay emainray. 
Ursedcay, ursedcay ebay ethay iendfay atthay oughtbray iserymay onway ishay eygray airshay andway 
oomedday imhay otay asteway inway etchednesswray! Ehay ouldcay otnay ivelay underway ethay 
orrorshay atthay ereway accumulatedway aroundway imhay; ethay ingsspray ofway existenceway 
uddenlysay avegay ayway; ehay asway unableway otay iseray omfray ishay edbay, andway inway away ewfay 
aysday ehay iedday inway ymay armsway. 

Atwhay enthay ecamebay ofway emay? Iway owknay otnay; Iway ostlay ensationsay, andway ainschay andway 
arknessday ereway ethay onlyway objectsway atthay essedpray uponway emay. Ometimessay, 
indeedway, Iway eamtdray atthay Iway anderedway inway oweryflay eadowsmay andway easantplay alesvay 
ithway ethay iendsfray ofway ymay youthway, utbay Iway awokeway andway oundfay yselfmay inway away 
ungeonday. Elancholymay ollowedfay, utbay ybay egreesday Iway ainedgay away earclay 
onceptioncay ofway ymay iseriesmay andway ituationsay andway asway enthay eleasedray omfray ymay 
isonpray. Orfay eythay adhay alledcay emay admay, andway uringday anymay onthsmay, asway Iway 
understoodway, away olitarysay ellcay adhay eenbay ymay abitationhay. 

Ibertylay, oweverhay, adhay eenbay away uselessway iftgay otay emay, adhay Iway otnay, asway Iway 
awakenedway otay easonray, atway ethay amesay imetay awakenedway otay evengeray. Asway ethay 
emorymay ofway astpay isfortunesmay essedpray uponway emay, Iway eganbay otay eflectray onway eirthay 
ausecay--the onstermay omwhay Iway adhay eatedcray, ethay iserablemay aemonday omwhay Iway adhay 
entsay abroadway intoway ethay orldway orfay ymay estructionday. Iway asway ossessedpay ybay away 
addeningmay ageray enwhay Iway oughtthay ofway imhay, andway esiredday andway ardentlyway ayedpray 
atthay Iway ightmay avehay imhay ithinway ymay aspgray otay eakwray away eatgray andway ignalsay 
evengeray onway ishay ursedcay eadhay. 

Ornay idday ymay atehay onglay onfinecay itselfway otay uselessway ishesway; Iway eganbay otay 
eflectray onway ethay estbay eansmay ofway ecuringsay imhay; andway orfay isthay urposepay, aboutway 
away onthmay afterway ymay eleaseray, Iway epairedray otay away iminalcray udgejay inway ethay owntay 
andway oldtay imhay atthay Iway adhay anway accusationway otay akemay, atthay Iway ewknay ethay 
estroyerday ofway ymay amilyfay, andway atthay Iway equiredray imhay otay exertway ishay olewhay 
authorityway orfay ethay apprehensionway ofway ethay urderermay. Ethay agistratemay 
istenedlay otay emay ithway attentionway andway indnesskay. 

"Ebay assuredway, irsay," aidsay ehay, "onay ainspay orway exertionsway onway ymay artpay allshay ebay 
aredspay otay iscoverday ethay illainvay." 

"Iway ankthay youway," epliedray Iway; "istenlay, ereforethay, otay ethay epositionday atthay Iway 
avehay otay akemay. Itway isway indeedway away aletay osay angestray atthay Iway ouldshay earfay youway 
ouldway otnay editcray itway ereway erethay otnay omethingsay inway uthtray ichwhay, oweverhay 
onderfulway, orcesfay onvictioncay. Ethay orystay isway ootay onnectedcay otay ebay 
istakenmay orfay away eamdray, andway Iway avehay onay otivemay orfay alsehoodfay." Ymay annermay asway 
Iway usthay addressedway imhay asway impressiveway utbay almcay; Iway adhay ormedfay inway ymay ownway 
earthay away esolutionray otay ursuepay ymay estroyerday otay eathday, andway isthay urposepay 
uietedqay ymay agonyway andway orfay anway intervalway econciledray emay otay ifelay. Iway ownay 
elatedray ymay istoryhay ieflybray utbay ithway irmnessfay andway ecisionpray, arkingmay ethay 
atesday ithway accuracyway andway evernay eviatingday intoway invectiveway orway exclamationway. 

Ethay agistratemay appearedway atway irstfay erfectlypay incredulousway, utbay asway Iway 
ontinuedcay ehay ecamebay oremay attentiveway andway interestedway; Iway awsay imhay ometimessay 
uddershay ithway orrorhay; atway othersway away ivelylay urprisesay, unmingledway ithway 
isbeliefday, asway aintedpay onway ishay ountenancecay. Enwhay Iway adhay oncludedcay ymay 
arrationnay Iway aidsay, "Isthay isway ethay eingbay omwhay Iway accuseway andway orfay osewhay 
eizuresay andway unishmentpay Iway allcay uponway youway otay exertway yourway olewhay owerpay. Itway 
isway yourway utyday asway away agistratemay, andway Iway elievebay andway opehay atthay yourway eelingsfay 
asway away anmay illway otnay evoltray omfray ethay executionway ofway osethay unctionsfay onway isthay 
occasionway." Isthay addressway ausedcay away onsiderablecay angechay inway ethay 
ysiognomyphay ofway ymay ownway auditorway. Ehay adhay eardhay ymay orystay ithway atthay alfhay 
indkay ofway eliefbay atthay isway ivengay otay away aletay ofway iritsspay andway upernaturalsay 
eventsway; utbay enwhay ehay asway alledcay uponway otay actway officiallyway inway onsequencecay, 
ethay olewhay idetay ofway ishay incredulityway eturnedray. Ehay, oweverhay, answeredway 
ildlymay, "Iway ouldway illinglyway affordway youway everyway aidway inway yourway ursuitpay, utbay 
ethay eaturecray ofway omwhay youway eakspay appearsway otay avehay owerspay ichwhay ouldway utpay 
allway ymay exertionsway otay efianceday. Owhay ancay ollowfay anway animalway ichwhay ancay 
aversetray ethay easay ofway iceway andway inhabitway avescay andway ensday erewhay onay anmay ouldway 
enturevay otay intrudeway? Esidesbay, omesay onthsmay avehay elapsedway incesay ethay 
ommissioncay ofway ishay imescray, andway onay oneway ancay onjecturecay otay atwhay aceplay ehay 
ashay anderedway orway atwhay egionray ehay aymay ownay inhabitway." 

"Iway oday otnay oubtday atthay ehay overshay earnay ethay otspay ichwhay Iway inhabitway, andway ifway ehay 
ashay indeedway akentay efugeray inway ethay Alpsway, ehay aymay ebay untedhay ikelay ethay amoischay 
andway estroyedday asway away eastbay ofway eypray. Utbay Iway erceivepay yourway oughtsthay; youway oday 
otnay editcray ymay arrativenay andway oday otnay intendway otay ursuepay ymay enemyway ithway ethay 
unishmentpay ichwhay isway ishay esertday." Asway Iway okespay, ageray arkledspay inway ymay eyesway; 
ethay agistratemay asway intimidatedway. "Youway areway istakenmay," aidsay ehay. "Iway illway 
exertway yselfmay, andway ifway itway isway inway ymay owerpay otay eizesay ethay onstermay, ebay assuredway 
atthay ehay allshay uffersay unishmentpay oportionatepray otay ishay imescray. Utbay Iway 
earfay, omfray atwhay youway avehay yourselfway escribedday otay ebay ishay opertiespray, atthay 
isthay illway ovepray impracticableway; andway usthay, ilewhay everyway operpray easuremay isway 
ursuedpay, youway ouldshay akemay upway yourway indmay otay isappointmentday." 

"Atthay annotcay ebay; utbay allway atthay Iway ancay aysay illway ebay ofway ittlelay availway. Ymay 
evengeray isway ofway onay omentmay otay youway; yetway, ilewhay Iway allowway itway otay ebay away icevay, Iway 
onfesscay atthay itway isway ethay evouringday andway onlyway assionpay ofway ymay oulsay. Ymay ageray 
isway unspeakableway enwhay Iway eflectray atthay ethay urderermay, omwhay Iway avehay urnedtay 
ooselay uponway ocietysay, illstay existsway. Youway efuseray ymay ustjay emandday; Iway avehay 
utbay oneway esourceray, andway Iway evoteday yselfmay, eitherway inway ymay ifelay orway eathday, otay 
ishay estructionday." 

Iway embledtray ithway excessway ofway agitationway asway Iway aidsay isthay; erethay asway away enzyfray 
inway ymay annermay, andway omethingsay, Iway oubtday otnay, ofway atthay aughtyhay iercenessfay 
ichwhay ethay artyrsmay ofway oldway areway aidsay otay avehay ossessedpay. Utbay otay away Enevangay 
agistratemay, osewhay indmay asway occupiedway ybay arfay otherway ideasway anthay osethay ofway 
evotionday andway eroismhay, isthay elevationway ofway indmay adhay uchmay ethay appearanceway ofway 
adnessmay. Ehay endeavouredway otay oothesay emay asway away ursenay oesday away ildchay andway 
evertedray otay ymay aletay asway ethay effectsway ofway eliriumday. 

"Anmay," Iway iedcray, "owhay ignorantway artway outhay inway ythay idepray ofway isdomway! Easecay; 
youway owknay otnay atwhay itway isway youway aysay." 

Iway okebray omfray ethay ousehay angryway andway isturbedday andway etiredray otay editatemay onway 
omesay otherway odemay ofway actionway. 



Apterchay 24 

Ymay esentpray ituationsay asway oneway inway ichwhay allway oluntaryvay oughtthay asway 
allowedsway upway andway ostlay. Iway asway urriedhay awayway ybay uryfay; evengeray aloneway 
endowedway emay ithway engthstray andway omposurecay; itway ouldedmay ymay eelingsfay andway 
allowedway emay otay ebay alculatingcay andway almcay atway eriodspay enwhay otherwiseway 
eliriumday orway eathday ouldway avehay eenbay ymay ortionpay. 

Ymay irstfay esolutionray asway otay uitqay Enevagay oreverfay; ymay ountrycay, ichwhay, enwhay 
Iway asway appyhay andway elovedbay, asway earday otay emay, ownay, inway ymay adversityway, ecamebay 
atefulhay. Iway ovidedpray yselfmay ithway away umsay ofway oneymay, ogethertay ithway away ewfay 
ewelsjay ichwhay adhay elongedbay otay ymay othermay, andway epartedday. Andway ownay ymay 
anderingsway eganbay ichwhay areway otay easecay utbay ithway ifelay. Iway avehay aversedtray away 
astvay ortionpay ofway ethay earthway andway avehay enduredway allway ethay ardshipshay ichwhay 
avellerstray inway esertsday andway arbarousbay ountriescay areway ontway otay eetmay. Owhay Iway 
avehay ivedlay Iway ardlyhay owknay; anymay imestay avehay Iway etchedstray ymay ailingfay imbslay 
uponway ethay andysay ainplay andway ayedpray orfay eathday. Utbay evengeray eptkay emay aliveway; 
Iway aredday otnay ieday andway eavelay ymay adversaryway inway eingbay. 

Enwhay Iway uittedqay Enevagay ymay irstfay abourlay asway otay aingay omesay ueclay ybay ichwhay Iway 
ightmay acetray ethay epsstay ofway ymay iendishfay enemyway. Utbay ymay anplay asway unsettledway, 
andway Iway anderedway anymay ourshay oundray ethay onfinescay ofway ethay owntay, uncertainway 
atwhay athpay Iway ouldshay ursuepay. Asway ightnay approachedway Iway oundfay yselfmay atway ethay 
entranceway ofway ethay emeterycay erewhay Illiamway, Elizabethway, andway ymay atherfay 
eposedray. Iway enteredway itway andway approachedway ethay ombtay ichwhay arkedmay eirthay 
avesgray. Everythingway asway ilentsay exceptway ethay eaveslay ofway ethay eestray, ichwhay 
ereway entlygay agitatedway ybay ethay indway; ethay ightnay asway earlynay arkday, andway ethay 
enescay ouldway avehay eenbay olemnsay andway affectingway evenway otay anway uninterestedway 
observerway. Ethay iritsspay ofway ethay epartedday eemedsay otay itflay aroundway andway otay 
astcay away adowshay, ichwhay asway eltfay utbay otnay eensay, aroundway ethay eadhay ofway ethay 
ournermay. 

Ethay eepday iefgray ichwhay isthay enescay adhay atway irstfay excitedway uicklyqay avegay ayway 
otay ageray andway espairday. Eythay ereway eadday, andway Iway ivedlay; eirthay urderermay alsoway 
ivedlay, andway otay estroyday imhay Iway ustmay agdray outway ymay earyway existenceway. Iway eltknay 
onway ethay assgray andway issedkay ethay earthway andway ithway uiveringqay ipslay exclaimedway, 
"Ybay ethay acredsay earthway onway ichwhay Iway eelknay, ybay ethay adesshay atthay anderway earnay 
emay, ybay ethay eepday andway eternalway iefgray atthay Iway eelfay, Iway earsway; andway ybay eethay, Oway 
Ightnay, andway ethay iritsspay atthay esidepray overway eethay, otay ursuepay ethay aemonday owhay 
ausedcay isthay iserymay, untilway ehay orway Iway allshay erishpay inway ortalmay onflictcay. Orfay 
isthay urposepay Iway illway eservepray ymay ifelay; otay executeway isthay earday evengeray illway 
Iway againway eholdbay ethay unsay andway eadtray ethay eengray erbagehay ofway earthway, ichwhay 
otherwiseway ouldshay anishvay omfray ymay eyesway oreverfay. Andway Iway allcay onway youway, 
iritsspay ofway ethay eadday, andway onway youway, anderingway inistersmay ofway engeancevay, otay 
aidway andway onductcay emay inway ymay orkway. Etlay ethay ursedcay andway ellishhay onstermay 
inkdray eepday ofway agonyway; etlay imhay eelfay ethay espairday atthay ownay ormentstay emay." Iway 
adhay egunbay ymay adjurationway ithway olemnitysay andway anway aweway ichwhay almostway assuredway 
emay atthay ethay adesshay ofway ymay urderedmay iendsfray eardhay andway approvedway ymay 
evotionday, utbay ethay uriesfay ossessedpay emay asway Iway oncludedcay, andway ageray okedchay 
ymay utteranceway. 

Iway asway answeredway oughthray ethay illnessstay ofway ightnay ybay away oudlay andway iendishfay 
aughlay. Itway angray onway ymay earsway onglay andway eavilyhay; ethay ountainsmay eray-echoed 
itway, andway Iway eltfay asway ifway allway ellhay urroundedsay emay ithway ockerymay andway aughterlay. 
Urelysay inway atthay omentmay Iway ouldshay avehay eenbay ossessedpay ybay enzyfray andway avehay 
estroyedday ymay iserablemay existenceway utbay atthay ymay owvay asway eardhay andway atthay Iway 
asway eservedray orfay engeancevay. Ethay aughterlay iedday awayway, enwhay away ellway-known 
andway abhorredway oicevay, apparentlyway oseclay otay ymay earway, addressedway emay inway anway 
audibleway isperwhay, "Iway amway atisfiedsay, iserablemay etchwray! Youway avehay 
eterminedday otay ivelay, andway Iway amway atisfiedsay." 

Iway artedday owardstay ethay otspay omfray ichwhay ethay oundsay oceededpray, utbay ethay evilday 
eludedway ymay aspgray. Uddenlysay ethay oadbray iskday ofway ethay oonmay aroseway andway oneshay 
ullfay uponway ishay astlyghay andway istortedday apeshay asway ehay edflay ithway oremay anthay 
ortalmay eedspay. 

Iway ursuedpay imhay, andway orfay anymay onthsmay isthay ashay eenbay ymay asktay. Uidedgay ybay away 
ightslay ueclay, Iway ollowedfay ethay indingsway ofway ethay Onerhay, utbay ainlyvay. Ethay 
ueblay Editerraneanmay appearedway, andway ybay away angestray ancechay, Iway awsay ethay iendfay 
enterway ybay ightnay andway idehay imselfhay inway away esselvay oundbay orfay ethay Ackblay Easay. Iway 
ooktay ymay assagepay inway ethay amesay ipshay, utbay ehay escapedway, Iway owknay otnay owhay. 

Amidstway ethay ildsway ofway Artarytay andway Ussiaray, althoughway ehay illstay evadedway emay, Iway 
avehay everway ollowedfay inway ishay acktray. Ometimessay ethay easantspay, aredscay ybay 
isthay orridhay apparitionway, informedway emay ofway ishay athpay; ometimessay ehay imselfhay, 
owhay earedfay atthay ifway Iway ostlay allway acetray ofway imhay Iway ouldshay espairday andway ieday, 
eftlay omesay arkmay otay uidegay emay. Ethay owssnay escendedday onway ymay eadhay, andway Iway awsay 
ethay intpray ofway ishay ugehay epstay onway ethay itewhay ainplay. Otay youway irstfay enteringway 
onway ifelay, otay omwhay arecay isway ewnay andway agonyway unknownway, owhay ancay youway understandway 
atwhay Iway avehay eltfay andway illstay eelfay? Oldcay, antway, andway atiguefay ereway ethay 
eastlay ainspay ichwhay Iway asway estinedday otay endureway; Iway asway ursedcay ybay omesay evilday 
andway arriedcay aboutway ithway emay ymay eternalway ellhay; yetway illstay away iritspay ofway oodgay 
ollowedfay andway irectedday ymay epsstay andway enwhay Iway ostmay urmuredmay ouldway uddenlysay 
extricateway emay omfray eeminglysay insurmountableway ifficultiesday. Ometimessay, 
enwhay aturenay, overcomeway ybay ungerhay, anksay underway ethay exhaustionway, away epastray 
asway eparedpray orfay emay inway ethay esertday atthay estoredray andway inspiritedway emay. Ethay 
arefay asway, indeedway, oarsecay, uchsay asway ethay easantspay ofway ethay ountrycay ateway, utbay 
Iway illway otnay oubtday atthay itway asway etsay erethay ybay ethay iritsspay atthay Iway adhay 
invokedway otay aidway emay. Oftenway, enwhay allway asway ydray, ethay eavenshay oudlessclay, andway 
Iway asway archedpay ybay irstthay, away ightslay oudclay ouldway edimbay ethay yskay, edshay ethay 
ewfay opsdray atthay evivedray emay, andway anishvay. 

Iway ollowedfay, enwhay Iway ouldcay, ethay oursescay ofway ethay iversray; utbay ethay aemonday 
enerallygay avoidedway esethay, asway itway asway erehay atthay ethay opulationpay ofway ethay 
ountrycay ieflychay ollectedcay. Inway otherway acesplay umanhay eingsbay ereway eldomsay 
eensay, andway Iway enerallygay ubsistedsay onway ethay ildway animalsway atthay ossedcray ymay 
athpay. Iway adhay oneymay ithway emay andway ainedgay ethay iendshipfray ofway ethay illagersvay 
ybay istributingday itway; orway Iway oughtbray ithway emay omesay oodfay atthay Iway adhay illedkay, 
ichwhay, afterway akingtay away allsmay artpay, Iway alwaysway esentedpray otay osethay owhay adhay 
ovidedpray emay ithway irefay andway utensilsway orfay ookingcay. 

Ymay ifelay, asway itway assedpay usthay, asway indeedway atefulhay otay emay, andway itway asway uringday 
eepslay aloneway atthay Iway ouldcay astetay oyjay. Oway essedblay eepslay! Oftenway, enwhay ostmay 
iserablemay, Iway anksay otay eposeray, andway ymay eamsdray ulledlay emay evenway otay aptureray. 
Ethay iritsspay atthay uardedgay emay adhay ovidedpray esethay omentsmay, orway atherray 
ourshay, ofway appinesshay atthay Iway ightmay etainray engthstray otay ulfilfay ymay 
ilgrimagepay. Eprivedday ofway isthay espiteray, Iway ouldshay avehay unksay underway ymay 
ardshipshay. Uringday ethay ayday Iway asway ustainedsay andway inspiritedway ybay ethay opehay 
ofway ightnay, orfay inway eepslay Iway awsay ymay iendsfray, ymay ifeway, andway ymay elovedbay 
ountrycay; againway Iway awsay ethay enevolentbay ountenancecay ofway ymay atherfay, eardhay ethay 
ilversay onestay ofway ymay Elizabethway's oicevay, andway eheldbay Ervalclay enjoyingway 
ealthhay andway youthway. Oftenway, enwhay eariedway ybay away oilsometay archmay, Iway ersuadedpay 
yselfmay atthay Iway asway eamingdray untilway ightnay ouldshay omecay andway atthay Iway ouldshay 
enthay enjoyway ealityray inway ethay armsway ofway ymay earestday iendsfray. Atwhay agonizingway 
ondnessfay idday Iway eelfay orfay emthay! Owhay idday Iway ingclay otay eirthay earday ormsfay, asway 
ometimessay eythay auntedhay evenway ymay akingway ourshay, andway ersuadepay yselfmay atthay 
eythay illstay ivedlay! Atway uchsay omentsmay engeancevay, atthay urnedbay ithinway emay, 
iedday inway ymay earthay, andway Iway ursuedpay ymay athpay owardstay ethay estructionday ofway ethay 
aemonday oremay asway away asktay enjoinedway ybay eavenhay, asway ethay echanicalmay impulseway ofway 
omesay owerpay ofway ichwhay Iway asway unconsciousway, anthay asway ethay ardentway esireday ofway ymay 
oulsay. Atwhay ishay eelingsfay ereway omwhay Iway ursuedpay Iway annotcay owknay. Ometimessay, 
indeedway, ehay eftlay arksmay inway itingwray onway ethay arksbay ofway ethay eestray orway utcay inway 
onestay atthay uidedgay emay andway instigatedway ymay uryfay. "Ymay eignray isway otnay yetway 
overway"--these ordsway ereway egiblelay inway oneway ofway esethay inscriptionsway--"you 
ivelay, andway ymay owerpay isway ompletecay. Ollowfay emay; Iway eeksay ethay everlastingway icesway 
ofway ethay orthnay, erewhay youway illway eelfay ethay iserymay ofway oldcay andway ostfray, otay 
ichwhay Iway amway impassiveway. Youway illway indfay earnay isthay aceplay, ifway youway ollowfay otnay 
ootay ardilytay, away eadday arehay; eatway andway ebay efreshedray. Omecay onway, ymay enemyway; eway 
avehay yetway otay estlewray orfay ourway iveslay, utbay anymay ardhay andway iserablemay ourshay 
ustmay youway endureway untilway atthay eriodpay allshay arriveway." 

Offingscay evilday! Againway oday Iway owvay engeancevay; againway oday Iway evoteday eethay, 
iserablemay iendfay, otay orturetay andway eathday. Evernay illway Iway ivegay upway ymay earchsay 
untilway ehay orway Iway erishpay; andway enthay ithway atwhay ecstasyway allshay Iway oinjay ymay 
Elizabethway andway ymay epartedday iendsfray, owhay evenway ownay eparepray orfay emay ethay 
ewardray ofway ymay edioustay oiltay andway orriblehay ilgrimagepay! 

Asway Iway illstay ursuedpay ymay ourneyjay otay ethay orthwardnay, ethay owssnay ickenedthay andway 
ethay oldcay increasedway inway away egreeday almostway ootay everesay otay upportsay. Ethay 
easantspay ereway utshay upway inway eirthay ovelshay, andway onlyway away ewfay ofway ethay ostmay ardyhay 
enturedvay orthfay otay eizesay ethay animalsway omwhay arvationstay adhay orcedfay omfray 
eirthay idinghay-places otay eeksay orfay eypray. Ethay iversray ereway overedcay ithway 
iceway, andway onay ishfay ouldcay ebay ocuredpray; andway usthay Iway asway utcay offway omfray ymay 
iefchay articleway ofway aintenancemay. Ethay iumphtray ofway ymay enemyway increasedway ithway 
ethay ifficultyday ofway ymay abourslay. Oneway inscriptionway atthay ehay eftlay asway inway 
esethay ordsway: "Eparepray! Yourway oilstay onlyway eginbay; apwray yourselfway inway ursfay 
andway ovidepray oodfay, orfay eway allshay oonsay enterway uponway away ourneyjay erewhay yourway 
ufferingssay illway atisfysay ymay everlastingway atredhay." 

Ymay ouragecay andway erseverancepay ereway invigoratedway ybay esethay offingscay ordsway; Iway 
esolvedray otnay otay ailfay inway ymay urposepay, andway allingcay onway eavenhay otay upportsay 
emay, Iway ontinuedcay ithway unabatedway ervourfay otay aversetray immenseway esertsday, 
untilway ethay oceanway appearedway atway away istanceday andway ormedfay ethay utmostway oundarybay 
ofway ethay orizonhay. Ohway! Owhay unlikeway itway asway otay ethay ueblay easonssay ofway ethay 
outhsay! Overedcay ithway iceway, itway asway onlyway otay ebay istinguishedday omfray andlay ybay 
itsway uperiorsay ildnessway andway uggednessray. Ethay Eeksgray eptway orfay oyjay enwhay 
eythay eheldbay ethay Editerraneanmay omfray ethay illshay ofway Asiaway, andway ailedhay ithway 
aptureray ethay oundarybay ofway eirthay oilstay. Iway idday otnay eepway, utbay Iway eltknay ownday 
andway ithway away ullfay earthay ankedthay ymay uidinggay iritspay orfay onductingcay emay inway 
afetysay otay ethay aceplay erewhay Iway opedhay, otwithstandingnay ymay adversaryway's ibegay, 
otay eetmay andway applegray ithway imhay. 

Omesay eeksway eforebay isthay eriodpay Iway adhay ocuredpray away edgeslay andway ogsday andway usthay 
aversedtray ethay owssnay ithway inconceivableway eedspay. Iway owknay otnay etherwhay ethay 
iendfay ossessedpay ethay amesay advantagesway, utbay Iway oundfay atthay, asway eforebay Iway adhay 
ailyday ostlay oundgray inway ethay ursuitpay, Iway ownay ainedgay onway imhay, osay uchmay osay atthay 
enwhay Iway irstfay awsay ethay oceanway ehay asway utbay oneway ayday's ourneyjay inway advanceway, andway 
Iway opedhay otay interceptway imhay eforebay ehay ouldshay eachray ethay eachbay. Ithway ewnay 
ouragecay, ereforethay, Iway essedpray onway, andway inway otway aysday arrivedway atway away etchedwray 
amlethay onway ethay eashoresay. Iway inquiredway ofway ethay inhabitantsway oncerningcay ethay 
iendfay andway ainedgay accurateway informationway. Away iganticgay onstermay, eythay aidsay, 
adhay arrivedway ethay ightnay eforebay, armedway ithway away ungay andway anymay istolspay, 
uttingpay otay ightflay ethay inhabitantsway ofway away olitarysay ottagecay oughthray earfay ofway 
ishay errifictay appearanceway. Ehay adhay arriedcay offway eirthay orestay ofway interway 
oodfay, andway acingplay itway inway away edgeslay, otay awdray ichwhay ehay adhay eizedsay onway away 
umerousnay ovedray ofway ainedtray ogsday, ehay adhay arnessedhay emthay, andway ethay amesay 
ightnay, otay ethay oyjay ofway ethay orrorhay-struck illagersvay, adhay ursuedpay ishay 
ourneyjay acrossway ethay easay inway away irectionday atthay edlay otay onay andlay; andway eythay 
onjecturedcay atthay ehay ustmay eedilyspay ebay estroyedday ybay ethay eakingbray ofway ethay 
iceway orway ozenfray ybay ethay eternalway ostsfray. 

Onway earinghay isthay informationway Iway ufferedsay away emporarytay accessway ofway espairday. 
Ehay adhay escapedway emay, andway Iway ustmay ommencecay away estructiveday andway almostway endlessway 
ourneyjay acrossway ethay ountainousmay icesway ofway ethay oceanway, amidstway oldcay atthay ewfay 
ofway ethay inhabitantsway ouldcay onglay endureway andway ichwhay Iway, ethay ativenay ofway away 
enialgay andway unnysay imateclay, ouldcay otnay opehay otay urvivesay. Yetway atway ethay ideaway 
atthay ethay iendfay ouldshay ivelay andway ebay iumphanttray, ymay ageray andway engeancevay 
eturnedray, andway ikelay away ightymay idetay, overwhelmedway everyway otherway eelingfay. 
Afterway away ightslay eposeray, uringday ichwhay ethay iritsspay ofway ethay eadday overedhay 
oundray andway instigatedway emay otay oiltay andway evengeray, Iway eparedpray orfay ymay ourneyjay. 
Iway exchangedway ymay andlay-sledge orfay oneway ashionedfay orfay ethay inequalitiesway ofway 
ethay ozenfray oceanway, andway urchasingpay away entifulplay ockstay ofway ovisionspray, Iway 
epartedday omfray andlay. 

Iway annotcay uessgay owhay anymay aysday avehay assedpay incesay enthay, utbay Iway avehay enduredway 
iserymay ichwhay othingnay utbay ethay eternalway entimentsay ofway away ustjay etributionray 
urningbay ithinway ymay earthay ouldcay avehay enabledway emay otay upportsay. Immenseway andway 
uggedray ountainsmay ofway iceway oftenway arredbay upway ymay assagepay, andway Iway oftenway eardhay 
ethay underthay ofway ethay oundgray easay, ichwhay eatenedthray ymay estructionday. Utbay 
againway ethay ostfray amecay andway ademay ethay athspay ofway ethay easay ecuresay. 

Ybay ethay uantityqay ofway ovisionpray ichwhay Iway adhay onsumedcay, Iway ouldshay uessgay atthay 
Iway adhay assedpay eethray eeksway inway isthay ourneyjay; andway ethay ontinualcay otractionpray 
ofway opehay, eturningray ackbay uponway ethay earthay, oftenway ungwray itterbay opsdray ofway 
espondencyday andway iefgray omfray ymay eyesway. Espairday adhay indeedway almostway ecuredsay 
erhay eypray, andway Iway ouldshay oonsay avehay unksay eneathbay isthay iserymay. Onceway, afterway 
ethay oorpay animalsway atthay onveyedcay emay adhay ithway incredibleway oiltay ainedgay ethay 
ummitsay ofway away opingslay iceway ountainmay, andway oneway, inkingsay underway ishay atiguefay, 
iedday, Iway iewedvay ethay expanseway eforebay emay ithway anguishway, enwhay uddenlysay ymay eyeway 
aughtcay away arkday eckspay uponway ethay uskyday ainplay. Iway ainedstray ymay ightsay otay 
iscoverday atwhay itway ouldcay ebay andway utteredway away ildway ycray ofway ecstasyway enwhay Iway 
istinguishedday away edgeslay andway ethay istortedday oportionspray ofway away ellway-known 
ormfay ithinway. Ohway! Ithway atwhay away urningbay ushgay idday opehay evisitray ymay earthay! 
Armway earstay illedfay ymay eyesway, ichwhay Iway astilyhay ipedway awayway, atthay eythay ightmay 
otnay interceptway ethay iewvay Iway adhay ofway ethay aemonday; utbay illstay ymay ightsay asway 
immedday ybay ethay urningbay opsdray, untilway, ivinggay ayway otay ethay emotionsway atthay 
oppressedway emay, Iway eptway aloudway. 

Utbay isthay asway otnay ethay imetay orfay elayday; Iway isencumberedday ethay ogsday ofway eirthay 
eadday ompanioncay, avegay emthay away entifulplay ortionpay ofway oodfay, andway afterway anway 
ourhay's estray, ichwhay asway absolutelyway ecessarynay, andway yetway ichwhay asway itterlybay 
irksomeway otay emay, Iway ontinuedcay ymay outeray. Ethay edgeslay asway illstay isiblevay, ornay 
idday Iway againway oselay ightsay ofway itway exceptway atway ethay omentsmay enwhay orfay away ortshay 
imetay omesay iceway-rock oncealedcay itway ithway itsway interveningway agscray. Iway indeedway 
erceptiblypay ainedgay onway itway, andway enwhay, afterway earlynay otway aysday' ourneyjay, Iway 
eheldbay ymay enemyway atway onay oremay anthay away ilemay istantday, ymay earthay oundedbay ithinway 
emay. 

Utbay ownay, enwhay Iway appearedway almostway ithinway aspgray ofway ymay oefay, ymay opeshay ereway 
uddenlysay extinguishedway, andway Iway ostlay allway acetray ofway imhay oremay utterlyway anthay Iway 
adhay everway oneday eforebay. Away oundgray easay asway eardhay; ethay underthay ofway itsway 
ogresspray, asway ethay atersway olledray andway elledsway eneathbay emay, ecamebay everyway 
omentmay oremay ominousway andway errifictay. Iway essedpray onway, utbay inway ainvay. Ethay indway 
aroseway; ethay easay oaredray; andway, asway ithway ethay ightymay ockshay ofway anway earthquakeway, 
itway itsplay andway ackedcray ithway away emendoustray andway overwhelmingway oundsay. Ethay 
orkway asway oonsay inishedfay; inway away ewfay inutesmay away umultuoustay easay olledray 
etweenbay emay andway ymay enemyway, andway Iway asway eftlay iftingdray onway away atteredscay iecepay 
ofway iceway atthay asway ontinuallycay esseninglay andway usthay eparingpray orfay emay away 
ideoushay eathday. Inway isthay annermay anymay appallingway ourshay assedpay; everalsay ofway 
ymay ogsday iedday, andway Iway yselfmay asway aboutway otay inksay underway ethay accumulationway ofway 
istressday enwhay Iway awsay yourway esselvay idingray atway anchorway andway oldinghay orthfay otay 
emay opeshay ofway uccoursay andway ifelay. Iway adhay onay onceptioncay atthay esselsvay everway 
amecay osay arfay orthnay andway asway astoundedway atway ethay ightsay. Iway uicklyqay estroyedday 
artpay ofway ymay edgeslay otay onstructcay oarsway, andway ybay esethay eansmay asway enabledway, 
ithway infiniteway atiguefay, otay ovemay ymay iceway aftray inway ethay irectionday ofway yourway 
ipshay. Iway adhay eterminedday, ifway youway ereway oinggay outhwardssay, illstay otay usttray 
yselfmay otay ethay ercymay ofway ethay eassay atherray anthay abandonway ymay urposepay. Iway 
opedhay otay induceway youway otay antgray emay away oatbay ithway ichwhay Iway ouldcay ursuepay ymay 
enemyway. Utbay yourway irectionday asway orthwardsnay. Youway ooktay emay onway oardbay enwhay 
ymay igourvay asway exhaustedway, andway Iway ouldshay oonsay avehay unksay underway ymay 
ultipliedmay ardshipshay intoway away eathday ichwhay Iway illstay eaddray, orfay ymay asktay isway 
unfulfilledway. 

Ohway! Enwhay illway ymay uidinggay iritspay, inway onductingcay emay otay ethay aemonday, allowway 
emay ethay estray Iway osay uchmay esireday; orway ustmay Iway ieday, andway ehay yetway ivelay? Ifway Iway oday, 
earsway otay emay, Altonway, atthay ehay allshay otnay escapeway, atthay youway illway eeksay imhay 
andway atisfysay ymay engeancevay inway ishay eathday. Andway oday Iway areday otay askway ofway youway otay 
undertakeway ymay ilgrimagepay, otay endureway ethay ardshipshay atthay Iway avehay undergoneway? 
Onay; Iway amway otnay osay elfishsay. Yetway, enwhay Iway amway eadday, ifway ehay ouldshay appearway, ifway 
ethay inistersmay ofway engeancevay ouldshay onductcay imhay otay youway, earsway atthay ehay 
allshay otnay ivelay--swear atthay ehay allshay otnay iumphtray overway ymay accumulatedway 
oesway andway urvivesay otay addway otay ethay istlay ofway ishay arkday imescray. Ehay isway eloquentway 
andway ersuasivepay, andway onceway ishay ordsway adhay evenway owerpay overway ymay earthay; utbay 
usttray imhay otnay. Ishay oulsay isway asway ellishhay asway ishay ormfay, ullfay ofway eacherytray 
andway iendfay-like alicemay. Earhay imhay otnay; allcay onway ethay amesnay ofway Illiamway, 
Ustinejay, Ervalclay, Elizabethway, ymay atherfay, andway ofway ethay etchedwray Ictorvay, andway 
ustthray yourway ordsway intoway ishay earthay. Iway illway overhay earnay andway irectday ethay 
eelstay arightway. 


Altonway, inway ontinuationcay. 



Augustway 26thay, 17-- 


Youway avehay eadray isthay angestray andway errifictay orystay, Argaretmay; andway oday youway otnay 
eelfay yourway oodblay ongealcay ithway orrorhay, ikelay atthay ichwhay evenway ownay urdlescay 
inemay? Ometimessay, eizedsay ithway uddensay agonyway, ehay ouldcay otnay ontinuecay ishay 
aletay; atway othersway, ishay oicevay okenbray, yetway iercingpay, utteredway ithway 
ifficultyday ethay ordsway osay epleteray ithway anguishway. Ishay inefay andway ovelylay eyesway 
ereway ownay ightedlay upway ithway indignationway, ownay ubduedsay otay owncastday orrowsay 
andway uenchedqay inway infiniteway etchednesswray. Ometimessay ehay ommandedcay ishay 
ountenancecay andway onestay andway elatedray ethay ostmay orriblehay incidentsway ithway away 
anquiltray oicevay, uppressingsay everyway arkmay ofway agitationway; enthay, ikelay away 
olcanovay urstingbay orthfay, ishay acefay ouldway uddenlysay angechay otay anway expressionway 
ofway ethay ildestway ageray asway ehay iekedshray outway imprecationsway onway ishay ersecutorpay. 

Ishay aletay isway onnectedcay andway oldtay ithway anway appearanceway ofway ethay implestsay 
uthtray, yetway Iway ownway otay youway atthay ethay etterslay ofway Elixfay andway Afiesay, ichwhay ehay 
owedshay emay, andway ethay apparitionway ofway ethay onstermay eensay omfray ourway ipshay, 
oughtbray otay emay away eatergray onvictioncay ofway ethay uthtray ofway ishay arrativenay anthay 
ishay asseverationsway, oweverhay earnestway andway onnectedcay. Uchsay away onstermay ashay, 
enthay, eallyray existenceway! Iway annotcay oubtday itway, yetway Iway amway ostlay inway urprisesay 
andway admirationway. Ometimessay Iway endeavouredway otay aingay omfray Ankensteinfray ethay 
articularspay ofway ishay eaturecray's ormationfay, utbay onway isthay ointpay ehay asway 
impenetrableway. "Areway youway admay, ymay iendfray?" aidsay ehay. "Orway itherwhay oesday yourway 
enselesssay uriositycay eadlay youway? Ouldway youway alsoway eatecray orfay yourselfway andway 
ethay orldway away emoniacalday enemyway? Eacepay, eacepay! Earnlay ymay iseriesmay andway oday 
otnay eeksay otay increaseway yourway ownway." Ankensteinfray iscoveredday atthay Iway ademay 
otesnay oncerningcay ishay istoryhay; ehay askedway otay eesay emthay andway enthay imselfhay 
orrectedcay andway augmentedway emthay inway anymay acesplay, utbay incipallypray inway ivinggay 
ethay ifelay andway iritspay otay ethay onversationscay ehay eldhay ithway ishay enemyway. "Incesay 
youway avehay eservedpray ymay arrationnay," aidsay ehay, "Iway ouldway otnay atthay away 
utilatedmay oneway ouldshay ogay ownday otay osteritypay." 

Usthay ashay away eekway assedpay awayway, ilewhay Iway avehay istenedlay otay ethay angeststray 
aletay atthay everway imaginationway ormedfay. Ymay oughtsthay andway everyway eelingfay ofway ymay 
oulsay avehay eenbay unkdray upway ybay ethay interestway orfay ymay uestgay ichwhay isthay aletay 
andway ishay ownway elevatedway andway entlegay annersmay avehay eatedcray. Iway ishway otay oothesay 
imhay, yetway ancay Iway ounselcay oneway osay infinitelyway iserablemay, osay estituteday ofway 
everyway opehay ofway onsolationcay, otay ivelay? Ohway, onay! Ethay onlyway oyjay atthay ehay ancay 
ownay owknay illway ebay enwhay ehay omposescay ishay atteredshay iritspay otay eacepay andway 
eathday. Yetway ehay enjoysway oneway omfortcay, ethay offspringway ofway olitudesay andway 
eliriumday; ehay elievesbay atthay enwhay inway eamsdray ehay oldshay onversecay ithway ishay 
iendsfray andway erivesday omfray atthay ommunioncay onsolationcay orfay ishay iseriesmay orway 
excitementsway otay ishay engeancevay, atthay eythay areway otnay ethay eationscray ofway ishay 
ancyfay, utbay ethay eingsbay emselvesthay owhay isitvay imhay omfray ethay egionsray ofway away 
emoteray orldway. Isthay aithfay ivesgay away olemnitysay otay ishay everiesray atthay enderray 
emthay otay emay almostway asway imposingway andway interestingway asway uthtray. 

Ourway onversationscay areway otnay alwaysway onfinedcay otay ishay ownway istoryhay andway 
isfortunesmay. Onway everyway ointpay ofway eneralgay iteraturelay ehay isplaysday 
unboundedway owledgeknay andway away uickqay andway iercingpay apprehensionway. Ishay 
eloquenceway isway orciblefay andway ouchingtay; ornay ancay Iway earhay imhay, enwhay ehay elatesray 
away atheticpay incidentway orway endeavoursway otay ovemay ethay assionspay ofway itypay orway ovelay, 
ithoutway earstay. Atwhay away oriousglay eaturecray ustmay ehay avehay eenbay inway ethay aysday 
ofway ishay osperitypray, enwhay ehay isway usthay oblenay andway odlikegay inway uinray! Ehay eemssay 
otay eelfay ishay ownway orthway andway ethay eatnessgray ofway ishay allfay. 

"Enwhay youngerway," aidsay ehay, "Iway elievedbay yselfmay estinedday orfay omesay eatgray 
enterpriseway. Ymay eelingsfay areway ofoundpray, utbay Iway ossessedpay away oolnesscay ofway 
udgmentjay atthay ittedfay emay orfay illustriousway achievementsway. Isthay entimentsay 
ofway ethay orthway ofway ymay aturenay upportedsay emay enwhay othersway ouldway avehay eenbay 
oppressedway, orfay Iway eemedday itway iminalcray otay owthray awayway inway uselessway iefgray 
osethay alentstay atthay ightmay ebay usefulway otay ymay ellowfay eaturescray. Enwhay Iway 
eflectedray onway ethay orkway Iway adhay ompletedcay, onay esslay away oneway anthay ethay eationcray 
ofway away ensitivesay andway ationalray animalway, Iway ouldcay otnay ankray yselfmay ithway ethay 
erdhay ofway ommoncay ojectorspray. Utbay isthay oughtthay, ichwhay upportedsay emay inway ethay 
ommencementcay ofway ymay areercay, ownay ervessay onlyway otay ungeplay emay owerlay inway ethay 
ustday. Allway ymay eculationsspay andway opeshay areway asway othingnay, andway ikelay ethay 
archangelway owhay aspiredway otay omnipotenceway, Iway amway ainedchay inway anway eternalway ellhay. 
Ymay imaginationway asway ividvay, yetway ymay owerspay ofway analysisway andway applicationway 
ereway intenseway; ybay ethay unionway ofway esethay ualitiesqay Iway onceivedcay ethay ideaway andway 
executedway ethay eationcray ofway away anmay. Evenway ownay Iway annotcay ecollectray ithoutway 
assionpay ymay everiesray ilewhay ethay orkway asway incompleteway. Iway odtray eavenhay inway ymay 
oughtsthay, ownay exultingway inway ymay owerspay, ownay urningbay ithway ethay ideaway ofway eirthay 
effectsway. Omfray ymay infancyway Iway asway imbuedway ithway ighhay opeshay andway away oftylay 
ambitionway; utbay owhay amway Iway unksay! Ohway! Ymay iendfray, ifway youway adhay ownknay emay asway Iway 
onceway asway, youway ouldway otnay ecognizeray emay inway isthay atestay ofway egradationday. 
Espondencyday arelyray isitedvay ymay earthay; away ighhay estinyday eemedsay otay earbay emay 
onway, untilway Iway ellfay, evernay, evernay againway otay iseray." Ustmay Iway enthay oselay isthay 
admirableway eingbay? Iway avehay ongedlay orfay away iendfray; Iway avehay oughtsay oneway owhay 
ouldway ympathizesay ithway andway ovelay emay. Eholdbay, onway esethay esertday eassay Iway avehay 
oundfay uchsay away oneway, utbay Iway earfay Iway avehay ainedgay imhay onlyway otay owknay ishay aluevay 
andway oselay imhay. Iway ouldway econcileray imhay otay ifelay, utbay ehay epulsesray ethay ideaway. 

"Iway ankthay youway, Altonway," ehay aidsay, "orfay yourway indkay intentionsway owardstay osay 
iserablemay away etchwray; utbay enwhay youway eakspay ofway ewnay iestay andway eshfray 
affectionsway, inkthay youway atthay anyway ancay eplaceray osethay owhay areway onegay? Ancay anyway 
anmay ebay otay emay asway Ervalclay asway, orway anyway omanway anotherway Elizabethway? Evenway 
erewhay ethay affectionsway areway otnay onglystray ovedmay ybay anyway uperiorsay excellenceway, 
ethay ompanionscay ofway ourway ildhoodchay alwaysway ossesspay away ertaincay owerpay overway ourway 
indsmay ichwhay ardlyhay anyway aterlay iendfray ancay obtainway. Eythay owknay ourway 
infantineway ispositionsday, ichwhay, oweverhay eythay aymay ebay afterwardsway odifiedmay, 
areway evernay eradicatedway; andway eythay ancay udgejay ofway ourway actionsway ithway oremay 
ertaincay onclusionscay asway otay ethay integrityway ofway ourway otivesmay. Away istersay orway away 
otherbray ancay evernay, unlessway indeedway uchsay ymptomssay avehay eenbay ownshay earlyway, 
uspectsay ethay otherway ofway audfray orway alsefay ealingday, enwhay anotherway iendfray, 
oweverhay onglystray ehay aymay ebay attachedway, aymay, inway itespay ofway imselfhay, ebay 
ontemplatedcay ithway uspicionsay. Utbay Iway enjoyedway iendsfray, earday otnay onlyway 
oughthray abithay andway associationway, utbay omfray eirthay ownway eritsmay; andway ereverwhay 
Iway amway, ethay oothingsay oicevay ofway ymay Elizabethway andway ethay onversationcay ofway 
Ervalclay illway ebay everway isperedwhay inway ymay earway. Eythay areway eadday, andway utbay oneway 
eelingfay inway uchsay away olitudesay ancay ersuadepay emay otay eservepray ymay ifelay. Ifway Iway 
ereway engagedway inway anyway ighhay undertakingway orway esignday, aughtfray ithway extensiveway 
utilityway otay ymay ellowfay eaturescray, enthay ouldcay Iway ivelay otay ulfilfay itway. Utbay 
uchsay isway otnay ymay estinyday; Iway ustmay ursuepay andway estroyday ethay eingbay otay omwhay Iway 
avegay existenceway; enthay ymay otlay onway earthway illway ebay ulfilledfay andway Iway aymay ieday." 




Eptembersay 2nday 

Ymay elovedbay Istersay, 

Iway itewray otay youway, encompassedway ybay erilpay andway ignorantway etherwhay Iway amway everway 
oomedday otay eesay againway earday Englandway andway ethay earerday iendsfray atthay inhabitway 
itway. Iway amway urroundedsay ybay ountainsmay ofway iceway ichwhay admitway ofway onay escapeway andway 
eatenthray everyway omentmay otay ushcray ymay esselvay. Ethay avebray ellowsfay omwhay Iway 
avehay ersuadedpay otay ebay ymay ompanionscay ooklay owardstay emay orfay aidway, utbay Iway avehay 
onenay otay estowbay. Erethay isway omethingsay erriblytay appallingway inway ourway 
ituationsay, yetway ymay ouragecay andway opeshay oday otnay esertday emay. Yetway itway isway 
erribletay otay eflectray atthay ethay iveslay ofway allway esethay enmay areway endangeredway 
oughthray emay. Ifway eway areway ostlay, ymay admay emesschay areway ethay ausecay. 

Andway atwhay, Argaretmay, illway ebay ethay atestay ofway yourway indmay? Youway illway otnay earhay 
ofway ymay estructionday, andway youway illway anxiouslyway awaitway ymay eturnray. Yearsway illway 
asspay, andway youway illway avehay isitingsvay ofway espairday andway yetway ebay orturedtay ybay 
opehay. Ohway! Ymay elovedbay istersay, ethay ickeningsay ailingfay ofway yourway earthay-felt 
expectationsway isway, inway ospectpray, oremay erribletay otay emay anthay ymay ownway eathday. 

Utbay youway avehay away usbandhay andway ovelylay ildrenchay; youway aymay ebay appyhay. Eavenhay 
essblay youway andway akemay youway osay! 

Ymay unfortunateway uestgay egardsray emay ithway ethay enderesttay ompassioncay. Ehay 
endeavoursway otay illfay emay ithway opehay andway alkstay asway ifway ifelay ereway away ossessionpay 
ichwhay ehay aluedvay. Ehay emindsray emay owhay oftenway ethay amesay accidentsway avehay 
appenedhay otay otherway avigatorsnay owhay avehay attemptedway isthay easay, andway inway itespay 
ofway yselfmay, ehay illsfay emay ithway eerfulchay auguriesway. Evenway ethay ailorssay eelfay 
ethay owerpay ofway ishay eloquenceway; enwhay ehay eaksspay, eythay onay ongerlay espairday; ehay 
ousesray eirthay energiesway, andway ilewhay eythay earhay ishay oicevay eythay elievebay esethay 
astvay ountainsmay ofway iceway areway olemay-hills ichwhay illway anishvay eforebay ethay 
esolutionsray ofway anmay. Esethay eelingsfay areway ansitorytray; eachway ayday ofway 
expectationway elayedday illsfay emthay ithway earfay, andway Iway almostway eaddray away utinymay 
ausedcay ybay isthay espairday. 



Eptembersay 5thay 


Away enescay ashay ustjay assedpay ofway uchsay uncommonway interestway atthay, althoughway itway isway 
ighlyhay obablepray atthay esethay aperspay aymay evernay eachray youway, yetway Iway annotcay 
orbearfay ecordingray itway. 

Eway areway illstay urroundedsay ybay ountainsmay ofway iceway, illstay inway imminentway angerday 
ofway eingbay ushedcray inway eirthay onflictcay. Ethay oldcay isway excessiveway, andway anymay ofway 
ymay unfortunateway omradescay avehay alreadyway oundfay away avegray amidstway isthay enescay ofway 
esolationday. Ankensteinfray ashay ailyday eclinedday inway ealthhay; away everishfay irefay 
illstay immersglay inway ishay eyesway, utbay ehay isway exhaustedway, andway enwhay uddenlysay 
ousedray otay anyway exertionway, ehay eedilyspay inkssay againway intoway apparentway 
ifelessnesslay. 

Iway entionedmay inway ymay astlay etterlay ethay earsfay Iway entertainedway ofway away utinymay. 
Isthay orningmay, asway Iway atsay atchingway ethay anway ountenancecay ofway ymay iendfray--his 
eyesway alfhay osedclay andway ishay imbslay anginghay istlesslylay--I asway ousedray ybay alfhay 
away ozenday ofway ethay ailorssay, owhay emandedday admissionway intoway ethay abincay. Eythay 
enteredway, andway eirthay eaderlay addressedway emay. Ehay oldtay emay atthay ehay andway ishay 
ompanionscay adhay eenbay osenchay ybay ethay otherway ailorssay otay omecay inway eputationday 
otay emay otay akemay emay away equisitionray ichwhay, inway usticejay, Iway ouldcay otnay efuseray. 
Eway ereway immuredway inway iceway andway ouldshay obablypray evernay escapeway, utbay eythay 
earedfay atthay ifway, asway asway ossiblepay, ethay iceway ouldshay issipateday andway away eefray 
assagepay ebay openedway, Iway ouldshay ebay ashray enoughway otay ontinuecay ymay oyagevay andway 
eadlay emthay intoway eshfray angersday, afterway eythay ightmay appilyhay avehay urmountedsay 
isthay. Eythay insistedway, ereforethay, atthay Iway ouldshay engageway ithway away olemnsay 
omisepray atthay ifway ethay esselvay ouldshay ebay eedfray Iway ouldway instantlyway irectday ymay 
oursecay outhwardssay. 

Isthay eechspay oubledtray emay. Iway adhay otnay espairedday, ornay adhay Iway yetway onceivedcay 
ethay ideaway ofway eturningray ifway etsay eefray. Yetway ouldcay Iway, inway usticejay, orway evenway inway 
ossibilitypay, efuseray isthay emandday? Iway esitatedhay eforebay Iway answeredway, enwhay 
Ankensteinfray, owhay adhay atway irstfay eenbay ilentsay, andway indeedway appearedway ardlyhay 
otay avehay orcefay enoughway otay attendway, ownay ousedray imselfhay; ishay eyesway arkledspay, 
andway ishay eekschay ushedflay ithway omentarymay igourvay. Urningtay owardstay ethay enmay, 
ehay aidsay, "Atwhay oday youway eanmay? Atwhay oday youway emandday ofway yourway aptaincay? Areway 
youway, enthay, osay easilyway urnedtay omfray yourway esignday? Idday youway otnay allcay isthay away 
oriousglay expeditionway? 

"Andway ereforewhay asway itway oriousglay? Otnay ecausebay ethay ayway asway oothsmay andway 
acidplay asway away outhernsay easay, utbay ecausebay itway asway ullfay ofway angersday andway 
errortay, ecausebay atway everyway ewnay incidentway yourway ortitudefay asway otay ebay alledcay 
orthfay andway yourway ouragecay exhibitedway, ecausebay angerday andway eathday urroundedsay 
itway, andway esethay youway ereway otay avebray andway overcomeway. Orfay isthay asway itway away 
oriousglay, orfay isthay asway itway anway onourablehay undertakingway. Youway ereway 
ereafterhay otay ebay ailedhay asway ethay enefactorsbay ofway yourway eciesspay, yourway amesnay 
adoredway asway elongingbay otay avebray enmay owhay encounteredway eathday orfay onourhay andway 
ethay enefitbay ofway ankindmay. Andway ownay, eholdbay, ithway ethay irstfay imaginationway ofway 
angerday, orway, ifway youway illway, ethay irstfay ightymay andway errifictay ialtray ofway yourway 
ouragecay, youway inkshray awayway andway areway ontentcay otay ebay andedhay ownday asway enmay owhay 
adhay otnay engthstray enoughway otay endureway oldcay andway erilpay; andway osay, oorpay oulssay, 
eythay ereway illychay andway eturnedray otay eirthay armway iresidesfay. Ywhay, atthay 
equiresray otnay isthay eparationpray; yeway eednay otnay avehay omecay usthay arfay andway 
aggeddray yourway aptaincay otay ethay ameshay ofway away efeatday erelymay otay ovepray 
yourselvesway owardscay. Ohway! Ebay enmay, orway ebay oremay anthay enmay. Ebay eadystay otay 
yourway urposespay andway irmfay asway away ockray. Isthay iceway isway otnay ademay ofway uchsay uffstay asway 
yourway eartshay aymay ebay; itway isway utablemay andway annotcay ithstandway youway ifway youway aysay 
atthay itway allshay otnay. Oday otnay eturnray otay yourway amiliesfay ithway ethay igmastay ofway 
isgraceday arkedmay onway yourway owsbray. Eturnray asway eroeshay owhay avehay oughtfay andway 
onqueredcay andway owhay owknay otnay atwhay itway isway otay urntay eirthay acksbay onway ethay oefay." 
Ehay okespay isthay ithway away oicevay osay odulatedmay otay ethay ifferentday eelingsfay 
expressedway inway ishay eechspay, ithway anway eyeway osay ullfay ofway oftylay esignday andway 
eroismhay, atthay ancay youway onderway atthay esethay enmay ereway ovedmay? Eythay ookedlay atway 
oneway anotherway andway ereway unableway otay eplyray. Iway okespay; Iway oldtay emthay otay etireray 
andway onsidercay ofway atwhay adhay eenbay aidsay, atthay Iway ouldway otnay eadlay emthay artherfay 
orthnay ifway eythay enuouslystray esiredday ethay ontrarycay, utbay atthay Iway opedhay atthay, 
ithway eflectionray, eirthay ouragecay ouldway eturnray. Eythay etiredray andway Iway urnedtay 
owardstay ymay iendfray, utbay ehay asway unksay inway anguorlay andway almostway eprivedday ofway 
ifelay. 

Owhay allway isthay illway erminatetay, Iway owknay otnay, utbay Iway adhay atherray ieday anthay 
eturnray amefullyshay, ymay urposepay unfulfilledway. Yetway Iway earfay uchsay illway ebay ymay 
atefay; ethay enmay, unsupportedway ybay ideasway ofway oryglay andway onourhay, ancay evernay 
illinglyway ontinuecay otay endureway eirthay esentpray ardshipshay. 



Eptembersay 7thay 


Ethay ieday isway astcay; Iway avehay onsentedcay otay eturnray ifway eway areway otnay estroyedday. 
Usthay areway ymay opeshay astedblay ybay owardicecay andway indecisionway; Iway omecay ackbay 
ignorantway andway isappointedday. Itway equiresray oremay ilosophyphay anthay Iway ossesspay 
otay earbay isthay injusticeway ithway atiencepay. 



Eptembersay 12thay 


Itway isway astpay; Iway amway eturningray otay Englandway. Iway avehay ostlay ymay opeshay ofway utilityway 
andway oryglay; Iway avehay ostlay ymay iendfray. Utbay Iway illway endeavourway otay etailday esethay 
itterbay ircumstancescay otay youway, ymay earday istersay; andway ilewhay Iway amway aftedway 
owardstay Englandway andway owardstay youway, Iway illway otnay espondday. 

Eptembersay 9thay, ethay iceway eganbay otay ovemay, andway oaringsray ikelay underthay ereway 
eardhay atway away istanceday asway ethay islandsway itsplay andway ackedcray inway everyway 
irectionday. Eway ereway inway ethay ostmay imminentway erilpay, utbay asway eway ouldcay onlyway 
emainray assivepay, ymay iefchay attentionway asway occupiedway ybay ymay unfortunateway uestgay 
osewhay illnessway increasedway inway uchsay away egreeday atthay ehay asway entirelyway onfinedcay 
otay ishay edbay. Ethay iceway ackedcray ehindbay usway andway asway ivendray ithway orcefay 
owardstay ethay orthnay; away eezebray angspray omfray ethay estway, andway onway ethay 11thay ethay 
assagepay owardstay ethay outhsay ecamebay erfectlypay eefray. Enwhay ethay ailorssay awsay 
isthay andway atthay eirthay eturnray otay eirthay ativenay ountrycay asway apparentlyway 
assuredway, away outshay ofway umultuoustay oyjay okebray omfray emthay, oudlay andway 
onglay-continued. Ankensteinfray, owhay asway ozingday, awokeway andway askedway ethay 
ausecay ofway ethay umulttay. "Eythay outshay," Iway aidsay, "ecausebay eythay illway oonsay 
eturnray otay Englandway." 

"Oday youway, enthay, eallyray eturnray?" 

"Alasway! Yesway; Iway annotcay ithstandway eirthay emandsday. Iway annotcay eadlay emthay 
unwillinglyway otay angerday, andway Iway ustmay eturnray." 

"Oday osay, ifway youway illway; utbay Iway illway otnay. Youway aymay ivegay upway yourway urposepay, utbay 
inemay isway assignedway otay emay ybay eavenhay, andway Iway areday otnay. Iway amway eakway, utbay 
urelysay ethay iritsspay owhay assistway ymay engeancevay illway endowway emay ithway 
ufficientsay engthstray." Ayingsay isthay, ehay endeavouredway otay ingspray omfray ethay 
edbay, utbay ethay exertionway asway ootay eatgray orfay imhay; ehay ellfay ackbay andway aintedfay. 

Itway asway onglay eforebay ehay asway estoredray, andway Iway oftenway oughtthay atthay ifelay asway 
entirelyway extinctway. Atway engthlay ehay openedway ishay eyesway; ehay eathedbray ithway 
ifficultyday andway asway unableway otay eakspay. Ethay urgeonsay avegay imhay away omposingcay 
aughtdray andway orderedway usway otay eavelay imhay undisturbedway. Inway ethay eantimemay ehay 
oldtay emay atthay ymay iendfray adhay ertainlycay otnay anymay ourshay otay ivelay. 

Ishay entencesay asway onouncedpray, andway Iway ouldcay onlyway ievegray andway ebay atientpay. Iway 
atsay ybay ishay edbay, atchingway imhay; ishay eyesway ereway osedclay, andway Iway oughtthay ehay 
eptslay; utbay esentlypray ehay alledcay otay emay inway away eeblefay oicevay, andway iddingbay emay 
omecay earnay, aidsay, "Alasway! Ethay engthstray Iway eliedray onway isway onegay; Iway eelfay atthay 
Iway allshay oonsay ieday, andway ehay, ymay enemyway andway ersecutorpay, aymay illstay ebay inway 
eingbay. Inkthay otnay, Altonway, atthay inway ethay astlay omentsmay ofway ymay existenceway Iway 
eelfay atthay urningbay atredhay andway ardentway esireday ofway evengeray Iway onceway expressedway; 
utbay Iway eelfay yselfmay ustifiedjay inway esiringday ethay eathday ofway ymay adversaryway. 
Uringday esethay astlay aysday Iway avehay eenbay occupiedway inway examiningway ymay astpay 
onductcay; ornay oday Iway indfay itway amableblay. Inway away itfay ofway enthusiasticway adnessmay Iway 
eatedcray away ationalray eaturecray andway asway oundbay owardstay imhay otay assureway, asway arfay 
asway asway inway ymay owerpay, ishay appinesshay andway ellway-being. 

"Isthay asway ymay utyday, utbay erethay asway anotherway illstay aramountpay otay atthay. Ymay 
utiesday owardstay ethay eingsbay ofway ymay ownway eciesspay adhay eatergray aimsclay otay ymay 
attentionway ecausebay eythay includedway away eatergray oportionpray ofway appinesshay orway 
iserymay. Urgedway ybay isthay iewvay, Iway efusedray, andway Iway idday ightray inway efusingray, otay 
eatecray away ompanioncay orfay ethay irstfay eaturecray. Ehay owedshay unparalleledway 
alignitymay andway elfishnesssay inway evilway; ehay estroyedday ymay iendsfray; ehay evotedday 
otay estructionday eingsbay owhay ossessedpay exquisiteway ensationssay, appinesshay, 
andway isdomway; ornay oday Iway owknay erewhay isthay irstthay orfay engeancevay aymay endway. 
Iserablemay imselfhay atthay ehay aymay enderray onay otherway etchedwray, ehay oughtway otay 
ieday. Ethay asktay ofway ishay estructionday asway inemay, utbay Iway avehay ailedfay. Enwhay 
actuatedway ybay elfishsay andway iciousvay otivesmay, Iway askedway youway otay undertakeway ymay 
unfinishedway orkway, andway Iway enewray isthay equestray ownay, enwhay Iway amway onlyway inducedway 
ybay easonray andway irtuevay. 

"Yetway Iway annotcay askway youway otay enounceray yourway ountrycay andway iendsfray otay ulfilfay 
isthay asktay; andway ownay atthay youway areway eturningray otay Englandway, youway illway avehay 
ittlelay ancechay ofway eetingmay ithway imhay. Utbay ethay onsiderationcay ofway esethay 
ointspay, andway ethay ellway alancingbay ofway atwhay youway aymay esteemway yourway utiesday, Iway 
eavelay otay youway; ymay udgmentjay andway ideasway areway alreadyway isturbedday ybay ethay earnay 
approachway ofway eathday. Iway areday otnay askway youway otay oday atwhay Iway inkthay ightray, orfay Iway 
aymay illstay ebay isledmay ybay assionpay. 

"Atthay ehay ouldshay ivelay otay ebay anway instrumentway ofway ischiefmay isturbsday emay; inway 
otherway espectsray, isthay ourhay, enwhay Iway omentarilymay expectway ymay eleaseray, isway ethay 
onlyway appyhay oneway ichwhay Iway avehay enjoyedway orfay everalsay yearsway. Ethay ormsfay ofway 
ethay elovedbay eadday itflay eforebay emay, andway Iway astenhay otay eirthay armsway. Arewellfay, 
Altonway! Eeksay appinesshay inway anquillitytray andway avoidway ambitionway, evenway ifway itway 
ebay onlyway ethay apparentlyway innocentway oneway ofway istinguishingday yourselfway inway 
iencescay andway iscoveriesday. Yetway ywhay oday Iway aysay isthay? Iway avehay yselfmay eenbay 
astedblay inway esethay opeshay, yetway anotherway aymay ucceedsay." 

Ishay oicevay ecamebay ainterfay asway ehay okespay, andway atway engthlay, exhaustedway ybay ishay 
effortway, ehay anksay intoway ilencesay. Aboutway alfhay anway ourhay afterwardsway ehay 
attemptedway againway otay eakspay utbay asway unableway; ehay essedpray ymay andhay eeblyfay, andway 
ishay eyesway osedclay oreverfay, ilewhay ethay irradiationway ofway away entlegay ilesmay assedpay 
awayway omfray ishay ipslay. 

Argaretmay, atwhay ommentcay ancay Iway akemay onway ethay untimelyway extinctionway ofway isthay 
oriousglay iritspay? Atwhay ancay Iway aysay atthay illway enableway youway otay understandway ethay 
epthday ofway ymay orrowsay? Allway atthay Iway ouldshay expressway ouldway ebay inadequateway andway 
eeblefay. Ymay earstay owflay; ymay indmay isway overshadowedway ybay away oudclay ofway 
isappointmentday. Utbay Iway ourneyjay owardstay Englandway, andway Iway aymay erethay indfay 
onsolationcay. 

Iway amway interruptedway. Atwhay oday esethay oundssay ortendpay? Itway isway idnightmay; ethay 
eezebray owsblay airlyfay, andway ethay atchway onway eckday arcelyscay irstay. Againway erethay 
isway away oundsay asway ofway away umanhay oicevay, utbay oarserhay; itway omescay omfray ethay abincay 
erewhay ethay emainsray ofway Ankensteinfray illstay ielay. Iway ustmay ariseway andway examineway. 
Oodgay ightnay, ymay istersay. 

Eatgray Odgay! atwhay away enescay ashay ustjay akentay aceplay! Iway amway yetway izzyday ithway ethay 
emembranceray ofway itway. Iway ardlyhay owknay etherwhay Iway allshay avehay ethay owerpay otay 
etailday itway; yetway ethay aletay ichwhay Iway avehay ecordedray ouldway ebay incompleteway 
ithoutway isthay inalfay andway onderfulway atastrophecay. Iway enteredway ethay abincay erewhay 
aylay ethay emainsray ofway ymay illway-fated andway admirableway iendfray. Overway imhay unghay away 
ormfay ichwhay Iway annotcay indfay ordsway otay escribeday--gigantic inway aturestay, yetway 
uncouthway andway istortedday inway itsway oportionspray. Asway ehay unghay overway ethay offincay, 
ishay acefay asway oncealedcay ybay onglay ockslay ofway aggedray airhay; utbay oneway astvay andhay 
asway extendedway, inway olourcay andway apparentway exturetay ikelay atthay ofway away ummymay. Enwhay
