ehay eardhay ethay oundsay ofway ymay approachway, ehay easedcay otay utterway exclamationsway ofway 
iefgray andway orrorhay andway ungspray owardstay ethay indowway. Evernay idday Iway eholdbay away 
isionvay osay orriblehay asway ishay acefay, ofway uchsay oathsomelay yetway appallingway 
ideousnesshay. Iway utshay ymay eyesway involuntarilyway andway endeavouredway otay ecollectray 
atwhay ereway ymay utiesday ithway egardray otay isthay estroyerday. Iway alledcay onway imhay otay 
aystay. 

Ehay ausedpay, ookinglay onway emay ithway onderway, andway againway urningtay owardstay ethay 
ifelesslay ormfay ofway ishay eatorcray, ehay eemedsay otay orgetfay ymay esencepray, andway 
everyway eaturefay andway esturegay eemedsay instigatedway ybay ethay ildestway ageray ofway omesay 
uncontrollableway assionpay. 

"Atthay isway alsoway ymay ictimvay!" ehay exclaimedway. "Inway ishay urdermay ymay imescray areway 
onsummatedcay; ethay iserablemay eriessay ofway ymay eingbay isway oundway otay itsway oseclay! 
Ohway, Ankensteinfray! Enerousgay andway elfsay-devoted eingbay! Atwhay oesday itway availway 
atthay Iway ownay askway eethay otay ardonpay emay? Iway, owhay irretrievablyway estroyedday eethay 
ybay estroyingday allway outhay ovedstlay. Alasway! Ehay isway oldcay, ehay annotcay answerway 
emay." Ishay oicevay eemedsay uffocatedsay, andway ymay irstfay impulsesway, ichwhay adhay 
uggestedsay otay emay ethay utyday ofway obeyingway ethay yingday equestray ofway ymay iendfray inway 
estroyingday ishay enemyway, ereway ownay uspendedsay ybay away ixturemay ofway uriositycay andway 
ompassioncay. Iway approachedway isthay emendoustray eingbay; Iway aredday otnay againway 
aiseray ymay eyesway otay ishay acefay, erethay asway omethingsay osay aringscay andway unearthlyway 
inway ishay uglinessway. Iway attemptedway otay eakspay, utbay ethay ordsway iedday awayway onway ymay 
ipslay. Ethay onstermay ontinuedcay otay utterway ildway andway incoherentway 
elfsay-reproaches. Atway engthlay Iway atheredgay esolutionray otay addressway imhay inway away 
ausepay ofway ethay empesttay ofway ishay assionpay. 

"Yourway epentanceray," Iway aidsay, "isway ownay uperfluoussay. Ifway youway adhay istenedlay otay 
ethay oicevay ofway onsciencecay andway eededhay ethay ingsstay ofway emorseray eforebay youway adhay 
urgedway yourway iabolicalday engeancevay otay isthay extremityway, Ankensteinfray ouldway 
yetway avehay ivedlay." 

"Andway oday youway eamdray?" aidsay ethay aemonday. "Oday youway inkthay atthay Iway asway enthay 
eadday otay agonyway andway emorseray? Ehay," ehay ontinuedcay, ointingpay otay ethay orpsecay, 
"ehay ufferedsay otnay inway ethay onsummationcay ofway ethay eedday. Ohway! Otnay ethay 
entay-thousandth ortionpay ofway ethay anguishway atthay asway inemay uringday ethay 
ingeringlay etailday ofway itsway executionway. Away ightfulfray elfishnesssay urriedhay emay 
onway, ilewhay ymay earthay asway oisonedpay ithway emorseray. Inkthay youway atthay ethay 
oansgray ofway Ervalclay ereway usicmay otay ymay earsway? Ymay earthay asway ashionedfay otay ebay 
usceptiblesay ofway ovelay andway ympathysay, andway enwhay enchedwray ybay iserymay otay icevay 
andway atredhay, itway idday otnay endureway ethay iolencevay ofway ethay angechay ithoutway 
orturetay uchsay asway youway annotcay evenway imagineway. 

"Afterway ethay urdermay ofway Ervalclay Iway eturnedray otay Itzerlandsway, earthay-broken 
andway overcomeway. Iway itiedpay Ankensteinfray; ymay itypay amountedway otay orrorhay; Iway 
abhorredway yselfmay. Utbay enwhay Iway iscoveredday atthay ehay, ethay authorway atway onceway ofway 
ymay existenceway andway ofway itsway unspeakableway ormentstay, aredday otay opehay orfay 
appinesshay, atthay ilewhay ehay accumulatedway etchednesswray andway espairday uponway emay 
ehay oughtsay ishay ownway enjoymentway inway eelingsfay andway assionspay omfray ethay 
indulgenceway ofway ichwhay Iway asway oreverfay arredbay, enthay impotentway envyway andway itterbay 
indignationway illedfay emay ithway anway insatiableway irstthay orfay engeancevay. Iway 
ecollectedray ymay eatthray andway esolvedray atthay itway ouldshay ebay accomplishedway. Iway 
ewknay atthay Iway asway eparingpray orfay yselfmay away eadlyday orturetay, utbay Iway asway ethay 
aveslay, otnay ethay astermay, ofway anway impulseway ichwhay Iway etestedday yetway ouldcay otnay 
isobeyday. Yetway enwhay eshay iedday! Aynay, enthay Iway asway otnay iserablemay. Iway adhay 
astcay offway allway eelingfay, ubduedsay allway anguishway, otay iotray inway ethay excessway ofway ymay 
espairday. Evilway enceforththay ecamebay ymay oodgay. Urgedway usthay arfay, Iway adhay onay 
oicechay utbay otay adaptway ymay aturenay otay anway elementway ichwhay Iway adhay illinglyway 
osenchay. Ethay ompletioncay ofway ymay emoniacalday esignday ecamebay anway insatiableway 
assionpay. Andway ownay itway isway endedway; erethay isway ymay astlay ictimvay!" 

Iway asway atway irstfay ouchedtay ybay ethay expressionsway ofway ishay iserymay; yetway, enwhay Iway 
alledcay otay indmay atwhay Ankensteinfray adhay aidsay ofway ishay owerspay ofway eloquenceway 
andway ersuasionpay, andway enwhay Iway againway astcay ymay eyesway onway ethay ifelesslay ormfay ofway 
ymay iendfray, indignationway asway ekindledray ithinway emay. "Etchwray!" Iway aidsay. "Itway 
isway ellway atthay youway omecay erehay otay inewhay overway ethay esolationday atthay youway avehay 
ademay. Youway owthray away orchtay intoway away ilepay ofway uildingsbay, andway enwhay eythay areway 
onsumedcay, youway itsay amongway ethay uinsray andway amentlay ethay allfay. Ypocriticalhay 
iendfay! Ifway ehay omwhay youway ournmay illstay ivedlay, illstay ouldway ehay ebay ethay objectway, 
againway ouldway ehay ecomebay ethay eypray, ofway yourway accursedway engeancevay. Itway isway otnay 
itypay atthay youway eelfay; youway amentlay onlyway ecausebay ethay ictimvay ofway yourway 
alignitymay isway ithdrawnway omfray yourway owerpay." 

"Ohway, itway isway otnay usthay--not usthay," interruptedway ethay eingbay. "Yetway uchsay ustmay 
ebay ethay impressionway onveyedcay otay youway ybay atwhay appearsway otay ebay ethay urportpay ofway 
ymay actionsway. Yetway Iway eeksay otnay away ellowfay eelingfay inway ymay iserymay. Onay ympathysay 
aymay Iway everway indfay. Enwhay Iway irstfay oughtsay itway, itway asway ethay ovelay ofway irtuevay, 
ethay eelingsfay ofway appinesshay andway affectionway ithway ichwhay ymay olewhay eingbay 
overflowedway, atthay Iway ishedway otay ebay articipatedpay. Utbay ownay atthay irtuevay ashay 
ecomebay otay emay away adowshay, andway atthay appinesshay andway affectionway areway urnedtay intoway 
itterbay andway oathinglay espairday, inway atwhay ouldshay Iway eeksay orfay ympathysay? Iway amway 
ontentcay otay uffersay aloneway ilewhay ymay ufferingssay allshay endureway; enwhay Iway ieday, Iway 
amway ellway atisfiedsay atthay abhorrenceway andway opprobriumway ouldshay oadlay ymay emorymay. 
Onceway ymay ancyfay asway oothedsay ithway eamsdray ofway irtuevay, ofway amefay, andway ofway 
enjoymentway. Onceway Iway alselyfay opedhay otay eetmay ithway eingsbay owhay, ardoningpay ymay 
outwardway ormfay, ouldway ovelay emay orfay ethay excellentway ualitiesqay ichwhay Iway asway 
apablecay ofway unfoldingway. Iway asway ourishednay ithway ighhay oughtsthay ofway onourhay andway 
evotionday. Utbay ownay imecray ashay egradedday emay eneathbay ethay eanestmay animalway. Onay 
uiltgay, onay ischiefmay, onay alignitymay, onay iserymay, ancay ebay oundfay omparablecay otay 
inemay. Enwhay Iway unray overway ethay ightfulfray ataloguecay ofway ymay inssay, Iway annotcay 
elievebay atthay Iway amway ethay amesay eaturecray osewhay oughtsthay ereway onceway illedfay 
ithway ublimesay andway anscendenttray isionsvay ofway ethay eautybay andway ethay ajestymay ofway 
oodnessgay. Utbay itway isway evenway osay; ethay allenfay angelway ecomesbay away alignantmay 
evilday. Yetway evenway atthay enemyway ofway Odgay andway anmay adhay iendsfray andway associatesway 
inway ishay esolationday; Iway amway aloneway. 

"Youway, owhay allcay Ankensteinfray yourway iendfray, eemsay otay avehay away owledgeknay ofway ymay 
imescray andway ishay isfortunesmay. Utbay inway ethay etailday ichwhay ehay avegay youway ofway emthay 
ehay ouldcay otnay umsay upway ethay ourshay andway onthsmay ofway iserymay ichwhay Iway enduredway 
astingway inway impotentway assionspay. Orfay ilewhay Iway estroyedday ishay opeshay, Iway idday 
otnay atisfysay ymay ownway esiresday. Eythay ereway oreverfay ardentway andway avingcray; illstay 
Iway esiredday ovelay andway ellowshipfay, andway Iway asway illstay urnedspay. Asway erethay onay 
injusticeway inway isthay? Amway Iway otay ebay oughtthay ethay onlyway iminalcray, enwhay allway 
umankindhay innedsay againstway emay? Ywhay oday youway otnay atehay Elixfay, owhay ovedray ishay 
iendfray omfray ishay oorday ithway ontumelycay? Ywhay oday youway otnay execrateway ethay usticray 
owhay oughtsay otay estroyday ethay avioursay ofway ishay ildchay? Aynay, esethay areway irtuousvay 
andway immaculateway eingsbay! Iway, ethay iserablemay andway ethay abandonedway, amway anway 
abortionway, otay ebay urnedspay atway, andway ickedkay, andway ampledtray onway. Evenway ownay ymay 
oodblay oilsbay atway ethay ecollectionray ofway isthay injusticeway. 

"Utbay itway isway uetray atthay Iway amway away etchwray. Iway avehay urderedmay ethay ovelylay andway ethay 
elplesshay; Iway avehay angledstray ethay innocentway asway eythay eptslay andway aspedgray otay 
eathday ishay oatthray owhay evernay injuredway emay orway anyway otherway ivinglay ingthay. Iway 
avehay evotedday ymay eatorcray, ethay electsay ecimenspay ofway allway atthay isway orthyway ofway 
ovelay andway admirationway amongway enmay, otay iserymay; Iway avehay ursuedpay imhay evenway otay 
atthay irremediableway uinray. 

"Erethay ehay ieslay, itewhay andway oldcay inway eathday. Youway atehay emay, utbay yourway 
abhorrenceway annotcay equalway atthay ithway ichwhay Iway egardray yselfmay. Iway ooklay onway ethay 
andshay ichwhay executedway ethay eedday; Iway inkthay onway ethay earthay inway ichwhay ethay 
imaginationway ofway itway asway onceivedcay andway onglay orfay ethay omentmay enwhay esethay 
andshay illway eetmay ymay eyesway, enwhay atthay imaginationway illway aunthay ymay oughtsthay 
onay oremay. 

"Earfay otnay atthay Iway allshay ebay ethay instrumentway ofway uturefay ischiefmay. Ymay orkway 
isway earlynay ompletecay. Eithernay yoursway ornay anyway anmay's eathday isway eedednay otay 
onsummatecay ethay eriessay ofway ymay eingbay andway accomplishway atthay ichwhay ustmay ebay 
oneday, utbay itway equiresray ymay ownway. Oday otnay inkthay atthay Iway allshay ebay owslay otay 
erformpay isthay acrificesay. Iway allshay uitqay yourway esselvay onway ethay iceway aftray ichwhay 
oughtbray emay itherthay andway allshay eeksay ethay ostmay orthernnay extremityway ofway ethay 
obeglay; Iway allshay ollectcay ymay uneralfay ilepay andway onsumecay otay ashesway isthay 
iserablemay amefray, atthay itsway emainsray aymay affordway onay ightlay otay anyway uriouscay 
andway unhallowedway etchwray owhay ouldway eatecray uchsay anotherway asway Iway avehay eenbay. Iway 
allshay ieday. Iway allshay onay ongerlay eelfay ethay agoniesway ichwhay ownay onsumecay emay orway 
ebay ethay eypray ofway eelingsfay unsatisfiedway, yetway unquenchedway. Ehay isway eadday owhay 
alledcay emay intoway eingbay; andway enwhay Iway allshay ebay onay oremay, ethay eryvay emembranceray 
ofway usway othbay illway eedilyspay anishvay. Iway allshay onay ongerlay eesay ethay unsay orway 
arsstay orway eelfay ethay indsway ayplay onway ymay eekschay. 

"Ightlay, eelingfay, andway ensesay illway asspay awayway; andway inway isthay onditioncay ustmay Iway 
indfay ymay appinesshay. Omesay yearsway agoway, enwhay ethay imagesway ichwhay isthay orldway 
affordsway irstfay openedway uponway emay, enwhay Iway eltfay ethay eeringchay armthway ofway ummersay 
andway eardhay ethay ustlingray ofway ethay eaveslay andway ethay arblingway ofway ethay irdsbay, andway 
esethay ereway allway otay emay, Iway ouldshay avehay eptway otay ieday; ownay itway isway ymay onlyway 
onsolationcay. Ollutedpay ybay imescray andway orntay ybay ethay itterestbay emorseray, 
erewhay ancay Iway indfay estray utbay inway eathday? 

"Arewellfay! Iway eavelay youway, andway inway youway ethay astlay ofway umankindhay omwhay esethay 
eyesway illway everway eholdbay. Arewellfay, Ankensteinfray! Ifway outhay ertway yetway aliveway 
andway yetway erishedchay away esireday ofway evengeray againstway emay, itway ouldway ebay etterbay 
atiatedsay inway ymay ifelay anthay inway ymay estructionday. Utbay itway asway otnay osay; outhay 
idstday eeksay ymay extinctionway, atthay Iway ightmay otnay ausecay eatergray etchednesswray; 
andway ifway yetway, inway omesay odemay unknownway otay emay, outhay adsthay otnay easedcay otay inkthay 
andway eelfay, outhay ouldstway otnay esireday againstway emay away engeancevay eatergray anthay 
atthay ichwhay Iway eelfay. Astedblay asway outhay ertway, ymay agonyway asway illstay uperiorsay otay 
inethay, orfay ethay itterbay ingstay ofway emorseray illway otnay easecay otay ankleray inway ymay 
oundsway untilway eathday allshay oseclay emthay oreverfay. 

"Utbay oonsay," ehay iedcray ithway adsay andway olemnsay enthusiasmway, "Iway allshay ieday, andway 
atwhay Iway ownay eelfay ebay onay ongerlay eltfay. Oonsay esethay urningbay iseriesmay illway ebay 
extinctway. Iway allshay ascendway ymay uneralfay ilepay iumphantlytray andway exultway inway ethay 
agonyway ofway ethay orturingtay amesflay. Ethay ightlay ofway atthay onflagrationcay illway 
adefay awayway; ymay ashesway illway ebay eptsway intoway ethay easay ybay ethay indsway. Ymay iritspay 
illway eepslay inway eacepay, orway ifway itway inksthay, itway illway otnay urelysay inkthay usthay. 
Arewellfay." 

Ehay angspray omfray ethay abincay indowway asway ehay aidsay isthay, uponway ethay iceway aftray 
ichwhay aylay oseclay otay ethay esselvay. Ehay asway oonsay ornebay awayway ybay ethay avesway andway 
ostlay inway arknessday andway istanceday. 










Endway ofway ethay Ojectpray Utenberggay EBookway ofway Ankensteinfray, ybay 
Arymay Ollstonecraftway (Odwingay) Elleyshay
